-----title
商丘（宋城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='76c39eda091044aa9f15f9caa0a9498e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("76c39eda091044aa9f15f9caa0a9498e");'><span id='76c39eda091044aa9f15f9caa0a9498e_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年</a>　本年，被母嵇氏送往睢阳，由其舅父嵇颖教之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年</a>　本年，入应天府学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1020&endYear=1026')">1020-1026年</a>　本年，从学于舅父嵇颖。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4a396b82634d40f3ba4dd039111b8308_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a396b82634d40f3ba4dd039111b8308");'><span id='4a396b82634d40f3ba4dd039111b8308_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>，22岁</div><div id='4a396b82634d40f3ba4dd039111b8308' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　本年，居宋城。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8510c9210e8f4f4dbadea6e909ca9f5e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8510c9210e8f4f4dbadea6e909ca9f5e");'><span id='8510c9210e8f4f4dbadea6e909ca9f5e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1032')">1030-1032年</a>，24-26岁</div><div id='8510c9210e8f4f4dbadea6e909ca9f5e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　秋，古卞北游，作序宋之。作品：送古卞北游序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三四。）</span><div id='poem_1163458' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163458' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163458?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送古卞北游序<span class='inlineComment2'>（天圣八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163458")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163458_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163458'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163458'>昔六国时，赵之忧在秦，备在邻国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163458_comment'></div>李牧为赵将，守北边，顾独以其边民战，破匈奴，降东胡，灭澹林，尽牧之世，胡马不敢南下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163458_comment'></div>况举其国之力，又况用夫天下之力！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163458_comment'></div>然自楚汉相持，不暇北略，而冒顿始大，为中国敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163458_comment'></div>晋氏之微，小雅尽废，隋唐之际，更为盛衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163458_comment'></div>自石晋割我幽蓟，以自济于祸难，而冀方之地乃戎夏共处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163458_comment'></div>国家用文德怀远，以交好息民，于今三纪，天下安于太平，民不知战，公卿士人耻言兵事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163458_comment'></div>子常何哉，独留意于孙、吴家也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163458_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163458_comment'></div>诚得将如李牧辈，朝廷能尽其用，庙堂之上，智者谋之，复山北之地，雪中原百年之耻，系呼韩邪之颈，縻致阙下，使岁时贡贺如汉宣帝时，子行观之，其易难也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163458_comment'></div>凉风暮秋，木叶霜脱，砺长剑以自卫，冒北风而径去，惟我知子天下奇士，汗漫之伎无所施尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163458_comment'></div>酒酣日下，驾而将行，聊歌一引，以起其倦游之意云：夷夏不敌兮，乃古其然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163458_comment'></div>中国大耻兮，有石之迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163458_comment'></div>顾瞻幽蓟兮，崆峒之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163458_comment'></div>逝将去汝兮，相从来庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163458_comment'></div>太白宿兮箕尾宫，旄头北指兮虏地空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163458_comment'></div>念颇、牧之无所用兮，吁嗟奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163458_comment'></div>感子征兮永歌。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1163458_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年3月</a>　清明节，作感事诗。作品：辛未清明感事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辛未清明感事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495496")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495496'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495496'>二十四年流水东，早为名误逐飞蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495496'>事随过鸟去无迹，愁似浊醪倾更浓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495496'>好是把花歌北榭，更休提剑哭西风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495496'>壮心郁郁身牢落，几见中林鹤发翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495496_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495496'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年</a>　本年，在宋城，蔡齐归朝，有诗送之。作品：送内阁蔡公归阙。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_495351' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495351' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495351?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送内阁蔡公归阙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495351")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495351_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495351'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495351'>丰宫周旧宅，梁国汉东关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495351'>尹正司留钥，贤公出近班。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495351'>教条推爱利，滋蔓悉除删。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495351'>狭野耕桑急，终年狱市閒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495351'>燕申铃阁静，荣养彩衣斑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495351'>治迹经纶外，阴功造化间。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495351'>士林归北海，人望在东山。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495351'>一节遄趋召，西辕不可攀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495351'>前旌霜树晓，候骑古河湾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495351'>和气均生物，淳风复海寰。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495351'>具瞻知可副<span class='inlineComment2'>（季本、清抄本作具民瞻盖久）</span>，盛德致无艰。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495351'>他日开炉冶，馀功为铸颜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495351_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495351'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_495351_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　本年，在宋城，从学于舅父嵇颖。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='73082fb5dbdc4c71ba1af3fb14e4597c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("73082fb5dbdc4c71ba1af3fb14e4597c");'><span id='73082fb5dbdc4c71ba1af3fb14e4597c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>，41岁</div><div id='73082fb5dbdc4c71ba1af3fb14e4597c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年6月</a>　六月，受命为礼仪使，往南京奉安太祖、太宗、真宗神御。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4da141daffe44be7a8eb635429f528e9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4da141daffe44be7a8eb635429f528e9");'><span id='4da141daffe44be7a8eb635429f528e9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>，46岁</div><div id='4da141daffe44be7a8eb635429f528e9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年6月1日</a>　六月一日，在应天府居母丧，作文祭韩综。作品：祭紫微韩舍人文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163639' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163639?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭紫微韩舍人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年6月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163639")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163639_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163639'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163639'>维皇祐四年岁次壬辰，六月一日甲戌，具官某谨以清酌果羞之荐，致奠于亡友紫微韩君仲文之灵：维夏皋月，晓魄隅出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163639_comment'></div>明发不寐，悲缠心骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163639_comment'></div>念母氏之劬劳，复檀衣于兹日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163639_comment'></div>晨有使来，致君慰札，发函号读，怪非手笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163639_comment'></div>云感外寒，方偃诸室，口占书辞，意殊详密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163639_comment'></div>我弗以忧，谁不有疾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163639_comment'></div>缄报章而未遣，传凶问于奄忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163639_comment'></div>怛人事之无常，何变故之仓卒也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163639_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163639_comment'></div>惟我与君，义则友生，情犹天伦，忘形莫逆，写照存真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163639_comment'></div>音适埙篪之和，气袭茝兰之薰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163639_comment'></div>在明道之癸酉，始倾盖于京辇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163639_comment'></div>洎宝元之庚辰，并飞绥于文苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163639_comment'></div>钦才致之开敏，挹风局之通简；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163639_comment'></div>景行业之英实，味辞义之腴隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163639_comment'></div>何宴嬉之不同，谅趋舍之无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163639_comment'></div>会浃日以惊疏，朝异班而恨远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163639_comment'></div>岁困敦以南谪，同江淮之往蹇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163639_comment'></div>俄叨命于秣陵，君来司兮漕挽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163639_comment'></div>及春物之未阑，见画舻于津馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163639_comment'></div>挥醉袂以相属，觉迟景之遽短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163639_comment'></div>邈江山兮清旷，澹怀抱之摅展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163639_comment'></div>喜嘉召兮暮秋，帐石城兮饮饯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163639_comment'></div>久相望兮中流，君之舟兮已缓，策余马以独归，城鸦噪兮落晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163639_comment'></div>恃年华之未徂，奚离索之多叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163639_comment'></div>亦孰谓乎夫君，遂中天于此旦？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163639_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163639_comment'></div>人伦赏裁，嗟我不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163639_comment'></div>谓君器业，实时之英，必当机柄，而立功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163639_comment'></div>此盖公议，匪私交情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163639_comment'></div>甫庆掖垣之擢，方参法从之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163639_comment'></div>曾毫釐之未售，矧灵府之从衡！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163639_comment'></div>摧鹏翼于顺风，偾骥御于修程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163639_comment'></div>世大体兮多艰，天施化兮靡平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163639_comment'></div>惟才彦之不可多得，余哀君兮乃为圣朝与苍生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163639_comment'></div>哭之恸兮寝门，重余忧兮峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163639_comment'></div>指幻泡之起灭，彼真谛之论精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163639_comment'></div>纷物我兮异同，亦达观之齐冥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163639_comment'></div>惟延促兮妄立，缅胡为兮殇、彭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163639_comment'></div>寄余诚于一酹，时无忽于友声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163639_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1163639_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年7月1日</a>　七月一日，在应天府居母丧，作文祭范仲淹。作品：祭资政范侍郎文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163636' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163636' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163636?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭资政范侍郎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年7月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163636")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163636_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163636'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163636'>维皇祐四年岁次壬辰，七月甲辰朔，具官某谨以清酌果羞之奠，致祭于故资政殿学士、户部侍郎、赠兵部尚书范文正公之灵：呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163636_comment'></div>孔氏之门，四科高第，惟达者之十子，得圣人之一体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163636_comment'></div>猗嗟乎公，德行则充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163636_comment'></div>文学纯深，政事闳通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163636_comment'></div>风节是勉，名教是践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163636_comment'></div>玉气千寻，金精百鍊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163636_comment'></div>赤墀清规，正色谠辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163636_comment'></div>引义忼慨，主尊臣卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163636_comment'></div>夏戎不虔，文告弗悛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163636_comment'></div>付公萧斧，《诗》、《书》在边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163636_comment'></div>公允文武，威行士附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163636_comment'></div>革其鸮音，乱亦遄沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163636_comment'></div>复节还台，皇皇泰阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163636_comment'></div>缙绅谓言，股肱良哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163636_comment'></div>维直方大，熙帝之载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163636_comment'></div>古训是式，王猷亶迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163636_comment'></div>惟日孜孜，爱莫助之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163636_comment'></div>时望去朝，识者曰咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163636_comment'></div>比釐南夏，爰徙东社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163636_comment'></div>遘疠避剧，汝阴促驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163636_comment'></div>弥留泗滨，竟号车棼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163636_comment'></div>精气归天，复其清纯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163636_comment'></div>死生去来，于达奚哀？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163636_comment'></div>渠渠大厦，怛此栋摧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163636_comment'></div>公陪宰席，尝僚右掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163636_comment'></div>炳然丝纶，赏有馀色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163636_comment'></div>涛江汤汤，往袭遗芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163636_comment'></div>见公禾兴，德音未忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163636_comment'></div>念言薄祜，遭家艰疚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163636_comment'></div>莫适匍匐，殒涕如溜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163636_comment'></div>平生素琴，已矣知音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163636_comment'></div>寄衷一酹，髣髴垂临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163636_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1163636_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年8月4日</a>　八月四日，在应天府居母丧，作《祭张密学文》作品：祭张密学文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。张密学，名不详。）</span><div id='poem_1163641' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163641' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163641?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭张密学文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年8月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163641")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163641_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163641'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163641'>维皇祐四年岁次壬辰，八月癸酉朔，四日丙子，具官某谨以清酌果羞之奠，致祭于故京东西路安抚使、枢密直学士、给事中张公之灵：在《坤》六二，臣道之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163641_comment'></div>曰直方大，维德之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163641_comment'></div>公仕初艰，实勤素履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163641_comment'></div>肃以直内，有劲如矢，义以方外，其平如砥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163641_comment'></div>守长郡邑，忠恕恺悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163641_comment'></div>承介台省，清规远惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163641_comment'></div>陟降侍从，周密庄厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163641_comment'></div>斡输馈边，总戎在鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163641_comment'></div>宽国之忧，急民之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163641_comment'></div>知无不为，于公之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163641_comment'></div>闻无不革，于政之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163641_comment'></div>惟日不足，竭精尽瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163641_comment'></div>竟亏冲啬，以遘瘥沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163641_comment'></div>靡究志用，遽沦智气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163641_comment'></div>比者秣陵，尝踵风轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163641_comment'></div>帐軷津馆，徽音在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163641_comment'></div>洛师汶上，讯幐接置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163641_comment'></div>晤言未谐，素车倏至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163641_comment'></div>苴杖在庐，阻从吊位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163641_comment'></div>惨怛盈衷，寄兹一酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163641_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1163641_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163641'><span class='label'>按：</span>《乐全集》卷三五。又见《永乐大典》卷一四〇四六。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1163641_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='eb037d978b864c1aae19a17d29189bfd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb037d978b864c1aae19a17d29189bfd");'><span id='eb037d978b864c1aae19a17d29189bfd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1060')">1059-1060年</a>，53-54岁</div><div id='eb037d978b864c1aae19a17d29189bfd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年3月</a>　三月，在知应天府任，有谢上表。作品：南京谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1163300' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163300' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163300?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南京谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163300")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163300_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163300'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163300'>伏奉制命，除臣端明殿学士兼龙图阁学士、守尚书左丞、知应天府兼南京留守司，已于今月十日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163300_comment'></div>陪京分守，实王业之所基；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163300_comment'></div>故社言归，在仕游之为宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163300_comment'></div>肃膺期命，已布守条<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163300_comment'></div>伏念臣植性冥顽，逢时熙盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163300_comment'></div>荷圣神之眷察，繇文史以误知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163300_comment'></div>漫历岁华，荐承官乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163300_comment'></div>词垣、禁署，间黩详延；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163300_comment'></div>宪府、计筹，尝尘器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163300_comment'></div>斥麾去国，就日来朝，洎蒙右蜀之迁，复有大农之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163300_comment'></div>司均九式，顾调度以靡充；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163300_comment'></div>营职一心，亦勚勤而敢怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163300_comment'></div>叙升省辖，出领留都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163300_comment'></div>仍还籍于禁严，示推慈之渥洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163300_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下幽而必烛，覆以无私，隐其有不移之愚，俾之以自求之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163300_comment'></div>典兹宫钥之重，绰然里闬之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163300_comment'></div>顾莫称于恩光，徒有惭于委寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163300_comment'></div>抚心自省，当益励于乃修；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163300_comment'></div>有躯可捐，尚更图于所报。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1163300_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年11月</a>　十一月，在知应天府任，为冠日用撰墓志铭。作品：唐州桐柏县令上谷寇府君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1163614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐州桐柏县令上谷寇府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　嘉祐四年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163614")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163614'>府君讳日用，字□□，蓟人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163614_comment'></div>汉雍奴侯恂本上谷昌平著姓，佐光武成大业，后裔蕃于河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163614_comment'></div>五代晋高祖资契丹援立而赂以山后之地，幽蓟隔绝，君陷北鄙，不敢自晦，仕为应州节度判官、检校礼部郎中兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163614_comment'></div>太皇之北征也，先自拔归，得见行在，上甚佳赏，将不次旌擢，大臣有间言，又值王师无功而还，故君不蒙褒录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163614_comment'></div>久之，授绛州司理参军，后除抚州临川县主簿、宋州司理、莱州即墨令、唐州桐柏令，卒官，享年七十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163614_comment'></div>燕涿勃碣，其人精急懻忮，悲歌忼慨，矜夸功名，少礼文，事游侠，风谣气俗颇杂戎索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163614_comment'></div>君家世独传儒艺，曾祖德诚，以廉直立，名义不侵，重然诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163614_comment'></div>当唐季，诸侯专土，诈力相雄，争欲致于宾佐，莫之能屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163614_comment'></div>朝廷知其节，诏起为右补阙，一至京师，寻归老于家，当时河朔谓之高士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163614_comment'></div>祖安仁，以才略累历藩镇幕府，终于真定节度行军副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163614_comment'></div>父显赟，尤笃志于学，通经术，不肯仕，居乡里教授，齐鲁诸生更过河受业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163614_comment'></div>及终，门人诔行，追谥曰「有道先生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163614_comment'></div>君既归国，久困州县，喟然叹曰：「吾得违于北鄙，以至中原，谓有以发所蕴，今乃为禄仕乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163614_comment'></div>犹有民人焉，是亦足以为政矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163614_comment'></div>惟日孜孜，以诚心恤隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163614_comment'></div>始至绛，有重囚将决，察其辞色，若怀未尽者，徐以私问之，果大豪买直，掠服取竟，一讯情得，脱垂死之冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163614_comment'></div>凡再掌狱，尝分俸营餐剂济缧系之饥病者，至家无馀赀，去官不能就选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163614_comment'></div>即墨濒海，多豪桀，侵夺细民，收倍称之息，役恶少督责，势严官赋，君悉收其券焚之，乡闾为之一苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163614_comment'></div>凡历官专意贫弱，举多爱利，笃矣乎，仁者之心也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163614_comment'></div>惜乎势卑位微，不得行其志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163614_comment'></div>直躬孤官，莫或知其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163614_comment'></div>使得据土疆之大，抚吏民之众，政平讼理，推之慈惠，古之循吏何以尚兹！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163614_comment'></div>至性忠厚，动有规准，言无游饰，居无惰狎，凛凛然庶几古君子遗风者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163614_comment'></div>夫人高氏，淑慎克配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163614_comment'></div>子某，承教义方，再举进士，赠尚书职方员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163614_comment'></div>长孙平，时吉履休，有令望，历东京、淮南转运使，今以尚书工部郎中知徐州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163614_comment'></div>嘉祐四年，岁次在大渊献，十一月二十六日，始奉君輤帷即安垄兆，实颍川阳翟县之麦秀乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163614_comment'></div>工部少孤，艰勤自致，葬是以缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163614_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1163614'>崆峒阴方，勃碣边裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163614_comment'></div>俗本用武，人知尚气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163614_comment'></div>有美昌平，德名奕世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163614_comment'></div>补衮风节，隐居经义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163614_comment'></div>君初归朝，亶怀远志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163614_comment'></div>尺蠖之屈，干将莫试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163614_comment'></div>笃哉若人，循乎为吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163614_comment'></div>生虽逢时，壮图弗遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163614_comment'></div>没而不朽，孝孙是似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163614_comment'></div>勒铭幽堂，矢辞无愧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1163614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　春，在知应天府任，迁工部尚书、秦凤路兵马都部署、经略安抚使兼知秦州，上辞免奏状。作品：辞免知秦州奏状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163301' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163301' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163301?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免知秦州奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163301")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163301_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163301'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163301'>今月十九日，进奏院递到敕告一道，除臣工部尚书、秦凤路兵马都部署、经略安抚使兼知秦州者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163301_comment'></div>秦州重镇，尚书重官，伏蒙圣恩，俯及孤外，在臣虚薄，岂堪眷委？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163301_comment'></div>兼臣父年老，久患脚膝，不任骑乘，关陇山阻，实难迎侍远行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163301_comment'></div>敢望天慈，矜察情恳，特赐追寝新命，许令终满今任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163301_comment'></div>非但便臣庭闱之养，抑免误国方面之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163301_comment'></div>所降敕告，未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163301_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　春，在知应天府任，迁工部尚书、秦凤路兵马都部署、经略安抚使兼知秦州，上谢赐手诏表。作品：谢赐手诏第一表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163302' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163302' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163302?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐手诏第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163302")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163302_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163302'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163302'>今月初八日，进奏院递到赐臣诏敕一道，以臣奏陈为父老乞免秦州，满今任，不许辞免，便令受告敕发赴本任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163302_comment'></div>锡命自天，烜日星之下烛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163302_comment'></div>跼身无地，懔渊谷以内惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163302_comment'></div>进退徊徨，启居震恐<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163302_comment'></div>伏念臣性资疏拙，自奋单微，实乏出伦之才，误蒙不次之举，寅缘资历，跻躐显荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163302_comment'></div>向解计图，叨司留钥，荣归故里，养展私庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163302_comment'></div>曾微治效之闻，敢冀光灵之及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163302_comment'></div>伏蒙尊号皇帝陛下俯矜愚守，久缀近班，进文昌八座之联，委西州一面之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163302_comment'></div>惟是行能之下，忝兹推择之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163302_comment'></div>天地生成，曾未侔于全度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163302_comment'></div>形骸捐废，固莫报于深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163302_comment'></div>曷敢逡巡，妄为激洁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163302_comment'></div>但以臣父筋力已谢，齿发寖衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163302_comment'></div>孝德训人，不责便亲之请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163302_comment'></div>愧心即路，是专冒宠之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163302_comment'></div>被细札之丁宁，增懦衷之陨穫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163302_comment'></div>粗致其乐，愿伸一二之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163302_comment'></div>深察其情，傥宥再三之黩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1163302_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　春，在知应天府任，迁工部尚书、秦凤路兵马都部署、经略安抚使兼知秦州，再上辞免奏状。作品：辞免第二状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163303")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163303'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163303'>右，臣昨蒙圣恩除工部尚书知秦州，以父老患脚膝，难以迎侍远行，寻具奏陈，乞满今任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163303_comment'></div>今月八日，伏奉诏敕不许辞免，便令受告敕疾速发付本任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163303_comment'></div>臣已具表称谢外，敢倾私恳，再黩天威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163303_comment'></div>伏以宠命迁除，边方委寄，猥加虚薄，实冒恩荣，前所陈情，非缘矫激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163303_comment'></div>臣父年逾七十，脚膝早衰，跋履远行，艰于骑乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163303_comment'></div>臣去年外补，上荷天慈，陪都乡里，方安奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163303_comment'></div>今塞徼清谧，戎虏辑和，中外畯良，足备推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163303_comment'></div>敢祈宸造，俯遂微衷，特寝新除，许仍旧任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163303_comment'></div>荐烦睿听，敢逃罪责！</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1163303_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　春，在知应天府任，迁工部尚书、秦凤路兵马都部署、经略安抚使兼知秦州，再上谢赐手诏表。作品：谢赐手诏第二表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163304' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163304' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163304?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐手诏第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163304")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163304_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163304'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163304'>今月二十六日，进奏院递到赐臣诏书一道，不许辞免秦州，令依前命疾速赴任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163304_comment'></div>天听盖高，念微诚之难彻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163304_comment'></div>威光孔迩，感慈旨之下颁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163304_comment'></div>有愧拜嘉，尚祈得请<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163304_comment'></div>伏念臣材资至下，地望尤寒，幸遘熙辰，久尘清贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163304_comment'></div>出当方面，曾风迹以无闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163304_comment'></div>入总计图，顾事功之不立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163304_comment'></div>顷分留钥，获养私庭，未易岁筒，遽迁边阃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163304_comment'></div>中台喉舌之重，西藩斧戟之雄，朝寄非轻，宠光甚渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163304_comment'></div>在王臣之义，况无难而可辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163304_comment'></div>但人子之心，幸奉亲之为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163304_comment'></div>爰罄由衷之请，愿终奉计之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163304_comment'></div>荐叩公车，再窥方面，垂矜危悃，未寘严诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163304_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下舜孝格天，尧仁被世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163304_comment'></div>君使臣以礼，允昭德教之隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163304_comment'></div>臣承命为恭，甘俟典刑之及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163304_comment'></div>窃惟覆照，俯逮幽微，遂愚志于一夫，致欢心于万国。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1163304_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　春，在知应天府任，迁工部尚书、秦凤路兵马都部署、经略安抚使兼知秦州，三上辞免奏状。作品：辞免第三状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免第三状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163305")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163305'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163305'>右，臣昨蒙圣恩，除工部尚书、知秦州，以父老患脚膝，难以迎侍远行，再具奏陈，乞满今任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163305_comment'></div>今月二十六日复奉诏敕，不许辞免，令依前命疾速赴任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163305_comment'></div>臣已具表称谢外，窃惟愚诚，有所未尽，上烦聪听，遂至再三干黩天威，分当严宪，朝廷不以臣才下，付之方面，加宠而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163305_comment'></div>齿发尚壮，稍任剧使，奚事顾惮，妄为避免？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163305_comment'></div>但以父年高末弱，不堪乘骑，须至远冒炎暑，舆而就道，风气有隙，或以愆和，由臣贪冒恩荣，亏玷风教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163305_comment'></div>圣仁孝治，及人之老，区区危悃，敢祈矜亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163305_comment'></div>今月二十五日，赵槩已到本府交割公事管勾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163305_comment'></div>徐、济州并系京东，去南京不远，迎侍便近，伏望圣慈就移一郡，少安孤拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163305_comment'></div>臣见在本府祗听朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163305_comment'></div>君命至重，诏敕再降，臣不即祗受，自速典刑，不任战越待罪之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1163305_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　春，在知应天府任，迁工部尚书、秦凤路兵马都部署、经略安抚使兼知秦州，三上谢赐手诏表。作品：谢赐手诏第三表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐手诏第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163306")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163306'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163306'>今月十五日，进奏院递到诏敕一道赐臣，令依前降指挥发赴秦州本任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163306_comment'></div>需章沥恳，屡干旒扆之严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163306_comment'></div>温诏遣行，荐被丝纶之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163306_comment'></div>拜嘉优重，积虑兢惶<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163306_comment'></div>伏念臣向奉制函，亟更蕃棨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163306_comment'></div>文昌八座，进陟卿联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163306_comment'></div>陇坻一隅，俾专阃制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163306_comment'></div>退惟亲便，屡以诚陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163306_comment'></div>愿回涣汗之恩，少适循陔之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163306_comment'></div>愚衷所冀，宸鉴未俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163306_comment'></div>稽留一尺之书，合从吏讯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163306_comment'></div>继奉十行之札，仍促驾行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163306_comment'></div>祗觌褒章，实增厚愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163306_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下照临施普，覆载均休，远微一物之遗，慎择四方之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163306_comment'></div>眷存孤旧，预在选抡，示以大方，采其微效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163306_comment'></div>仰聆睿训，俯极腼颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163306_comment'></div>顾惟三渎之烦，实有再思之惧，敢不恪趋官守，躬布诏条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163306_comment'></div>揭节戒徒，指西州而即路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163306_comment'></div>瞻云结恋，望北阙以驰诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1163306_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5cd0db90283246229bb7c3b1d545f74b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5cd0db90283246229bb7c3b1d545f74b");'><span id='5cd0db90283246229bb7c3b1d545f74b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>，57岁</div><div id='5cd0db90283246229bb7c3b1d545f74b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年2月</a>　二月，在知应天府任，迁礼部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年7月</a>　七月，在知应天府任，为岳父马绛撰墓志铭。作品：朝奉郎守太常少卿权北京留守御史台公事上柱国扶风县开国男食邑三百户赐紫金鱼袋马公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷四〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163625' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163625' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163625?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉郎守太常少卿权北京留守御史台公事上柱国扶风县开国男食邑三百户赐紫金鱼袋马公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　嘉祐八年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163625")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163625_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163625'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163625'>公讳绛，字某，魏大名人，世仕魏军，为河朔豪杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163625_comment'></div>祖昭美，始易士服，读书养志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163625_comment'></div>父诰，举进士第，有器望，终于侍御史、知桂州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163625_comment'></div>公护𧚫车北还魏，至蔡毁甚，太夫人忧之，命留蔡，遂寓居汝阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163625_comment'></div>言忠信，行笃厚，蔡人重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163625_comment'></div>景德元年，诏下贡举，诸举子推公就试，守令劝驾，遂首荐登甲科，释褐试秘省校书郎、知婺州义乌县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163625_comment'></div>至则辟县扉，凡辨讼者径造于庭，为之别白是非，因勉之，以义教民，辄听命罢去，无复词牒，案牍大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163625_comment'></div>后数十年，父老犹有称道公名者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163625_comment'></div>再调寿州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163625_comment'></div>还赴铨集，引对御前，选补职事官，除莱州防御判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163625_comment'></div>时蔡文忠齐在诸生，未知名，公一见，曰：「海滨有此奇士」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163625_comment'></div>忘年定交，日与游，甚欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163625_comment'></div>是秋主试贡士，首送蔡公春榜，至蔡公冠天下士，公得知人之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163625_comment'></div>秩满，改著作佐郎，知永兴咸阳县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163625_comment'></div>就徙益州双流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163625_comment'></div>丁内艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163625_comment'></div>既除，迁秘书丞、知梧州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163625_comment'></div>公性刚直，不屈上官，耻为茍合，以是滞留，常调官不遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163625_comment'></div>尝曰：「吾资不适时，与其求容之辱，不若全吾道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163625_comment'></div>故于鄠杜终南圭峰之下，就水竹营别墅，为栖逸之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163625_comment'></div>及自岭外归，称疾罢官，慨然有丘壑之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163625_comment'></div>故枢相王文康公在西府，雅知公，蔡文忠公亦在内署，数勉公起还朝，相与称荐，遂以太常博士通判秦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163625_comment'></div>时河阳相王文穆公知州事，多回挠，公持法不阿，河阳不悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163625_comment'></div>僚佐为公言，宜姑为和，公曰：「守正之谓和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163625_comment'></div>朝廷置吏，岂使茍相顺适以为和哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163625_comment'></div>吾知奉公而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163625_comment'></div>内珰乘驿奏边事，承河阳指，阴诬中公，遂徙延州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163625_comment'></div>代还，知坊州，赐五品服章，就迁屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163625_comment'></div>蔡文忠公拜御史中丞，被命举御史，而以公名上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163625_comment'></div>时王河阳作相，三奏而三却之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163625_comment'></div>文忠怀敕至中书曰：「被旨举御史，某之所知无易马某，朝廷不用，请纳此敕」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163625_comment'></div>执政不得已，除公殿中侍御史，寻改侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163625_comment'></div>公素厉风节，及在司察之职，危言无顾惮，不为击抟悻悻近名事，称为知大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163625_comment'></div>稍迁兵部员外郎、三司户部判官，出为江南东路转运使，改工部郎中，徙京东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163625_comment'></div>巡按郡县，必为官吏言：「赋役狱市，生民之命所以舒惨者也，从政者知于是尽心焉，可以上副明主求理之意矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163625_comment'></div>复入领三司度支判官，擢授兵部郎中，赐三品服章，知梓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163625_comment'></div>还授知越州，改太常少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163625_comment'></div>公老于政事，练达人情，左蜀远方，东吴轻俗，因民所便，为之保息，条教清约，不严而治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163625_comment'></div>归阙，将请老，朝议为于北京置留司御史台，俾得归乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163625_comment'></div>庆历八年六月二十五日，考终于台寝，享年七十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163625_comment'></div>公在台省，王沂公、吕许公当国，重公方介有守，从容谓公：「直而温，宽而栗，所以成德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163625_comment'></div>君道少为委蛇，不亦裕欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163625_comment'></div>公曰：「良农能稼而不能穑，士固有志，违道干誉，非鄙志者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163625_comment'></div>其自守如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163625_comment'></div>孔子曰：「巧言、令色、足恭，左丘明耻之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163625_comment'></div>公可谓耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163625_comment'></div>又曰：「不曰坚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163625_comment'></div>磨而不磷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163625_comment'></div>不曰白乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163625_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1163625", 1163625, "Clauses/172/Comments/1")'>涅而不缁</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163625_comment'></div>公之志行有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163625_comment'></div>性清简少欲，菲衣食，家居对妻子，未尝易言色狎侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163625_comment'></div>惟好读书，素多目疾，而不能释卷，为子弟讲说常至夜分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163625_comment'></div>夫人孔氏，魏之名族，主客郎中毅之女，贤明有法义，后公十五年，年七十八以卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163625_comment'></div>二男：曰仲孙，秦州节度推官，早世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163625_comment'></div>曰孝孙，湖州观察推官、监泗州仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163625_comment'></div>二女：长适张氏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163625_comment'></div>次适刑部郎中、集贤校理王绎，先公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163625_comment'></div>嘉祐八年七月某日，孝孙克尽诚志，葬公、夫人于应天府宋城县之长乐乡，不归魏，公之里，命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163625_comment'></div>某早托姻媾，雅闻话言，纳铭泉扃，传信来裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163625_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1163625'>太常直清，浑然自成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163625_comment'></div>少私寡与，实性其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163625_comment'></div>学以从政，仕以行义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163625_comment'></div>不为利回，以湛世伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163625_comment'></div>如玉在涂，洁不可污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163625_comment'></div>如金在镕，坚不可渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163625_comment'></div>方正无疑，则犹蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163625_comment'></div>涤除明览，亦如冰鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163625_comment'></div>达道之士，命曰知本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163625_comment'></div>万物变迁，道奚有尽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163625_comment'></div>公之体魄，与物同尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163625_comment'></div>公之神明，斯还道真。</div><div id='poem_sentence_71_1163625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163625'><span class='label'>按：</span>《乐全集》卷四〇。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1163625_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='745695c313704af2860684d14eb715a5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("745695c313704af2860684d14eb715a5");'><span id='745695c313704af2860684d14eb715a5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1069')">1068-1069年</a>，62-63岁</div><div id='745695c313704af2860684d14eb715a5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　春，居乡丁父忧，上表乞免起复。作品：免起复除参知政事第一表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。系年据《乐全集》卷二八所附诏书。）</span><div id='poem_1163310' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163310' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163310?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免起复除参知政事第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163310")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163310_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163310'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163310'>今月某日，试秘书省校书郎、充睦亲广亲北宅小学教授蔡天申赍到诏书一道，授臣起复前官赴阙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163310_comment'></div>三年之制，天下之达丧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163310_comment'></div>终身之忧，人伦之大义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163310_comment'></div>承恩命之至重，在情理而匪安<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163310_comment'></div>伏念臣早冒宠荣，久尸禄养，无事功之可纪，积咎衅以为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163310_comment'></div>蒙圣神之误知，假名器而虚授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163310_comment'></div>上辜天造，莫效于涓埃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163310_comment'></div>不意慈亲，遽罹于祸酷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163310_comment'></div>怀兹钜痛，岂冀馀生？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163310_comment'></div>使传忽临，朝恩特降，举权宜之故事，爰追召以还朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163310_comment'></div>闻命哀迷，抚心悸慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163310_comment'></div>矧惟衔恤，甫此逾时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163310_comment'></div>孑然一身，未复同生之戚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163310_comment'></div>敢有二事，居然从利之为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163310_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下隐恻上仁，恫矜微志，绌夺情之弊典，惟致孝之永怀，特寝天恩，用敦本俗，许毕倚庐之慕，免累圣朝之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163310_comment'></div>蝼蚁之微，傥获终其所愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163310_comment'></div>犬马之力，期得尽于他时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163310_comment'></div>臣不胜号殒俟命激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163310_comment'></div>其诏书不敢捧承，谨令某人赍赴阙，于通进司投纳，兼奉表陈乞以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1163310_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　春，居乡丁父忧，再上表乞免起复。作品：免起复除参知政事第二表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。系年据《乐全集》卷二八所附诏书。）</span><div id='poem_1163311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免起复除参知政事第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163311")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163311'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163311'>今月某日，某官再赍赐诏书一道，授臣起复前官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163311_comment'></div>哀诚激切，未谅于清衷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163311_comment'></div>诏札丁宁，复申于明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163311_comment'></div>忧惶失措，悲哽莫胜，重沥恳情，冀垂察允<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163311_comment'></div>臣闻圣人制礼，愚者企而及之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163311_comment'></div>君子笃亲，天下从而化矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163311_comment'></div>顾鲰生之无状，蔑介善以自名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163311_comment'></div>昔自弱微，实勤力养，终鲜兄弟，素无田庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163311_comment'></div>徒用丐游，以给晨昏之事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163311_comment'></div>暨叨宦达，遂蒙根业之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163311_comment'></div>自念孤单，每怀喜惧，数陈情而闻请，求解职以便私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163311_comment'></div>顷复禁严，寖违志愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163311_comment'></div>先臣年虽耋老，气本清和，小爽起居之常，未切忧危之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163311_comment'></div>昨承宣对，垂谕选除，仰奉德音，已陈深恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163311_comment'></div>逮明廷之赞授，面法座以控辞，聪听不回，天心具照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163311_comment'></div>诚荷及亲之幸，遽罹过隙之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163311_comment'></div>退守几筵，甫更时序，岂期宸眷，猥降玺封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163311_comment'></div>承命不惶，悼心自失；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163311_comment'></div>上稽严旨，敢尽苦辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163311_comment'></div>伏念皇帝陛下大义爱人，深恩恕物，伸终祥禫，以报劬劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163311_comment'></div>则所守粗完，免作乱常之首；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163311_comment'></div>馀生未谢，永酬锡类之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163311_comment'></div>陨涕摧心，期于得请，臣无任号诉激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163311_comment'></div>其诏书不敢捧承，谨因蔡天申赍还赴阙，于通进司投纳，兼奉表陈乞以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1163311_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　春，居乡丁父忧，又上表乞免起复。作品：免起复除参知政事第三表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。系年据《乐全集》卷二八所附诏书。）</span><div id='poem_1163312' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163312' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163312?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免起复除参知政事第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163312")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163312_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163312'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163312'>今月二日，某官再赍赐诏书一道，授臣起复前官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163312_comment'></div>朝命至严，已辱再三之重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163312_comment'></div>私情所切，期伸万一之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163312_comment'></div>哀迫靡遑，矜从是幸<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163312_comment'></div>臣闻孔子曰：人鲜有能自致者，其惟父母之丧乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163312_comment'></div>故三年之制，天下之达礼，尊卑所同，古今不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163312_comment'></div>用纪人伦之厚，兹为王化之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163312_comment'></div>在国朝之制，繇庆历以还，近自亲贤，外通文武，悉优容于在疚，申钜创以尽情，岂独孤臣，敢忘大义？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163312_comment'></div>方圣神之独化，会杰俊以熙朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163312_comment'></div>群材并施，自成乎大厦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163312_comment'></div>一毛虽落，谁谓乎无牛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163312_comment'></div>曾是庸虚，奚为损益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163312_comment'></div>惟践修之常守，乃补道之近规，虽出下中，犹知企及，敢作乱伦之首，以伤则哲之明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163312_comment'></div>辄冒罪诛，讫陈情恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163312_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下天无私覆，物有曲成，溥推亭育之仁，俯轸盖高之听，上全王体，下尽私恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163312_comment'></div>傥前毕于祥除，或幸存于视息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163312_comment'></div>则区区薄志，获伸永慕之怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163312_comment'></div>穆穆清光，犹有再瞻之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163312_comment'></div>兴言哽塞，实切忧惶，臣无任号诉屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163312_comment'></div>其诏书不敢捧当，谨因某人赍赴阙进纳，兼奉表陈乞以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1163312_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　春，居乡丁父忧，随表上劄子乞免起复。作品：随第三表劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。系年据《乐全集》卷二八所附诏书。）</span><div id='poem_1163313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163313?labeling=true' target='_blank'>随第三表劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163313")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163313'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163313'>臣顷因进对，仰奉德音，以为君人之道，当正纪律、审命令，兹谓持重之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163313_comment'></div>盖礼烦则黩，恩过则轻，节以制度，驭下之操术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163313_comment'></div>祖宗朝臣僚表章之仪，朝廷诏答之体，公式所著，旧典具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163313_comment'></div>近岁以来，颇逾故事，或因劳旧，特加异数，后来何者，遂沿为例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163313_comment'></div>既无甄别，徒紊宪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163313_comment'></div>至如两府起复，仁宗朝富弼以宰臣当国，释位服丧，五降诏书，竟许终制，即是起复之命决不可复行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163313_comment'></div>至于吴奎，召旨尤峻，奎历陈将相执丧近事，亦蒙报允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163313_comment'></div>臣昨膺擢用，曾未旬浃，莫展丝毫之效，遽罹荼毒之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163313_comment'></div>甫经时序，三辱玺封，衔哀抱愧，容身靡所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163313_comment'></div>在臣之分，恩典已过，过此以往，恐非所谓正纪律、审命令之深旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163313_comment'></div>臣已上表，披沥情恳，伏望陛下天日光明，委照万物，察臣薄守，非有诡激，寝罢后命，以明等威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163313_comment'></div>早图俊贤，裨赞国论，积精会神，共熙庶绩，上以尊乎王体，下以全于拙艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163313_comment'></div>苫块馀息，不胜愿望，谨具劄子以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1163313_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　春，居乡丁父忧，上表谢许终丧。作品：谢许终丧表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。系年据《乐全集》卷二八所附诏书。）</span><div id='poem_1163314' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163314' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163314?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢许终丧表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163314")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163314_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163314'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163314'>今月十五日，进奏院递到诏书一道，伏蒙圣恩以臣上表辞免起复，特许终丧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163314_comment'></div>哀恳怔忪，数尘于睿览；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163314_comment'></div>俞音轸恻，许毕于丧期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163314_comment'></div>追成命之已行，遂私恩之罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163314_comment'></div>微诚既达，馀息再生<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163314_comment'></div>伏念臣起自单微，久尘通显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163314_comment'></div>国之厚禄，早伸反哺之怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163314_comment'></div>朝有荣阶，实荷流根之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163314_comment'></div>仰繄仁治，获报义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163314_comment'></div>向繇疏薄之材，上被圣神之选，捧承纶命，及见庭闱，虽迫隙光，备蒙赠典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163314_comment'></div>惟是称情之制，斯为致孝之终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163314_comment'></div>方伏垩庐，遽闻诏检，辄稽留于严旨，屡披沥于血诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163314_comment'></div>孰云在阴之微，亦有闻天之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163314_comment'></div>俯回英听，垂亮孤衷，许循致治之常，以尽免怀之慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163314_comment'></div>丁宁细札，徇人欲以矜从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163314_comment'></div>荒疚馀生，戴天恩而殒绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163314_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下远存古道，下厚时风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163314_comment'></div>本盛德以兴仁，扩宝慈之恻隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163314_comment'></div>章明大义，沛发温俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163314_comment'></div>谓墨绖之非经，著素冠之得礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163314_comment'></div>赐周存没，施厚生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163314_comment'></div>草芥寸心，亦抱太阳之炤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163314_comment'></div>潢污一勺，期归沧海之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163314_comment'></div>毕命王家，敢有遗力？</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1163314_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　本年，居乡丁父忧，上劄子辞免减半支给参知政事俸禄。作品：免俸劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。王智勇系此文于熙宁二年，不确。）</span><div id='poem_1163315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免俸劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163315")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163315'>臣今月二十一日得应天府送到中书劄子一道，奉圣旨：特令依见任参知政事俸请减半支给者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163315_comment'></div>臣闻以庸制禄，自古为国之大经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163315_comment'></div>设官分职，量其功勤而赋之禄，未有安坐而享之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163315_comment'></div>臣执丧在庐，无所事事，承此恩旨，义何可当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163315_comment'></div>况近时将相重位居丧而蒙恩给俸者，辞免皆得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163315_comment'></div>臣今所授中书劄子不敢捧承，已封缴纳中书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　本年，居乡丁父忧，再上劄子辞免减半支给参知政事俸禄。作品：免俸第二劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。王智勇系此文于熙宁二年，不确。）</span><div id='poem_1163316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163316?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免俸第二劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163316")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163316_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163316'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163316'>臣今月五日得应天府送到中书劄子一道，以臣昨奉圣恩，特令依见任参知政事请俸减半支给，具劄子辞免，奉圣旨所乞不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163316_comment'></div>切以先王立制，为邦大经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163316_comment'></div>位所以待才，禄所以报功，国之操柄，于是乎在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163316_comment'></div>若其忧服之中，已致官职之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163316_comment'></div>而乃叨冒重恩，蒙享厚禄，内于情而不称，外于义而有伤，虽甚鄙庸，敢辱名教？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163316_comment'></div>伏望天慈许循近例，特从停寝，少安愧惧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163316_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年4月</a>　四月，居乡丁父忧，为蔡抗作墓志铭。作品：宋故枢密直学士朝散大夫尚书兵部郎中秦凤路驻泊马步军都总管经略安抚使兼知秦州军州事本路劝农使上骑都尉南阳县开国男食邑三百户赐紫金鱼袋赠尚书礼部侍郎蔡公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷四〇。系年据文中所记蔡抗下葬时间。）</span><div id='poem_1163624' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163624' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163624?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故枢密直学士朝散大夫尚书兵部郎中秦凤路驻泊马步军都总管经略安抚使兼知秦州军州事本路劝农使上骑都尉南阳县开国男食邑三百户赐紫金鱼袋赠尚书礼部侍郎蔡公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　熙宁二年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163624")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163624_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163624'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163624'>英宗皇帝初潜宗邸，龙德而隐，留情艺文，以尊德性，顾莫与讲习者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163624_comment'></div>启濮安懿王曰：「睦亲广亲宅讲书著作佐郎蔡君某贤有行，愿得与之游」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163624_comment'></div>王致此意于公，公曰：「某在职且累年，惟旅见大宗正，未尝私谒诸宗室，敢辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163624_comment'></div>他日，王为置酒，从容谓公，欲请于朝，使诸子受学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163624_comment'></div>公虑若有邀也，始别见帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163624_comment'></div>帝待君尽礼，见必朝服，义兼傅友，咨询道艺，休闻日远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163624_comment'></div>尝访宫僚臧否，公对若人行谊，若人经术，皆非某所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163624_comment'></div>帝以白王，王曰：「蔡君非但文雅，诚长者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163624_comment'></div>然间造帝所，竟岁不过数见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163624_comment'></div>帝尤多其庄重，常以相从之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163624_comment'></div>而接之不得数且欸为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163624_comment'></div>久之，求外补，因解宫职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163624_comment'></div>英宗入纂大统，问辅臣：「蔡某何官？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163624_comment'></div>今何在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163624_comment'></div>执政白：「今以兵部员外郎、秘阁校理、广南东路转运使」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163624_comment'></div>帝曰：「兹人德行，朕所深知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163624_comment'></div>即以三司判官召还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163624_comment'></div>南海至都数千里，江行淹久，帝每对朝臣之南来者，辄问曰：「蔡学士何时可到？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163624_comment'></div>道途安否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163624_comment'></div>既至对见，慰劳殊渥，日将旰，屡留之，且曰：「君，朕故人，朕望于君者厚，勿以常礼自疏也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163624_comment'></div>俄除起居舍人、史馆修撰、知谏院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163624_comment'></div>恳辞再三，帝曰：「惟朕耳目心膂，不属君，将属何人」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163624_comment'></div>趣令受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163624_comment'></div>公自以被遇特达，思竭其心力，以致补报之效，事有涉嫌，说有至难，知无不言，言无不尽，诚心为质，引义忼慨，凡所启闻，多见纳用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163624_comment'></div>属有请追尊亲庙者，事下三省集议，公别请对，言礼为人后、大一统之义，指陈切至，涕下被面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163624_comment'></div>此议既非帝本意，又雅信重公，因大感悟，亦为公泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163624_comment'></div>会京师大水，公入对，帝侧席迎问变故，公推致咎徵，精言其端，意犹主于前议，论因中止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163624_comment'></div>然纳说者将终遂所建，以公在言路，不便之，适召试西掖，除知制诰，遂罢谏职，且俾出聘契丹国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163624_comment'></div>往返阅时，使还，而众论未已，公于中间通上下之情，安异同之意，弥缝周密，主于忠信，孜孜辨释，为士大夫道地，恩全体正，补益实多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163624_comment'></div>虽去谏垣，越月不对，帝必形于言，每被顾问，禁省秘事亦为及之，其沃心造膝，机柄之地有不得与闻者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163624_comment'></div>判吏部流内铨，因言铨审官冗甚，朝廷遂议新制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163624_comment'></div>将救时弊，多所建发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163624_comment'></div>帝益知其材可大用，欲其践历中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163624_comment'></div>进龙图阁学士，出知定州，然意惜其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163624_comment'></div>既入辞，帝曰：「第行，且召矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163624_comment'></div>行未浃日，英皇违豫，语数及公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163624_comment'></div>今上升储，帝疾日侵，犹曰「蔡某正人，促召来」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163624_comment'></div>因除太子詹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163624_comment'></div>未至，先帝升遐，东朝亦罢，改枢密直学士、知秦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163624_comment'></div>至阙觐对，今上望公，哀动左右，且言先帝大渐，犹不忘公卿之拜宫正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163624_comment'></div>帝问还期者再三，深意有所属者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163624_comment'></div>孤忠直道，左右莫为之容，乃畀需代者，竟不及得见卧内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163624_comment'></div>凭几训命，遂成虚格，忠义之士为先帝恨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163624_comment'></div>八月八日，灵驾发引，公以其旦东望号慕，避厅事，见僚佐于便斋，退就私寝，无疾而终，享年六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163624_comment'></div>前三日晨兴，语家人曰：「吾梦先帝召对顾问如平日，欲退复留」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163624_comment'></div>因叹息感念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163624_comment'></div>及终，人皆异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163624_comment'></div>天子震伤，累对近臣嗟恻，遣中人护丧以归，赙赐加等，特赠尚书礼部侍郎，奉先志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163624_comment'></div>公讳抗，字子直，宋人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163624_comment'></div>祖某，赠尚书度支员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163624_comment'></div>父某，泗州军事推官，累赠工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163624_comment'></div>世以明经仕进，实罕与进士游，尚书虽治经，有时才器识，所交结皆当世豪俊，故公兄弟皆举进士，早得时誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163624_comment'></div>蔡文忠公有重望，喜奖拔人伦，深器公，处之甥侄，竟妻以妻之宗女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163624_comment'></div>景祐中，登甲科，一命太平州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163624_comment'></div>尚书在临淮寝疾，旁无子弟，公委官自劾，单骑奔省，得及理命，越再宿而尚书以殁，乡里称其至孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163624_comment'></div>外除调平江军节度掌书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163624_comment'></div>秩满，近臣举充颍川郡王院伴读，寻迁删定编敕，迁著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163624_comment'></div>俄兼两宅讲书，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163624_comment'></div>久在宗邸，独不受饷遗，衎衎然不可得而亲，不可得而疏，故英宗皇帝深察重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163624_comment'></div>间迁秘书丞、太常博士、通判秦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163624_comment'></div>钟内艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163624_comment'></div>服除还朝，召试禁林，除秘阁校理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163624_comment'></div>淮西水，民流散，命公体量赈济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163624_comment'></div>至郡，亟请发廪食之，郡请俟奏可，公曰：「饿莩容待报耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163624_comment'></div>晨坐庾门，出粟全活至众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163624_comment'></div>使还，朝论称善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163624_comment'></div>吴人荐饥，朝廷察循良办治之才，以公知苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163624_comment'></div>姑苏土沃而卑，并江湖，积水渺㳽，常苦风潮害民田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163624_comment'></div>公既习知吴俗，至则为筑长堤，自郡城属昆山，横亘八十里，中断水势，民得因立塍堨，且通水陆之行，工省利大，民安于业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163624_comment'></div>吴俗浮薄，衣冠侨寓猥众，干请多事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163624_comment'></div>公患其然也，采士族之守操行者辄加宾礼，岁时馈劳，以褒厉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163624_comment'></div>士之承此，差知自重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1163624_comment'></div>发奸擿伏，听断精甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1163624_comment'></div>苏州吏役不均，纤猾得职，公为请于朝，先贷官泉，视役费之轻重而给之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1163624_comment'></div>籍诸酒榷征埭之利，旧用酬吏劳者，悉入县官，以偿所贷，吏皆便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1163624_comment'></div>后传其法，不能易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1163624_comment'></div>就迁广南东路转运使，吴民于今思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1163624_comment'></div>先是，岑水铜冶大发官市之民，止给空文，积逋钜万，里民大事私铸，奸游群聚，与江西盐盗合，郡县不能讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1163624_comment'></div>时公仲弟挺以选按刑江西，专治盐事，朝议谓岭南北并力则利害共功，故委公将漕南越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1163624_comment'></div>时朝旨责捕群盗甚峻，公曰：「采铜非诚民，惰游者为之，今悉入之官，而不畀其直，非私铸，衣食安取资？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1163624_comment'></div>又从而诛之，匪但民犯法也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1163624_comment'></div>乃度经用，斥冗费，铜入而受泉，民用乐输，彻炉毁橐，刑报立省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1163624_comment'></div>岭外州县多摄官，广东凡数百员，悉自部司注补，大吏操事为奸利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1163624_comment'></div>公至，收案致法，选用平均，吏员为清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1163624_comment'></div>番禺煮海，运给英、韶，溯流洄险，因以逗遛，侵窃杂恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1163624_comment'></div>公命十舟为一运，择摄官主之，岁终会其课，以为殿最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1163624_comment'></div>是岁，英、韶二州增盐课十五馀万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1163624_comment'></div>有司劾以奏未得报，而擅立约束，且废其法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1163624_comment'></div>适被召赴阙，既对，言南方便事，天子嘉纳，悉如公请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1163624_comment'></div>在岭外，惩摄官之弊，悯远人不知学问而茍禄无耻，人士无可称者，乃盛修庠序，择官劝讲，凡乡民之秀及官吏之子弟皆入学，亲为程校其文艺，恩意深美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1163624_comment'></div>由是诸生率教，仍岁有登进士科者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1163624_comment'></div>后在中山，见河朔军籍世家相承，狃于姑息，前人至垦阅场取蓏蔬之利，公至辟之，日命一军亲肄习焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1163624_comment'></div>军士番戍，妇人游佚于外，归辄首原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1163624_comment'></div>公下令连营，逋荡者无得首，必尽法，戍兵传闻，莫不怀德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1163624_comment'></div>缮甲兵，完壁橹，皆起功绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1163624_comment'></div>在镇未几，其首公勤职如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1163624_comment'></div>秦州西鄙皆杂羌，有种落叛，官兵击灭，取其地以建寨，板筑仅已而公至，守御器备举未集，公规营指顾如宿计，民不知有兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1163624_comment'></div>度其土田，募千户以为守，公私后无劳费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1163624_comment'></div>州有质院，质诸羌数百十人，扃系严密，被质者自少而长，且老死无得出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1163624_comment'></div>公为阅本末，其非利害所存，皆释遣之，由是恩信著于诸羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1163624_comment'></div>且约部族，不得擅仇杀，俄而有犯者，即斩以徇，戎人詟服，莫敢奸令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1163624_comment'></div>在秦不半年而殁，然于精虑，不遗力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1163624_comment'></div>公性静密，而资长于政事，公家之利，知无不为，为必有成，成则可久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1163624_comment'></div>居家理，赒恤宗族，与同休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1163624_comment'></div>仲弟天章阁待制某，友爱尤笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1163624_comment'></div>公在秦亭，内阁经略平凉，帅府接封，搢绅以为宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1163624_comment'></div>历官自祠部改度支、兵部员外，工部、兵部郎中，皆叙迁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1163624_comment'></div>先娶彭城刘氏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1163624_comment'></div>继室张氏，天章阁待制温之之女，封会昌县君，亦先公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1163624_comment'></div>三子：煜，登进士第，大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1163624_comment'></div>潜、钦，并秘书省正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1163624_comment'></div>五女：适滁州来安县令江懋简，大理评事曾孝序，馀未笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1163624_comment'></div>熙宁二年岁在己酉四月十三日，葬于宋城县仁孝曲，从先茔，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1163624_comment'></div>仆与公乡党交游之旧，故知公为深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1163624_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_114_1163624'>英皇在宗，储精学问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1163624_comment'></div>寤寐多闻，得公儒隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1163624_comment'></div>道义惟傅，艺文则友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1163624_comment'></div>造次法度，克常厥守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1163624_comment'></div>帝用知公，资本诚正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1163624_comment'></div>于朝有言，称其德行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1163624_comment'></div>岂不尔思，召自南服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1163624_comment'></div>谏省史观，作朕耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1163624_comment'></div>沃心嘉告，造膝危辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1163624_comment'></div>罔或不以，挹彼注兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1163624_comment'></div>中山扼戎，依依属公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1163624_comment'></div>行未弥月，金縢以封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1163624_comment'></div>帝凭玉几，仍有训命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1163624_comment'></div>谓公正人，畀翊储圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1163624_comment'></div>缀衣出庭，奔号见星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1163624_comment'></div>永怀靡及，之死弗瞑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1163624_comment'></div>宅忧未言，孤忠少与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1163624_comment'></div>于藩冀门，深诚莫吐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1163624_comment'></div>龙辒发引，攀胡奄终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1163624_comment'></div>先期感兆，神明恍通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1163624_comment'></div>天子震伤，哀形宸笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1163624_comment'></div>追襚亚卿，恩隆赙恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1163624_comment'></div>公之业蕴，足与大为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1163624_comment'></div>独迫于年，莫究发施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1163624_comment'></div>治民东南，守边西北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1163624_comment'></div>于以观政，可推风迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1163624_comment'></div>天子大孝，义笃于亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1163624_comment'></div>岂忘先志？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1163624_comment'></div>公违盛辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1163624_comment'></div>睢阳北原，三陵之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1163624_comment'></div>松梓森森，匪亲伊旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1163624_comment'></div>有子克家，载世其昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1163624_comment'></div>斯文不朽，流徽共长。</div><div id='poem_sentence_146_1163624_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163624'><span class='label'>按：</span>《乐全集》卷四〇。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1163624_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年闰11月</a>　闰十一月，居乡丁父忧，为王贽作墓志铭。作品：朝散大夫守尚书户部侍郎致仕上柱国太原郡开国公食邑二千九百户食实封五百户赐紫金鱼袋王公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1163604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163604?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫守尚书户部侍郎致仕上柱国太原郡开国公食邑二千九百户食实封五百户赐紫金鱼袋王公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年闰11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163604")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163604'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163604'>英宗治平二年，龙图阁学士、给事中、知陈州王公年七十，请致君事，以尚书礼部侍郎得谢归乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163604_comment'></div>今上即位，改户部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163604_comment'></div>熙宁二年岁次己酉闰十一月八日，无疾燕坐，终于正寝，享年七十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163604_comment'></div>公讳贽，字至之，庐陵太和人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163604_comment'></div>王氏自晋太傅导，为江左盛族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163604_comment'></div>唐末，公之从伯祖绾从杨行密定江淮有功，其子崇文终吉州刺史，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163604_comment'></div>公天禧三年进士擢第，释褐邵州防御推官，历衡、连、郴三州军事判官，初仕即以风干著称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163604_comment'></div>本部任材，监兴国军大冶县茶场、兼知县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163604_comment'></div>大冶，江西剧县，吏猾民豪，久不治，讼有至数年不决，敝事尤多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163604_comment'></div>公到未几，政以清简闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163604_comment'></div>迁著作佐郎、监益州军资库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163604_comment'></div>枢密直学士王公鬷领益部，辟公幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163604_comment'></div>流内铨已注官在路，公闻，诣府白曰：「选人远官勤矣，如之何使之中途而返也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163604_comment'></div>坚请，复奏寝前章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163604_comment'></div>王公善其意，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163604_comment'></div>就改秘书丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163604_comment'></div>京尹举知开封府尉氏县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163604_comment'></div>时承献后垂箔之后，中人擅势，衔命出邑，下者邀索挠民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163604_comment'></div>公密疏其事以闻，朝廷因以正法，中人威暴由是始沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163604_comment'></div>后尹杜祁公知之，深所嗟赏，以为由一邑而正天下之法，可谓之能才矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163604_comment'></div>叙迁太常博士，用三司使荐，提举江淮、广东榷盐，陛辞，赐五品服章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163604_comment'></div>规画功利，务便公私，不专为聚歛上课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163604_comment'></div>召还，将有以擢用，操事者有不悦，故但除尚书屯田员外郎、通判信州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163604_comment'></div>公常谓，吏道以精勤为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163604_comment'></div>阅诸帐籍，至获隐没官物数百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163604_comment'></div>上言：「州县之治，簿书为要，一郡之敝，推而知其积矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163604_comment'></div>因条上钩考之法，周防详密，遂为著令，至今奉行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163604_comment'></div>庆历初，湖南溪峒骚动，择用并边牧守，公以选知道州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163604_comment'></div>朝廷专遣使安抚，至州，分布兵屯，多非要害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163604_comment'></div>公执不可，使者方责拒命，俄而蛮寇来袭，公击走之，遂不敢犯境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163604_comment'></div>监司列上功状，玺书褒谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163604_comment'></div>宪台荐公文中御史，召除殿中侍御史，乘传赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163604_comment'></div>真宗天禧中，诏置谏院，定除谏官六员，而难用人，员常不足，乃命于三院选二员充言事御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163604_comment'></div>中间久废，及是公犹未至，道除此职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163604_comment'></div>既对见，仁宗问公：「近臣称卿才，今将何以称职」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163604_comment'></div>公对曰：「臣远方寒士，过属言责之地，若事系朝廷大体，或奸邪罔惑聪明，有犯无隐，死且不避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163604_comment'></div>至于人臣闺门暧昧之私，交构爱憎之迹，险危之说，实伤美化，臣窃耻之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163604_comment'></div>仁宗曰：「卿言是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163604_comment'></div>近日言事官章疏大率如卿言，朕深不取」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163604_comment'></div>入台供职，迁侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163604_comment'></div>未几，换尚书刑部员外郎、知谏院、判国子监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163604_comment'></div>逾年，改起居舍人、直史馆、判司农寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163604_comment'></div>未期，除天章阁待制，仍知谏院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163604_comment'></div>仁宗尝御迎阳门，召两禁台谏官，亲策问时政得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163604_comment'></div>公既上对，复赐手诏，令尽所未言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163604_comment'></div>益条当世所急十馀事，多见纳用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163604_comment'></div>庆历、皇祐间，政尚宽易，公有以开发者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163604_comment'></div>间因进对，书思对命于笏搢而读奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163604_comment'></div>上指之问曰：「此记何等事也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163604_comment'></div>公因得一一条陈，时对甚久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163604_comment'></div>既退，上顾谓入内都知张永和曰：「五方异禀，风俗不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163604_comment'></div>或南士而有燕赵之气，是人资必忠厚，仕亦贵显，王某之谓也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163604_comment'></div>殿上闻者莫不属目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163604_comment'></div>公论事能揣知人主深旨，情辞婉顺，不为矫激，切摩归之正而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163604_comment'></div>中贵人王守忠以储邸旧恩眷遇任事，尝缘薄劳而迁重职，台谏官章疏继上，不纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163604_comment'></div>公请对，上迎谓之曰：「卿岂非论王守忠耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163604_comment'></div>公曰：「臣所论非一事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163604_comment'></div>既而徐及守忠，所言精切，信而有稽，仁宗亟命内臣宣谕中书，收寝诰命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163604_comment'></div>久在言路，终守初对之意，以大体自任不渝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163604_comment'></div>别受命知贡举、领三班院、判吏部流内铨，犹兼谏省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163604_comment'></div>初置天章阁直学士，选名臣充员，首以命公，即拜河北都转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163604_comment'></div>公时具庆，父牧以赞善大夫致政，后赠工部尚书，母安定郡太君潘氏，年偕八十馀，恳辞河北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163604_comment'></div>仁宗曰：「欲卿谙历边事，行且召矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163604_comment'></div>即遣内珰就私第赐尚书绯衣、银鱼，太夫人冠帔，又为发内帑缗一百万，俾资储峙，其宠遇如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163604_comment'></div>到部，均赋役，固河防，振灾害，节冗费，权倖忌其公，朝廷称其勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163604_comment'></div>考绩迁礼部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163604_comment'></div>岁中祀明堂霈恩，迁吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163604_comment'></div>以二亲耋老，数求江外一州，以便迎养，就移知洪州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163604_comment'></div>未离部，丁外艰，安定继终于路，护丧南归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163604_comment'></div>服除还阙，时朝议以寰内陈、许、郑、滑、曹为辅郡，增设兵防，而置京畿转运使，除公枢密直学士充使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163604_comment'></div>岁馀职罢还朝，复领三班院，迁左谏议大夫，出知郑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163604_comment'></div>久之，迁龙图阁学士，移高阳关路马步军都总管兼安抚使、知瀛州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1163604_comment'></div>高阳，北道之冲，旧城隘，军民居城外，以盟书故，难于兴筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1163604_comment'></div>庆历初，契丹来渝平，鄙上缮亭障，因此展关城，累更守将而功不就。<div class='inline'
