id='poem_sentence_73_1163604_comment'></div>公巡视，曰：「城以保民，军政宜先此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1163604_comment'></div>即计徒庸，增版干，不日而雉堞楼橹完备，军府增气，后人赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1163604_comment'></div>边吏偷安，法防多弛，公谨关市，严讥禁，毋习茍简，必守故常，方略设施，毅然得镇守之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1163604_comment'></div>以任官坐累，降秩一等，内阁如故，知池州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1163604_comment'></div>寻复左谏议大夫，知江宁府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1163604_comment'></div>英宗践阼，进给事中，移陈州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1163604_comment'></div>引年得请，遂归庐陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1163604_comment'></div>雅知养生，夙明性理，心量虚旷而得安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1163604_comment'></div>好书画，能鉴赏，古之名笔多购得之，聚书万馀卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1163604_comment'></div>所居有林塘之胜，高僧野客谈禅话道，间从诗酒，优游自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1163604_comment'></div>世事一不屑意，萧然有方外之趣，以至泊然委化，神明不动，其所得精矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1163604_comment'></div>特被仁宗厚遇，每见玉色怡然，退而犹若不及，左右常候知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1163604_comment'></div>命知贡举，御书「博学」字赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1163604_comment'></div>领畿漕，御书「安民」字赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1163604_comment'></div>往帅瀛关，宸章宠行，意皆有所褒藉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1163604_comment'></div>旨在大用，而竟不及，士友以为惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1163604_comment'></div>夫人刘氏，封同安郡君，前二年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1163604_comment'></div>子二人，曰仪，终殿中丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1163604_comment'></div>曰亿，今为职方员外郎，前知袁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1163604_comment'></div>一女，适筠州军事推官萧迅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1163604_comment'></div>四孙：曰球，曰瑰，大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1163604_comment'></div>曰瑜，曰玠，郊社斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1163604_comment'></div>平生论述多切时务，有《奏议集》二十卷，《别集》二十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1163604_comment'></div>以某年月日葬于某县某乡，夫人不祔，从本俗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1163604_comment'></div>仆与公义，有莫逆之契，故亿以迅所撰行状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1163604_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_1163604'>仁皇在御，四十二祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1163604_comment'></div>万邦黎献，惟帝时举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1163604_comment'></div>皇无好恶，遵王之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1163604_comment'></div>阅人则多，鲜承殊顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1163604_comment'></div>公来远方，孰先为容？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1163604_comment'></div>惟其诚心，于以自通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1163604_comment'></div>诚至心精，百里斯顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1163604_comment'></div>以此事君，不结而信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1163604_comment'></div>宪台谏省，匪卷则折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1163604_comment'></div>公居累年，始终一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1163604_comment'></div>河朔之行，临遣依依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1163604_comment'></div>后命未申，泣血南归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1163604_comment'></div>历守五州，载其善政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1163604_comment'></div>为治不同，所同清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1163604_comment'></div>七十得谢，遂老而传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1163604_comment'></div>筑居幽閒，邃兼林泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1163604_comment'></div>和以天倪，自得为得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1163604_comment'></div>采真之游，诣其冥极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1163604_comment'></div>又达宗乘，即动非动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1163604_comment'></div>入理之门，契其妙用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1163604_comment'></div>逍遥乐地，如是七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1163604_comment'></div>泊尔宴寂，还其本然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1163604_comment'></div>迷有生死，悟无去住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1163604_comment'></div>一切一如，是公归处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_122_1163604_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dd6423b0f50e4c498d4bc544d02f0a9b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dd6423b0f50e4c498d4bc544d02f0a9b");'><span id='dd6423b0f50e4c498d4bc544d02f0a9b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1073')">1071-1073年</a>，65-67岁</div><div id='dd6423b0f50e4c498d4bc544d02f0a9b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　本年，在判南京御史台任，筑乐全堂，自号乐全居士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　本年，在判南京御史台任，有诗。作品：题乐全堂。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题乐全堂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495467")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495467_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_495467_0'>① 庄子云乐全之谓得志。古之所谓得志者，非轩冕之谓也，谓其无以益其乐而已矣</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495467'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495467'>乐全得意自庄书，静阅流光乐有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495467'>四句幻泡明般若，一篇力命信冲虚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495467'>心閒自觉浮云薄，才拙诚知与世疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495467'>只此空名漫儿戏，何王城阙不丘墟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495467'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495467_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　本年，在判南京御史台任，有诗寄吕宝臣、欧阳修、王仲义。作品：熙宁壬子岁寄丁未同甲诸公秦亭吕宣徽宝臣汝阴欧阳公少师永叔京下王尚书仲义。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_495450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>熙宁壬子岁寄丁未同甲诸公秦亭吕宣徽宝臣汝阴欧阳少师永叔京下王尚书仲仪<span class='inlineComment2'>（时并六十六岁）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495450")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495450'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495450'>百二十年名上寿，浮生百岁实稀闻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495450'>百年三万六千日，今已三分过二分。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495450'>啸歌独喜齿全在，文字看来眼未昏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495450'>酒量虽衰犹得醉，尘中人事自纷纷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495450_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495450'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495450_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年5月</a>　五月，在判南京御史台任，为王素作神道碑铭。作品：宋故端明殿学士金紫光禄大夫行工部尚书致仕上柱国太原郡开国公食邑三千八百户食实封一千二百户谥懿敏王公神道碑铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三七。）</span><div id='poem_1163570' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故端明殿学士金紫光禄大夫行工部尚书致仕上柱国太原郡开国公食邑三千八百户食实封一千二百户谥懿敏王公神道碑铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　熙宁六年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163570")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163570_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163570'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163570'>公讳素，字某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163570_comment'></div>其先大名莘人，曾祖五代唐庄宗时左拾遗，祖国初以尚书兵部侍郎知制诰，始家京下，著籍开封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163570_comment'></div>考以太尉相真宗，并赠太师、尚书令兼中书令，封鲁、晋、魏国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163570_comment'></div>景德、祥符间，天下无事，生民安乐，功成垂统，号称太平，太尉位居朝首，执其政柄，故生极隆名，殁而从享于庙，为一代之宗臣，盛矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163570_comment'></div>其薨也，章圣问诸孤，公犹未官，更以嗟恻，始授太常寺太祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163570_comment'></div>服阕，特迁大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163570_comment'></div>召试学士院，赐进士出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163570_comment'></div>复召试，擢通判颍州，更怀州、许州，三迁太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163570_comment'></div>近臣荐其材高，复召试，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163570_comment'></div>凡三试禁林，当登馆阁之选，每以大臣亲嫌见抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163570_comment'></div>出知濮州，年尚少，下观望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163570_comment'></div>有大姓倚要人横猾，公弹治竟法，吏民耸慑，政有能名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163570_comment'></div>河决，始复故道，转运使按濒河之田，檄郡县增赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163570_comment'></div>公上言：流散方归，正宜保息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163570_comment'></div>特诏无得增赋，自濮七州之民皆被惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163570_comment'></div>秩满，领宣州，未行，御史中丞孔道辅举充侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163570_comment'></div>未几，道辅外补，公亦出知鄂州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163570_comment'></div>荆湖一道，配民率口鬻盐，公持利害不从，鄂人独免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163570_comment'></div>徙宿州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163570_comment'></div>庆历初，夏戎阻命，契丹来渝平，仁宗格以至诚，邻敌自怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163570_comment'></div>益修政事，首增谏员，召公自宿知谏院、同判国子监，悉情献替，多见向纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163570_comment'></div>皇子生，将大庆赉，公曰：「西师尚严，劳臣在边，士苦战戍之勤，民疲赍送之役，而金帛散于不急，爵禄加于无功，庆赉非宜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163570_comment'></div>朝议为止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163570_comment'></div>论天下贡士不得才行之实，请罢糊名，以取诚士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163570_comment'></div>论郡国置学校，择师官，以渐复里选之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163570_comment'></div>论中书凡中外奏事不即裁定，辄下近臣集议，盖执政者莫肯任咎，为此纷纷，由是集议稀阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163570_comment'></div>论请置官三司，会校国计，省诸冗费以不訾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163570_comment'></div>仁宗间御天章阁，召二府，出手诏访时务，公因列疏阙政十馀条，皆人所难言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163570_comment'></div>他日帝坐延和殿，特召赐三品服，寻迁天章阁待制，领淮南都转运、按察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163570_comment'></div>时初加按察之名，以假司官之重，奉使者率以苛峻为称职，公独处之以平易，惟贪暴吏莫容焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163570_comment'></div>故常更易贰税，致羡钱上供，以自为劳，公彻其敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163570_comment'></div>朝廷闻而善之，举以戒诸路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163570_comment'></div>就迁泾原路经略使、知渭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163570_comment'></div>有操权者不悦公，伺衅危之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163570_comment'></div>河东转运使因事被劾，辞有及公者，坐徙华州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163570_comment'></div>按推者与公薄亲，而不以闻，又坐是夺职徙江州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163570_comment'></div>未至，改汝州，徙潞州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163570_comment'></div>丁太夫人袁氏忧，服除，知兖州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163570_comment'></div>还待制，复知渭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163570_comment'></div>就拜龙图阁直学士，还领三班院，遂除枢密直学士、知开封府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163570_comment'></div>至和二年，仁宗不豫，内外忧恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163570_comment'></div>秋，大雨水，蔡河堤坏，垫安上门，漂没军民庐舍，中旨遣马军帅范恪塞朱雀门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163570_comment'></div>公密启止之，众心以安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163570_comment'></div>公白：今兹惟宜镇静，精察奸盗尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163570_comment'></div>故狱市无扰，京下肃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163570_comment'></div>于时识者谓公处动危时得体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163570_comment'></div>阅岁，迁龙图阁学士、定州路马步军都总管、安抚使、知定州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163570_comment'></div>寻除翰林侍读学士、知益州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163570_comment'></div>益部会府，宴设岁费为钱数千万，取给牙校，习以为常，公为裁节，所损几半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163570_comment'></div>川峡用铁钱，诸炉岁课，嘉、邛苦之，公请停铸，而货币以平，关市无乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163570_comment'></div>汉中饥，遣赈廪而后以闻，朝廷适议救恤而奏至，见谓适便宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163570_comment'></div>公临下以恕，简而易从，条教明审，人情安便，故西川之政，蜀人纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163570_comment'></div>代还，复知开封府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163570_comment'></div>尝建请置使院判官，主赋役之政令，置八厢官以决小罪，置发放司勾朱官以检稽违，后皆施行，称便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163570_comment'></div>久之请解，领群牧使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163570_comment'></div>请补外，知许州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163570_comment'></div>英宗初，羌入平凉塞，连犯堡塞，朝议择帅，谓无易公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163570_comment'></div>除端明殿学士，复知渭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163570_comment'></div>边人闻公至，曰：「无事矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163570_comment'></div>羌积服公威信，即解散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163570_comment'></div>既下车，境上恬然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163570_comment'></div>公三帅平凉，御将卒有恩，阔略不苛急，人皆乐为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163570_comment'></div>临事毅然，不可犯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163570_comment'></div>时谓三边统率，公称最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163570_comment'></div>初在平凉，部将蒋偕筑堡境外，为羌要击，间道窜归，公贳，令复往讫役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163570_comment'></div>总管狄青曰：「偕往必复败」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163570_comment'></div>公曰：「偕死，君行矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163570_comment'></div>偕知不可徒还，故以死就功，而堡竟立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163570_comment'></div>有番官密悉，天水羌也，粗有计略，群羌所信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163570_comment'></div>前帅欲羁縻之，请以为诸族巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163570_comment'></div>事下公议，公数其罪，械送本道，中路亡去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163570_comment'></div>诸将请重购之，以绝后患，公曰：「是乌足以为者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1163570_comment'></div>不购，亦竟无能为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1163570_comment'></div>一日方燕飨，边民惊哗，奔入城，将佐请阖门，防奸变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1163570_comment'></div>公曰：「妄相恐尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1163570_comment'></div>寇至，吾不知耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1163570_comment'></div>传令敢妄有言者斩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1163570_comment'></div>俄而自定，众服其明决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1163570_comment'></div>西陲诸路内属番部因事质留者，有至老死不得出，公阅其籍，情非甚恶而系久者，戒谕散遣之，莫不感悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1163570_comment'></div>弓箭手，边劲兵也，先有千馀家在境上，无城栅，寇至莫自保，公筑八堡分处之，老幼感泣曰：「自此有生计矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1163570_comment'></div>旧事，弓箭手人骑分领于东西路巡检，公曰：「是属官但给田，使自衣食；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1163570_comment'></div>聚而役之，是废其业」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1163570_comment'></div>趣使就耕，有警则发之，故战士竞劝，怀于自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1163570_comment'></div>拓州之西南城，浚隍三周，无虑二十万工，而民不知役，渭人刻功于石，画像于祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1163570_comment'></div>改澶州廉察，知成德军、真定府路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1163570_comment'></div>太原帅缺，上顾谓辅臣：「河东节制四路，其议宿望以行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1163570_comment'></div>柄臣以公应诏，复端明殿学士，迁尚书左丞、河东四路经略安抚监牧使、知太原府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1163570_comment'></div>汾河暴溢，命筑诸堤防之缺，曰：「汇平晋，势必及郛」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1163570_comment'></div>既而水果至，不为害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1163570_comment'></div>年大杀，发公私粟，蠲诸赋，救荒之政甚设，民皆获济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1163570_comment'></div>还朝，知通进银台司、门下封驳事，以疾请外补，留提举醴泉观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1163570_comment'></div>复请知汝州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1163570_comment'></div>岁馀，疾稍侵，遂请老，以工部尚书致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1163570_comment'></div>繇博士及此，凡历尚书省员外郎、郎中、侍郎，并三迁，中间除谏议大夫，给事中，澶州、青州、观察使，尚书左丞，而以冬官老焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1163570_comment'></div>故事，致仕虽三公，无兼职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1163570_comment'></div>朝廷初立亲制，公首以学士就第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1163570_comment'></div>公宰相子，自励学问，洁操行，与游皆时俊，故朝论不敢以世家子弟等比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1163570_comment'></div>台省清要官缺，物望必及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1163570_comment'></div>资尤劲，善谈论，及为御史谏官，论事上前，不挠权势，不顾嫌忌，称为敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1163570_comment'></div>侍读经阁，至于前言往行，必精切开说，因以讽劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1163570_comment'></div>仁宗常命公悉上御史谏官时所论事，间省阅之，盖有简于上心者深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1163570_comment'></div>晚之泾原，英宗面谕曰：「朕知学士久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1163570_comment'></div>边有警，其勉以行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1163570_comment'></div>且及进用意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1163570_comment'></div>公还在道，英宗疾大渐，犹问辅臣：「王某至何所」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1163570_comment'></div>公至，会英宗上仙，遂赴真定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1163570_comment'></div>上亦旧闻公名，其往汝州，谓之曰：「汝，非卿所宜处，从所便尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1163570_comment'></div>性恺易，无城府，善与人交，久而弥笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1163570_comment'></div>早从公游，及所尝奖荐，至于幕府文武，间登公卿，或至将相，而公处之自如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1163570_comment'></div>熙宁六年三月甲寅，薨于京师，享年六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1163570_comment'></div>上闻，为辍视朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1163570_comment'></div>奉常易名曰「懿敏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1163570_comment'></div>公生长富贵，及解绂私第，葺虚斋，悉屏平日玩好，陶器野服，放怀方外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1163570_comment'></div>至于启手足，神志不乱，泊然怛化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1163570_comment'></div>五月庚申，归葬文正公先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1163570_comment'></div>文集二十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1163570_comment'></div>娶李氏，同安郡夫人，礼部尚书维之女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1163570_comment'></div>滕氏，安康郡夫人，给事中涉之女；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1163570_comment'></div>张氏，永嘉郡夫人，太傅士逊之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1163570_comment'></div>九男：厚，将作监主簿，早世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1163570_comment'></div>固，大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1163570_comment'></div>坚，光禄寺丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1163570_comment'></div>巩、本、硕，大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1163570_comment'></div>凝，秘书省正字；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1163570_comment'></div>常、奥，将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1163570_comment'></div>二女，适将作监丞李祥、文居中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1163570_comment'></div>仆与公义兼姻友，故得详为纪述，后之载笔者有以传信于斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1163570_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_127_1163570'>宋有贤相，太尉魏公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1163570_comment'></div>昭事乃辟，于变时雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1163570_comment'></div>公其才子，祗服是似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1163570_comment'></div>泱泱大风，德音载韪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1163570_comment'></div>惟国之良，于朝有光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1163570_comment'></div>令问令望，金玉其相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1163570_comment'></div>御史谏官，世家鲜处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1163570_comment'></div>帝曰惟才，独蒙察举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1163570_comment'></div>不将不迎，直躬以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1163570_comment'></div>思我王度，尚有典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1163570_comment'></div>国之重防，守在三边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1163570_comment'></div>公秉帅节，于蕃于宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1163570_comment'></div>卒乘辑睦，农狎于野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1163570_comment'></div>赤囊弗驰，壶歌以雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1163570_comment'></div>英皇有言，公余旧知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1163570_comment'></div>图任共政，既面命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1163570_comment'></div>召自平凉，缀衣已没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1163570_comment'></div>攀胡靡及，朔门复軷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1163570_comment'></div>岩廊吁谟，匪咎匪诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1163570_comment'></div>时莫我与，将谁不如！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1163570_comment'></div>汝海之行，依依怀止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1163570_comment'></div>驾言于归，遂致君事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1163570_comment'></div>幅巾虚斋，萧然遗照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1163570_comment'></div>回阅平生，恍如梦觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1163570_comment'></div>人生而静，泊湛诸情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1163570_comment'></div>公将北首，静如厥生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1163570_comment'></div>圣人贵真，真谓性命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1163570_comment'></div>公乎庶几，知终以正。</div><div id='poem_sentence_154_1163570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年12月4日</a>　十二月四日，在判南京御史台任，移知陈州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　本年，在判南京御史台任，上疏论汴河利害。作品：论汴河利害事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1163249' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163249' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163249?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论汴河利害事<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163249")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163249_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163249'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163249'>臣窃惟今之京师，古所谓陈留，天下四冲八达之地者也，非如函秦天府，百二之固，洛宅九州之中，表里山河，形胜足恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163249_comment'></div>自唐末朱温受封于梁，因而建都，至于石晋，割幽、蓟之地以入契丹，遂与强虏共平原之利，故五代争夺，戎狄乱华，其患由乎畿甸无藩篱之限，本根无所庇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163249_comment'></div>祖宗受命，规摹毕讲，不还周汉之旧，而梁氏是因，岂乐是而处之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163249_comment'></div>势有所不获已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163249_comment'></div>大体利漕运而赡师旅，依重师而为国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163249_comment'></div>则是今日之势，国依兵而立，兵以食为命，食以漕运为本，漕运以河渠为主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163249_comment'></div>国家初浚河渠三道，通京城漕运，自后定立上供年额，汴河斛㪷六百万石，广济河六十二万石，惠民河六十万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163249_comment'></div>广济河所运多是杂色粟豆，但充口食马料；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163249_comment'></div>惠民河所运止给太康、咸平、尉氏等县军粮而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163249_comment'></div>惟汴河所运，一色粳米，相兼小麦，此乃太仓蓄积之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163249_comment'></div>今仰食于官廪者不惟三军，至于京师士庶以亿万计，大半待饱于军稍之馀，故国家于漕事至急至重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163249_comment'></div>京，大也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163249_comment'></div>师，众也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163249_comment'></div>大众所聚，故谓之京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163249_comment'></div>有食则京师可立，汴河废，则大众不可聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163249_comment'></div>汴河之于京城，乃是建国之本，非可与区区沟洫水利同言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163249_comment'></div>近岁已罢广济河，而惠民河斛㪷不入太仓，大众之命，惟汴河是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163249_comment'></div>近岁陈说利害，以汴河为议者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163249_comment'></div>臣恐议者不已，屡作改更，必致汴河日失其旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163249_comment'></div>国家大计，殊非小事，惟陛下特回圣鉴，深赐省察，留神远虑，以固基本。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1163249_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163249'><span class='label'>按：</span>《乐全集》卷二七。又见《续资治通鉴长编》卷二六九，《宋名臣奏议》卷一二七，《文献通考》卷二五，《宋史》卷九三《河渠志》三、卷一七五《食货志》上三，《历代名臣奏议》卷二六一，《汴京遗迹志》卷六，《古今图书集成》山川典卷二三七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1163249_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5ff6032dc7dc459b88d5a7b7c8199e62_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5ff6032dc7dc459b88d5a7b7c8199e62");'><span id='5ff6032dc7dc459b88d5a7b7c8199e62_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1092')">1076-1092年</a>，70-卒后1年</div><div id='5ff6032dc7dc459b88d5a7b7c8199e62' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年6月</a>　六月，在知应天府任，上疏论讨岭南利害。作品：论讨岭南利害九事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1163240' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163240' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163240?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论讨岭南利害九事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163240")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163240_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163240'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163240'>臣窃惟百粤之区，三代为荒服，正朔声教所不加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163240_comment'></div>秦并天下，始开置三郡，曰南海、桂林、象郡，乃今广州、桂州、交州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163240_comment'></div>汉武平南越，拓为九郡，元帝弃儋、崖，但存七郡，以至后汉，交州刺史部郡七，县五十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163240_comment'></div>今自岭以南，皆七郡之地，而交趾得其三郡二十二城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163240_comment'></div>其土地下湿，多瘴疠，人短折，性躁悍，好雠怨，相杀害，易兴逆节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163240_comment'></div>历吴、晋至隋，皆内属，除吏，供赋役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163240_comment'></div>唐南海节度兼岭南五府经略使，交州是为安南府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163240_comment'></div>唐末，刘陟窃据岭外，并有交州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163240_comment'></div>国初，交州帅吴昌文卒，管内十二州大乱，其大将丁部击定之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163240_comment'></div>部死，子琏承袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163240_comment'></div>太祖擒刘鋹，琏请内附，因而抚纳，授安南都护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163240_comment'></div>自昌文至今，争夺篡盗，已易四姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163240_comment'></div>太平兴国中，其大将黎桓篡丁氏，太宗下诏讨伐，兴兵由邕、广水陆两路入，诸将孙全兴等逗挠擅退，并戮于邕州市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163240_comment'></div>黎桓上表谢罪，降诏赦之，遂除安南都护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163240_comment'></div>景德中，桓死，诸子争立，国复乱，广州守臣奏请乘衅取之，真宗不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163240_comment'></div>既而大校李公蕴又篡黎氏，朝议以其遐荒异俗，置之度外，因亦用桓故事，授公蕴旄节，及此传四世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163240_comment'></div>向自日南贡职已废，朝廷阔略不问，边臣茍慢，防禁益弛，凶恶盗贼、奸蠹之民、诸配徙者不无逋逃，颇从亡匿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163240_comment'></div>亦有士人顽嚚不逞，挺身亡命，赴其招集，教之治兵，助为邪计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163240_comment'></div>故令乾德敢奸王命，凶党用事，多是华人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163240_comment'></div>往时遣使，例抵其国，见城中无居民，府舍湫陋，有茅竹屋数十百区，以为军营，兵器有弓弩、木牌、梭枪、竹枪，弱不堪用，势不能为中国患，故远而易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163240_comment'></div>至景德中，李氏窃此疆域，及今七十馀年，王人久不涉其地，不复知其虚实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163240_comment'></div>今闻其城栅隍堑，乃有数重兵力，民众必益充足，颇略旁占城等诸小国，事势施设比前为强大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163240_comment'></div>而岭南长吏犹习故常，本非经远之才，又忽不虞之戒，狂妄轻脱，为国生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163240_comment'></div>蛮性狠悍，有不能堪，告诉不听，投书不受，事情壅塞，积成忿恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163240_comment'></div>及其战舰抵岸，军鼓叩城，如入无人之境，略无交锋之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163240_comment'></div>寇兵所至，城邑为墟，迁致其货财，系累其妇女，封豕长蛇，恣其酷毒，传闻其事，可为痛心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163240_comment'></div>然此为既往之咎，方当虑将来之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163240_comment'></div>昔汉诛南粤，兵会番禺，道便近，故为功易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163240_comment'></div>至后汉马援击交趾，缘海而进，随山刊道，千馀里崎岖，三年始得贼，讨袭转战至九真、日南境上，以定汉界，吏士得还者十四、五，而象郡南境由是竟分为林邑国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163240_comment'></div>历代或小叛乱，寻即平之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163240_comment'></div>隋破林邑，以其地入于交州，终亦不能有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163240_comment'></div>唐懿宗时，安南都护李琢侵暴獠民，群獠引林邑蛮攻安南府，遣将率江西、湖南之兵赴援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163240_comment'></div>既而交州陷，遂集诸道兵赴之，积六年方破蛮众，收复安南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163240_comment'></div>而藩镇之兵犹戍桂林、徐州，戍卒遂倒戈剽掠湘潭，破宿州、徐州、滁州、和州、濠州，攻围泗州，扬、楚、庐、寿、兖、海、沂、密、曹、濮皆被其害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163240_comment'></div>诏会蕃汉诸镇之兵十八将进讨，又二年方殄凶逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163240_comment'></div>由是天下骚敝，跨接五代，遂为异域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163240_comment'></div>故太祖皇帝弃之，不欲勤中国以事荒徼，列之外蕃，使隔限诸蛮，此天机神算，长辔远御之术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163240_comment'></div>逮今百馀年，故无岛夷之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163240_comment'></div>此时窃发，穷凶极毒，逆天理，黩神道，自古蛮夷猾夏，寇贼奸宄，未有如是之暴害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163240_comment'></div>天衷惨恒，为之旰食，顾此滔天之恶，遂兴问罪之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163240_comment'></div>天下切齿，恨不即执其凶徒，诛裂菹醢之，潴其邑落，以为凶虚，宣九庙之威灵，谢一方之冤痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163240_comment'></div>伏惟命将行军，授成制胜，既已审之于岩廊，定之于帷幄，攻取形势，谅无遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163240_comment'></div>然臣闻处重位，食厚禄，国之休戚，义当共之，不待迫于咎责而后励勉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163240_comment'></div>况臣虽守陪都，服在近职，上荷恩眷，无补圣明，岂可自同常人，坐观国家之事，犹秦人视楚人之肥瘠，无惨动怵惕之心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163240_comment'></div>思虑所及，敢怀不尽，谨条九事，列于左方，上达衡石，冒尘睿鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163240_comment'></div>傥有一得，微助涓尘，至于填沟壑之日，亦无遗恨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1163240'>一事：即今淮甸、两浙、江东西、湖南北州县仍岁旱蝗，陂泽竭涸，野无青草，人户流散，穷荒极敝，事可忧痛，方当散利薄征，缓刑弛役，布德施惠，以抚存保息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163240_comment'></div>而盗起南裔，王师大兴，正出荆、潭之路，此时民力何以复堪赋发？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163240_comment'></div>后汉永和中，日南、象林徼外蛮夷数千人反乱，交阯刺史发交阯、九真二郡兵万馀人救之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163240_comment'></div>兵士惮远役，遂反攻其府，州郡并力讨之，不能制，为所攻围岁馀，而兵谷不继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163240_comment'></div>朝廷以为忧，召公卿百官、四府掾属问以方略，皆议遣大将，发荆、扬、兖、豫四万人赴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163240_comment'></div>李固驳以七不可之说，而请选有勇略仁惠、材任将帅者以为刺史、太守，令募蛮夷，使自相攻击，转输金帛以为其资，有能反间致头首者，许以封侯列土之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163240_comment'></div>因荐祝良、张乔可任用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163240_comment'></div>四府悉从固议，即拜祝良为九真太守，张乔为交阯刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163240_comment'></div>乔至，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1163240", 1163240, "Clauses/257/Comments/0")'>开示</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1163240", 1163240, "Clauses/257/Comments/1")'>慰诱</span>，并皆降散；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163240_comment'></div>良到九真，单车入贼中，设方略，招以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1163240", 1163240, "Clauses/262/Comments/0")'>威信</span>，降者数万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163240_comment'></div>由是岭外复平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163240_comment'></div>今南蛮叛乱，始由长吏侵扰，积忿无告，及其致寇，曾无戒备，故令屠陷城邑，流毒一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163240_comment'></div>然事已失之于前，谋当善于其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163240_comment'></div>臣愚以谓今兹上策，当以谋取，不可以力胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163240_comment'></div>谓宜且择广、桂二守臣精密毅重、识略足任者，属之方面，付以便宜，使各选举部下文武将吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163240_comment'></div>其两路职司官，朝廷为之慎选，令协力从事，招集户口，各安本业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163240_comment'></div>为发禁卒以代荆、湖见兵，益令募本土丁壮，分屯缘边城邑，使足以保守要害，更相救赴，则贼不敢复窥徼内，自取歼夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163240_comment'></div>峙糗粮，积刍藁，惟事事乃其有备，揣情观变，临事制宜，岁年之时，经营进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163240_comment'></div>盖中国御蛮夷固有大体，图功宜审，虑害宜深，务在保威灵，纾民力，全士马之用，惜金帛之费，先收多福，以绝后虞，此为全胜之算，经远之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163240_comment'></div>傥谓业已兴举，难于散遣，犹有中策，具诸下条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1163240'>二事：蛮寇自入钦、廉，以至陷邕州，残暴黎庶，践食城邑，既而席卷还其薮穴，及今已累月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163240_comment'></div>朝廷旌死事者，而录其孤，推恩厚矣，然及民之惠，犹有阙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163240_comment'></div>《春秋传》：鲁与齐战，曹刿请见鲁君，问将何以战，公曰：「小大之狱，虽不能察，必以情」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163240_comment'></div>刿曰：「此可以一战」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163240_comment'></div>盖谓其重人之命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163240_comment'></div>谓宜特降德音下广南、荆湖，以慰安远人之情，使知陛下哀痛伤恻之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1163240_comment'></div>凡四路百姓耗病之事，加意优恤之，庶国家仁恩有所下逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1163240_comment'></div>至如宥释罜误，以安吏卒之反侧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1163240_comment'></div>开设赏募，以招溪洞之酋豪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1163240_comment'></div>祭酹其亡魂，掩藏其残骼，皆前代常行之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1163240_comment'></div>夫文之所加者深，即武之所服者大；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1163240_comment'></div>德之所施者博，即威之所制者广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1163240_comment'></div>震耀杀戮，生殖长育，功用相承，此天之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1163240'>三事：东南六路，灾荒已甚，官私匮乏，莫相救恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1163240_comment'></div>又缘青苗、助役、市易之法，农民困于输钱，工商窘于射利，谓之钱荒，人情日急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1163240_comment'></div>今王师薄伐，聚于荆潭，调发赋输，即以军兴从事，荐饥之际，供亿实劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1163240_comment'></div>臣闻安民丰财，用兵之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1163240_comment'></div>所有荆湖南北、广南东西四路青苗、助役、市易法，伏望特赐先罢其役法，令复依旧制施行，以此宣布德泽，慰悦民心<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1163240'>四事：臣闻兵者国之大事，死生之地，存亡之道，不可不忧深而思远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1163240_comment'></div>知天知地，胜乃可全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1163240_comment'></div>地者，远近、险易、广狭、生死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1163240_comment'></div>彼蛮之举事，非谓其众可以抗王师，非谓其智谋可以胜中国，而敢为暴害至是者，负山海之险，林薮之深，可以出为寇患，难以入与战斗，乘我无备，因而得逞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1163240_comment'></div>传闻蛮界，其崖壑阻处，篁竹丛薄，不通人行，人有操持器仗者，纵横不得回转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1163240_comment'></div>顷年贡象治路，劣容象行，谓之象路，象过寻复蓊塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1163240_comment'></div>蛮行如鸟兽，穿窜山薮间，自知其路，外人不得而入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1163240_comment'></div>自汉武之伐南粤时，淮南王安已上书谏曰：粤地草木深昧而多水险，中国人入其地，虽百不当一，攻之不可暴取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1163240_comment'></div>兵入其地，必逃散依险阻，委而去，则复相群聚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1163240_comment'></div>留守之，历岁经年，则士卒罢倦，食粮乏绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1163240_comment'></div>方夏暑湿，瘅热呕泄霍乱之病皆作，水居蝮蛇蠚虫，曾未接刃，死伤者已众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1163240_comment'></div>兵法曰：地形者兵之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1163240_comment'></div>故用兵有九地，行山林阻险沮泽，凡难行之道者为圯地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1163240_comment'></div>所由入者隘，所从归者迂，彼寡可以击吾众者为围地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1163240_comment'></div>李靖《兵法》亦曰，夫决胜之策者，在乎断地之形势，观时之利宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1163240_comment'></div>历观前代征蛮者，未尝举大众，非不欲一举殄灭之，地利形势，众不得用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1163240_comment'></div>以故率常羁縻驯养，不使至于决骤，候察警戒，以固疆圉而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1163240_comment'></div>今业已失备，致蛮寇，又悉众而归，王师于征，是行天讨，非救急之兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1163240_comment'></div>救急则欲速，行讨则要之致诛而已，不许收功之缓，当图全胜之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1163240_comment'></div>今兴师十万，日费千金，锐士不可久于瘴乡，骁骑不能驰于鸟径，营栅无所立，粮道不能通，长兵无所施，利器无所用，财殚力屈，徒沮国威，先有自困之形，未见必举之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1163240_comment'></div>何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1163240_comment'></div>若士马而得为用，则蝼蚁之众何足平？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1163240_comment'></div>若士马而不得用，则熊虎之力无所展。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1163240_comment'></div>傥今冬蛮未扑灭，则前春兵须抽退，更图后举，臣窃难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1163240_comment'></div>臣识闇志衰，安知军旅之事，但以古今方册，亦足比测事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1163240_comment'></div>向者岭南有万兵，蛮何敢轻入？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1163240_comment'></div>窃谓今来吊伐，兵在于精，不在于众，可以计取，难以力争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1163240_comment'></div>况淮、浙、江、湖，公私罄匮，人至相食，岂有蓄积？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1163240_comment'></div>计置刍粮，财费过倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1163240_comment'></div>若令诸军且驻襄、邓，将佐僚吏省去冗员，随行厢军量留充役，自馀浮食一切勒回，以宽转输，省赍送，国财民力，实为大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1163240_comment'></div>襄、邓间比年丰稔，仓庾充实，军留就食，足支岁月，士饱马肥，暮秋引发，乘锐诛贼，军气自振，后无艰乏，方可图功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_115_1163240'>五事：臣观蛮事可以计取，难以力争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1163240_comment'></div>盖交阯气俗与诸蛮不类，诸蛮贵种姓，服从贵种，义不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1163240_comment'></div>交阯自国朝已来，已易四姓，皆由大校以权党篡夺，乃是唐末藩镇遗风，故其势易为翻动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1163240_comment'></div>窃闻乾德尚幼，诸酋共事而主谋者三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1163240_comment'></div>今入寇大获金帛子女，各得所欲，蛮夷不义，惟利是贪，归国争功，岂能相下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1163240_comment'></div>如裂其三郡，分授三酋，各为主领，被之告命，使达蛮中，事纵不行，必生猜贰，以至他日衅端常在，多方以挠之，则功易举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1163240_comment'></div>兵法曰：军莫亲于间，事莫密于间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1163240_comment'></div>非精知微密，不能用间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1163240_comment'></div>用间之术，神妙之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1163240_comment'></div>惟时会之为难得，今实得其时会，惟陛下深念所以可付之人，诚上策矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_125_1163240'>六事：林邑国在交阯南境，本象林之地，汉时列为郡县，后有功曹区连者杀县令自立为王，因别名国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1163240_comment'></div>历江南六朝，常羁属之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1163240_comment'></div>隋仁寿中，击破其国，寻而自复，至唐，朝贡不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1163240_comment'></div>国朝以来，为交阯所隔，遂不复至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1163240_comment'></div>然自晋、宋，历代常侵寇交州，《南史》以为林邑素无土田，贪日南地沃，常欲略有之，故乘衅即入日南、九德诸郡，辄留不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1163240_comment'></div>唐末，亦是为群獠构扇，以陷交州，为中国患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1163240_comment'></div>今揣能害交阯者惟林邑，且林邑与交阯相去才千里，本共象林一州之地，今桂州至邕州尚十四程，则是林邑、交阯之间，比邕、桂中间程途犹近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1163240_comment'></div>意者募能使外国之人，谕以讨交阯事，约之师期，使自一面入会王师，如能破交阯者，以日南、九德之地委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1163240_comment'></div>蛮夷贪重利，必自为力，亦伐国一奇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_134_1163240'>七事：窃见安南后军，见在本府待师期，所领南京一将外，又泾原、秦陇之兵约二千五百骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1163240_comment'></div>闻约取七月到本府，正是六、七月间在路，到此又便南行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1163240_comment'></div>夏秋盛热，比至桂州，已行万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1163240_comment'></div>臣前已陈蛮界山林崖壑之险，不通人行，马实难用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1163240_comment'></div>顷年侬贼构乱，狄青破之，闻在邕州西北适近山坂，地势宽平，马得施力，故当时破贼，马军之力为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1163240_comment'></div>今日行军深入蛮地，事与侬贼不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1163240_comment'></div>侬贼，溪洞一首领，入我郡县之间，止是剧盗，击破即糜烂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1163240_comment'></div>今交阯自是一国，窃有土宇，恃其险远，主客势殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1163240_comment'></div>秦渭马军、弓箭手本备羌戎，皆是捍边锐兵劲骑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1163240_comment'></div>有到京师，犹谓不伏水土，辄生疾病，而乃驱之瘴雾沮洳之中，巉崿𥰭蘖之地，水多沙毒，草无藁秸，进又不可以驰突决胜，其能还者无几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1163240_comment'></div>况西北戎虏睢盱顾望，如闻王师远出，边骑多行，忽起风尘，来犯亭障，东西往还，万里莫相赴应，又不比海隅之失备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1163240_comment'></div>凡言国家大事，必曰军马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1163240_comment'></div>军马者，戎事之本，不可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1163240_comment'></div>今边塞简选一锐士，调习一壮马，甚不易得，尽心于国者方知之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1163240_comment'></div>所有昨召边要将官及备边骑兵，愿各遣还本道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1163240_comment'></div>使荆湖多募丁壮，蒐补诸土军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1163240_comment'></div>其将士服习土风，谙识山川地利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1163240_comment'></div>其骑亦只用南马，格式虽小，筋力自壮，惯行险隘，安其水草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1163240_comment'></div>使与中国之人相先后，势之便者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1163240_comment'></div>且使戎虏知朝廷之力，一方有警，边备晏然，不为动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_154_1163240'>八事：伏见安南招讨司期诸留兵，以八月中旬悉至潭州，潭州去桂州十四程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1163240_comment'></div>窃闻岭外岚瘴，八月九月尤甚，谓之黄茅瘴，草黄时瘴气方盛，十月已后，气候始肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1163240_comment'></div>湖南饥荒，粮草难致，久留就食，实费供输；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1163240_comment'></div>若便引行，触冒瘴毒，士马未用，恐多病疫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1163240_comment'></div>若展一月期会，可省一月刍粮，湖湘之民大宽事力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1163240_comment'></div>比至其时，新米已熟，暮秋湖外风土调适，免致人骑枉有损伤，国计军行，两为便利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_160_1163240'>九事：汉宣帝时，先零羌背畔犯塞，用后将军赵充国将击羌虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1163240_comment'></div>充国以为击虏以殄灭为期，必先计策，以待利便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1163240_comment'></div>酒泉太守辛武贤持异，请出击之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1163240_comment'></div>帝下其书，令充国与校尉以下吏士知羌事者博议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1163240_comment'></div>充国执意如初，下其书公卿，议者多同武贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1163240_comment'></div>帝以书敕责充国，督之出战，充国上书谢，因陈兵利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1163240_comment'></div>六月戊申奏，七月甲寅玺书报从充国计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1163240_comment'></div>其秋帝复赐书，令因吏士锐气击虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1163240_comment'></div>充国策虏有必可破之形，上奏请罢骑兵屯田，以待其敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1163240_comment'></div>上报书曰：「皇帝问后将军，言欲罢骑兵万人留田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1163240_comment'></div>如将军之计，虏当何时伏诛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1163240_comment'></div>兵当何时得决？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1163240_comment'></div>熟计其便，复奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1163240_comment'></div>充国上状，言屯田得十二便，出兵失十二利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1163240_comment'></div>上复赐书报曰：「皇帝问后将军，言十二便，闻之，将军其更熟计复奏」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1163240_comment'></div>充国奏言兵以计为本，故多算胜少算，因策虏情以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1163240_comment'></div>充国奏每上，辄下公卿，议臣初是充国计者什三，中什五，最后什八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1163240_comment'></div>有诏诘前言不便者，皆顿首服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1163240_comment'></div>丞相魏相曰：「臣愚不习兵事利害，后将军数画军册，其言常是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1163240_comment'></div>臣任其计必可用也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1163240_comment'></div>上于是报充国曰：「皇帝问后将军，上书言羌虏可胜之道，今听将军，将军计善」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1163240_comment'></div>明年充国上言：羌本可五万人军，凡斩首七千六百级，降者三万一千二百人，溺河饥饿死者五、六千人，定计遗脱入杂羌亡者不过四千人，请罢兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1163240_comment'></div>奏可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1163240_comment'></div>宣帝承汉之盛业，天下富实，四夷宾服，先零小羌顾未足为患害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1163240_comment'></div>遣将出兵，充国所陈皆全师保胜安边之册；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1163240_comment'></div>及上屯田之利，止用吏士万人留屯，因田致谷，以省大费，不失农业，而为武备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1163240_comment'></div>宣帝玺书往复问难，可谓筹计精熟矣，而犹每下公卿议者，以参其得失，其于兵事详重如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1163240_comment'></div>本朝祖宗有边防大事，亦尝博采群议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1163240_comment'></div>今安南之举，兴师十万，万里讨伐，涉危渡险，利害甚多，然圣志先定，国论已协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1163240_comment'></div>伏愿特降玺书，内外近职之臣各令献策，以示博访之道，使四方知陛下重慎之意，三军知陛下忧轸之怀，观其否臧，亦以见群臣之材识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1163240_comment'></div>愚者千虑，尚须有得，采择所长，不为无补。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_190_1163240'></div><div id='poem_sentence_190_1163240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163240'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_83_1163240_0'>⑴ 《易》曰：「悦以先民，民忘其劳；悦以犯难，民忘其死；悦之大，民劝矣哉！」</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163240_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年8月</a>　八月，在知应天府任，上疏论司农寺卖祠庙事。作品：论祠庙事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1163241' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163241' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163241?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论祠庙事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163241")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163241_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163241'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163241'>臣伏见司农寺奏请降下新制，应祠庙并依坊场、河渡之例，召人承买，收取净利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163241_comment'></div>本府勘会在府及管下所管祠庙五十馀处，寻已依应施行讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163241_comment'></div>内有阏伯庙、宋公微子庙已系百姓承买，阏伯庙纳钱四十六贯五百文，微子庙十二贯文，并系三年为一界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163241_comment'></div>臣窃以阏伯远自唐尧迁此商丘之土，主祀大火，而火为国家盛德所乘而王，本朝历世尊为大祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163241_comment'></div>微子，宋之始封君，开国于此，亦为本朝受命建号所因，载于典礼，垂之著令，所当虔洁，以奉时事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163241_comment'></div>又有双庙，乃是唐张巡、许远以孤城死贼，所谓能捍大患者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163241_comment'></div>今既许承买之后，小人以利为事，必于其间营为招聚，纷杂冗亵，何所不至，慢神黩礼，莫甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163241_comment'></div>盖闻有天下者祭百神，故咸秩无文，毖于群祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163241_comment'></div>先圣哲王所以致恭于鬼神者，所以为国家万民，六经训典备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163241_comment'></div>故曰「克典神天，俾作神主」，此人君之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163241_comment'></div>今既岁收细微，而损国体至大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163241_comment'></div>臣愚欲乞朝廷详酌，留此三庙，更不出卖，以称国家严恭典祀、追尚前烈之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1163241_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　秋，在知应天府任，上表乞致仕。作品：乞致仕第一表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163327?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕第一表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163327")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163327'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163327'>臣闻事君主于无隐，诚必自通；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163327_comment'></div>陈力至于不能，势宜知止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163327_comment'></div>辄露引年之恳，仰干从欲之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163327_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163327_comment'></div>伏念臣亲际盛明，早尘华显，文章不足以润色，才业有愧于经纶，历事三朝，殆通四纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163327_comment'></div>内之清涂严闼，极侍从之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163327_comment'></div>外之名城大都，遍藩守之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163327_comment'></div>乏嘉猷以告于后，无膏泽以下于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163327_comment'></div>徒以朴忠愚直之心，资不能改；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163327_comment'></div>至于利害得失之际，初不自谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163327_comment'></div>缘兹过被于圣知，尝亦与闻于国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163327_comment'></div>士儒至此，幸遇已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163327_comment'></div>比奉对于清问，每自陈于衰拙，莫保留宫之钥，坐安乔木之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163327_comment'></div>惟饕顾良时，忽焉而如失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163327_comment'></div>年龄浸迈，疾疹交乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163327_comment'></div>神明溃虚，难支于外虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163327_comment'></div>筋骸摧苶，顿异于前时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163327_comment'></div>荣敢尚贪，福知已过，非独招满盈之祸，惧将累覆焘之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163327_comment'></div>迫此忧危，期于引谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163327_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下曲矜旧物，深烛至诚，贷其无补于涓尘，哀此已疲之犬马，许上还于冠绂，俾退养于丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163327_comment'></div>顺服生经，傥保完于馀喘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163327_comment'></div>愿陪乡老，永歌诵于太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163327_comment'></div>上以成君父始终之仁，下以全臣子进退之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163327_comment'></div>伏乞圣慈特许臣致仕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1163327_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　秋，在知应天府任，上疏论募役法之害。作品：论募役奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1163251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论募役奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年秋）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163251")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163251'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163251'>臣伏睹见行役法，天下共苦不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163251_comment'></div>陛下天高听卑，必闻其利害，切恐中外臣僚未有为国家深忧远虑，精言其本末者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163251_comment'></div>臣既以方拙，上荷知眷，今拜章乞致仕，方俟命解谢，念言重恩，思有以补报而去，故不避诛绝，上此奏封，极陈保邦便民之大计切务，非徒诡激以抗高论而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163251_comment'></div>陛下至圣大明，傥察臣言实有益于国家，即乞发自清衷，特下明诏，停罢此法，复行旧制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163251_comment'></div>旧制之中，有所未安，稍为增损，参定施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163251_comment'></div>诏下之日，四方万姓若有匹夫匹妇不慰悦抃蹈，上感德泽者，则臣请受罔上迷国、坏法乱纪之罪，投放遐裔，以正典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163251_comment'></div>若陛下犹谓臣言未足为信，古者有大疑，谋及卿士、庶人，协同而后有作，即乞露布臣章，俾在廷百辟以至诸路郡县官吏共得尽其公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163251_comment'></div>二者惟在陛下发于神断，以定天下是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163251_comment'></div>若但送之中书，询之执政，无益也，则乞留中不下，非惟有以保全孤臣，抑以致忠义之言，以广四聪之达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163251_comment'></div>不胜为国忧虑，区区之心，惟圣明谅察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163251_comment'></div>所上劄子，具别封进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1163251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年10月</a>　十月，在知应天府任，上疏论京、府、州、军接送高丽使者仪式。作品：论高丽使人相见仪式事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1163252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论高丽使人相见仪式事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163252")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163252'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163252'>臣近见江淮发运司牒报，高丽国进奉使人已到明州，见赴阙前来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163252_comment'></div>次检会先录到枢密院劄子，降下仪式一卷看详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163252_comment'></div>内一项，所至京府州军，知州、通判出城迎接，管设饯送仪式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163252_comment'></div>伏见契丹国信使过北京，只是通判摄少尹接送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163252_comment'></div>今高丽系外蕃，其进奉使人乃陪臣也，宣徽使班秩同见任两府，出城接送，礼更重于契丹，非所以崇国体，示威灵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163252_comment'></div>前次过南京，虽已曾行新仪，其时知府系两省官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163252_comment'></div>今来接送管设相见仪式，伏乞朝廷特行再定颁下，以凭遵守施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　冬，在知应天府任，再上表乞致仕。作品：乞致仕第二表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。系年据《乐全集》卷二九所附诏书。）</span><div id='poem_1163328' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163328' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163328?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163328")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163328_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163328'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163328'>近者辄具奏封，乞从致仁，伏承温诏，未赐俞音，惧汗莫胜，危诚难止<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163328_comment'></div>伏念臣材资极陋，身世至孤，幸缘明主之知，简拔众人之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163328_comment'></div>功勤何有，禄位过盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163328_comment'></div>虽存王室之心，死然后已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163328_comment'></div>而徇公家之事，耄矣无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163328_comment'></div>尚被优容，复叨居守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163328_comment'></div>厉衰残而矍铄，不免旷官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163328_comment'></div>怀宠遇而留连，又将满岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163328_comment'></div>灾衅时作，罢癃日增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163328_comment'></div>念治世之难遭，抑重恩之未报，迫兹颓朽，无以勉彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163328_comment'></div>况今时不乏人，人得其所，自惟进退，何系重轻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163328_comment'></div>捧细札之丁宁，益孤衷之感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163328_comment'></div>朝经所著，惟礼分之有常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163328_comment'></div>天听盖高，冀精诚之可彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163328_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下天无私覆，物遂其生，俯推保息之慈，特轸矜从之造，幸全拙守，俾佚馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163328_comment'></div>既以免钟鸣不止之讥，又以脱器满则倾之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163328_comment'></div>咏陶乐圣，恬莫终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163328_comment'></div>虽在林丘之微，不忘君父之赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1163328_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　冬，在知应天府任，又上表乞致仕。作品：乞致仕第三表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。系年据《乐全集》卷二九所附诏书。）</span><div id='poem_1163329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163329?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163329")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163329'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163329'>伏奉诏敕，以臣近上第二表陈乞致仕所请不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163329_comment'></div>恩由特旨，礼过旧章，恭被训词，倍深感愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163329_comment'></div>在念旧之仁既厚，顾吁天之愿未从，敢沥肺膺，再干黈纩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163329_comment'></div>伏念臣蚤缘一介，获事三朝，滥沐恩荣，祇缘幸遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163329_comment'></div>积岁时而徒久，曾报称之蔑闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163329_comment'></div>比陪近缀之严，每虑素餐之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163329_comment'></div>间因燕见，屡尝恳激于引年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163329_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1163329", 1163329, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>虔奉</span>德音，乃复逡巡而就次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163329_comment'></div>出司留钥，又浃岁筒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163329_comment'></div>桑榆之光，徒引高年之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163329_comment'></div>犬马之力，岂堪长路之驰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163329_comment'></div>虽复勉强，良难振起，故倾丹悃，以乞残骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163329_comment'></div>敢谓圣度宽大，而曲容拙疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163329_comment'></div>天眷恻怛，而尚加抚遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163329_comment'></div>切念事君之礼，虽以承命而为恭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163329_comment'></div>然其陈力有期，至于不能而则止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163329_comment'></div>冀念微守，仰答深仁，谨复尽辞，庶希得谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163329_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下廓日月之照而幽无不烛，推天地之造而物皆遂生，许上麾符，俾安田里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163329_comment'></div>黄发儿齿，退从乡社之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163329_comment'></div>文陛赤墀，徒望天衢之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163329_comment'></div>逶迤末路，诵咏昌辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163329_comment'></div>兹惟君父之慈，岂特丘山之重！</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1163329_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　本年，在知应天府任，上劄子乞立皇子。作品：乞立皇子劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1163239' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163239' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163239?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞立皇子劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163239")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163239_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163239'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163239'>臣闻王者大居正，谓王者君国，当先正其统本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163239_comment'></div>三代远矣，汉唐之盛，君即位，太后、太子多同时建立，立太子不以长幼，其缓者不过二三年，不然则必有故，史策具存矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163239_comment'></div>本朝太祖开国，知天命属于太宗，故不与子，然以储位寓于京尹，太宗自京尹践祚，真宗自京尹登储位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163239_comment'></div>仁宗未尝出閤，即登储位，先帝入纂天统，寻登尊位，尹京故事盖未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163239_comment'></div>陛下即位，及今九年，受天之祜，早有前星之庆，正统大本谓宜时定，上以尊宗庙，下以系天下之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163239_comment'></div>国之大事，僭议罪也，然陛下特以恩意留臣在朝，愚虑所及，敢有不尽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163239_comment'></div>故不避严宪，辄陈忠悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163239_comment'></div>候进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1163239_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年2月12日</a>　二月十二日，在知应天府任，辟苏辙为签书应天府判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　春，在知应天府任，上劄子乞致仕。作品：乞致仕劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。王智勇系此文于熙宁九年秋，此据文中“犬马之年，七十有一”、“涉春以来”云云改。）</span><div id='poem_1163330' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163330' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163330?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163330")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163330'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163330'>臣昨者上章陈乞致仕，伏蒙圣恩降赐诏书不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163330_comment'></div>固合上禀德音，姑安分守，然义不获已，理难茍安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163330_comment'></div>臣自念荒疏，久尘近列，犬马之年七十有一，本期过同天节，方伸前请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163330_comment'></div>涉春以来，旧所患眼疾频发昏痛，至于签押案牍，披览词讼，每委僚佐，一面发遣，事属妨阙，切不自遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163330_comment'></div>而又心气虚烦，动多遗忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163330_comment'></div>深惟此疾非旦夕可愈，虽欲勉强，难以迁延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163330_comment'></div>仰祈天慈，俯垂矜念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163330_comment'></div>前未得谢，已为恩礼之隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163330_comment'></div>今复自陈，可谅恳诚之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163330_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷检会前后奏请，特许致仕，上荷大君之德，下从乡老之游，乐圣安时，以全素履。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1163330_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　春，在知应天府任，再上劄子乞致仕。作品：乞致仕第二劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。王智勇系此文于熙宁九年秋，此据文中“自到南京，又一年半”云云改。）</span><div id='poem_1163331' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163331' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163331?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞致仕第二劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163331")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163331_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163331'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163331'>臣近奏乞致仕，准中书劄子，奉圣旨：所乞不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163331_comment'></div>臣资惷愚，然切尝闻事君之道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163331_comment'></div>盖君犹天也，天可欺欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163331_comment'></div>人之悖德，敢于欺天，而后忍于欺君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163331_comment'></div>臣虽不令，不敢以忠信自期，然一介之守亦粗有所存矣，当有闻于天听，敢不以诚者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163331_comment'></div>臣自熙宁三年赴任陈州，于路得疾，面目偏急，后医治虽痊损，然终不复旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163331_comment'></div>至今语謇涩，心多悸，易忘，时昏眩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163331_comment'></div>故向者在朝，因对屡常面求谢退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163331_comment'></div>夫隆名重禄，是人之所欲，臣非事诡激，独异于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163331_comment'></div>盖自度不任，恐无益于国，以上累于圣知，此实深情所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163331_comment'></div>自到南京又一年半，精力寖衰，惟自知觉，加之目痛，心气虚烦，其于公事，实多妨阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163331_comment'></div>以臣素好道养，故外若可观，然实无功效，譬之土木偶，其中朽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163331_comment'></div>故事，曾处近司而乞致仕者，章再上而得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163331_comment'></div>臣已四请而不允，天恩可谓隆厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163331_comment'></div>今者不避诛殛，复上干于宸扆，言出肝鬲，非有饰辞游说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163331_comment'></div>大明在上，无幽不烛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163331_comment'></div>覆育之下，生物咸遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163331_comment'></div>况臣孤拙，夙被慈眷，今兹微恳，可无感彻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163331_comment'></div>伏乞特开恩旨，许令致仕，仰冀曲成之赐，俾蒙保息之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163331_comment'></div>荷天之休，以终暮齿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1163331_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年5月1日</a>　五月一日，在知应天府任，除东太一宫使，听居南京。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年1月</a>　正月，在应天府，赠苏辙马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1078&endYear=1078')">1078年8月</a>　八月，在应天府，令王巩携《乐全堂杂咏》一卷往徐州请苏轼题封。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年5月14日</a>　五月，在应天府，祭蔡挺。作品：祭蔡资政文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　夏，在应天府，上表乞致仕。作品：再陈乞致仕表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再陈乞致仕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163334")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163334'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163334'>七十致仕，礼有常经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163334_comment'></div>再三上言，情非虚饰<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163334_comment'></div>伏念臣早尘显仕，才本空疏，荐历要途，事无称纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163334_comment'></div>幸遘宝图之肇启，预闻玉几之道扬，首承日月之光，先沾河海之润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163334_comment'></div>特蒙褒举，迥出等夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163334_comment'></div>虚被宠灵，讫微报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163334_comment'></div>久从外补，遂迫颓龄，致章绂以上还，丐筋骸而归尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163334_comment'></div>陛下矜怜庸朽，宽屈典常，加使领于祠宫，俾便安于乡社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163334_comment'></div>臣感恋德泽，难以固辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163334_comment'></div>留连衰迟，体此深养，坐糜厚禄，行复二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163334_comment'></div>诚恐一朝沟壑之虞，遂成终身负乘之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163334_comment'></div>逮兹未耄，得以自陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163334_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下天施无私，父慈均笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163334_comment'></div>出处之际，既曲尽于恩荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163334_comment'></div>进退之间，得粗全于名节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163334_comment'></div>屏伏闾里，咏歌圣时，行苇无牛羊之忧，蒲柳免风霜之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163334_comment'></div>向用五福，式彰皇极之隆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163334_comment'></div>国有四维，少穆民风之厚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1163334_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　夏，在应天府，再上表乞致仕。作品：再陈乞致仕第二表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再陈乞致仕第二表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163335")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163335'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163335'>近上表乞致仕，蒙圣恩降诏不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163335_comment'></div>切以大君保息之慈，人之老者疾者得所养；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163335_comment'></div>治国经常之制，士之进者退者惟其宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163335_comment'></div>不堪陈力之劳，爰上乞骸之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163335_comment'></div>诏函下降，天旨未俞<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163335_comment'></div>臣闻委质大方，前经明训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163335_comment'></div>自古不得谢者，在礼虽或有之，然皆德业高贤，功勋夙望，邦家倚以为重，中外赖之为安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163335_comment'></div>加恩所以特优，被宠诚为无愧，是以义全大体，众罔间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163335_comment'></div>如臣徒以空疏，早蒙简擢，事猷弗逮，报称蔑施，遽及衰疲，遂求引罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163335_comment'></div>而更滥当渥命，遥领真祠，位陪执政之班，禄倍大夫之秩，职优靡预，官责不加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163335_comment'></div>上紊彝章，俯惭私倖，敢循旧典，谨复自陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163335_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下一气均私，大圆丕冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163335_comment'></div>匹夫自尽，各伸所志之微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163335_comment'></div>万物由庚，皆受曲成之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163335_comment'></div>俯谅虔勤之恳，特垂开可之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163335_comment'></div>精骛紫宸，犹结<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1163335", 1163335, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>望云</span>之恋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163335_comment'></div>迹还白社，终怀乐圣之心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1163335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年</a>　夏，在应天府，又上表乞致仕。作品：再陈乞致仕第三表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163336' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163336' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163336?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再陈乞致仕第三表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163336")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163336_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163336'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163336'>臣昨再上表乞致仕，伏蒙圣慈降赐诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163336_comment'></div>章达御前，至诚上彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163336_comment'></div>恩加望外，再请未从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163336_comment'></div>顾惟衰朽之年，久切优安之地，祗膺异数，益不遑宁<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163336_comment'></div>臣闻事君之方，本取精神之用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163336_comment'></div>行己之义，当思名节之存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163336_comment'></div>壮而不勉则非忠，老而不归则忘耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163336_comment'></div>今臣心力日耗，耳目加昏，谢事之期，已逾三岁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163336_comment'></div>瞻天沥恳，盖亦累年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163336_comment'></div>且士之立朝，古有垂训，四十曰强而仕，七十曰老而傅，非异禀之粹灵，必同伦于荒耄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163336_comment'></div>坐糜重禄，虚占近班，偃息在床，优游卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163336_comment'></div>进退非据，俯仰厚颜，众将谓何，没有遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163336_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下金玉百度，纪纲四方，元首股肱，既熙万事，奔走先后，各效所长，在臣去留，奚系轻重？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163336_comment'></div>盖年及而引去，人臣谓之令终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163336_comment'></div>礼得而许归，人君所以加惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163336_comment'></div>仰希慈造，浚发俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163336_comment'></div>国制坦明，式遂区区之分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163336_comment'></div>王道正直，益恢荡荡之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163336_comment'></div>生成亭育之仁，始卒保全之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163336_comment'></div>抚心殒咽，之死靡它。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1163336_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年7月8日</a>　七月八日，在应天府，以太子少师、宣徽南院使致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年8月</a>　八月，致仕居南京，上疏论救苏轼。作品：论苏内翰奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1163242' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163242' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163242?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论苏内翰奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1079年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163242")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163242_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163242'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163242'>臣读《春秋传》，晋叔向被囚时，祁奚老矣，闻之，乘驿而见执政韩起，为言叔向谋而寡过，惠训不倦，宜蒙宽宥之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163242_comment'></div>起与之同乘，以言诸公而免之，祁奚不见叔向而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163242_comment'></div>盖祁奚之言为国，非私叔向也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163242_comment'></div>今日传闻，有使者追苏轼过南京，当属吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163242_comment'></div>臣不详知轼之所坐，而早尝识其为人，起远方孤生，遭遇盛明之世，然其文学实天下之奇才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163242_comment'></div>向举制策高等，而犹碌碌无以异于流辈，陛下振拔，特加眷奖，由是材誉益著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163242_comment'></div>轼自谓见知明主，亦慨然有报上之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163242_comment'></div>但其性资疏率，阙于慎重，出位多言，以速尤悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163242_comment'></div>顷年以来，闻轼屡有封章，特为陛下优容，四方闻之，莫不感叹圣明宽大之德，而尤轼僭易轻发之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163242_comment'></div>今其得罪，必缘故态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163242_comment'></div>但陛下于四海生灵，譬如天之无不覆冒，如地之无不持载，如四时之无不化育，于一苏轼岂所好恶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163242_comment'></div>伏惟英圣之主，方立非常之功，固在广收材能，使之以器，若不弃瑕含垢，则人才有可惜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163242_comment'></div>昔季布亲窘高祖，夏侯胜诽谤世宗，鲍永不从光武，陈琳毁诋魏武，魏徵谋危太宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163242_comment'></div>此五臣者，罪至大而不可赦者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163242_comment'></div>遭遇明主，皆为曲法而全之，卒为忠臣，有补于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163242_comment'></div>自夫子删《诗》，取诸讽刺，以为言之者无罪，闻之者足以戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163242_comment'></div>故诗人之作，其甚者以至指斥当世之事，语涉谤黩不恭，亦未闻见收而下狱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163242_comment'></div>唐韩愈上疏宪宗，以为人主事佛则寿促。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163242_comment'></div>此言至不顺，宪宗初大怒，欲诛而恕之，其后思之，曰：「愈亦是爱我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163242_comment'></div>今轼但以文辞为罪，非大过恶，臣恐付之狴牢，罪有不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163242_comment'></div>惟陛下圣度免其禁系，以全始终之赐，虽重加谴谪，敢不甘心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163242_comment'></div>臣自念朽质，上荷异恩，今伏在田庐，无复涓埃之补，窃慕祁奚虽老，犹不忘公室，而申请叔向之义，僭越上言，自干鼎钺，不任惶惧待罪之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1163242_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1079&endYear=1079')">1079年12月26日</a>　十二月二十六日，致仕居南京，以苏轼“乌台诗案”，罚铜三十斤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年1月</a>　正月，致仕居南京，苏辙谪监筠州酒税，作诗送之。作品：赠别。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见苏辙《栾城三集》卷一《追和张公安道赠别绝句并引》）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年9月</a>　九月，致仕居南京，苏轼以铁藤杖为寿，作诗记之。作品：苏子瞻寄铁藤杖。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。王智勇系此诗于八月，以张方平生日在九月，故改系于九月。）</span><div id='poem_495461' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495461' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495461?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏子瞻寄铁藤杖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495461")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495461_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495461'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495461'>随书初见一枝藤，入手方知锻鍊精。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495461'>远寄只缘怜我老，閒携常似共君行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495461'>静轩独倚身同瘦，小圃频游脚为轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495461'>何日归舟上新洛，拄来河岸笑相迎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495461_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495461'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495461_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年</a>　本年，致仕居南京，有病。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年4月16日</a>　四月十六日，致仕居南京，作文祭赵概。作品：祭赵少师文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭赵少师文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年4月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163646")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163646'>维元丰六年岁次癸亥，四月丙午朔，十六日辛酉，宣徽南院使、检校太傅、太子少师致仕、上柱国张某，谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于乡老赠太子太师赵公之灵：呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163646_comment'></div>仕显王庭，老归乡社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163646_comment'></div>我思故人，今谁存者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163646_comment'></div>并游辞场，麻衣如雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163646_comment'></div>接武重金，同兹大耋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163646_comment'></div>得谢掩关，相望一陌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163646_comment'></div>樽酒笑言，累经青白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163646_comment'></div>公病再期，去年我病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163646_comment'></div>四旬往来，亦足有省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163646_comment'></div>公来视我，欲兴不能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163646_comment'></div>我往候公，公莫能兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163646_comment'></div>忽闻钟声，公已脱屦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163646_comment'></div>非幻不灭，何云去住？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163646_comment'></div>倚户而歌，此事惊俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163646_comment'></div>于行一酹，众哭亦哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163646_comment'></div>先茔拱木，体魄则降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163646_comment'></div>如其知气，岂埋泉壤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163646_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1163646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　本年，致仕居南京。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年3月27日</a>　三月二十七日，致仕居南京，受哲宗赐宽衣、金带、银、帛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年5月22日</a>　五月二十二日，致仕居南京，作文祭王龙图。作品：祭王龙图文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。王龙图，名不详。）</span><div id='poem_1163643' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163643' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163643?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭王龙图文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年5月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163643")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163643_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163643'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163643'>维元祐元年岁次丙寅，五月丁巳朔，二十二日戊寅，太子太保致仕张某谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于故龙图阁直学士、知应天府王公之灵：先正文康，仁朝枢宰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163643_comment'></div>有显事功，国策收载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163643_comment'></div>公起世家，学优而仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163643_comment'></div>直哉维清，风类是似。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163643_comment'></div>惟公之资，信厚为质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163643_comment'></div>颇僻之萌，不接心术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163643_comment'></div>故其立朝，克秉常德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163643_comment'></div>施于政事，允蹈淳则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163643_comment'></div>天地之理，见于简易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163643_comment'></div>君子之道，本于恺悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163643_comment'></div>陪京二年，治用诚恕，民悦无苛，先吝其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163643_comment'></div>方谋借留，言上未及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163643_comment'></div>忽惊钟声，父老相泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163643_comment'></div>虽未上寿，星纪六周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163643_comment'></div>乘其积善，邈与天游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163643_comment'></div>有子克孝，白华之洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163643_comment'></div>逝莫能从，一号三绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163643_comment'></div>我闻伤之，爰作斯诔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163643_comment'></div>著其至性，以章于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163643_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163643_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1163643_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163643'><span class='label'>按：</span>《乐全集》卷三五。又见《永乐大典》卷一四〇四六。<br /></div><div
