id='poem_sentence_130_1163475_comment'></div>诚朝廷慎择守宰，摧抑豪猾，稍宽利路，以优齐民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1163475_comment'></div>刊定律令，除文致毛细之法，务从简易，便于遵守，使民不敢欺冒而试法，吏无以轻重而舞文，则刑虽未尽措而罗阱宽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1163475_comment'></div>臣所谓官师或昧于廉平，以其澄劝之义废者，按周典小宰以六计弊群吏之治，虽治行不同，而同主于廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1163475_comment'></div>故驭吏之法，丽重惟货，而受赇抵禁，相继有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1163475_comment'></div>意者官刑稍以宽弛，部长多所故纵欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1163475_comment'></div>夫贪吏侵刻下民，善事上官，腹心爪牙，各有施设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1163475_comment'></div>及贯盈灭趾，官以墨败，而又赦令屡下，亟蒙释解，丹书未乾，已冀收叙，此所谓官刑稍以宽弛者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1163475_comment'></div>今夫令宰有滥黩之迹，而守倅纵不考验；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1163475_comment'></div>守倅有贪暴之政，而司官隐不上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1163475_comment'></div>及乎恶积而不可掩，事播而不可逭，罪止不察，厥罚至轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1163475_comment'></div>倘使诸统摄之司及于联事之职赃罪相坐，以重其累，则人自为计，下无容奸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1163475_comment'></div>夫峻刑苛禁，诚非治世善化之意，然今风俗流溢，踰轨者众，不严官制，何以立法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1163475_comment'></div>犹乎驭駻突而不利乎衔策，且奔踶而冲蹶矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1163475_comment'></div>古所谓惟齐非齐者，谓此道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1163475_comment'></div>臣所谓风俗颇亏于素朴，以其分度之礼踰者，《书》曰：「惟民生厚，因物有迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1163475_comment'></div>违上所令，从厥攸好」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1163475_comment'></div>故君人者章好以示民俗，慎恶以御民淫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1163475_comment'></div>夫风化之所起，必由上以达下，内而及外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1163475_comment'></div>且万邦表则，在乎王国，今夫彫饰巧伪之器，奇邪纤靡之服，陈鬻于市，流于四方，诈伪奸欺，聚为渊薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1163475_comment'></div>按《周官》以仪辨等则民不越，以度教节则民知足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1163475_comment'></div>古之制民者，使之虽富不异服，无故不食珍，纳币无过五两，合亲不踰一肉，故王道之端，必自制节始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1163475_comment'></div>谓宜益条其僭侈之弊，惟事事为之分度，所示制令，期于必信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1163475_comment'></div>如此，则争夺踰靡之俗革，礼义敦厚之教行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「夷貊虽率化，而时有陵犯边鄙者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1163475_comment'></div>岁时虽嘉靖，而时有儆戒变异者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1163475_comment'></div>兹又以见陛下过虞寇聚之渐，祗畏天戒之重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1163475_comment'></div>然陵犯之扰，虽特徼裔之小丑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1163475_comment'></div>变异之来，兹乃阴阳之大事，何陛下问之后乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1163475_comment'></div>彼群蛮依溪峒之险，恃林岭之阻，窥伺无备，潜出攘掠，结集如蜂蚁，飞迸如鸟兽，守臣无状，自投亡地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1163475_comment'></div>然此之区区者，亦何足以累国威，烦圣虑哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1163475_comment'></div>臣谓边事之重，其在西北乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1163475_comment'></div>北戎通好于我馀三十年，自汉氏已来，夷夏之和而能坚守信誓如今之久者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1163475_comment'></div>非惟怀我恩信，利我聘币，抑当我盛德之世，无衅可乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1163475_comment'></div>夫以利相结者，利尽则交疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1163475_comment'></div>以势相合者，势解则难作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1163475_comment'></div>故有备无患谓之善，无恃不来，在乎多算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1163475_comment'></div>又西陲虽受羁縻，姑息盖久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1163475_comment'></div>自国家失朔方，弃灵武，置戍内地，控扼益蹙，虽贡职外谨，而巢穴内坚，鄙上之防，不可不戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1163475_comment'></div>且自唐氏中世以降，兵农之业离，文武之权分，而政事不齐，国谋相乖矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1163475_comment'></div>今之边事根本，在于庙堂措置设施，固非下臣所得而详，然三军之命系于主帅，是以择将之重，兵事之本，臣请因平寇之问，著于后篇以言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1163475_comment'></div>深惟陛下以天日高明之德，承祖宗淳耀之灵，夙兴视朝，中昃勤听，敕天之命，临此下人，无疆惟休，亦无疆惟恤，宜乎自天降休，百嘉来应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1163475_comment'></div>而灾异数作，谲变仍见，上天勤勤之意，谅不徒发，而必有所属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1163475_comment'></div>间者殒星如雨，流扰失次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1163475_comment'></div>地震定襄，裂而涌泉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1163475_comment'></div>雷不收声，泄于穷冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1163475_comment'></div>又正月以来，日蒙少光，辄或数日不解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1163475_comment'></div>臣鄙儒，昧于天官之学，窃考《春秋》之义及前志天文五行之占，其咎皆由乎阳德微弱，阴道专纵，下为阿比，盗用威柄者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1163475_comment'></div>夫阴之为象，臣道也，妻道也，夷狄之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1163475_comment'></div>天意若曰，将俾陛下察左右之奸，正宫闱以礼，谨边防之备者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1163475_comment'></div>夫人君之道，所以配乾而法天者，盖取乎乾体之刚，天行以健也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1163475_comment'></div>刚故中正无邪，健故运用不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1163475_comment'></div>《洪范》曰：「惟辟作福，惟辟作威」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1163475_comment'></div>《春秋》之义，讥大夫之专者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1163475_comment'></div>夫臣下能窃威福之柄，亦不专在乎执政当国者，茍信听之或过，则欺诬之随生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1163475_comment'></div>蚁漏坏堤，炬遗燎原，杜渐防微，在慎厥始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1163475_comment'></div>此所谓察左右之奸者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1163475_comment'></div>若夫防戚党之侵预，绝女谒之请求，御进取周典之文，均选循汉氏之制，戒留连之害政事，省幽怨以延和气，此所谓正宫闱以礼者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1163475_comment'></div>若夫将校之列，思其智勇可任者为谁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1163475_comment'></div>卒伍之众，察其锐骁无前者有几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1163475_comment'></div>边垒守将，孰有捍城之材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1163475_comment'></div>帷幄谋臣，孰有折冲之算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1163475_comment'></div>至于储峙输发之术，兵械精完之数，有一未备，非先胜之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1163475_comment'></div>此所谓谨边防之备者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1163475_comment'></div>夫是三者，惟在陛下存神而远照，凝虑而深思，利柄勿以假人，主威贵乎独运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1163475_comment'></div>虽箧椟已固，扃钥不可不严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1163475_comment'></div>虽垣墉既修，关键不可不设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1163475_comment'></div>用乾刚以弭阴异，谨人事以应天心，如此，则灾异不足消，休祥不足致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1163475_comment'></div>且圣策俾臣精心极虑，无有所隐，臣既冒陛下斯举矣，敢悼后害而为身谋者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1163475_comment'></div>亦在陛下宽狂妄之诛，以来天下至当之言焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「古之制度可用于今，今之章程有盭于古，并宜条列，勿事猥并」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1163475_comment'></div>臣谨按《春秋》之义，讥变古易常者，而又善变之正者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1163475_comment'></div>盖国之善制，不可轻变，其未至者，变之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1163475_comment'></div>伏以先制旧法，彼此一时，事体权宜，各有云设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1163475_comment'></div>诚大制度或大典章，为世规摹，著在甲令，故当守而勿失，谨以奉行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1163475_comment'></div>至于凡小事为，因时消息，或迹存而理异，或法久而奸生，必践而行，以为无改于祖宗之道，此所谓胶柱而鼓瑟，刻舟以求剑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1163475_comment'></div>《易》曰：「穷则变，变则通，通则久」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1163475_comment'></div>故复而不厌，久而不弊之谓道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1163475_comment'></div>昔先王之作为爵禄赏罚，以亲揽其柄，是以为天下之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1163475_comment'></div>见劳授赏，则众誉不能进无功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1163475_comment'></div>见恶行诛，则众谗不能退无罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1163475_comment'></div>若政无大小，人无善恶，进退用舍，一取诸旧，是爵禄赏罚不在人主而在例也，与夺之柄于陛下何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1163475_comment'></div>臣愿陛下革弊去蠹，无不忍之爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1163475_comment'></div>拔材赏忠，无疏贱之隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1163475_comment'></div>大稽诸古，小度于今，使天下之耳目常新，万务之本原必正，无曰引例合义而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1163475_comment'></div>如此，则古之制度斯用于今，今之章程自合于古矣，帝王之制，不亦光大乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「立乐之方，何以答神祇而来瑞物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1163475_comment'></div>祥刑之要，何以空囹圄而致和气」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1163475_comment'></div>臣前所谓谨工师之职，齐货利之制者备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1163475_comment'></div>夫乐作而顺气成象则和，和则瑞物至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1163475_comment'></div>故夔曰：「于！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1163475_comment'></div>予击石拊石」，「鸟兽跄跄，《箫韶》九成，凤凰来仪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1163475_comment'></div>刑得中则清，清则和气应矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1163475_comment'></div>故《周官》曰：「以刑教中，则民不暴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1163475_comment'></div>夫是，则和气其有不通乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「遴拣多士，懋建庶官，咸有常规，可为来范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1163475_comment'></div>唐氏考功之格，善最悉陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1163475_comment'></div>汉家刺部之仪，科条具举」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1163475_comment'></div>臣按《唐六典》考功考课之法有四善：一曰德义有闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1163475_comment'></div>二曰清慎明著；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1163475_comment'></div>三曰公平可称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1163475_comment'></div>四曰恪勤匪懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1163475_comment'></div>善状之外，有二十七最：献可替否，拾遗补阙，为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_232_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/801/Comments/0")'>近侍</span>之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1163475_comment'></div>铨衡人物，简擢良材，为选司之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1163475_comment'></div>扬清激浊，褒贬必当，为考校之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1163475_comment'></div>礼制仪式，动合经典，为礼官之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1163475_comment'></div>音律克谐，不失节奏，为乐官之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1163475_comment'></div>决断不滞，与夺合理，为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_237_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/816/Comments/0")'>判事</span>之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1163475_comment'></div>部统有方，警守无失，为宿卫之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1163475_comment'></div>兵士调习，戎装充备，为督领之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1163475_comment'></div>推鞫得情，处断平允，为法官之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1163475_comment'></div>雠校精审，明于刊定，为校正之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1163475_comment'></div>承旨敷奏，吐纳明敏，为宣纳之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1163475_comment'></div>训道有方，生徒充业，为学官之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1163475_comment'></div>赏罚严明，攻战必胜，为将帅之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1163475_comment'></div>礼义兴行，肃清所部，为政教之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1163475_comment'></div>详录典正，词理兼举，为文史之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1163475_comment'></div>访察精审，弹举必当，为纠正之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1163475_comment'></div>明于勘覆，稽失无隐，为勾检之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1163475_comment'></div>职事修理，供承强济，为监掌之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1163475_comment'></div>功课皆充，丁匠无怨，为役使之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1163475_comment'></div>耕耨以时，收穫成课，为屯官之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1163475_comment'></div>谨于盖藏，明于出纳，为仓库之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1163475_comment'></div>推步盈虚，究理精密，为历官之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1163475_comment'></div>占候医卜，效验居多，为方术之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1163475_comment'></div>讥察有方，行旅无壅，为关津之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1163475_comment'></div>市廛不扰，奸滥不行，为市司之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1163475_comment'></div>收养肥硕，蕃息孳多，为牧官之最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1163475_comment'></div>边境肃清，城隍修理，为镇防之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1163475_comment'></div>类其善最，校定内外文武官吏之课为九等焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1163475_comment'></div>汉刺史以六条察所部二千石，其略曰豪右兼并，占田过制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1163475_comment'></div>曰二千石纳引赇贿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1163475_comment'></div>曰喜怒任情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1163475_comment'></div>曰选署不平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1163475_comment'></div>曰子弟请托；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1163475_comment'></div>曰违公下比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1163475_comment'></div>此科条之目也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「士民之类，愚众贤寡，奢僭相尚，习以成风，不严而化，其术安在」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1163475_comment'></div>夫戒奢防僭之术，臣既略陈于前矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1163475_comment'></div>盖民之为名，谓其泯然无知辨者，愚之众也，所禀盖然，其动静趣习，惟上是视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1163475_comment'></div>故曰：「君子之德风，小人之德草，草上之风必偃」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1163475_comment'></div>言下化上之速也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1163475_comment'></div>在《易·履卦》《象》曰：「君子以辨上下，定民志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1163475_comment'></div>故上下诚辨，则民志斯定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1163475_comment'></div>其在《节卦》《象》曰：节「以制数度，议德行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1163475_comment'></div>夫数度有等，则贵贱章别；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1163475_comment'></div>德行见奖，则贤愚自分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1163475_comment'></div>此则节之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1163475_comment'></div>陛下念民习侈，屡以为问，有以见圣意之深悯乎末俗之不厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1163475_comment'></div>间者颁下诏旨，戒服用之尤溢者，媮靡少损矣，然未足以称陛下淳俭之教，意者民之所效者，其本未正欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1163475_comment'></div>《春秋》之义，法之所建，必自贵者始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1163475_comment'></div>陛下诚欲清天下之弊，其自诸戚里豪贵大臣之家以先之，上徐趋而下奔走矣，不严而化，此其术也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「蠢尔微寇，何以革其非心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1163475_comment'></div>漠然大钧，何以致其顺序」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1163475_comment'></div>夫裔夷微孽，臣既列于前篇矣，其择将之事，请得复尽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1163475_comment'></div>今禁卫千幕，环络京甸，什五相长，偏裨相承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1163475_comment'></div>六军之重，统乎元帅，而皆起奔走之勤旧，积恩泽以稍迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1163475_comment'></div>以躯力为武，以引强为材，智不足以达机变，惠不足以抚部伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1163475_comment'></div>冒没宠利，优游太平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1163475_comment'></div>轻肥相夸，坐受姑息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1163475_comment'></div>设不幸遐陬有啸聚之寇，边隅有侵牧之扰，虽受成于上，指纵在人，非惟师律之不臧，智勇之无恃，是其肯委易得之富庶，冒难死之锋刃乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1163475_comment'></div>故将不知兵，主不择将，无功厚赐，无劳重禄，皆法所忌者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1163475_comment'></div>向者朝廷念将帅之材难，是以择搢绅之能者，然其所得，率多善奔走人事，以为宠利之路而已，其钤略才艺不谓无之，然固鲜焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1163475_comment'></div>诚国家因为科条，损益其制，使夫衣冠之应诏者，为设机宜十问以策之，必有稽于军志精合，于时体者为通，擢之理戎，参于列校，其方略智勇固未之尽，抑犹愈于徒进者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1163475_comment'></div>至于和大钧，致大顺，兹由民心下和，则和气上应尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1163475_comment'></div>时使薄歛以富之，缓刑弛力以佚之，制节谨度以平之，择吏审令以安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1163475_comment'></div>是以政和则民和，民和而后阴阳和，阴阳和则大钧调而顺气序矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「且道者万世无弊，而前代有忠文相救之说；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1163475_comment'></div>法者百王不易，而旧典著轻重异用之宜」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1163475_comment'></div>夫董生推道，盖探其本而言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1163475_comment'></div>荀卿论刑，盖有所激而发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1163475_comment'></div>彼三代之弊，虽有忠文相救之说，至于法天顺人之意，其可改乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1163475_comment'></div>此则万世无弊之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1163475_comment'></div>彼治乱之世，虽有轻重异用之宜，至于遏恶扶善之用，其可殊乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1163475_comment'></div>此则百王不易之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「《戴记》为国有九经，所宜诠次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1163475_comment'></div>《周官》辨地以五物，咸为敷陈」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1163475_comment'></div>夫为国有九经者：脩身则不惑，尊贤则道立，亲亲则诸父昆弟无怨，礼大臣则不悖，体群臣则士之报礼重，子庶民则百姓劝，来百工则财用足，柔远人则四方归之，怀诸侯则天下畏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1163475_comment'></div>此为国之九经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1163475_comment'></div>《周官》大司徒之职，以土会之法，辨五地之物生：一曰山林，其动物宜毛物，其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_309_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1047/Comments/0")'>植物</span>宜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_309_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1047/Comments/1")'>皂物</span>，其民毛而方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1163475_comment'></div>二曰川泽，其动物宜鳞物，其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_310_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1051/Comments/0")'>植物</span>宜膏物，其民黑而津；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1163475_comment'></div>三曰丘陵，其动物宜羽物，其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_311_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1055/Comments/0")'>植物</span>宜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_311_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1055/Comments/1")'>皂物</span>，其民专而长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1163475_comment'></div>四曰坟衍，其动物宜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_312_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1058/Comments/0")'>介物</span>，其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_312_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1059/Comments/0")'>植物</span>宜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_312_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1059/Comments/1")'>荚物</span>，其民皙而瘠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1163475_comment'></div>五曰原隰，其动物宜裸物，其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_313_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1063/Comments/0")'>植物</span>宜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_313_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1063/Comments/1")'>丛物</span>，其民<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_313_1163475", 1163475, "Clauses/1064/Comments/0")'>丰肉</span>而庳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1163475_comment'></div>此五地之物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1163475_comment'></div>圣策曰：「固将施之于行事，匪独取之于虚文」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1163475_comment'></div>兹以见陛下虚己以咨询，留听于葑菲者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1163475_comment'></div>臣才识迂鄙，不通于政，至于所发，亦庶几有以上当圣心者，陛下不废其言，择其近是者粉泽而用之，使天下知国家设科取士之道不为虚名，则岂惟臣之独被宠灵也哉，固朝廷之盛美者已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1163475_comment'></div>臣昧死上对<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1163475_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_319_1163475'>「虽」原作「匪」，据右引改；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1163475_comment'></div>「小丑」原作「强敌」，据汪藏本及右引改。</div><div id='poem_sentence_320_1163475_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163475'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_318_1163475_0'>⑴ 《乐全集》卷一八。又见《历代名臣奏议》卷三〇。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163475_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年7月</a>　七月，在京作《谢贤良方正登科启》作品：谢贤良方正登科启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三二。）</span><div id='poem_1163433' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163433' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163433?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢贤良方正登科启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163433")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163433_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163433'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163433'>伏奉制恩，滥蒙选第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163433_comment'></div>丹扆出策，临问乎大政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163433_comment'></div>青幄陈对，居惭于昧理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163433_comment'></div>惟设科之体大，矧取人之材难，敢自谓能，期于一得，抚心知忝，被恩良优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163433_comment'></div>昔汉之官人，并开数路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163433_comment'></div>唐之辨论，广设众科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163433_comment'></div>故其名公伟人，磊落之器，由此其选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163433_comment'></div>昌言谠论，经济之具，于是乎在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163433_comment'></div>国家受命，祖宗稽古，已治不有，咨周于下，时延特起之士，求闻警切之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163433_comment'></div>奇杰之才，间复出萃，风流不绝，于兹有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163433_comment'></div>皇上统揽九维，缉熙百志，惟是事事之备，念夫安安之难，复举方闻，讲求王务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163433_comment'></div>自非发论合乎正道，可以美教化；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163433_comment'></div>策事得其远体，可以尊朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163433_comment'></div>有大制度，能探沿革之本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163433_comment'></div>当大施舍，能折损益之衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163433_comment'></div>理之渊源无不贯，物之情伪无不通，则安能沛然来思，膺兹访逮，建高谊而列上，副清衷之虚伫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163433_comment'></div>如某者一介自守，诸虑本恬，生遘昌期，世蹈淳则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163433_comment'></div>幼居里社，知从田苏之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163433_comment'></div>早喜古学，时就君山之讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163433_comment'></div>逍遥内乐，拂略世纷，未知朝市之中，为趋利名之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163433_comment'></div>一廛莽甚，四壁落然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163433_comment'></div>无如亲甘，始谋禄食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163433_comment'></div>属深诏之再下，辱宗工之交荐，时以异等，对于大廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163433_comment'></div>初命起家，典校四部之籍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163433_comment'></div>有民与社，庇身百乘之邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163433_comment'></div>幸在僻处，居多暇时，因得缉所管窥，暨尝道听，聊补稗官之说，归备遒人之献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163433_comment'></div>亦既奏御，留置乎尚方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163433_comment'></div>俄复得旨，许预乎大对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163433_comment'></div>延阁覆实，有司上名，得召便殿，咸如初礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163433_comment'></div>射之饮羽，往尝出于邂逅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163433_comment'></div>昏于注金，大惧失乎兢跼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163433_comment'></div>上倚公朝之明，不恤狂言之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163433_comment'></div>十驾已病，未知税鞅之所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163433_comment'></div>九霄云远，莫遇便风之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163433_comment'></div>昔平津再上，初非优等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163433_comment'></div>刘蕡如何，乃犹不第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163433_comment'></div>敢以一得之虑，邀乎万全之功？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163433_comment'></div>且自复六科，逮兹十祀，诏书三下，中选几人，夫何不材，再滥名等？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163433_comment'></div>自非朝家乐育，宗儒慎择，岂此孤陋，而能致然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163433_comment'></div>此盖某官公议无阿，斯文自任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163433_comment'></div>四方依乎光景，下自成蹊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163433_comment'></div>深虑属乎孤平，优为之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163433_comment'></div>致兹庸薄，获被甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163433_comment'></div>得不夙夜丹心，初终一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163433_comment'></div>敢趋末路，以徇耳目之前，义不茍生，而为戮笑之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163433_comment'></div>上全国体之重，下报化钧之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163433_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1163433_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='aeb96f7112a14a22867c4d677dac3ff2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aeb96f7112a14a22867c4d677dac3ff2");'><span id='aeb96f7112a14a22867c4d677dac3ff2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1042')">1041-1042年</a>，35-36岁</div><div id='aeb96f7112a14a22867c4d677dac3ff2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年3月</a>　三月，被召赴阙，赐五品服章，除直集贤院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年3月</a>　三月，在京直集贤院，有《谢直集贤院启》作品：谢直集贤院启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三二。此启所上对象不详。）</span><div id='poem_1163432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢直集贤院启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163432")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163432'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163432'>蒙恩充前件职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163432_comment'></div>伏以国家懋建百职，分治众政，惟是图书之府，为养材用之宅，天下英俊，萃为渊薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163432_comment'></div>至于岩廊承弼之重，帷幄侍从之列，凡邦之彦，由此其选，服命无忝，必士之择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163432_comment'></div>如某者，材靡堪乎诸用，艺弗精于一家，天与愚野之姿，早习汗漫之技，遭时获售，解巾从政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163432_comment'></div>姑胥下邑，吴江之水清；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163432_comment'></div>会稽东郡，越山之云白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163432_comment'></div>皆仕宦逍遥之地，实朝廷爱育之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163432_comment'></div>况堂有二人，年高多病，旁无手足，与同喜惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163432_comment'></div>所畏迹涉乎宠利之末，敢以身徇乎耳目之前？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163432_comment'></div>而辟书交来，皆自其听过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163432_comment'></div>朝旨除遣，抑由于名使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163432_comment'></div>引趋陛戟，临锡笥衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163432_comment'></div>且谓陋才，顷尘诏选，免给尚书之札，遂参丽正之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163432_comment'></div>岂无老成之人，盖有肤敏之士，学则稽古，才堪成务，居然厩騄未登伯乐之图，奚此社樗翻回匠石之顾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163432_comment'></div>此盖某官深怀奖善，助国树人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163432_comment'></div>导源使流，本乎长者之论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163432_comment'></div>凭风载响，成兹竖子之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163432_comment'></div>致此莝微，谬膺推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163432_comment'></div>敢不深考所履，益期寡咎，冀于风雨之晦，见乎雪霜之色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163432_comment'></div>愚柔自勉，无怠乎百千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163432_comment'></div>涓撮未遗，或增乎万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163432_comment'></div>上报施生之大，次酬荐宠之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163432_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1163432_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年6月</a>　六月，除太常丞、知谏院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年6月</a>　六月，在京知谏院，有《让除谏官表》作品：让除谏官表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163282' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163282' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163282?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让除谏官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163282")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163282_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163282'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163282'>今月二十一日，閤门领告敕一道，授臣直集贤院、知谏院事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163282_comment'></div>肤短之材，孤远之迹，选除忽及，愧惕无涯<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163282_comment'></div>伏以国家分命百工，并釐众务，惟兹谏职，实裨治要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163282_comment'></div>自非素履约乎中道，处议得其远体，详晓事物，该知典故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163282_comment'></div>有大制度，能探沿革之本；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163282_comment'></div>当大施舍，能折损益之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163282_comment'></div>茍尘献替之地，是贻朝廷之辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163282_comment'></div>况今陛下励精于上，大臣宣力于下，听纳不倦，谋能并进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163282_comment'></div>是方辑明纪律，式遏寇暴，宜得通识，上助有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163282_comment'></div>众材森如，多士萃止，上简天眷，岂少臣者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163282_comment'></div>傥陛下矜其愚而锡保全之造，公朝体其介而敦爱育之仁，许臣且以旧官就馆供职，上免旷官之咎，下逃十指之讥，兹实由衷之私，窃积听卑之望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1163282_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月</a>　七月，在京知谏院，撰《四箴》作品：四箴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年7月</a>　七月，在京知谏院，上《请止中使传宣诸司奏》作品：请止中使传宣诸司奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1163220' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163220' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163220?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请止中使传宣诸司奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163220")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163220_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163220'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163220'>切闻近日中使传宣诸司，颇为烦数，其至三司，日或数次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163220_comment'></div>臣闻「王言惟作命」，「百官承式」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163220_comment'></div>《洪范》五事，「言曰从」，「从作乂」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163220_comment'></div>故王者之言，是谓号令，令出惟行，不行则权纲亏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163220_comment'></div>今夫屑屑冗微之事，皆贱者之所亲，责在攸司，各有程式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163220_comment'></div>发输督促，动烦宣下，所司既被受，其有不可奉行者，又须禀复，或却寝罢，下成废命，上为损威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163220_comment'></div>习以为常，恬弗知怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163220_comment'></div>欲乞今后除有指挥中书、枢密院事特降中使外，自馀细务合下三司提举司、开封府等处者，只乞传宣中书、枢密院劄下逐处，有司或敢违慢，自应合行勘责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163220_comment'></div>即事干急速，不容留滞，即乞宣付入内内侍省相度事体缓急，须即施行者，具录宣旨报下所司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163220_comment'></div>所冀出纳有章，上下得体。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1163220_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年8月</a>　八月，在京知谏院，劾王逵肆情害物。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年8月</a>　八月，在京知谏院，连续上疏论陕西、河东等募强壮弓手充兵不便。作品：论遣使往陕西河东等募强壮充兵奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二一。）</span>论弓手强壮充军不便事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1163165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163165?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论遣使往陕西河东等募强壮充兵奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163165")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163165'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163165'>臣伏见宣差朝臣分路往陕西、河东、京东西路，于前来点差强壮、弓手中招募愿充军人分配宣毅、保捷指挥者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163165_comment'></div>臣切思此举事系安危，敢竭微衷，上裨国论，谨列不便事件及臣愚所见如左：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1163165'>一、自去岁初降敕命点差强壮、弓手之时，民间喧然，皆言此时点差，虽以强壮、弓手为名，实欲黥补军籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163165_comment'></div>敕旨屡下，丁宁再三，谕以朝廷点差之意，只要各护县乡，必不起从征戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163165_comment'></div>郡县又多方安辑，民犹猜哗及今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163165_comment'></div>去冬教习，寻放归业，乡闾窃语方以少定，然名在弓手之籍者，居常摇恐不自安，每闻一使出行州县，辄相扇动，谓来调发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163165_comment'></div>今此命忽下，果如民所素料，此后命令无复可信，此其不便一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163165_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1163165'>一、宣命虽令使人招召情愿，缘先来点差弓手多是高赀之家，例皆衣食无阙，岂有情愿充军之人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163165_comment'></div>臣闻所差朝臣已相与议云：此来受命朝廷，意在倚办，若至郡县无人应募，须与逐处官吏迫致之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163165_comment'></div>窃惟所差使臣，盖以朝行集事寻常浅见之人，复思郡县官吏材术足任者无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163165_comment'></div>今既设以赏利，惟知用心干蹈，若其谋之匪臧，或至变生不测，奸猾乘衅，相激噪聚，万一惊扰，更成厉阶，此其不便二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163165_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1163165'>一、所差使臣既与郡县官吏抑迫百姓，令伏充军，即须团结押赴京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163165_comment'></div>充军之人既非情愿，若其上路，因与亲戚离诀，更有悔心，中道逃散，安能防遏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163165_comment'></div>既不敢各归本土，聚依萑苻，远近相应，展转结连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163165_comment'></div>或奸豪之有谋，乘郡县之无备，其势一扰，必劳安辑，此其不便三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163165_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1163165'>一、今京东西路颇为饥歉，民既艰食，居常犹为寇盗，一夫首难，奔赴必多，此其不便四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163165_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1163165'>一、强壮、弓手各在郡县，未去农业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163165_comment'></div>若朝廷用汉代更之术，因唐防秋之法，入耕出战，递为防戍，则是农不去业，兵不乏备，不困帑廪之积，常得丁壮之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163165_comment'></div>今既籍为正兵，处之连营，则其衣食财用终身仰给县官，此其不便五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163165_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1163165'>一、已降御札，冬至将行郊礼，远近郡县尤宜肃静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163165_comment'></div>夫愚而不可欺，弱而不可胜者，百姓也，绥之斯和，动之斯危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163165_comment'></div>武有七德，安民为本，事规未兆，敝犹不救，若又迫之，是启乱也，则朝廷之忧不在四鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163165_comment'></div>夫祸起所忽，慝生有阶，秦之胜、广，汉之黄巾，唐之巢、让，是皆始于乌合之众，此其不便六也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163165_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1163165'>凡此六患，昭然在目，不可不深虑，不可不过防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163165_comment'></div>臣以一介贱微，见识浅近，诚不足以参国论，赞圣谋，但以职在谏曹，义当有犯无隐，故陈愚管，上祈裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163165_comment'></div>臣谓陕西、河东其近里州郡，乞将前来点差强壮、弓手等中分，其半戍边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163165_comment'></div>每九月防秋，至二月放归，岁一代更；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163165_comment'></div>留其半防守本州，以时训练。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163165_comment'></div>当就戍之时，依出军人官与装费，冬给衣赐，日支口食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163165_comment'></div>盖民所以惧乎籍之为兵者，不惟前冒锋刃矢石之难，且重去其土，终身与亲爱姻族永相隔别，此其大戚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163165_comment'></div>今若番休递戍，终是不离本乡，冀望边事渐宁，即当息肩安业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163165_comment'></div>昔太宗皇帝籍两河之人以为乡兵，于时识者亦悼其失策，盖不若因两河强壮，使之捍边，壮者入籍，衰者出役，不衣库帛，不食廪粟，边不阙戍，民不去农，何在乎蓄之营堡而后为官军也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163165_comment'></div>又闻于时籍乡兵之际，因大军方集之威，犹恐其乱，乃密诫诸州郡尅期一日而事毕，故民虽奸谋相动，不复及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163165_comment'></div>今朝廷既惜强籍之名，又为必籍之事，命两朝臣分使一路，周环三二十郡，幅员三数千里，或未能亲到，但行文移州县官吏，方且各率所见，异同纷起，但恐使人一出，民心一摇，后虽悔之，或所难及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163165_comment'></div>愿朝廷审加图议，事不惮改，追还所下逐路转运司宣命，停所差官勿遣，实天下幸甚，国家之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163165_comment'></div>慺慺丹诚，窃冀昭纳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1163165_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1163166' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163166' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163166?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论弓手强壮充军不便事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163166")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163166_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163166'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163166'>近睹宣命差官往陕西等四路募强壮、弓手之充军者，事甚不便，已于十九日具状奏论，未闻朝廷别有处分，臣不胜忧疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163166_comment'></div>敢再论其事，至诸召募之状已具条陈，今但言其必不可之理有二：若召人情愿充军者，而后籍之，臣料必不集事，今此遣使，徒使朝廷失大信于天下，州县惶惑，人心惊扰而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163166_comment'></div>必欲集事，则非强致之不可，果强而致之，喧哗相动，祸变不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163166_comment'></div>故此召募，宽之则事不集，急之则促乱，臣前言所谓必不可之理有二，此之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163166_comment'></div>臣虽愚浅，忝居谏列，非不知边陲势急，戍备事大，卫兵禁旅调发不足，今日之举，盖朝廷非所获已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163166_comment'></div>臣愚深思，募人所以防祸难，若今之为，人未必为国家用，适所以致祸难者，但恐朝廷之忧不在边鄙，而在四郊之外矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163166_comment'></div>向者群盗窃发，潜匿山谷，发卒数十倍捕之，犹不能即擒，久乃幸得自溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163166_comment'></div>近日州郡奏报，比比有奸盗相聚，又京东西旱涝相仍，民方艰食，正月向尽，首种未入，朝廷尚须留意安辑，振其不足，更下此令，民心谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163166_comment'></div>凡民之籍者，四路不啻三十万人，今各不自保，于去留之间，此其搆扇唱和，可不过为防虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163166_comment'></div>万一不逞之辈乘隙啸动，臣恐郡县官吏不弃城而遁，即拱手就拘，虽以墨翟之智，不能以无备守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163166_comment'></div>以陛下神圣威德而宗庙之灵，天赞神助，则臣非所敢知者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163166_comment'></div>若专以人事料之，但见危形，未见安理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163166_comment'></div>往者，唐氏自高祖至懿宗传十九主矣，其间戎狄侵轶，数至畿甸，大盗滔天，舆驾出狩屡矣，而卒全大业者，所恃民心不去，根本未摇，信令尚行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163166_comment'></div>及懿宗之世，南蛮陷交州，大起天下兵，转货食以事之，徐方戍卒相率回戈，连陷江淮，遂启仙芝、巢、让之寇，生民涂炭，因此危社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163166_comment'></div>今日之举，唐鉴未远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163166_comment'></div>夫贤智之谋事，有万全之形，而后有一跌之虞，犹不以侥倖为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163166_comment'></div>今天下犹古也，陛下奈何处成败之计如是之易乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163166_comment'></div>伏愿陛下更与大臣从容讲求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163166_comment'></div>至如京东、西州郡见管厢禁诸军亦不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163166_comment'></div>比州郡患于乏人，每使命拣选，不无多名留占。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163166_comment'></div>若量逐处民兵，随其众寡分番于本州防守，尽代见军赴边，此亦人情所便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163166_comment'></div>朝廷机事，非臣详知，揣摩以言，精切未尽，屡展螗螂之臂，上冒雷霆之威，盖惟大义之所存，故于蕞躯而无爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163166_comment'></div>不胜宗庙之忧，区区激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1163166_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年8月</a>　八月，在京知谏院，上疏请节录《唐书》纪传进御。作品：请节录唐书纪传进御奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1163207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163207?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请节录唐书纪传进御奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163207")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163207'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163207'>荀子曰：「圣王有百，吾孰法焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163207_comment'></div>「欲观圣王之迹，则于其粲然者矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163207_comment'></div>「禹、汤有传政，而不若周之察也，非无善政也，久故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163207_comment'></div>传者久则论略，近则论详」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163207_comment'></div>当今之世而君必谈尧、舜，臣必称禹、稷，是迂儒拘生之论，非适时济用者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163207_comment'></div>伏以唐氏有天下三百年，其间治乱得失详矣，朝廷立国之纪，典刑制度因于唐者也，故观今之政，唐氏最近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163207_comment'></div>臣以不敏，忝职谏司，思有以荐乙夜之亲程，广观文之典学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163207_comment'></div>欲乞今后节略《唐书》纪传中事迹，今可施行、有益治道者，间录一两条上进，伏乞万几之暇，特赐开览，善者可以为准的，恶者可以为鉴戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163207_comment'></div>兹亦贾谊、晁错借秦以喻汉事之意也。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1163207'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1163207_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年8月</a>　八月，在京知谏院，上疏请禁止内臣、外戚等侥求过分。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年8月</a>　八月，在京知谏院，上疏请罢陕西招讨经略司。作品：请罢陕西招讨经略司事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_1163150' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163150' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163150?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请罢陕西招讨经略司事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163150")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163150_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163150'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163150'>窃惟羌虏叛命，王师致讨，分命重臣，委之统帅，故授夏竦陕西招讨等使，四路军政实节制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163150_comment'></div>空国事边，于兹三岁，师惟不出，出则丧败；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163150_comment'></div>寇惟不来，来必得志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163150_comment'></div>控要城寨，残荡无几，内属藩落，驱掠向尽，钝兵挫锐，财殚力屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163150_comment'></div>去岁刘平、石元孙之没，夺范雍节钺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163150_comment'></div>今春任福之败，罢韩琦经略使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163150_comment'></div>中外皆谓朝廷威罚不举，责效太轻，然犹薄示损惩，微塞物论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163150_comment'></div>安有权握大众，坐玩寇敌，至于覆军杀将，蹙国损威，而曰我不预知，是安用名为统帅也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163150_comment'></div>昔自三代至于春秋列国，凡起军旅，未有其国君不亲预戎事者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163150_comment'></div>自汉至唐，兴兵举众，未有元帅不身先士卒在于行阵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163150_comment'></div>后汉段颎征西羌，二十馀年未尝蓐寝，讫平羌虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163150_comment'></div>若将帅奋身许国，发愤殄寇，有如是之臣，则陛下何忧焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163150_comment'></div>事既乖失，理须更张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163150_comment'></div>臣窃听舆人之议，皆谓前后丧师，非贼能败我，我自取败尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163150_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163150_comment'></div>凡诸边臣禀令招讨司，机宜事会不失之急，即失之缓，勇者不得施其力，智者不得专其谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163150_comment'></div>而又爱恶相攻，异同相戾，文檄矛盾，人无适从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163150_comment'></div>且朝廷设此司，所以使臂指相用，首尾相救，决众谋于独断，通四路为一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163150_comment'></div>近如麟、府之围，虽非陕西疆域，然为统帅，茍急国患，即未能请行赴救，犹须耀师境上，助为声援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163150_comment'></div>陛下旰食轸虑，遣敕使赍玺书督之出偏师，使遥牵贼后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163150_comment'></div>逗遛立异，竟不奉命，至使贼如蹈无人之境，因以平丰州，夷宁远，麟州几陷，今虽仅存，势已孤绝，如秦人视越人之肥瘠，一不动念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163150_comment'></div>但恐泾原、鄜延即有警急，亦必不能如首尾之相为救也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163150_comment'></div>陛下曲全事体，乞还竦旧官，与之一郡，遂其自全之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163150_comment'></div>且精择逐路守将，使人自为功，家自为固，量其边势，配之兵力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163150_comment'></div>仍于永兴益置重兵，以为诸路根本，以为人心镇重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163150_comment'></div>春秋择遣重臣出巡边，春则量御备之力，迁其军马，入就仓牧，命守将修治城堑，完利器用，以待防秋之政令焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163150_comment'></div>秋则阅其训练之法，蒐补之术，审官吏劳能，以明升降之典，按赋舆盈虚，以通货食之计，以严其战守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163150_comment'></div>但边城能坚其守，已足弊贼，若将率各尽其用，自当有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163150_comment'></div>伏愿天衷垂纳裁择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1163150_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年9月</a>　九月，在京知谏院，上疏论列刘从德妻出入内庭事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年10月</a>　十月，在京知谏院，劾罢夏竦陕西兵柄。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年10月</a>　十月，在京知谏院，上疏论除渭州路招讨使事。作品：论除渭州路招讨使事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_1163151' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163151' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163151?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论除渭州路招讨使事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163151")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163151_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163151'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163151'>臣伏见制除某官代王沿充渭州路招讨安抚等使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163151_comment'></div>朝廷比分四路以藩屏西边，其间道路坦夷，众得大入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163151_comment'></div>且车骑之利惟泾原，故贼连年亲来，犯此一路，覆军杀将，每来益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163151_comment'></div>去年好水之役，任福等犹力战而败，骁将精卒器械殚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163151_comment'></div>朝夕竭力，完补二年，仅得成军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163151_comment'></div>此来定川贼无亡矢遗镞之费，一举而悉卷以去，如蹈无人之境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163151_comment'></div>贼骤胜而不骄，令明而众整，凡四大举，动无遗策，气燄益炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163151_comment'></div>今既胜归，休养士马，若来年春首倾国复来，我以残破败亡之馀，稍更拓落不定，势且堂堂长驱，有饮马渭河之志，则关中摇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163151_comment'></div>而北有强虏睢盱睥睨，外为和约济其贪婪，实用此贼困我，意在坐收其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163151_comment'></div>以是虑之，则今关中轻重之势，天下安危之形在泾原矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163151_comment'></div>某虽涖官临事粗有风力，然未更重任，恐不易当此剧贼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163151_comment'></div>又新蒙奖擢，中外未之信服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163151_comment'></div>至于三路旧宣力人，见其骤为之伍，顾亦心有慊然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163151_comment'></div>且今来泾原人畜殆尽，兵马亡几，一路萧然，无藩篱之限，此时施为经置，动系机宜，乃老将之所难，非全才而孰与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163151_comment'></div>成败所寄，理无试可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163151_comment'></div>切惟朝论更加审察，必不得已，或于三路中替换一人，且当此路，所贵谙练边政，通知虏事，人心物望抑有属焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163151_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年10月</a>　十月，在京知谏院，上疏请因冬郊赦书招怀西夏。作品：请因郊禋肆赦招还西贼劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163149' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163149?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请因郊禋肆赦招怀西贼劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163149")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163149'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163149'>伏以前景祐五年有事于圜丘，西戎贡职不至，始发衅端，次年春遂构兵犯边，杀掠吏民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163149_comment'></div>边将备御无策，贼数入寇，辄以胜归，济其凶谋，气燄益盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163149_comment'></div>今自陕西四路、河东麟府，远近屯戍，输挽供给，天下为之劳弊，而解严息甲，未可以日月期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163149_comment'></div>臣尝问自边来者，询贼中事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163149_comment'></div>盖今羌戎乃汉唐郡县，非以逐水草射猎为生，皆待耕穫而食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163149_comment'></div>贼每点集资粮器用，人自为备，须岁年为计，乃能一大举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163149_comment'></div>虽破城寨，不能有我寸土也，而又绝其俸赐，禁其关市，贼中尺布直钱三数百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163149_comment'></div>边防守备缮完益固，贼情见势屈，自当改图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163149_comment'></div>然犹骑虎不可复下，虽有悔心，亦何由自通诚款？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163149_comment'></div>朝廷虽欲招来，若非时无名，事亦难举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163149_comment'></div>倘因今来郊礼覃庆之时，特开旷荡之恩，示以绥怀之意，或特降一诏，或著之赦书，其辞意大略则曰：夫王者以天下为度，含生之类，罔不亭育，况朔方、灵武、河西五郡，声教所暨，莫非王民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163149_comment'></div>顷自德明已来，克保外臣之节，朝廷眷待，恩礼至隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163149_comment'></div>去年元昊遣使人来，称为本藩推戴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163149_comment'></div>缘其附顺三十馀年，忽此奏陈，不无疑骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163149_comment'></div>见情未审，遂至兴兵，使边人不宁，师徒暴露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163149_comment'></div>今亲郊上帝，盛礼告成，庆赐大行，囚系尽释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163149_comment'></div>乃眷西顾，恻然轸念，亏于抚育，吾甚伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163149_comment'></div>今后夏州或有使人至者，候人不得遏绝，或有愿通于朝廷之意，即令边臣受而上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163149_comment'></div>且泛告边臣以谨守封略，罔或生事，令榜而揭诸塞上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163149_comment'></div>或边臣之有威望者，遣单使以朝旨往为开谕，足彰陛下德义之厚，无损朝廷威重之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163149_comment'></div>且贼妄自尊大于巢窟中久矣，王者固宜以鸟兽畜之，岂足与之辨名器等威之分哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163149_comment'></div>贼若有悔祸之心，称藩纳贡，陛下优为封爵名号以服扰之，出府库之馀以岁时豢饵之，使天下知陛下深诚远虑，为生灵计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163149_comment'></div>至于天地鬼神，亦当助仁而佑顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163149_comment'></div>仁者无敌于天下，况一贼欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163149_comment'></div>若贼悍然自恃，凶愎不移，亦足以骄怠彼心，激怒我众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163149_comment'></div>边臣必曰：天子之恩意如此，贼无革心，我不可以不奋身而为国致讨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163149_comment'></div>战士必曰：天子不以贼之不义而必穷诛，是哀吾属之久戍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163149_comment'></div>今贼无革心，吾属不可以不效命而斗战矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163149_comment'></div>自边之民至于天下之民必曰：天子所以赦贼，盖念赋役之烦扰，吾人之困劳，今贼无革心，吾人不得不竭力以奉边矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163149_comment'></div>贼党必曰：天子幸加恩而不我诛也，而其主茍不思焉，是驱我于锋刃之下，以济其欲而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163149_comment'></div>夫兵犹火也，不戢将自焚，使我怒彼怨，贼有自焚之势，则成败有所分矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163149_comment'></div>今议者闻臣之说，必难臣曰：贼自入寇，无不克，何困之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163149_comment'></div>今虽招怀之，徒示国之弱，贼肯革心乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163149_comment'></div>臣请对曰：昔迁贼之为边患也，号为骁悍有谋略者，陷朔方、灵武，国家丧地且千里，而其众亦大弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163149_comment'></div>尔时继迁虽不为六谷所杀，势亦不支矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163149_comment'></div>故其死时戒德明曰：「尔当倾心归顺朝廷，如一两表未蒙开纳，但连上封章，以祈见听」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163149_comment'></div>故德明款附，毕世不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163149_comment'></div>今贼非迁比也，不幸自其初叛，而我守边匪人，是故贼累得志，而其众嗜为寇之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163149_comment'></div>向使我无大败，彼无大获，而以贼之虐用其下，寻应疲溃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163149_comment'></div>今朝廷处画边事，守遏益固，将卒用命，财用不乏，虽未能大残其众，姑使来无所掠获，即贼自穷蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163149_comment'></div>今先开其归路，以为后图，纵贼未怀，与国何损？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163149_comment'></div>必又难臣曰：贼虽致款，戎心可保乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163149_comment'></div>即有其实，边备得以彻之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163149_comment'></div>臣请对曰：昔景德初，契丹大入河朔，先帝亲驾，北狩于澶渊，虏主始遣使议通和好，俄又其统军达兰中伏弩以死，和议遂定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163149_comment'></div>于时边陲可保戎心，彻警备，而谓继好至今之坚乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163149_comment'></div>在朝廷所以抚纳控驭而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163149_comment'></div>今事边之费，岁且千万，用师以来，系累杀戮几十万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163149_comment'></div>故自古以来论边事者，莫不以和戎为利，征戍为害，盖深念此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163149_comment'></div>伏愿陛下延召二府大臣，试详此议，傥蒙采听，则生民之福，实所系赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163149_comment'></div>臣不胜区区之恳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1163149_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年10月</a>　十月，在京知谏院，为丁立撰墓志铭。作品：泉州清溪县令丁府君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1163615' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163615' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163615?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泉州清溪县令丁府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　康定二年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163615")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163615_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163615'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163615'>康定二年辛巳阳月，丁氏启新阡于睢阳宋城县之某乡，司农少卿府君占丙穴，清溪府君占辛穴，司农之穆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163615_comment'></div>凡世系世德，则翰林学士王公伯庸为司农志铭具矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163615_comment'></div>府君讳立，字某，司农之长子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163615_comment'></div>以荫补太庙斋郎，历邵武军建宁尉，单之鱼台、陕之胡城、宋之宁陵三邑簿，复调通州静海尉，迁泉州清溪令，卒官，享年六十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163615_comment'></div>君在鱼台，邑民甚苦前令佐贪苛，悦君之廉静，誉甚美，至达旁大府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163615_comment'></div>故相文节公守南都，闻之形言嘉叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163615_comment'></div>在宁陵，疏导沟洫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163615_comment'></div>得近官在静海，属岁饥，振廪救荒得免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163615_comment'></div>选在清溪，为政宽简，视人恐伤，闽俗虽犷猾，感君诚恕，率教不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163615_comment'></div>君天性和易，处家莅官，未始有忿言愠色，不惟不发形于外，盖亦未尝萌于心术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163615_comment'></div>恬于声利，不知人间有巧邪进取事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163615_comment'></div>游宦不择地，不惊不诡，浑然不为澄挠变，无贤不肖，虽至狂恶人，一见君，退必曰长者也，更无嫌忤意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163615_comment'></div>夫天道无亲，常与善人，君可谓善人矣，胡不黄耇，胡为禄仕之微？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163615_comment'></div>天之报宠，不在其身，将在其后乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163615_comment'></div>前夫人张氏，太子洗马某之女，有贤行，生二男：曰昉，南京留守推官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163615_comment'></div>曰晔，以济州录事参军搉酤畿邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163615_comment'></div>一女，适南京国子监直讲王鼎臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163615_comment'></div>张夫人先君而殁，兹实祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163615_comment'></div>今夫人王氏，某官某之女，顺于为妇，慈于为母，姻党称焉，生三男；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163615_comment'></div>曰某，举进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163615_comment'></div>曰某、某，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163615_comment'></div>昉、晔通敏方雅，皆有才志，君之积善将在其后，不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163615_comment'></div>某乡里晚辈，君不以年德间之，又与君之二子游，既来请铭，义不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163615_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1163615'>嘻夫君，涵天醇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163615_comment'></div>有时顺，无亨屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163615_comment'></div>惟德庆，遗后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163615_comment'></div>后人孝，神永宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163615_comment'></div>从先子，归泉扃，君不朽，在此铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1163615_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年11月</a>　十一月，在京知谏院，上《郊禋赦书事目》作品：郊禋赦书事目。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二〇。系年据《续资治通鉴长编》卷一三四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　本年，在京知谏院，荐韦不伐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　本年，在京知谏院，上疏论京师卫兵事。作品：论京师卫兵事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_1163158' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163158' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163158?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论京师卫兵事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163158")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163158_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163158'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163158'>京师本古之陈留郡，天下四通八达之地，自唐室已前，尝为重藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163158_comment'></div>五代朱温始封梁王，后因其宫府广而为都，五姓相承，共十一帝四十九年，乱亡之速，自古无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163158_comment'></div>抑由都城四向无险阻之形、藩篱之固，逼近戎狄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163158_comment'></div>方镇握强兵于外，乘禁卫之虚弱，末本倒置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163158_comment'></div>国朝太祖皇帝深虑安危之计，始削诸节度之权，屯兵于内，连营畿甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163158_comment'></div>又修完西京宫内，盖有建都之意，然利于汴渠漕挽之便，因循重迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163158_comment'></div>先帝通好北戎，即叙西戎，尔时可以减戍消兵，致生民于富厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163158_comment'></div>太平三十年，使军士坐费仓库，以困天下，非不深思远谋也，知祖宗本意，依重兵而为国势，不可去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163158_comment'></div>近昊贼犯边，渐发禁兵西屯四路，在京军旅所留无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163158_comment'></div>今又北虏事衅已萌，两敌合从，人心摇动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163158_comment'></div>外有武帅分总重兵，而宿卫之师日益单寡，尾大不掉，根虚必摇，势之当然，不可忽也，愿留圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163158_comment'></div>为社稷计，京都宜常宿重兵，以封殖根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163158_comment'></div>且乞勘会见在指挥人数，若果缺少，请从内出金帛召募材力，训齐教练，必须精锐，以充禁卫，无更外屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163158_comment'></div>夫猛虎所以百兽伏者，以其爪牙利也，若虎而去其爪牙，则犬豕鹿麋皆可以相狎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163158_comment'></div>兵卫者，国之爪牙也，足兵足食，乃可以威服四方，弹压奸乱矣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163158_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1163158'>庆历元年：原无，据《宋名臣奏议》、《历代名臣奏议》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163158_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163158'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1163158_0'>⑴ 《乐全集》卷二一。又见《宋名臣奏议》卷一二二，《源流至论》续集卷一，《历代名臣奏议》卷二二五。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163158_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年1月</a>　正月，在京知谏院，受命与欧阳修考试知举官亲戚举人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年2月</a>　二月，在京知谏院，上疏论王整改官事。作品：论王整改官奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1163227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163227?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论王整改官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163227")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163227_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163227'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163227'>新除河北同提典刑狱、崇仪副使王整，有旨以其昨奉使北朝曾借洛苑使，今授河北提刑，虑北使过境，讶其官名不同，特与改此使额者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163227_comment'></div>伏以崇仪、洛苑颇为超越，北使之来，提典刑狱不预宾主之事，整虽在职，使人岂知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163227_comment'></div>即恐以假官为嫌，自应改授别路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163227_comment'></div>每岁所遣使介，例皆假官以行，回而效整之为，遂成真拜之例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163227_comment'></div>今政之大弊，为多倖人，塞其蹊隧，犹不可遏，若又启之，何以为政？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163227_comment'></div>如整诚有是请，原情深涉欺诬，必朝廷惩沮纤邪，修明法度，不惟宜停恩旨，顾当下从吏议，别行谴斥，以戒为臣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163227_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　春，在京除修起居注，仍领谏职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年4月</a>　四月，在京知谏院，上疏请校会邦计。作品：请校会邦计事劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二三。系年据《续资治通鉴长编》卷一三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163185' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163185' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163185?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请校会邦计事劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163185")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163185_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163185'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163185'>伏见西事以来应副边备，天下被其劳，凡百赋率，至增数倍，当时朝旨盖为用兵之际权宜应急，岂敢承以为常？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163185_comment'></div>今边防虽已渐宁，而缘边戍守未能彻备，四方添置兵马数亦甚多，向之所增赋歛，必难复旧，何以慰天下百姓之望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163185_comment'></div>朝廷所以绥怀二虏者，正谓宽财用，纾民力，以厚为之备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163185_comment'></div>今乘边事之间，岂可优游虚度岁月，不切讲求经久之计？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163185_comment'></div>若遂恬然惮于有为，臣恐民力日困，财用日匮，难以善于后矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163185_comment'></div>今内自三司，外至发运、转运使，凡掌财利之官，簿书期会犹不暇给，岂暇为国家生民远虑者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163185_comment'></div>臣欲乞于两省已上官选差才敏之士三两员，就三司与使、副据国用岁计之数，量入以为出，平货物之轻重，通天下之有无，校其利害之源，以革因循之弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163185_comment'></div>旋具事节，先到中书、枢密院开陈，商量必久远可行者，奏上取裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163185_comment'></div>若细碎之事，无大损益，徒成烦扰，不须施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163185_comment'></div>所冀助财用，纾民力，当今之切务也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1163185_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年4月</a>　四月，在京知谏院，受命与贾昌朝、田况、张永和、姚仲孙同议裁减浮费。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年4月</a>　四月，在京知谏院，再上疏请校会邦计。作品：再奏请校会邦计劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二三。系年据《续资治通鉴长编》卷一三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163186?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再奏请校会邦计事劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163186")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163186'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163186'>方今天下切务，无先货食，货食之原，在于三司，而计臣事务烦综，簿书期会之不暇给，岂暇及于国家根本之虑哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163186_comment'></div>故于去年曾上言，乞于两省已上官选差三两员就三司，与使、副据岁计之所入，约中外之所费，移用之法则权其轻重，率敛之物则通其有无，参究利害之原，刬革因循之弊，所冀宽财用，纾民力，助三司均节之体者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163186_comment'></div>自后未蒙朝廷施行，不测所以难之之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163186_comment'></div>今不乘边事之间，急讲久远之策，臣恐民力日困，财用日匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163186_comment'></div>恐朝廷重于生事，欲乞且令三司将天圣中一年天下赋入之数，及中外支费之籍，与昨一年比并条上，则国家之大计可校而知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163186_comment'></div>如是而可以经久则善，如其不可，则岂得恬然不深虑哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163186_comment'></div>前所上劄子，伏乞更赐详择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163186_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年4月</a>　四月，在京知谏院，上疏论择西北将帅事。作品：论西北将率事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1163171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论西北将率事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163171")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163171'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163171'>昨戎使萧英等回，朝廷处置北鄙，虽增兵饬垒，事为之备，然所遣将率未尽推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163171_comment'></div>臣闻之军志，善待敌者，无恃其不来也，当为不可胜，恃我有以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163171_comment'></div>故城虽坚，兵虽众，财用诚给，茍将率非其人，无足恃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163171_comment'></div>故将者人之司命，国家安危之主，惟陛下念兹在兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163171_comment'></div>即戎骑敢越封略，使杨崇勋在镇定，夏守赟在瀛州，刘涣在沧州，张耆在河阳，陛下得高枕乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163171_comment'></div>虽愚夫童子，亦知其必败事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163171_comment'></div>盖朝廷非不知崇勋等之不足使也，迫于用人之常体，慊然而遣之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163171_comment'></div>必欲上宽倚注之忧，下为众论所信，自非已试之效者，不足赖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163171_comment'></div>势不得已，莫若且取陕西偏裨之知名者，如狄青、范全辈，每路辄徙一两人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163171_comment'></div>况自西鄙用兵已来，三年于兹，立功将士如青等，未尝得一到京辇，仰望天颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163171_comment'></div>若以此为名，召之赴阙，量其材器，稍迁用之，追崇勋等使奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163171_comment'></div>议者必谓西、北事均，若青等被夺，必恐西帅有辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163171_comment'></div>且陕西四路各据千里之地，连城数十，官吏将佐以千计，胜兵众矣，岂不能选练偏裨以自为用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163171_comment'></div>一旦天子登一小校于朝而辞焉，爱君体国者义不如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163171_comment'></div>及兹盛夏，边未有虞，可速致之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163171_comment'></div>比富弼使归，幸而盟好未渝，即各还之本路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163171_comment'></div>若犬羊南向，且使分捍北方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163171_comment'></div>事机所悬，乞赐裁察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1163171_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年5月</a>　五月，在京知谏院，上疏请节省财用。作品：请节省财用事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1163183' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163183' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163183?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请节省财用事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163183")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163183_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163183'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163183'>伏以天下承平为岁深远，而国用不赡，民力益困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163183_comment'></div>今聚师境上，调费寖广，倚于经入则财不给，加以横赋则人不堪，救兹交急，特在陛下身先于率下，惟事事乃其撙约而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163183_comment'></div>臣窃惟陛下躬勤节用，克自抑畏，凡诸服御，殊为菲薄，而兹中外之论，皆言用度之过，臣窃疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163183_comment'></div>盖宫闱嬖昵，左右近习，假威恣横，敢为欺诬，仰恃仁慈，缘为奸弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163183_comment'></div>且禁中呼索辄称圣旨，有司应奉皆为上供，故外人不知其详，而讥议累乎圣德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163183_comment'></div>国家帑藏之困，乃群下侵牟之蠹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163183_comment'></div>伏愿陛下上念宗社之计，下以生民为心，彼妇人、宦者，何烦过为姑息！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163183_comment'></div>超然远虑，断自天心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163183_comment'></div>试取先帝之世及陛下临御以来天圣之初宫司帐籍如内东门之类，比较近年支费金帛，则知增损丰俭之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163183_comment'></div>以一言裁减之恩，为万方富庶之本，兆民所赖，为幸实深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163183_comment'></div>先朝以前，事恐难继，若天圣初体例，夫岂远哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163183_comment'></div>因降诏书，谕天下以陛下忧边之心，爱民之故，则将卒闻之，孰不奋励以授命？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163183_comment'></div>士民闻之，孰不鼓舞以称仁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163183_comment'></div>至于外诸司库务，凡百横费，乞特置司局，选用公平通敏谙晓时务之士三两员条理之，而以大臣一人监领其事，其不便者，惟是左右主当之臣尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163183_comment'></div>诚陛下断之不疑，无容阻挠，则上可以资德美，下可以施恩惠，内可以集国计，外可以成武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163183_comment'></div>效速而利多，事近而德远，此当世之切务也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163183_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年5月</a>　五月，在京知谏院，上疏论节省财用事。作品：论减省财用事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1163184' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163184' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163184?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论减省财用事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163184")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163184_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163184'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163184'>臣近受敕，同贾昌朝等定夺减省财费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163184_comment'></div>窃闻渊旨先自宫禁裁省一切用度，至于圣躬奉给缗钱，亦令罢供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163184_comment'></div>此盖陛下身先勤俭，为生灵计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163184_comment'></div>夫减省所为者，自下而议上，则于体不顺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163184_comment'></div>由上以率下，则于名为正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163184_comment'></div>臣愿以禁中所行之事，择其大者三数节，宣示外廷，因发明诏，使天下共知圣意忧边爱人之深，则中外臣庶得不体国家之急，上承美德者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163184_comment'></div>特在陛下断之清衷，不屑细言，则成效可冀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163184_comment'></div>其有徇己之利，与则喜，夺则怒，此女子与小人之情，怨谤所由生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163184_comment'></div>臣辈敢不竭精尽虑，上副天心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1163184_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年7月</a>　七月，在京知谏院，上疏请并枢密院于中书。作品：论请通中书枢密院事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163122?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论请通中书枢密院事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年七月壬寅）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163122")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163122_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163122'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163122'>臣窃以朝廷政令之所出，万事之本原，一统于中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163122_comment'></div>若枢密院，则古无有也，起于后唐权宜之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163122_comment'></div>因循相承，兵柄寖重，乃与中书对秉衡轴，至于分军民为二体，别文武为两途，宣敕并行，议论难一，事无任责，更相顾望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163122_comment'></div>自古为理，患在多门，况今二府之中，岂尽材猷之士？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163122_comment'></div>朝纲内弛，边事日生，西戎北狄，交有凭陵中夏之志，财用殚窘，百职旷废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163122_comment'></div>此时庙堂之上，岂容非材？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163122_comment'></div>夫欲朝廷尊、边事宁，其要在乎拣别大臣才不才而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163122_comment'></div>陛下若去不才之人，又复谁当进用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163122_comment'></div>若使宴安朝列、容身养望者优游备位，则劳臣益解体，武士益离心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163122_comment'></div>兹事体大，实在详察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163122_comment'></div>谓宜讲求利害，稽复古制，省枢密院，归于中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163122_comment'></div>若又重于改为，则莫若通枢密院之职事于中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163122_comment'></div>见任枢密院使、副，才者留之，不才者去之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163122_comment'></div>其诸房吏史且皆如旧，措置施舍，徐更图议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163122_comment'></div>是足以一政事之本，重赏罚之权，汰冗滥之员，塞侥倖之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163122_comment'></div>改而张之不伤体，裁而成之不动众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163122_comment'></div>陛下幸与一二宗臣旧老深图此议，有益于国，愿断自圣心行之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1163122_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163122'><span class='label'>按：</span>年月日据《续资治通鉴长编》、《宋名臣奏议》补。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1163122_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年8月</a>　八月，在京知谏院，受命为契丹国主生辰使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年8月</a>　八月，在京知谏院，上言武举中选人请除京东捉贼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年9月</a>　九月，在京知谏院，上疏请省西北骑兵。作品：请省缘边兵事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1163176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163176?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请省缘边骑兵事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163176")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163176'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163176'>臣近因减省，见边戍供输之劳，天下物力之困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163176_comment'></div>今虽峻行裁节，精为鸠聚，若会所得，冀充诸费，是犹益之以畎浍，泄之以尾闾，量入为出，非所以持久者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163176_comment'></div>伏请选择近臣，令奉明诏，分使诸道，就诸边臣，与之深议所以丰财啬用、守备经远之计，内外相应，本末同体，庶几乎功利之可举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163176_comment'></div>即如缘边骑兵，计蓄一骑，可以赡卒五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163176_comment'></div>西戎出善马，地形险隘，我骑诚不得与较走集也，多留马军，既不足用，徒索刍粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163176_comment'></div>今方北备胡虏，乃是用骑之地，乞以陕西新团土兵多换马军东归，一以省关中之挽输，一以备河北之战守。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163176_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年闰9月</a>　闰九月，在京知谏院，上疏论四路将帅追兵不赴事。作品：论四路将率追兵不赴事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_1163155' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163155' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163155?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论四路将率追兵不赴事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年闰九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年闰9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163155")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163155_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163155'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163155'>臣伏见朝廷近以北虏有渝盟之渐，缘边之急奏继来，车驾声言亲征，有司各为备拟，抽换陕西兵马待河北事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163155_comment'></div>如闻诸路帅臣或有不时发遣，至烦敕使从而告谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163155_comment'></div>向若戎羯遂至冲突，銮舆果或顺动，仓卒之际，兵卫未集而又召发莫赴，则见大事去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163155_comment'></div>历观古今之变，为国理乱之形，四夷交侵，无代不有，惟是人主威命之不行，朝廷政令之不举，乱危之兆必从此始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163155_comment'></div>厥今事势，夫如何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163155_comment'></div>猛不济宽，威不克爱，朝廷命令，边臣易于违戾，边臣奏复，朝廷难于执持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163155_comment'></div>原此恣慢之端，悉由姑息之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163155_comment'></div>即如昨者除四帅观察使，故事：尚书丞郎之带职者，得换廉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163155_comment'></div>钱若水罢枢密副使，徐乃授之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163155_comment'></div>马知节罢枢密副使，止除防御使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163155_comment'></div>陛下优矜边寄，特示恩荣，今四人者职皆直学士，官郎、员外，而乃正其名使之总戎，厚其禄使之抚下，本朝之意，夫岂为薄？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163155_comment'></div>诰命已颁，章奏沓至，妄生意见，覆为疵嫌，就或强拜，乃怀大慊，甚焉者至欲系狱请罪，当之者犹以班叙为辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163155_comment'></div>朝廷一切含容，君命益成轻削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163155_comment'></div>臣诚愚褊，窃独愤然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163155_comment'></div>傥陛下之威命行，朝廷之政令举，罚戮在后，爵赏在前，必信如《春秋》，不测如雷霆，使中外僚寀震慑奔走，则天下之智力不胜其用矣，何故屈大公之法，伸群下之私，如是之惴惴为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163155_comment'></div>昔有志于尊主庇民者，遭世多难，感慨投袂，徒以大义激乌合之心，犹足以外攘夷狄，内宁社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163155_comment'></div>若据土宇，握士众，闻国有急，观望晏然，乃心王家，夫岂如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163155_comment'></div>儒臣犹尔，使武人暴夫顾望仿效，则履霜坚冰，渐不可长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163155_comment'></div>此臣所以窃怀愤惋，实为宗庙深虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163155_comment'></div>若中使回奏，其诸路有不奉诏，伏望圣断，特遣朝臣之通识理体者按问其状，严行责削，以谨下之衔勒，以正国之纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163155_comment'></div>思患预防，古之善戒，惟陛下亮察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1163155_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　冬，在京知谏院，作《喜雪》诗。作品：喜雪。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_495350' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495350' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495350?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜雪<span class='inlineComment2'>（原注：庆历二年，仁宗命作。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495350")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495350_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495350'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495350'>愆阳干岁事，斋殿轸予忧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495350'>默为斯民祷，心从六事求。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495350'>同云俄蔽景，盈尺忽呈休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495350'>淅沥千琼树，峥嵘万玉楼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495350'>尘氛开紫宙，气象露皇州。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495350'>雕鹗精神劲，松筠操禀优。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495350'>边庭伤久戍，农亩庆来麰。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495350'>咨尔臣邻地，常期九叙脩。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495350_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495350'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_495350_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cc73b56bc51b4786a10c7d9915da4b2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cc73b56bc51b4786a10c7d9915da4b2b");'><span id='cc73b56bc51b4786a10c7d9915da4b2b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1047')">1043-1047年</a>，37-41岁</div><div id='cc73b56bc51b4786a10c7d9915da4b2b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年2月</a>　二月，奉使契丹还。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年3月</a>　三月，召试中书，除右正言、知制诰，赐三品服章，有谢表。作品：谢除知制诰表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除知制诰表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163283")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163283'>伏奉制命，蒙恩授臣右正言、知制诰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163283_comment'></div>槐庭给札，甫上于奏篇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163283_comment'></div>星掖代言，遽陪于景从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163283_comment'></div>躐进论思之秩，预闻毖密之谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163283_comment'></div>俯偻拜嘉，兢凌失次<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163283_comment'></div>恭以邦家所重，典诰为先，故广延于翘英，俾对司于明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163283_comment'></div>尚书作诏，任处机衡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163283_comment'></div>内史出方，赞为爵禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163283_comment'></div>盖历朝之极任，为外廷之华阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163283_comment'></div>向非学本名家，代推杰笔，则何以发挥鸿业，徊翔近班，体汉家深厚之辞，演周公烦悉之诰？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163283_comment'></div>吁谟定命，鼓舞乎万方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163283_comment'></div>除书德音，竦动乎群听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163283_comment'></div>备咨访乎政事，专润色于王猷，必资东里之才，取重西台之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163283_comment'></div>伏念臣斗筲微器，樗栎散材，独奋草茅之愚，再举方闻之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163283_comment'></div>小冠宰邑，式敷慈惠之经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163283_comment'></div>别乘赞藩，无补中和之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163283_comment'></div>无何被旨，即追还台，升处乐卿之丞，留充谏省之缺。<div class='inline'
