id='poem_sentence_125_1163561_comment'></div>是日，除公户部侍郎、知郓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1163561_comment'></div>真驾升遐，贬公检校尚书、水部员外郎、衡州团练副使，志且杀公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1163561_comment'></div>或说谓：「衡州之谪，若士议何」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1163561_comment'></div>谓曰：「是庸何伤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1163561_comment'></div>他日好事生传衡州事，不过云『天下惜之』而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1163561_comment'></div>时乾兴元年三月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1163561_comment'></div>七月，谓败；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1163561_comment'></div>十二月，复秘书监、知舒州，徙建康，就改刑部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1163561_comment'></div>徙兖海，改兵部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1163561_comment'></div>徙东秦，又徙河南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1163561_comment'></div>诏朝京师，公既对留，五日而辞，绝口不及旧事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1163561_comment'></div>至洛师，改尚书右丞，徙三城，就迁工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1163561_comment'></div>耕籍之岁，献后上仙，今上驰驲还公，授资政殿学士，图旧共政，遂复相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1163561_comment'></div>章圣朝，公雅见亲重，君臣之际无间然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1163561_comment'></div>毅然庙堂，以身许国，自谓「临大故，贲育弗能夺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1163561_comment'></div>不结党友，取游说之助，见加彊诐，播越在外，故莫为之地者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1163561_comment'></div>精诚忠义，贯于神明，惟帝念兹，复我弼直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1163561_comment'></div>然天资刚劲，秉心醇一，虽历危难艰阻，仅全折而不挠，正色益厉，当轴处中，用是亦弗能久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1163561_comment'></div>景祐二年，以刑部尚书、资政殿大学士兼翰林侍读学士解机柄，留侍经筵，竟罥僿文，除太常卿、知高密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1163561_comment'></div>寻复秋官，徙彭门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1163561_comment'></div>又改地官，徙兖海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1163561_comment'></div>党羌不恭，大入内地，公上疏：「愿以属老臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1163561_comment'></div>上曰：「是岂宜以烦耆德乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1163561_comment'></div>诏慰答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1163561_comment'></div>西师在野，辽戎睢盱，朝议藉公威重，绥定河朔，因授彰信军节旄，判天雄军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1163561_comment'></div>吏民卒旅至于四夷，皆知公两朝二十年旧相，故不严而治，疆埸乂宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1163561_comment'></div>复徙青社，诏赴本镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1163561_comment'></div>过乡展墓，因慨然曰：「吾遭时至将相，幸全节义，不忝先人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1163561_comment'></div>盍归来乎，佚吾馀日也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1163561_comment'></div>及曹南，遂引年还君事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1163561_comment'></div>疏三上，天子悯以职务留，以除太子太傅致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1163561_comment'></div>归老濮上，放怀物外，逍遥六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1163561_comment'></div>子东之以侍御史知杂奉安舆至都，使珰饷茗饵，致上意存劳，谓公：「不可彊自力一见我欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1163561_comment'></div>公谢衰疾，竟弗入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1163561_comment'></div>谓故吏曰：「吾笃老，槁骸灰心，圣君念雅素，傥加恩，是吾为子孙见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1163561_comment'></div>张禹数视其儿，犹市攫尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1163561_comment'></div>启手足之日，无他恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1163561_comment'></div>时凝凛，偃毡庐中，顾左右曰：「安得大幄冒天下之寒者乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1163561_comment'></div>神爽恬泊，颓然委化，享年七十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1163561_comment'></div>配时氏，卒公约时，子东之请诸朝，追封永嘉郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1163561_comment'></div>继室荣国夫人皇甫氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1163561_comment'></div>皆有德礼，式宪宗姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1163561_comment'></div>三子：曰东之，尚书工部郎中、天章阁待制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1163561_comment'></div>徽之，度支员外郎、京西转运使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1163561_comment'></div>皆以才进，著名迹，称贤士大夫，不藉世家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1163561_comment'></div>幼辅之，太常寺太祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1163561_comment'></div>六女：长归国子博士向绛，次祠部员外、集贤校理张充，次太常博士王端，次未有行而亡，次归大理评事陈袭古，次在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1163561_comment'></div>诸孙、曾孙十一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1163561_comment'></div>德厚流光，宜乎世济其美者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1163561_comment'></div>公孝于亲，友于昆季，笃于朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1163561_comment'></div>不迁怒，不逆诈，计数回巧，不接心术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1163561_comment'></div>不茍进，不洁退，功美不居，患难不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1163561_comment'></div>誉善不为谄，嫉恶不为忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1163561_comment'></div>率由天至，非有勉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1163561_comment'></div>蕴之为行谊，发之为事业，在公之道，盖土苴尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1163561_comment'></div>夫夸者死权，矜者徇名，逞祸机而导争端，闻公之风，薄斯知敦，贪斯知约矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1163561_comment'></div>臣承学浅昧，然粗闻《春秋》义例矣，大君有命，敢诬信书？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1163561_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_183_1163561'>侍中刚塞，蕴涵纯德，发为正色，隐然柱石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1163561_comment'></div>章圣惠哲，察公忠烈，可临大节，托之喉舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1163561_comment'></div>遂付宰柄，爰属之政，实受端命，宾傅储圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1163561_comment'></div>孽臣专朝，僻讹奸骄，钩连日嚣，我心郁焦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1163561_comment'></div>感愤中激，志除邪偪，乃诚靖国，以宁社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1163561_comment'></div>缀衣出庭，遘闵南征，不远湘衡，顾怀周京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1163561_comment'></div>大人继照，图旧广孝，显扬辅导，俄还廊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1163561_comment'></div>乃平泰阶，谟明弼谐，若作梓材，尔惟盐梅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1163561_comment'></div>师戍羌落，帝念辽漠，公在河朔，敌崩厥角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1163561_comment'></div>宣力中外，文武尽瘁，若时进退，道德益大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1163561_comment'></div>攻夺为利，太息为义，处心云异，于道同敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1163561_comment'></div>公冲而用，不激不耸，率诚以动，不勉伊中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1163561_comment'></div>岩廊穆清，轸念老成，俾扬颂声，式昭典刑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_195_1163561_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年6月</a>　六月，在京任翰林学士，与叶清臣等上陕西钱议。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年6月</a>　六月，在京任翰林学士，为韦襄作墓志铭。作品：朝散大夫秘书丞上骑都尉杜陵韦府君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1163613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫秘书丞上骑都尉杜陵韦府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　庆历八年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163613")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163613'>韦氏世序远矣，汉丞相扶阳侯自邹徙杜陵，名德历朝，著为世家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163613_comment'></div>扶阳十六代至周逍遥公夐，始别其族为十三房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163613_comment'></div>观唐吏部肇宗会之约，则知韦氏之礼义与他族异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163613_comment'></div>第八房平齐公瑱之云孙万年县令象生台州刺史方宪，台州生福建观察判官钧，钧生襄州录事参军允之，府君之王考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163613_comment'></div>唐昭宗末，解襄阳掾，将集吏部，会梁氏革运，感朝代之变，不复北归，潜遁汉南谷城县青石川之峎下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163613_comment'></div>后唐庄宗入汴，诏访前朝衣冠不事朱氏者，命方镇优礼，传诣公车，郡劝君驾，叹曰：「吾耻梁而逸，奚为乎沙陀之廷」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163613_comment'></div>卧不起，时孔勍帅襄阳，本儒者，重君高节，善为之辞，而以疾闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163613_comment'></div>庄宗嘉之，不夺其志，录其子仁济试秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163613_comment'></div>没，因葬汉滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163613_comment'></div>校书以父隐居，躬耕钧以养，终丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163613_comment'></div>久之，卫王符彦卿总兵在上党，领太原行府，始应其召，终于陈州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163613_comment'></div>娶司空氏，实生府君于峎下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163613_comment'></div>府君讳襄，字逾中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163613_comment'></div>幼刻励好学，早有名誉，雅为冬官卿朱洞所知，从洞光州、庐州幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163613_comment'></div>国初，州郡辟署宾佐，犹袭唐五代旧事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163613_comment'></div>太皇纂极，诏悉罢之，一命黄绶以上皆遣王官，而益广科第之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163613_comment'></div>府君更就宾兴于谯，太平兴国八年登进士第，释褐临淮之盱眙尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163613_comment'></div>迁廷尉平，知虔州赣县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163613_comment'></div>邑多讼事，号难理，府君待以诚恕，狱市以清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163613_comment'></div>吏民悦之，因上官以请诸朝，遂留六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163613_comment'></div>就改光禄寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163613_comment'></div>南方卑溽，风淫于末，因以搆疠，宦意寖薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163613_comment'></div>代还，求榷酤聊城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163613_comment'></div>朝中知君者惜其才，或荐之上，因召赴都，授著作佐郎，复求监征宜春，盖禄仕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163613_comment'></div>还自宜春，迁秘书丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163613_comment'></div>至道三年正月二十六日，卒于京师，春秋六十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163613_comment'></div>君天性和易，识致冲远，从之游者皆一时高流名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163613_comment'></div>善与人交，淮阳孙茂兰、万适，南顿乔维岳，江南李虚己，睢阳戚同文、宗度，泰山张茂直，咸以趣尚相得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163613_comment'></div>同文子纶，西蜀李建中，雒阳崔遵度，钜野王禹偁，合淝姚铉，并以同年生定交，淡乎相欢，久而弥笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163613_comment'></div>每官下，士友自远方至，辄如归，为食饮具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163613_comment'></div>俸入随尽，口不言利，未尝问家有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163613_comment'></div>手不度货币，对客清谈，不及世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163613_comment'></div>在官若私，未尝斯须见忧愠之色，古所谓隤然其处顺，渊乎其似道者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163613_comment'></div>君之捐馆，四子皆未成立，无田产可归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163613_comment'></div>夫人吴氏，教抚之慈且严，母道称于宗姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163613_comment'></div>长子国祥，举明经不第，卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163613_comment'></div>仲曰不伐，字次德，通经术，有节义，士君子推重之，今为卫尉寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163613_comment'></div>次国华，次为道士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163613_comment'></div>一女，归程氏琬，今宣徽北院使、武昌军节度琳之兄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163613_comment'></div>某羁旅在睢上，次德忘年见友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163613_comment'></div>庆历甲申，某领审官，次德赍阀阅公谒曰：「不伐应受大县，愿掌山阴之征，以其去峎下四十里，便襄事也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163613_comment'></div>既得请，崎岖陈、蔡、颍、亳，凡缌以上丧悉负归汉上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163613_comment'></div>戊子孟秋十日，徙君、夫人，以葬于隐君之茔侧，盖治命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163613_comment'></div>且来丐铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163613_comment'></div>惟隐君之义，秘省之德，乃史官所宜录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163613_comment'></div>余，史官也，撰著宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163613_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1163613'>猗嗟韦公，沛乎其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163613_comment'></div>虽不公卿，道德则充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163613_comment'></div>如彼金石，《咸》、《韶》具然，不击不考，至音自全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163613_comment'></div>如彼杞梓，栋杗之分，不朴不斲，良材固存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163613_comment'></div>灏灏汪汪，浑浑粹醇，顺命悬解，以还氤氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163613_comment'></div>君子哉若人！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163613_comment'></div>尚德哉若人！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163613_comment'></div>奚糟粕之足留，而功名之异云！</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1163613_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年6月25日</a>　六月二十五日，在京任翰林学士，岳父马绛卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年8月</a>　八月，坐尝托杨仪市女口，罢职知滁州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='571a9e500d874704afe5784f763e0da8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("571a9e500d874704afe5784f763e0da8");'><span id='571a9e500d874704afe5784f763e0da8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1054')">1053-1054年</a>，47-48岁</div><div id='571a9e500d874704afe5784f763e0da8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年7月</a>　七月，服除，再授端明殿学士、兼龙图阁学士、给事中，举钱明逸自代。作品：服除再授端明殿学士兼龙图阁学士给事中举官自代状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>服除再授端明殿学士兼龙图阁学士给事中举官自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163357")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163357'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163357'>右，臣蒙恩除前件官职，准敕节文，举官自代者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163357_comment'></div>臣窃见翰林侍读学士、尚书右司郎中钱明逸业履端修，学识该敏，施于有政，议者曰才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163357_comment'></div>盍处深严，上资访对，代臣充职，实允佥言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1163357_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年7月</a>　七月，服除，再授端明殿学士、兼龙图阁学士、给事中，有谢恩表。作品：服除再授端明殿学士兼龙图阁学士给事中谢恩表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>服除再授端明殿学士兼龙图阁学士给事中谢恩表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163288")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163288'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163288'>伏奉制命，授臣某官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163288_comment'></div>礼方终制，恩许还朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163288_comment'></div>入觐黼帷，邈清光而在望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163288_comment'></div>登陪藻幄，簉近缀以为荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163288_comment'></div>伏念臣才匪通方，器惭适用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163288_comment'></div>从乡人之善者，幼择与游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163288_comment'></div>玷国士之品题，早尘上达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163288_comment'></div>荐承诏选，遽躐仕阶，见推英俊之场，周历华要之地，比繇禁署，分领翰垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163288_comment'></div>不图衅罚之深，靡究劬劳之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163288_comment'></div>久缠病苦，无望生全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163288_comment'></div>况晷景之不停，怅几筵之已彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163288_comment'></div>仰膺茂典，俾复通班，再趋户牖之严，仍处闺帷之密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163288_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下大圆周覆，一气均和，轸尘露之旧勤，收箕斗之浮象，匪遗輶曲，同被范围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163288_comment'></div>敢不进念竭忠，退思寡过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163288_comment'></div>日月献纳，庶尽近臣之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163288_comment'></div>夙夜切磋，以励在公之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163288_comment'></div>少期来效，上答鸿私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1163288_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年7月</a>　七月，服除，再授端明殿学士、兼龙图阁学士、给事中，有笏记。作品：服除授依前端明殿学士龙图阁学士给事中笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>服除授依前端明殿学士龙图阁学士给事中笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163402")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163402'>伏蒙圣恩赐臣官告、敕牒各一道，授臣前件官并职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163402_comment'></div>祗荷宠灵，载怀惕厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163402_comment'></div>伏念臣早缘素业，幸遘亨期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163402_comment'></div>待对广廷，尝再尘于圣选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163402_comment'></div>参华近缀，实历践于要途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163402_comment'></div>无补大猷，竟罹危议，方领麾于南夏，奄钟罚于慈闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163402_comment'></div>晷景不停，几筵已彻，遽召还于法从，复上觇于清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163402_comment'></div>此盖伏遇尊号皇帝陛下照揭大明，慈均洪覆，垂矜簪履之旧，俾陪殿阁之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163402_comment'></div>敢不鞭策蹇驽，砥磨铅钝，庶勉涓埃之效，上酬雨露之恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1163402_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年7月</a>　七月，服除，再授端明殿学士、兼龙图阁学士、给事中，获赐对衣腰带鞍辔马，有谢状。作品：服除再授端明殿学士龙图阁学士给事中谢赐对衣腰带鞍辔马状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>服除再授端明殿学士龙图阁学士给事中谢赐对衣腰带鞍辔马状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163396")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163396'>伏蒙圣慈以臣授前件官并职，特赐衣一对，金腰带一条，金镀银鞍辔马一匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163396_comment'></div>笥衣纤丽，厩马桓闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163396_comment'></div>九环增鞙璲之容，六辔副镂衢之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163396_comment'></div>荷恩殊渥，揣报奚胜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163396_comment'></div>伏念臣久去禁严，甫周服纪，遽被绨封之召，趣还藻幄之华，逮此拜嘉，复尔载锡，上沿仪秩，下辨等威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163396_comment'></div>服表身章，安吉既荣于动色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163396_comment'></div>乘资体养，驱驰式遂于代劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163396_comment'></div>祗愧便蕃，顾惭孱陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163396_comment'></div>稽古之力，敢援桓荣之言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163396_comment'></div>受宠若惊，惟思老氏之训。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1163396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年7月25日</a>　七月二十五日，判流内铨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年9月</a>　九月，在京判流内铨，上疏论内臣恩荫太过。作品：论内臣奏荫子弟奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1163229' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163229' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163229?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论内臣奏荫子弟奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163229")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163229_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163229'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163229'>昨闻重定二省都知押班等著在閤门使之上，物议杂起，深以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163229_comment'></div>当时有司无人论执，茍从其请，既已失之，今又闻二省陈乞奏授子孙恩泽，于见秩上更加一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163229_comment'></div>此事若行，不惟违越祖宗法度，隳紊朝廷典章，必致陛下有私近习之名，大臣有阿亲倖之丑，内侍有恣横之议，谏官御史有隐默之尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163229_comment'></div>且都知押班，地处亲近，宜为朝廷爱惜事体，动循轨度，孜孜徇公，如此侥求，何以示外？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163229_comment'></div>《易》曰「履霜坚冰至」，言当戒其渐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163229_comment'></div>汉唐之事，臣尝为陛下言之矣，伏乞圣断深赐察纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163229_comment'></div>其都知押班奏荫恩例，伏乞一仍旧制<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163229_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1163229'>见：宋刻本、清抄本作「视」，《宋名臣奏议》作「常」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1163229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163229'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163229_0'>⑴ 《乐全集》卷二五。又见《续资治通鉴长编》卷一七五，《宋名臣奏议》卷六一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163229_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年10月19日</a>　十月十九日，判太常寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年11月4日</a>　十一月四日，南郊礼成，有诗。作品：大祀礼成。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_495349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大祀礼成<span class='inlineComment2'>（原注：皇祐五年。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年11月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495349")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495349'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495349'>皇心奉先孝，盛德事天明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495349'>严配讲隆礼<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：三圣并侑，著为大典。）</span>，精禋格至诚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495349'>衣冠先示质<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，金石始谐声<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495349'>鬲享初登熟，锋和用启牲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495349'>百神虔受职，万物乐由庚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495349'>星斗罗空碧，柴烟彻紫清。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495349'>祥曦回羽卫，佳气覆瑶甍。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495349'>雷雨金鸡动，风云铁马轻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495349'>灵休纷报贶，宸念在持盈<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495349'>孤陋叨华近，何辞颂泰平。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495349'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_495349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495349'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_495349_0'>⑴ 自注：臣庆历四年摄太仆，升辂执绥，及此再摄太仆，窃睹衣冠及诸服御皆不易旧，圣心尚质贵诚之意也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_495349_0'>⑵ 自注：郊庙始用新制钟磬，及以晋鼓鼓金奏。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_495349_0'>⑶ 自注：始循古制铸牛羊豕鼎及用鸾刀启牲。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_495349_0'>⑷ 自注：臣陪辂，屡被顾问，闻持盈守成之言。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495349_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年12月</a>　十二月，加翰林侍读学士，知秦州，力辞不拜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年12月</a>　十二月，加翰林侍读学士，知秦州，作笏记。作品：兼侍读学士知秦州笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兼侍读学士知秦州笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163400")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163400'>伏蒙圣慈授臣前件职任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163400_comment'></div>仰服宠荣，交增感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163400_comment'></div>伏念臣亲逢盛际，早滥华涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163400_comment'></div>中假州符，尝适江湖之远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163400_comment'></div>近还禁琐，复攀日月之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163400_comment'></div>岂谓尊号皇帝陛下犹录虚名，未渝睿眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163400_comment'></div>惭叔子恩信之著，委殿边防；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163400_comment'></div>昧孟侯经艺之长，延登讲劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163400_comment'></div>惟坚忠竭，少谢恩褒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1163400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　春，以礼部侍郎知滑州，有让官表。作品：除尚书礼部侍郎知滑州让迁官表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除尚书礼部侍郎知滑州让迁官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163289")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163289_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163289'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163289'>伏奉制书，以臣差知滑州，特迁尚书礼部侍郎者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163289_comment'></div>甸服陪京，首膺东眷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163289_comment'></div>春官小宰，仍假宠名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163289_comment'></div>奖受有殊，兢忧无措<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163289_comment'></div>臣论材谫薄，语道迂疏，亲逢乐育之辰，屡塞方闻之诏，误蒙恩记，尝历事权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163289_comment'></div>向解禁扃，连纡州组，契阔江湖之远，流离岁月之赊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163289_comment'></div>近趋丹陛之严，复预紫垣之近，激扬懦气，仰奉清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163289_comment'></div>伏遇国家示壮邦畿，增崇屏卫，郊甸屯兵，慎择臣守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163289_comment'></div>岂期玩印之咨，首访遗簪之旧，迁贰六官之重，用优三辅之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163289_comment'></div>无镇抚方面之劳，有息偃铃斋之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163289_comment'></div>论今地望，虽体大而势雄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163289_comment'></div>较昔官居，本事稀而身逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163289_comment'></div>过加赏利，恐累典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163289_comment'></div>若非此际恳辞，必启后来侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163289_comment'></div>况臣职忝殿幄，官处琐闱，久尘侍从之华，足领藩宣之寄，曷烦丽泽，方重左符？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163289_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下特寝新恩，许还旧秩，往釐州务，躬布诏条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163289_comment'></div>虽去君前，稍违于户牖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163289_comment'></div>顾居寰内，何远于本朝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163289_comment'></div>仰祈宽大之慈，曲示保全之度，俯回照鉴，垂谅由衷，辄干九死之诛，冀完一介之守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163289_comment'></div>所有敕诰，未敢祗受。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1163289_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　春，以礼部侍郎知滑州，有乞免转官劄子。作品：知滑州乞免转官劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163290' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163290' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163290?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知滑州乞免转官劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163290")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163290_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163290'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163290'>臣伏奉敕告，授尚书礼部侍郎，差知滑州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163290_comment'></div>近者朝议升曹、滑等州为辅郡，增置兵卫，以壮王畿，所遣守臣，缘此诚重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163290_comment'></div>然滑州本实閒僻，公事绝稀，无宣力之烦，非藉才之地，更起迁官之例，恐开后倖之途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163290_comment'></div>又环都五州，并为陪辅，知州在任，迁易不常，必待加恩而行，益滋干赏之滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163290_comment'></div>况臣官叨两省，职居清近，出当屏翰，体亦非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163290_comment'></div>臣前日欲先陈论，又虑涉于辞避，故且受命，须至上言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163290_comment'></div>伏望圣恩许臣只以旧官前去赴任，慎重名器，兹为治本，在臣之分，亦获自安。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163290_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　春，以礼部侍郎知滑州，举曾公亮代任礼部侍郎。作品：迁礼部侍郎知滑州举官自代状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迁礼部侍郎知滑州举官自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163356")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163356'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163356'>右，臣蒙恩除尚书礼部侍郎，准敕节文，举官自代者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163356_comment'></div>窃见翰林学士、尚书刑部郎中曾公亮端良清慎，守道有文，爰自立朝，搢绅推重，使登省闼，实焕仪曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163356_comment'></div>乞回茂恩，庶允公论。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1163356_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　春，以礼部侍郎知滑州，有谢表。作品：谢迁礼部侍郎领辅郡表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢迁礼部侍郎领辅郡表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163291")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163291'>臣某言：伏奉制命，以臣差知滑州，特授臣尚书礼部侍郎者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163291_comment'></div>近服建侯，地升三辅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163291_comment'></div>中台分次，官贰六卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163291_comment'></div>并荷褒荣，交深愧惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163291_comment'></div>臣世凭儒素，天与朴忠，幸遘重雍之辰，滥膺特起之诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163291_comment'></div>造庙堂而干禄，兼冀亲甘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163291_comment'></div>轻藁锧以献言，累迂圣问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163291_comment'></div>蔑闻尘露之益，空收箕斗之名，频烦宠章，进点清贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163291_comment'></div>向间关于补郡，方契阔以还朝，重趋丹陛之华，再预皂囊之缀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163291_comment'></div>喜从遐邈，获际近严，嘿务安恬，绝希侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163291_comment'></div>会庙堂之深议，崇畿甸之迩封，盛修官仪，推峻地望，遄恤北门之旧，首蒙左竹之咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163291_comment'></div>谓密附日闱，虽居重寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163291_comment'></div>而轻辞天仗，亦动渊衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163291_comment'></div>因假仪曹，示优禁从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163291_comment'></div>露囊封而启让，承汗号以难回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163291_comment'></div>载省无功，徒坚自讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163291_comment'></div>此盖伏遇尊号皇帝陛下曲垂睿览，俯暨寒踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163291_comment'></div>念昔误知，非缘党援；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163291_comment'></div>推今同类，每异矜怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163291_comment'></div>偶赐节以殿邦，犹出纶而增秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163291_comment'></div>敢不祗循条教，恪佩训词，往殚夙夜之诚，少答乾坤之造。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1163291'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1163291_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　春，以礼部侍郎知滑州，作笏记。作品：迁礼部侍郎知滑州笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迁礼部侍郎知滑州笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163401")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163401'>伏蒙圣恩授臣前件官任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163401_comment'></div>仰服宠荣，交深兢惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163401_comment'></div>伏念臣叨逢盛旦，早窃虚名，久依帏幄之严，频蒙雨露之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163401_comment'></div>今建侯于三辅，首祗命于一麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163401_comment'></div>仍繇禁琐之班，进贰春官之秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163401_comment'></div>此盖伏遇尊号皇帝陛下特申睿奖，曲轸寒踪，谓立身之朴忠，常留意于抡采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163401_comment'></div>载钦乾造，愈励寸诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163401_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f0e4086fd1ba4f7bb2aef78e0c64f75e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f0e4086fd1ba4f7bb2aef78e0c64f75e");'><span id='f0e4086fd1ba4f7bb2aef78e0c64f75e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>，48岁</div><div id='f0e4086fd1ba4f7bb2aef78e0c64f75e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年7月</a>　七月，以父老子幼，再上劄子乞免知益州。作品：上殿再免知益州劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163294?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上殿再免知益州劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163294")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163294'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163294'>臣近被敕命，差知益州，奉表及劄子，以亲老乞且终满滑州见任，准中书劄子，奉圣旨不许辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163294_comment'></div>又闻已差梅挚知滑州，亦有朝旨，不许辞让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163294_comment'></div>梅挚缘辅郡加职，已朝谢，臣于事体难为更留本郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163294_comment'></div>今奉恩旨朝觐，获对天颜，敢再沥恳诚，上黩宸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163294_comment'></div>伏以益州方面甚重，朝廷寄任非轻，臣以庸虚，误膺推择，便当策励驽钝，往虔诏条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163294_comment'></div>但以臣父年俯传家，而臣终鲜兄弟，贱息尚幼，未堪承事，义难违远，茍冒宠灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163294_comment'></div>敢望圣慈，垂矜愚守，俾循陔之志获展于盛朝，则图报之心誓伸于异日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163294_comment'></div>臣无任激切待命之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1163294_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cdf54fc7ceca487caf95a472c69e5a71_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cdf54fc7ceca487caf95a472c69e5a71");'><span id='cdf54fc7ceca487caf95a472c69e5a71_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1059')">1056-1059年</a>，50-53岁</div><div id='cdf54fc7ceca487caf95a472c69e5a71' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　本年，在京任三司使，奏减免蜀赋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年8月7日</a>　八月七日，在京任三司使，与陈升之、吴奎、王畴就秘阁考试制科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年10月1日</a>　十月一日，在京任三司使，上《嘉祐禄令》十卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年11月13日</a>　十一月十三日，在京任三司使，上疏论京师军储事。作品：论京师军储事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1163192' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163192' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163192?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论京师军储事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐二年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163192")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163192_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163192'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163192'>臣窃惟今之京师，古所谓陈留，天下四冲八达之地者也，非如函秦天府百二之固，洛宅九州之中，表里山河，形胜足恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163192_comment'></div>自唐末朱温受封于梁，因而建都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163192_comment'></div>至于石晋割幽、蓟之地以入契丹，遂与强虏共平原之利，故五代争夺，戎马生郊，其患由乎畿甸无藩篱之限，本根无所庇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163192_comment'></div>祖宗受命，规摹毕讲，不还周、汉之宇，而梁氏是因，非乐是而处之，势有所不获已者，大体利漕运而赡师旅，依重师而为国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163192_comment'></div>则是今日之势，国依兵而立，兵以食为命，食以漕运为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163192_comment'></div>今仰食于官廪者，不惟三军，至于京城士庶以亿万计，大半待饱于军稍之馀，故国家于漕事最急最重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163192_comment'></div>臣庆历五年权三司使，尝取责到在京诸仓见在斛㪷数，人粮一千三百万石，是时每月约支三十四万有馀石，计可备二年一十一月日支遣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163192_comment'></div>马料三百二十万石，是时每月约支四万馀石，计可备七年支遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163192_comment'></div>今次受命，再领邦计，昨于三月中取责到在京诸仓见在斛㪷数，人粮八百万石，每月约支四十万石，计可备一年馀八月日支遣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163192_comment'></div>马料七十万石，每月约支四万七千馀石，计可备一年馀四月日支遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163192_comment'></div>自庆历及今，通十年之比，计所亏耗五分之二，为国远虑，窃所寒心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163192_comment'></div>究所以致然者，盖自庆历七年拣发京东西、江、湖、淮、浙宣毅兵士充填在京诸军，至于诸色冗食，顷来益众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163192_comment'></div>复自有事西边，内外支费不赡，屡减东南之籴，使输缗王府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163192_comment'></div>或州郡灾伤，朝旨辄辍粮运，以救赒艰急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163192_comment'></div>亦缘诸路转运积成废慢，年额亏减，上下因循，阙于督举，官失其守，事忘其旧，致令储备益乏如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163192_comment'></div>日侵月削，更五七年，京师仓廪无一年之蓄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163192_comment'></div>夫金帛轻货，缓急易聚，至于粮馈，非素为备，若因之以饥馑，倘别有不可预防之事，一旦阙误，岂可仓卒而致者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163192_comment'></div>倘有不给，虽大圣智，其将何术以济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163192_comment'></div>此国家安危之计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163192_comment'></div>臣才虑疏浅，然职思其忧，谨具所合举行之事，画一条件如右：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1163192'>一、汴河年额上供斛㪷六百万石，若每年般运及数，可以年支得给而有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163192_comment'></div>自康定年后，西边用兵，经费不足，每年常将上供斛㪷折纳见钱，一石千钱为率，或一百万石，或五十万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163192_comment'></div>是时王师外戍，在京军粮月支数少，减仓储，供边籴，犹为有名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163192_comment'></div>自后边兵还营，京师增置禁旅，人数益多，犹复时缘前例折纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163192_comment'></div>去年以恭谢大礼，亦是于江湖六路将斛㪷五十万石折钱五十万缗，起发上京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163192_comment'></div>乞特降敕命，三司今后更不得将年额上供斛㪷折变见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1163192'>一、汴河上供斛㪷，本为京师军储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163192_comment'></div>自明道年山东荐饥，朝廷以为忧，特令截拨运米，入清河赈济，自后缘此屡以上供粮斛外支诸路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163192_comment'></div>去年令截上供粮米六十万石应副河北，十五万石应副京东，五万二千有馀石自湖南起发，赴昭、桂州卸纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163192_comment'></div>然州县灾荒，理当赒救，若虑害轻重，则本末当有校矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163192_comment'></div>乞特降敕命，今后诸路灾伤，不得更议截拨上供斛㪷，只令三司多方擘画，就别路支移应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163192_comment'></div>若极于艰急，须至辍借内帑钱帛，犹愈于亏乏军储之患大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1163192'>一、广济河年额上供斛㪷六十二万石，其实五十万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163192_comment'></div>内十二万石，因庆历初京东转运使奏南京军营多，每岁计度军粮，支移徐单曹济州、广济军二税应副，民力劳敝，遂截上供运米十二万石，通旧八万石共二十万石，充本京军粮，却从广济河认数般运填纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163192_comment'></div>所截粳米、小麦，其填数多是杂色粟豆，已为亏损仓储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163192_comment'></div>而又每年三司折变钱帛，供助支费，至和二年折三十一万石，嘉祐元年二十万石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163192_comment'></div>或有尽数折纳之时，只是三司承例施行，亦不曾奏候朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163192_comment'></div>今年不曾更行折变，然亦虑本路递年不曾尽数起发斛㪷，以此纲运人船或有因循阙备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163192_comment'></div>乞降敕命，三司今后不得更将广济河年额上供斛㪷折变钱帛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163192_comment'></div>及下本路所般年额斛㪷，今后须得起发及数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163192_comment'></div>其纲船兵士常令本司添填有备，运路河道亦委本司相度擘画，取令通济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1163192'>一、惠民河年额上供斛㪷六十万石，内二十五万石系淮南年额，般赴咸平、太康、尉氏等县充军粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163192_comment'></div>比来发运司又于汴河上供年额内豁除此数，显是将此斛㪷两充数，省司见行根问次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163192_comment'></div>其三十五万石，合是京西管认起发，近岁并不曾赶办般运，其到京之数，每年五七万而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163192_comment'></div>勘会皇祐五年曾降朝旨，令蔡河拨发司每年添般上供斛㪷数目，本路辞诉部内伤，乞候丰熟应副，自后因循，亦是催促不前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163192_comment'></div>今相度本路财赋不至丰赡，诸色支费亦多，令办年额，必恐不迨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163192_comment'></div>乞降敕命，今后年额上供斛㪷特与减十五万石，只令般运二十万，须管到京数足，不得更有亏阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163192_comment'></div>内供御小麦并油、醋，库油、麻，逐时依省司抛数供纳外，许以大小麦、小豆、黑豆、谷粟充数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1163192'>一、黄河：检会景德二年敕，陕西转运司每年认定马料三十万石上京，所有细色斛㪷如有剩数，即行般运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163192_comment'></div>又检会三门、白波发运司编敕，黄河年额上供粮斛，委陕西转运司并支新好斛㪷赴缘河仓送纳，仍常预报三门白波发运司计度人船般运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163192_comment'></div>若计度支移有失，即罪在转运司；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163192_comment'></div>般运亏额，即罪发运司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163192_comment'></div>并令三门发运判官催驱般辇，每至冬终具般过数目比较申奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163192_comment'></div>臣看详景德二年，正是继迁骚扰，西陲用兵，陕右困敝之际，然犹漕运上供京师，未尝废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163192_comment'></div>勘会近岁以来，即不曾起发一船一运到京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163192_comment'></div>抑由中间天下无事，财力丰赡，仓廪充实，不以储蓄为切务，内外因循，及宝元中夏戎叛命，遂不暇给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163192_comment'></div>顷来边事宁息，关中累年丰熟，本路财费无阙，朝廷至今每年供给物帛不少，其旧额马料三十万石，合行计度上供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163192_comment'></div>乞特降敕旨，下陕西转运司、三门白波发运司，起嘉祐二年秋，一依先降敕命，据年额马料三十万石，须管般运到京数足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1163192'>一、在京岁支马料豆麦约六十万石，近年计度，多抛数下发运司起发，遂以大麦、黑豆粗色充数，每年常及三十万石，计兵船、口食、水脚，为费数倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163192_comment'></div>今若令陕西、京西及将京畿二税细色折纳粗色，岁计可以得足，则汴河漕挽专令般粳米，量以小麦充以年额，此所谓转江湖之谷，以实太仓者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1163192'>一、今以军储大计，欲仓廪充实，诸河所般年额上供斛㪷，据见今纲船、兵稍常患不足，难更添数般运，惟是在京坐仓收籴，可免漕挽之费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163192_comment'></div>即今京仓月支军粮四十万石，若坐仓收籴，每月以五万石为限，犹有宽剩，可以充民籴，如此每年可得六十万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163192_comment'></div>其价例当随时估定，然通计中等价例，每㪷一百文，用钱六十万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163192_comment'></div>勘会递年春初，内藏库拨钱六十万贯付三司添助支费，谓之年退钱，桩留此钱以充籴价可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163192_comment'></div>即今计天下财赋所入，中外军国所费，年支见在，不至交阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163192_comment'></div>昨以河北伤，又河防为患，本路艰急，自三司供给除军粮斛㪷外，支拨见钱银绢约八十五万贯疋两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163192_comment'></div>又约度今年年支粮草计置人粮马料二百万石，以本路丰稔，更于年计外添籴一百万石，准备军储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163192_comment'></div>凡此籴本价钱，今已计度有备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163192_comment'></div>又今年见将曲院、店宅务课利钱六十五万贯，拨还内藏库填纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163192_comment'></div>至和二年分辍过河北便籴本钱，约更用来年半年课利，可以拨填数足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163192_comment'></div>凡此钱数，并系年计外非泛支费，总计二百二十万贯有馀，即日犹据见在，粗无阙乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163192_comment'></div>若诸路丰熟，边陲宁静，朝廷每事撙节，别无横费，则年退钱一项桩充坐仓籴本，添备军粮，足可那容，不至阙误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_1163192'>一、备储廪，通漕运，当令河道疏通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1163192_comment'></div>艺祖开国，首浚诸河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1163192_comment'></div>按汴渠本禹迹也，春秋时已名见诸经，历代尝浚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1163192_comment'></div>隋大发民开凿通济渠，其去古汴依约不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1163192_comment'></div>自汉至唐虽都雍、洛，凡诸水运，咸资此渠漕引江湖，利尽南海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1163192_comment'></div>天圣已前，每岁开理，缘河人户各蓄开河器备，名品甚多，未尝有堙壅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1163192_comment'></div>天圣初，有张君平者陈利见，始罢春夫，继以浅妄小人茍规赏利，撙减役费，以为劳绩，致兹淤塞，有妨通漕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1163192_comment'></div>至于惠民、广济二河，皆所以致四方之货食，以会京邑，舳舻相接，赡给公私，近年以来，悉皆填塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1163192_comment'></div>盖图长利者不恤于小费，期永逸者无惮于一劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1163192_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷访问差择稍知水利，精力干事，不拘文武官三两员，经度计置，开通诸河，各据地分所历州县夫，令尽工料疏理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1163192_comment'></div>其木岸埧闸堰埭材用合缮修处，先为计备，严为责罚，必令经久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1163192_comment'></div>去年京畿大水，坏官私庐舍，自去秋至今春，半年之中所修诸军营房十馀万间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1163192_comment'></div>夫以国家物力，岂有不可成之事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1163192_comment'></div>但事败于因循，而成于果决，至于其所不获已，亦必成而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1163192_comment'></div>又诸修造无名不急之处，土木之工无时暂辍，所费不可胜计，此诸河道皆是祖宗留心之地，国家大计所资，忽而不图，是亦有司之过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_1163192'>一、里河折中仓，本是在京便籴，以添助军储，随时立法，旋行抛数，然于边籴轻重有妨，以此便入，不能及数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1163192_comment'></div>近庆历年中，令在京入中诸色斛㪷二百万石，用三说法，三十贯支见钱，三十五贯支向南州军末盐，三十五贯支香药茶交引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1163192_comment'></div>当时为河北缘边入便，亦用三说文钞，以此只入到十五万馀石，事体不便，遂罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1163192_comment'></div>今在库香药阙少，又江湖末盐自是见钱之法，邦计所赖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1163192_comment'></div>诸山场茶货已充河北粮草支用，若更将折中行使，必亦利害相攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1163192_comment'></div>故不若坐仓收籴，事简而利溥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1163192'>一、京东、淮南土壤宽广，财谷足赡，可容三五万人驻泊就粮，若遣京师禁军就粮淮南，河北兵士就粮京东，可以省仓储，留边谷，因其外屯，亦可拣退疲冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_1163192'>一、积粟太仓，本以强兵，而惰游冗食之人坐为糜耗，使储廪日以虚竭，玩而弗恤，斯为深弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1163192_comment'></div>勘会在京及畿县诸营剩员仅及三万人，至于京城六军兵士，其间老病不堪作役者至多，诸司库务疲癃游冗，不可胜计，是皆衣食于帑廪，牟蠹生民之膏泽者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1163192_comment'></div>夫山海之高深，不让涓尘之益，亿万之数，积于一二，故事聚蓄者必累微细，以成广大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1163192_comment'></div>凡此在京六军及京城府界剩员、诸司库务诸老病之人，欲乞朝廷详酌指挥，渐次拣选放停，免令虚耗仓库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_97_1163192'>一、府界税赋，准皇祐五年赦敕，应开封府诸县两税太重，特于元额上减落三分，永为定式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1163192_comment'></div>今勘会除依赦敕减三分外，即今夏秋二税斛㪷四十万有馀石，钱三十四万有馀贯，䌷绢十万有馀疋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1163192_comment'></div>向由赋重，百姓输送不迨，故因灾害，多是体量减放，务从宽恤，朝廷以此明降赦令，例行优除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1163192_comment'></div>奸游之民尚循故态，年谷顺成，亦复披诉，官吏自图省便，未尝按行检履，但据保甲，概为约免，茍容侥倖，习以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1163192_comment'></div>今后畿县灾伤，差官分检，令并依农田敕式样施行除放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1163192_comment'></div>盖租税之制，有国者所以取于民，至公之道尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1163192_comment'></div>若是岁之凶穰如法而弛歛，事举其中，理合于正，所谓「理财正辞，禁民为非曰义」者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_104_1163192'>一、转漕之职在发运使属之官，责当久其任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1163192_comment'></div>请精选才干之吏，曾历三司判官、合入第二任转运使资序人权充；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1163192_comment'></div>候及三年，职事办集，即与正除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1163192_comment'></div>又及三年，事务修举，与就除三司副使领职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1163192_comment'></div>又及三年，与除近职，或两省官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1163192_comment'></div>其有器略足用者，更自朝廷奖擢委任，其两员尝令先后除代，此则为官择人之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_110_1163192'>一、粮纲到京交纳，少欠每岁不下六七万石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1163192_comment'></div>其逐纲券历兵稍粮食，承例在路并权阁不请，及到仓卸纳，据逐船少数将在券阁留粮斛充偿所欠，谓之折会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1163192_comment'></div>据兵稍口食，合是缘路支请，辄行积留，却将太仓合纳军储消折，此皆起于近岁因循敝例，理合令发运司依数包认，每年候上供住运，具折会都数，下本司次第理纳补填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1163192_comment'></div>此小事，已从三司指挥行下，亦合以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_114_1163192'>右，臣所条画事节，乞自朝廷详议施行，倘相继持守，不遽隳改，则庶乎三年可以馀一年之储，十年可以致三年之积，通三十年而有九年之蓄，可谓盛王之大业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1163192_comment'></div>前史有言：尧之水，汤之旱，而无危忘之虑，以其储蓄有备尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1163192_comment'></div>尧、汤之圣，不能以无备而待天灾，天灾流行，亦无如人之有备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1163192_comment'></div>唐刘晏论漕运之事云：「三秦之人待此而饱，六军之众待此而强」，「四方旅拒者可以破胆，三河流离者于兹请命」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1163192_comment'></div>是谓安社稷之奇策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1163192_comment'></div>夫立人之道，建国之本，在乎衣食而已矣，惟陛下深留圣虑焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_119_1163192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163192'><span class='label'>按：</span>《乐全集》卷二三。又见《宋会要辑稿》食货四二之一八（第六册第五五七○页）、食货四六之一六（第六册第五六一一页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1163192_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年11月27日</a>　十一月二十七日，在京任三司使，荐举孙复之子孙大年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年3月20日</a>　三月二十日，在京任三司使，受诏主编《天下驿券则例》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年7月</a>　七月，在京任三司使，与包拯奏请复范祥制置解盐之职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年10月</a>　十月，在京任三司使，上疏请弛茶禁。作品：上仁宗乞弛茶禁。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《宋朝诸臣奏议》卷一〇八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年12月</a>　十二月，在京任三司使，上疏请宽益、梓、利三路所输军衣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　本年，在京任三司使，因辞免三司使不许，有谢答诏表。作品：乞免三司使不允谢答诏表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免三司使不允谢答诏表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163298")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163298'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163298'>伏蒙圣慈，以臣近上劄子乞解职出知郓州，特赐诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163298_comment'></div>备员主计，岁涉再期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163298_comment'></div>辞剧请藩，章凡六上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163298_comment'></div>荷渊衷之怜恻，纡玺札之丁宁，仍示抚存，未容罢免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163298_comment'></div>内循孤拙，愈极兢危<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163298_comment'></div>臣庆历中擢自宪台，长兹会府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163298_comment'></div>于时齿发方壮，精力尚彊，虽趣办应猝之非长，独居官任职而无废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163298_comment'></div>早以目疾，求解利权，久方开俞，得还禁近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163298_comment'></div>自尔出入中外，奔走川涂，更历数州，又逾一纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163298_comment'></div>向罢坤维之守，志图近郡而行，遽被诏除，复膺使任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163298_comment'></div>臣闻命之始，即以旧疾为言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163298_comment'></div>就职而来，每以旷务为虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163298_comment'></div>盖财用之均节，系剖析之谨严，急之则害于农商，缓之或容于奸利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163298_comment'></div>责其簿领之效，实存省察之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163298_comment'></div>而臣心之精微，比顷年而亦耗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163298_comment'></div>目之瞭眊，迪近岁而有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163298_comment'></div>或苦劳疼，乃移告谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163298_comment'></div>因控恳诚之切，屡形封奏之详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163298_comment'></div>愿停三使之浩繁，窃丐一麾而休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163298_comment'></div>公议幸宽于谴劾，朝恩亦尽于优容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163298_comment'></div>实陈力之不任，非无名而罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163298_comment'></div>岂谓尊号皇帝陛下俯矜愚守，早缀近班，不违道以求全，颇著诚而无伪，再颁温诏，曲谕训言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163298_comment'></div>重念臣所苦未平，知分颇熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163298_comment'></div>傥精神之可强，顾烦冗以何辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163298_comment'></div>但惧眩昏，致隳重害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163298_comment'></div>虽虚怀容纳，俾收累久之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163298_comment'></div>而列牍干祈，未免再三之渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163298_comment'></div>至明垂鉴，丹悃宁诬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1163298_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年1月7日</a>　正月七日，在京任三司使，上所编《嘉祐驿令》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年3月4日</a>　三月四日，为包拯劾奏，罢三司使，为端明殿学士、兼龙图阁学士、尚书左丞、知陈州。此前，已迁吏部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年3月</a>　三月，在京，由知陈州改知应天府。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='19a8aab1f77c4e51960748885b91fd6b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("19a8aab1f77c4e51960748885b91fd6b");'><span id='19a8aab1f77c4e51960748885b91fd6b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>，54岁</div><div id='19a8aab1f77c4e51960748885b91fd6b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　春，在京觐见仁宗，有辞免知秦州劄子。作品：上殿辞免劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163307' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163307' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163307?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上殿辞免劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163307")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163307_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163307'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163307'>臣近自应天府就移知秦州，以父年老患脚膝，难以迎侍远行，乞赐停寝，诏旨不俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163307_comment'></div>天听盖高，君命至重，不敢烦黩，祗受告敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163307_comment'></div>今蒙恩朝见，获面天颜，敢沥危衷，犹希矜亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163307_comment'></div>秦州于边镇尤为雄剧，朝廷择守，委任非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163307_comment'></div>况今疆琐晏清，顾臣齿发犹壮，猥承宠寄，何事恳辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163307_comment'></div>但义有未安，诚当开列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163307_comment'></div>臣皇祐五年曾差知此州，是时已为迎侍不便，尝所控陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163307_comment'></div>昨罢三司，知应天府，亦缘便亲得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163307_comment'></div>今陛下方以仁孝治天下，臣子于奉养之私，莫不得所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163307_comment'></div>臣若贪冒恩荣，事亲不尽，奚待典刑之及，故于名教有亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163307_comment'></div>仰冀天慈，曲全拙守，特与乡便一郡，徐、亳、济州，皆于南京为近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163307_comment'></div>乌鸟之情，傥得伸于兹日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163307_comment'></div>犬马之力，尚当效于他年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163307_comment'></div>干黩宸严，分甘诛窜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1163307_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='62d6908d2d68416fa2c9f17b644a2b3b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("62d6908d2d68416fa2c9f17b644a2b3b");'><span id='62d6908d2d68416fa2c9f17b644a2b3b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1064')">1063-1064年</a>，57-58岁</div><div id='62d6908d2d68416fa2c9f17b644a2b3b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年10月</a>　十月，徙知陈州，过都，留判尚书都省。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年10月</a>　十月，在京判尚书都省，请知郓州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　本年，在京判尚书都省，上疏乞知制诰详择人材。作品：请慎用两制资序事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1163202' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163202' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163202?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请慎用两制资序事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平元年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163202")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163202_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163202'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163202'>伏以知制诰之职，所以代王言为诰令，由此召入禁林充学士，非才誉允洽，何以当其选？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163202_comment'></div>比来朝廷率以体例次补，日近诰命，或有浅鄙，传为口实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163202_comment'></div>前代国家有事之际，或以单札之辞，折冲千里之外，使三军感励，万方悦劝，背逆凶丑，或以革心，夷狄异类，或以向化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163202_comment'></div>故知文词书命，有足以助国威、宣王泽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163202_comment'></div>祖宗之世，有自州县之职拔处辞禁，有自两禁黜为管库者，盖惟才而是用，岂为人而择官？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163202_comment'></div>其修起居注、史馆修撰，即次除知制诰之资序也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163202_comment'></div>今朝士不修廉耻，至冒宪章，法座之前，辄自干请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163202_comment'></div>窃谓若此除授，宜详加推择，必其人流才地、辞学器识他日可以备大臣之用，而后擢处其职，文物盛于本朝，光华照于天下，使名器以重，堂陛以隆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1163202_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2c49767dd8974d68960a617786a8a8dd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2c49767dd8974d68960a617786a8a8dd");'><span id='2c49767dd8974d68960a617786a8a8dd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1067')">1066-1067年</a>，60-61岁</div><div id='2c49767dd8974d68960a617786a8a8dd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年1月</a>　正月，由知徐州召还京城任翰林学士承旨，有劄子乞就闲职。作品：乞罢禁林就闲曹劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163309' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163309' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163309?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢禁林就閒曹劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1066年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163309")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163309_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163309'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163309'>臣祗奉圣恩，召还词禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163309_comment'></div>臣久患眼疾仅二十年，旧学废忘，无以备顾问；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163309_comment'></div>素业荒疏，无以应时用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163309_comment'></div>若复典司制命，自揆不堪供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163309_comment'></div>又臣父年八十有二，近在徐州卧疾半年，至今右手乏力，臂指不相为用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163309_comment'></div>今当更直省内，家无兼侍之人，早昏缓急，敢安愚虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163309_comment'></div>臣受命之日，即欲自言孤远之情，难期察允，故待到阙，幸对天颜，上谢宸慈采擢之赐，俯陈微衷深切之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163309_comment'></div>所祈覆育，曲赐矜容，俾就閒曹，获全拙守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163309_comment'></div>候近郡有阙，乞别就一差遣，奉法循理，少分忧寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163309_comment'></div>臣不任荷恩待罪激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1163309_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年3月4日</a>　三月四日，在京任翰林学士承旨，有诗。作品：清明连上巳。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清明连上巳<span class='inlineComment2'>（治平丙午三月四日清明）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1066年3月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495514")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495514'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495514'>踏青原上饮，祓禊水边歌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495514'>佳节相连好，游人一倍多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495514_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495514'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年3月</a>　三月，在京任翰林学士承旨，上疏论灾异。作品：论消复灾异奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二四。系年据《宋朝诸臣奏议》卷四二张方平《上英宗论星变》）</span><div id='poem_1163197' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163197' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163197?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论消复灾异奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163197")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163197_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163197'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163197'>臣自到阙，伏见陛下以垂象之变，避正殿，减膳降服，恤刑罢宴，彻乐声，弛力役，所以修省答天戒者甚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163197_comment'></div>窃闻退就宫閤，尤为忧劳，至以圣躬为民祈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163197_comment'></div>臣深惟陛下以上圣之资，自在藩邸，其稽古好德，令闻夙著于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163197_comment'></div>继天纂统，越今四年，始初清明，厉精求治，然未闻有以修明纪律，震耀威灵，以究安危治乱根本之议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163197_comment'></div>前史推彗星之占，率以为除旧布新之象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163197_comment'></div>中外之因循久矣，官失其守，事忘其旧，纲目颓紊，宪章隳弛，天其或者傥将以是为告？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163197_comment'></div>先贤以为政譬之鼓琴瑟，不调甚者，必当解而更张之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163197_comment'></div>窃观朝政，殊未遑及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163197_comment'></div>《晋书》纪《何曾传》：曾侍武帝，退而告其子曰：「吾每对见，未尝闻经国远图，惟说平生常事，非贻厥孙谋之兆也，及身而已，后嗣其殆乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163197_comment'></div>后天下乱危，果如其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163197_comment'></div>今夫万几庶政，属在两府，愿陛下以燕暇之时，就清閒之处，延召执政之臣，从容赐坐，垂意访逮，各使悉心陈治道之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163197_comment'></div>以陛下之明而参择其言，举其可施行者以兴敝举废，救时急务，匪惟修人事，抑以承天意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163197_comment'></div>又比来灾眚间作，率由阴沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163197_comment'></div>夫阴也者，臣道也，妻道也，夷狄之道也，庶民之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163197_comment'></div>陛下推是而求之，则天意可见，而消复之道得矣，惟陛下留神幸察<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163197_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1163197'>三月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163197_comment'></div>原无，据《宋名臣奏议》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1163197_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163197'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1163197_0'>⑴ 《乐全集》卷二四。又见《宋名臣奏议》卷四二，《历代名臣奏议》卷三○一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163197_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　春，在京任翰林学士承旨，有诗述怀。作品：再入禁林即事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再入禁林即事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1066年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495498")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495498'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495498'>重到金坡二十春<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，閒思出处一伤神。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495498'>略行大地山川遍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，再睹青天日月新<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：感昭陵也。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495498'>疏籁岂知谐律吕，散材无意入辕轮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495498'>何时却出都门去，静掩岩扉老此身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495498'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495498_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495498'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_495498_0'>⑴ 自注：庆历六年，自学士出领郡，迨今正二十年。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_495498_0'>⑵ 自注：历升、杭、秦、益、徐、郓等十郡府。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495498_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年4月</a>　四月，在京任翰林学士承旨，为程戡撰神道碑。作品：宋故推诚保德功臣宣徽南院使安武军节度使冀州管内观察处置等使开府仪同三司检校太傅使持节冀州诸军事冀州刺史兼御史大夫鄜延路马步军都总管经略安抚使判延州军州事管内劝农使上柱国广平郡开国公食邑五千二百户食实封一千六百户赠太尉谥曰康穆程公神道碑铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三六。）</span><div id='poem_1163562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故推诚保德功臣宣徽南院使安武军节度使冀州管内观察处置等使开府仪同三司检校太傅使持节冀州诸军事冀州刺史兼御史大夫鄜延路马步军都总管经略安抚使判延州军州事管内劝农使上柱国广平郡开国公食邑五千二百户食实封一千六百户赠太尉谥曰康穆程公神道碑铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　治平三年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1066年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163562")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163562'>昔高阳氏命南正重司天，北正黎司地，其后为羲氏、和氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163562_comment'></div>唐虞之际，实绍其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163562_comment'></div>至于夏商，故重、黎氏世序天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163562_comment'></div>在周，程伯休甫其后也，程氏世系盖远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163562_comment'></div>公之曾王父讳守瑰，仕周检校尚书、工部员外郎兼侍御史，尝更颍川阳翟令，乐其风土，自汴之封丘徙居焉，故今占籍阳翟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163562_comment'></div>公讳戡，字胜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163562_comment'></div>先公以治《春秋》登仕，故公初亦传三家之学，既习通矣，而委之曰：「君子惟多识前言往行以蓄其德，奚事一经」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163562_comment'></div>遂博综艺文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163562_comment'></div>天禧中，杨文公亿典礼部贡举，时推文宗，尤以藻鉴自任，考试进士精甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163562_comment'></div>见公程文，大器赏之，遂为举首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163562_comment'></div>及廷试，亦在第四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163562_comment'></div>于时公之名动天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163562_comment'></div>释褐泾州观察推官，代还，迁秘书省著作佐郎、知齐州长清、绛州翼城县，以爱利为政，有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163562_comment'></div>俄改秘书丞、通判许州、蕲州，迁太常博士，复通判虔州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163562_comment'></div>赣人巧滑嚚讼，公治明审，数辨冤狱，发奸慝，吏民畏服，刑平政清，风绩推最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163562_comment'></div>以尚书屯田员外郎徙知归州，转都官员外郎，数月代还，且甄用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163562_comment'></div>涂次襄阳，闻父丧，徒步而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163562_comment'></div>服除，召为侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163562_comment'></div>宝元元年，并、代地大震，坏城郭庐舍，民死伤者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163562_comment'></div>公以选为并、忻等州安抚使，入境以便宜从事，宣布上之恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163562_comment'></div>诸失业不能自存者，所以救赒安集，施设周及，人情大安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163562_comment'></div>还白利害称旨，所建皆见嘉纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163562_comment'></div>除三司度支判官，迁兵部员外郎，寻兼起居舍人、知谏院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163562_comment'></div>钟内艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163562_comment'></div>时西鄙有衅，朝廷多事，公纳忠开说，补益居多，时政赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163562_comment'></div>夺情俾领职，公确辞得终礼制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163562_comment'></div>既免丧，复还谏省，寻以本官兼侍御史、知台杂事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163562_comment'></div>公之任言责，司宪度，切磨献替，以尊王体，正国论，未尝龊龊及诸细也，故时议者重公有远识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163562_comment'></div>惟帝心简在殊深，以例换三司户部副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163562_comment'></div>不阅岁，擢授天章阁待制、陕西都转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163562_comment'></div>迁刑部郎中、知渭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163562_comment'></div>自戎虏为不义，出车遣戍，平凉当其冲，骑寇三大入残夷，及是始通款。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163562_comment'></div>公蒐补卒乘，缮完壁橹，绥抚新附，种落宁辑，军气以振，邑里始宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163562_comment'></div>时枢府缺员，仁宗顾谓辅臣曰：「程某厚重，可大任也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163562_comment'></div>有间公者，以为故事未有自待制擢二府者，遂不成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163562_comment'></div>拜枢密直学士、知益州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163562_comment'></div>属贝州军乱，州将张得一失守抵罪，公以尝任得一，褫职移知凤翔府，易河中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163562_comment'></div>朝论皆谓坐累太重，踰月还旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163562_comment'></div>顷之，徙永兴军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163562_comment'></div>未几，迁左司郎中，领瀛州高阳关路马步军都总管、安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163562_comment'></div>甫至，迁左谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163562_comment'></div>祀明堂覃庆，迁给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163562_comment'></div>契丹使过高阳关，称疾，请以纱巾见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163562_comment'></div>公曰：「疾可无见，见则以礼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163562_comment'></div>北使惮公严正，乃具冠服如仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163562_comment'></div>仁宗闻而嘉之，语曰：「程某有守，差强人意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163562_comment'></div>还知审官院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163562_comment'></div>他日，帝从容谕时相曰：「昔孟知祥以后唐甲午岁得蜀，至本朝咸平中，岁在甲午，盗发益州，西土大扰，故蜀父老识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163562_comment'></div>来岁复在甲午，蜀人以为恐，其精择可镇静者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163562_comment'></div>既而曰：「无易程某矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163562_comment'></div>召对便殿，亲谕此指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163562_comment'></div>且曰：「为朕再行，即召公执政」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163562_comment'></div>公顿首曰：「事君者有命无避，安敢以宠利居成功」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163562_comment'></div>帝属意良厚，优除端明殿学士、知益州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163562_comment'></div>到部，彭州果有讹传兵起者，即捕斩之，人心以定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163562_comment'></div>自孟昶归朝，守者务为安静，茍远嫌訾，至城堞毁圮，莫敢增葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163562_comment'></div>公曰：「城以保民者也，故萃以除戎器，戒不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163562_comment'></div>聚而莫保，民何依焉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163562_comment'></div>遂议版筑，浚池隍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163562_comment'></div>今蜀城脩完，公之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163562_comment'></div>明年，召除参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163562_comment'></div>屡表逊避，优诏敦促，中人抚问者数四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163562_comment'></div>在政府，有告急变者，称得遗札于路，关搆甚密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163562_comment'></div>尹以白于执政，相顾未决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163562_comment'></div>公曰：「独斩告者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163562_comment'></div>或曰：「何遽尔」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163562_comment'></div>公曰：「是情易得也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163562_comment'></div>尹试尝讯之，果告者二人，旧出入此军，微闻其中豪黠辈妄言，颇连诸校，因相与谋：此官司莫敢宽者，必当按状，竟之，因以图赏利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163562_comment'></div>不竟，亦无以反坐，非有同谋，莫取證尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163562_comment'></div>遂斩告者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163562_comment'></div>皆服公之发奸诈明且决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163562_comment'></div>至和二年，宰相文潞公复辅政，公以通姻引避，除尚书礼部侍郎，改枢密副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1163562_comment'></div>公才长于政事，既历二府，练达治要，处心积虑，期有以报特达之遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1163562_comment'></div>而时为枢密使者，与公情旨不相得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1163562_comment'></div>邕州守将以贿闻，而奏请增补溪洞酋长，且十馀上，公持不从，以为后必生事，数争辩帝前，因坚求解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1163562_comment'></div>五年，以吏部侍郎、观文殿学士、翰林侍读学士领群牧制置使罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1163562_comment'></div>然帝察公议，每长有忧深思远之致，内直公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1163562_comment'></div>寻亦罢枢密使者，拜公宣徽南院使、检校太保、鄜延路马步军都总管、经略安抚使、判延州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1163562_comment'></div>秋，大雨水，五龙川溢，东西两城将坏，居民詾惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1163562_comment'></div>公登城肃祷，水波稍复回还，遂退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1163562_comment'></div>众谓公诚心若有所感然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1163562_comment'></div>英宗践祚，视秩帝傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1163562_comment'></div>是岁，就锡命，以安武军节旄再判延州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1163562_comment'></div>初，夏戎承袭尚幼，没、臧、讹、庬四族颛国，谅祚益习事，患其逼，用季父磨乜之谋，诱讹、庬等诛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1163562_comment'></div>初，朝廷岁赐谅祚金帛，四族常分其半，首领入贡，辄货易图利，故四族盛彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1163562_comment'></div>至是并其所部，没入财畜，谅祚始擅其国，气骄意得，作为僭慢，遂改元，置官号，数为干请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1163562_comment'></div>公上言：「戎狄贪婪，乃其天性，十求九获，犹怀觖望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1163562_comment'></div>饥则噬人，饱则飏去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1163562_comment'></div>畜养之道，宜以威克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1163562_comment'></div>请专遣使，责其僭妄」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1163562_comment'></div>朝廷因降诏诘问，虏虽不悉禀命，因是知为裁折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1163562_comment'></div>公念西疆四道戍守千里，士马留屯，坐空储积，持久之计，必兼耕战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1163562_comment'></div>自古言边备者，必以其土人劲锐，便驰射战斗，习知山川险易，其气俗然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1163562_comment'></div>请籍边户，择取丁壮，籍以为义勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1163562_comment'></div>庙堂议协，自陕以西，无虑得十六万人，更戍番休，以农隙训阅，丰财足食，安民保大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1163562_comment'></div>武有七德，公近之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1163562_comment'></div>夏虏自继迁之叛，狃于狙诈之利，至元昊尤多狡数，故能猎服诸戎，敢为国患，谅祚实轻谲易与者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1163562_comment'></div>而朝论惩宝元、庆历之难，抑游说者多过其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1163562_comment'></div>虏每与契丹、洮人相攻击，辄大点集，声欲犯境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1163562_comment'></div>公独策其情，不为之动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1163562_comment'></div>而常励诸将曰：「夫兵事以严，终可无用，不可不戒也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1163562_comment'></div>克勤小物，备预益修，故时推公沈毅有方略，得将帅体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1163562_comment'></div>虏比年侵掠内属蕃部，秦渭尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1163562_comment'></div>或言帅臣蔽匿，不以实闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1163562_comment'></div>乃遣内珰专领诸路蕃部事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1163562_comment'></div>公上言：「熟户利于附汉，甚惮役属于虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1163562_comment'></div>我不能庇，内臣督领无益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1163562_comment'></div>且族帐星散，而数犒飨，呼召期会，更为烦扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1163562_comment'></div>不若委帅臣察其材勇，捍边有劳，部众所服者，间召赴阙，天子亲临抚阅，迁擢用之，此羁縻之术也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1163562_comment'></div>上善其言，以新命已行，难遽改，后竟以不便悉罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1163562_comment'></div>或请置重兵长安，为四路根本，选大臣总节制，诏公以利害闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1163562_comment'></div>公对：「四路距雍，远或千里，禀白待报，岂及机会？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1163562_comment'></div>责成四路，雅合事权，寇所侵轶，相为救便」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1163562_comment'></div>从焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1163562_comment'></div>既而引年谢事，章十数上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1163562_comment'></div>仁宗晚年赐诏曰：「卿年耆而德益隆，朕所加遇者，未可以期颐自高也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1163562_comment'></div>公惶恐不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1163562_comment'></div>及加旄钺，复申前请，表又十上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1163562_comment'></div>英宗特驰近侍赐手诏曰：「卿虽年高，而精力克壮，在廷历年，处置举合机要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1163562_comment'></div>顷边多事，正当为备，卿勿复更有请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1163562_comment'></div>厚赐手封茗剂，以将恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1163562_comment'></div>公陈情恳至，使者曰：「且有后命，勿受辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1163562_comment'></div>公不获已，下拜受赐，力疾视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1163562_comment'></div>宾佐共白：公其啬精神，近医药，厚自持，府事僚吏请尽力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1163562_comment'></div>公曰：「边帅岂深居养疾者耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1163562_comment'></div>旦夕无少解，疾益侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1163562_comment'></div>帝闻悯之，诏还阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1163562_comment'></div>就舆上道，军民远送郊，莫不号恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1163562_comment'></div>治平三年正月乙亥，行次同州澄城县，索笔牍欲自具遗奏，草数字而薨，享年七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1163562_comment'></div>外见大星殒于寝堂，而闻发哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1163562_comment'></div>先帝轸悼，辍视朝，遣中使吊抚，厚赙其家，追襚太尉章绂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1163562_comment'></div>太常考功阀，合「康穆」二法以易名，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1163562_comment'></div>诸子奉𧚫帷以归阳翟，四月，葬我康穆公于旧学乡先公之茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1163562_comment'></div>阳翟君后终濮州临濮令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1163562_comment'></div>祖思议，隐居不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1163562_comment'></div>考讳坦，国子博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1163562_comment'></div>以公贵，追命三代，普赠太师、中书令兼尚书令，博士封成国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1163562_comment'></div>曾祖妣田氏、祖妣刘氏、妣王氏，秦、魏、陈三国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1163562_comment'></div>公先娶谢氏，追封陈留郡夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1163562_comment'></div>再娶李氏，赠永昌县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1163562_comment'></div>继室以曹氏，枢密使、司空兼侍中襄悼公利用之女也，封新平郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1163562_comment'></div>三子：曰庄、曰荀，尚书虞部员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1163562_comment'></div>曰萃，内殿承制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1163562_comment'></div>七女，适供奉官郭承则，殿中丞崔良孺，大理寺丞宋彦国，虞部员外郎文恭祖，侍禁、閤门祗候王咸允，杭州节度掌书记孙贲，濮州推官李恂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1163562_comment'></div>六孙：高，光禄寺丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1163562_comment'></div>充、章、雍，太常寺太祝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1163562_comment'></div>奇，秘书省正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1163562_comment'></div>公温而庄，宽而栗，尤乐易，喜谈笑，不为城府崖岸，善与人交，其度豁如也。<div class='inline'
