id='poem_sentence_147_1163562_comment'></div>薄于自奉，食罕重味，器服仅给而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1163562_comment'></div>嗜读书，老而不倦，虽在戎旅，未尝释卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1163562_comment'></div>而首公勤职，盖天资然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1163562_comment'></div>《易》著《乾》之四德曰：「贞者事之干」，「贞固足以干事」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1163562_comment'></div>「理财正辞，禁民为非曰义」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1163562_comment'></div>若贞与义，公实有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1163562_comment'></div>用是出处显重且五十年，忠劳在朝，功利在民，为当时伟人，重德盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1163562_comment'></div>仆康定中与公并命处谏垣，至和末，又代公为益部，以常同僚，而从公之游也旧，故知公之器蕴为详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1163562_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_156_1163562'>贞以干事，义以治民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1163562_comment'></div>施于有政，康穆其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1163562_comment'></div>文学发身，贡名第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1163562_comment'></div>惟其德业，诚心为质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1163562_comment'></div>升列谏垣，实陈昌言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1163562_comment'></div>法冠纠违，王体以尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1163562_comment'></div>遂服迩僚，式虔亮采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1163562_comment'></div>帝察其衷，于心简在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1163562_comment'></div>帝念戎难，内储蜀忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1163562_comment'></div>畴咨文武，属之怀柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1163562_comment'></div>公有常德，维邦之翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1163562_comment'></div>四方于宣，先登于岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1163562_comment'></div>西圉既平，西州既宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1163562_comment'></div>还跻二府，参斡机衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1163562_comment'></div>无有作好，无有比德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1163562_comment'></div>刚亦不吐，王道正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1163562_comment'></div>高奴古塞，实扼氐羌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1163562_comment'></div>镇守之重，咨公岩廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1163562_comment'></div>蠢尔夏戎，奸黩宪度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1163562_comment'></div>公厉御策，奔踶入驭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1163562_comment'></div>卒乘辑睦，壁橹缮完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1163562_comment'></div>拊循蒐阅，军气桓桓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1163562_comment'></div>议建民兵，法古农战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1163562_comment'></div>保大经久，忧深思远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1163562_comment'></div>关河晏然，以公在边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1163562_comment'></div>两朝眷赖，弗遑引年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1163562_comment'></div>公不敢康，将吏伤悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1163562_comment'></div>君恩见还，大星已殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1163562_comment'></div>元戎于征，麾纛启行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1163562_comment'></div>及归里门，翩翩素旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1163562_comment'></div>一气同生，大期共尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1163562_comment'></div>惟此德名，流徽不泯。</div><div id='poem_sentence_187_1163562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年9月</a>　九月，在京任翰林学士承旨，上疏论冗官之患。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年12月22日</a>　十二月二十二日，在京任翰林学士承旨，草立皇太子制。作品：立皇太子制。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《宋文鉴》卷三四及《宋大诏令集》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1163098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163098' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163098?labeling=true' target='_blank'>立皇太子制</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年十二月壬寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163098")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163098_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163098'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163098'>维我祖宗，继天统业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163098_comment'></div>积有功德，克享上帝之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163098_comment'></div>肆其子孙，永承百世之祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163098_comment'></div>朕祗纂谟烈，详览古今，繄崇建于元良，实保安于国本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163098_comment'></div>上尊宗庙，孝无大于奉先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163098_comment'></div>下庇生民，教莫逾于居正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163098_comment'></div>式宣显册，敷告万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163098_comment'></div>皇长子具官顼，英粹日跻，中和自至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163098_comment'></div>仁义充涵之美，言动惟时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163098_comment'></div>礼乐交错之华，威仪可象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163098_comment'></div>抑畏疏封之重，敏修典学之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163098_comment'></div>亦既多闻，足当大受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163098_comment'></div>是宜诞膺徽命，肇启储闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163098_comment'></div>懋升明两之辉，益广在三之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163098_comment'></div>非余私于尔顼，惟天祐于余家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163098_comment'></div>衍宝祚之灵长，成寰区之庆赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163098_comment'></div>往慎厥德，以答扬我列圣之光训，不曰休哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163098_comment'></div>可立为皇太子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163098_comment'></div>有司择日备礼册命施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1163098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　本年，在京任翰林学士承旨，荐举马默为监察御史里行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　本年，在京任翰林学士承旨，上疏论颍王赵顼官属事。作品：论王府官属事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1163201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论王府官属事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163201")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163201'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163201'>窃惟颍王地居嫡长，春秋鼎盛，方今稽古向学，修诚进德，若其左右前后有位之士所以朝夕纳诲，咨告法度，出入起居，罔有不钦，一有元良，万国以正，社稷之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163201_comment'></div>今慎简宫僚，进用时俊，岁年之间，即复迁易，于此假途，以升要近，乃令搢绅之列指为仕宦捷径，非所以资王之重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163201_comment'></div>愿留圣虑，申谕执政，王府记室，顾当兼用词翰之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163201_comment'></div>至于翊善，保傅之业也，宜于两省以上推择老成旧望、行安而节和者，得以久处其职，俾典领宫中之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163201_comment'></div>至于侍御仆从便僻侧媚、以非正之事云为者，察而闻于王，小者惩戒，大者上闻而斥之，无有憸人得在王门，以著王之令闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163201_comment'></div>兹国家无疆之休，惟陛下留神幸察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163201_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　本年，在京任翰林学士承旨，议宋祁谥号为“景文”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年1月11日</a>　正月十一日，在京任翰林学士承旨，受命议英宗谥号。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年闰3月8日</a>　闰三月八日，在京任翰林学士承旨，上《太庙祧僖祖议》作品：太庙祧僖祖议。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三四。系年据《宋会要辑稿》礼一五之三六。）</span><div id='poem_1163404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163404?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太庙祧僖祖议<span class='inlineComment2'>（治平四年闰三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年闰3月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163404")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163404'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163404'>臣等参议，伏以天子七庙，著于《尚书》、《春秋传》、《礼》之《王制》、《祭法》、《礼器》，诸子之说、历代之议详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163404_comment'></div>故昭穆所以序世及之正，褅祫所以极仁义之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163404_comment'></div>三代以降，惟汉、晋、唐以其统祚之长，得及祧迁之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163404_comment'></div>国家继天而王，列圣重光，盛德在人，必百世祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163404_comment'></div>厚陵复土，虞主还宫，对越祖宗，升祔有日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163404_comment'></div>同堂八室，庙制已定，僖祖当祧，合于旧典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163404_comment'></div>请依太常礼院所奏，委为允当。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163404_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年闰3月28日</a>　闰三月二十八日，在京任翰林学士承旨，上疏论国计。作品：论国计事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二四。系年据《续资治通鉴长编》卷二〇九。）</span><div id='poem_1163193' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163193' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163193?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论国计事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（治平四年闰三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年闰3月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163193")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163193'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163193'>臣切惟天之生民，以衣食为命，圣人因是而为之均节，立君臣贵贱等威之分，以止其争且乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163193_comment'></div>故礼也者，文饰此者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163193_comment'></div>刑也者，防禁此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163193_comment'></div>凡所谓赏罚法令，仁义廉耻，皆缘此而后立者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163193_comment'></div>衣食不足，何礼刑之有哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163193_comment'></div>内无以保其社稷，外无以制其夷狄，国非其国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163193_comment'></div>故货食者人事之确论，非高谈虚辞之可致者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163193_comment'></div>今京师砥平冲会之地，连营设卫，以当山河之险，则是国依兵而立，兵待货食而后可聚，此今天下之大势也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163193_comment'></div>臣在仁宗朝，庆历中充三司使，嘉祐初再领邦计，尝为朝廷精言此事，累有奏议，所陈利害安危之体，究其本原，冗兵最为大患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163193_comment'></div>略计中等禁军一卒岁给约五十千，十万人岁费五百万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163193_comment'></div>臣前在三司，勘会庆历五年禁军之数，比景祐以前增置八百六十馀指挥，四十馀万人，是增岁费二千万缗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163193_comment'></div>太祖皇帝制折杖法，免天下徒，初置壮城牢城，备诸役使，谓之厢军，后乃展转增创军额，今遂与禁军数目几等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163193_comment'></div>此其岁增衣粮几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163193_comment'></div>是皆出于民力，则天下安得不困？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163193_comment'></div>臣庆历五年取诸路盐酒商税岁课，比《景德会计录》皆增及三数倍以上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163193_comment'></div>景德中收商税四百五十馀万贯，庆历中一千九百七十五万馀贯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163193_comment'></div>景德中收酒课四百二十八万馀贯，庆历中收一千七百一十万馀贯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163193_comment'></div>景德中收盐税课三百五十五万馀贯，庆历中收七百一十五万馀贯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163193_comment'></div>但茶亦有增而不多尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163193_comment'></div>天下和买䌷绢，本以利民，初行于河北，但资本路军衣，遂通其法以及京东、淮南、江浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163193_comment'></div>景祐中诸路所买不及二百万疋，庆历中乃至三百万疋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163193_comment'></div>自尔时及今及二十年，但闻比较督责，不闻有所宽减也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163193_comment'></div>如此浚取，天下岂复有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1163193", 1163193, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>遗利</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163193_comment'></div>自古有国者，货利之入无若是之多，其费用亦无若是之广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163193_comment'></div>昔唐室自天宝之乱，肃、代之后，国力大窘，禁军乏饷，畿甸百姓至挼穗以供兵食，登都城门以望四方贡奉之至，可谓危蹙已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163193_comment'></div>然患难既平，则兵有时而解，兵解则民力纾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163193_comment'></div>今中外诸军坐而衣食，无有解期，天下困敝已如此，而上下恬然，不图云救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163193_comment'></div>宝元、康定中，夏戎阻命，西师在野，既聚军马，即须入中粮草，在京支还交钞银钱物帛，一岁约支一千万贯以上，三司无以计置，即须内帑供给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163193_comment'></div>庆历二年、三年，连年支拨内库银䌷绢，只此两次六百万疋两，三司以补不足，寻即支尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163193_comment'></div>西事已定，二纪于兹，中间亦不闻有所处置者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163193_comment'></div>邦家不幸，大变仍臻，颁赉之馀，府库虚匮，宿藏旧积，盖无馀几，万一因之以饥馑，加之以寇戎，臣恐智者难以善于后矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163193_comment'></div>夫茍且者臣下及身之谋，远虑者陛下国家之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163193_comment'></div>兹事体大，在陛下所忧，无先于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163193_comment'></div>财计之任，虽三司之职，日生烦务，常程计度，簿书期会，则在有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163193_comment'></div>至于议有系于军国之体，事有关于安危之机，其根本在于中书、枢密院，非有司可得预也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163193_comment'></div>今夫赋歛必降敕，支给必降宣，是祖宗规摹二府，共司邦计之出入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163193_comment'></div>今欲保大丰财，安民固本，当自中书、枢密院同心协力，修明真宗已前旧典，先由兵籍减省，以次举其为弊之大，若宗室之制、官人之法，诸生事造端非简便者，裁而正之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163193_comment'></div>至于微末细故，于国计盈虚不足为损益，属之有司可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163193_comment'></div>提其纲则众目张，澄其原则下流清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163193_comment'></div>《易》曰：「穷则变，变则通，通则久」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163193_comment'></div>又曰：「变而通之以尽利」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163193_comment'></div>《节》卦之辞曰：「节以制度，不伤财，不害民」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163193_comment'></div>故伤财害民之事，当为制度以节之尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163193_comment'></div>若但遵常守故，龊龊细文，避猜嫌，顾形迹，恤浮议而废远图，忽人谋而徼天幸，日月逝矣，岁不我与，后虽噬脐，何嗟及矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163193_comment'></div>臣服在近列，荷恩三朝，窃见时事日以迫急，不胜忧愤，辄罄狂瞽，惟陛下留神省察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1163193_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年4月3日</a>　四月三日，在京任翰林学士承旨，上《英宗谥议》作品：英宗谥议。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《宋大诏令集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_1163426' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163426' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163426?labeling=true' target='_blank'>英宗谥议</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163426")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163426_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163426'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163426'>臣闻惟天为大，在形器而已分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163426_comment'></div>惟君为尊，抑德名而后显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163426_comment'></div>皇坟帝典，玉板金函，勒鸿垂休，略见方策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163426_comment'></div>我宋受命，以祚神主，乃武乃文，克明克类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163426_comment'></div>故七世之庙，可以观德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163426_comment'></div>三灵之心，怀于有仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163426_comment'></div>保定之眷，永锡景祚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163426_comment'></div>淳耀之烈，爰集治平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163426_comment'></div>恭惟大行皇帝浚哲应期，泰清抚运，体乾元之刚健，涵阳精之光铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163426_comment'></div>粤初清明在躬，隐而未见，则惟尊德性而道问学，致广大而极渊微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163426_comment'></div>储思养正，而圣功内充；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163426_comment'></div>处谦自牧，而物情已服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163426_comment'></div>仁宗皇帝深烛天意，知人神之依，曰惟汝贤，授之宗器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163426_comment'></div>乃怀抑畏，坚避历年，不易乎世，无然歆羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163426_comment'></div>至诚达节，天下莫际其量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163426_comment'></div>《文言》曰：「确乎其不可拔，潜龙也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163426_comment'></div>历数讴谣，谅非人事，遂膺图箓，正位凝命，景至而冬夏应，气动而风云从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163426_comment'></div>震声而离明，巽齐而兑说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163426_comment'></div>既已保富有之业，席嘉靖之治，敕天之命，严恭励翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163426_comment'></div>率时昭考之道，祗奉慈仪之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163426_comment'></div>肇禋圜丘，诚志内尽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163426_comment'></div>登祼清庙，孝思惟则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163426_comment'></div>君道王体，大本举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163426_comment'></div>若乃励精庶政，收采群策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163426_comment'></div>朝以听决，至于中昃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163426_comment'></div>夕而访览，迨于乙夜，稽考典刑，综核名实，谨宪度，振纲律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163426_comment'></div>《中庸》所谓审问慎思，笃行固守，其自致也悉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163426_comment'></div>惟其体貌丞弼，优遇耆老，辨章才品，慎重名器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163426_comment'></div>虚怀以待俊德，前席以尽嘉言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163426_comment'></div>纳用不专于亲近，眷接无间于疏逖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163426_comment'></div>推择髦秀，以充册府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163426_comment'></div>增置学官，以训宗胄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163426_comment'></div>惟日孜孜，每怀靡及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163426_comment'></div>喜老氏之清净，则乐行其道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163426_comment'></div>贵大《易》之简易，而尝以为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163426_comment'></div>故无有作好，用敦乎俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163426_comment'></div>器服才具，玩好不设；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163426_comment'></div>未尝致意于观于逸，于游于田；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163426_comment'></div>宫室苑囿无所增饰，左右嫔御无一名号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163426_comment'></div>爵罔及于私昵，恩无假于近习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163426_comment'></div>夙戒戚里，微濯龙车马之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163426_comment'></div>裁省主第，无堂邑山林之侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163426_comment'></div>身先处厚，以示四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163426_comment'></div>此皆治古之盛事，哲主之懿铄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163426_comment'></div>得其一二，足以垂光载籍，宣昭义问，矧翕受敷施，广大悉备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163426_comment'></div>兹士民之所目见，天下之所共闻者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163426_comment'></div>至于宽仁温厚，煦然若春阳之布和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163426_comment'></div>庄毅明察，凛然若秋霜之肃物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163426_comment'></div>其稽古也，多识前言往行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163426_comment'></div>其御今也，有以极深研几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163426_comment'></div>而犹罢朝则敷经于外阁，退食则开帙于内殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163426_comment'></div>惇序宗属，抚怀戎狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163426_comment'></div>钦恤刑辟，蠲薄赋繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163426_comment'></div>惠养鳏独，赈恤乏绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163426_comment'></div>凡曰仁政，不忘寤寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163426_comment'></div>傥若日月得天而能久照，四时更化而能久成，于万斯年，永绥寿恺，则雄才大略足以弥纶于高厚，丰功远烈足以辉掩于往初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163426_comment'></div>以此积德，则三代不必企也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163426_comment'></div>以此立威，则四夷不足攘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163426_comment'></div>上仪壮观，遗风茂实，奇伟倜傥，竹帛不可殚纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163426_comment'></div>爰厌世之已早，遽乘云而上宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163426_comment'></div>植璧于坛，顾金縢之靡兆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163426_comment'></div>遗弓在地，怅龙驭之莫攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163426_comment'></div>因山已穹，同轨斯会，爰饬旧典，申诏近臣，参考历代之法，崇荐对天之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163426_comment'></div>谨按《谥法》，圣能法天曰宪，经天纬地曰文，刚德克就曰肃，保大定功曰武，重光奠丽曰宣，尊仁安义曰孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163426_comment'></div>若夫惟天聪明，惟圣攸法，惟臣钦率，惟民从乂，兹所以为宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163426_comment'></div>典常是师，俊民用章，乂用明，以化成天下，兹所以为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163426_comment'></div>以义制事，以礼制心，王道正直，罔失法度，兹所以为肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163426_comment'></div>董正治官，威怀并设，六服八表，靡不承德，兹所以为武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163426_comment'></div>丕显哉皇祖之谟，丕承哉三宗之烈，缉熙景训，垂裕后昆，兹所以为宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163426_comment'></div>持盈保成，夤恭戒惧，顾諟明命，克昌统业，兹所以为孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163426_comment'></div>孔子曰：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1163426", 1163426, "Clauses/203/Comments/1")'>大道</span>之行也，与三代之英，丘未之逮也，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1163426", 1163426, "Clauses/206/Comments/1")'>有志</span>焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163426_comment'></div>盖禹、汤、文、武，三代之英者，惟德有以当之，不在乎禹、汤、文、武专其美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1163426_comment'></div>是故继《韶》《夏》，建鸿名，必本诸事业，质诸公论，考诸先圣而不谬，垂之万世而不疑，则可以昭告于郊，锡命于帝，宗庙享之，子孙保之，言而可为天下信，著而可为后王法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1163426_comment'></div>盖《诗》、《书》所存，断自唐虞以下，所以发扬盛德，诏于无穷者用此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1163426_comment'></div>大行皇帝尊谥，宜天锡之曰宪文肃武宣孝皇帝，庙曰英宗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1163426_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年4月14日</a>　四月十四日，受命与司马光详定内外所上封事以闻。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年9月1日</a>　九月一日，在京任翰林学士承旨，作《华山重修云台观记》作品：华山重修云台观记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1163548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华山重修云台观记</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163548")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163548'>太华三方，古迹远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163548_comment'></div>上方白云宫，在岳顶，据苍龙岭，云昔羽人焦道广常居之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163548_comment'></div>中方太清宫，枕太罗峰，今犹有老君像；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163548_comment'></div>下方即此观，因云台山名焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163548_comment'></div>唐明皇天宝中，因旧基构栋宇，命右补阙、集贤学士卫包撰《修三方记》，见存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163548_comment'></div>五代乱离，三方荒毁，高士陈抟披荆榛，筑室于下方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163548_comment'></div>太平兴国中，太宗皇帝累赐诏，赍御诗召抟赴阙，乃敕有司增葺隐庐，复给内府金钱，经始坛殿，规摹方备，今观是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163548_comment'></div>庆历初，某领史官，尝阅国书，见抟本传云：抟字图南，亳州真源人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163548_comment'></div>始四五岁，戏涡水之滨，有青衣媪召至怀中乳之，自是聪悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163548_comment'></div>及长，读经史百家之言，一见成诵，无复遗忘，尤工诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163548_comment'></div>后唐长兴中，举进士不第，遂不仕，肆意山水间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163548_comment'></div>自言尝遇孙君仿、獐皮处士二人者，语之曰：「武当山九室岩可以隐居」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163548_comment'></div>因往栖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163548_comment'></div>服气辟谷二十馀年，徙居云台，又止少华石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163548_comment'></div>每寝辄百馀日不兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163548_comment'></div>周世宗显德三年，召留禁中月馀，因问以黄冶之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163548_comment'></div>对曰：「陛下为四海之主，当以政治为念，奈何留意此小道」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163548_comment'></div>世宗不以为忤，命为谏义大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163548_comment'></div>固辞不受而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163548_comment'></div>诏本州长吏岁时存问，间因牧守西行过山下致赐物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163548_comment'></div>兴国初，始赴召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163548_comment'></div>九年，复来朝，上尤加礼重，谓宰相宋琪等曰：「抟方外之士，在华山已四十馀载，度其年盖百馀岁，语论甚高」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163548_comment'></div>因遣中使送至中书，琪等从容问曰：「先生得玄默修养之道，可以教人乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163548_comment'></div>对曰：「抟不知吐纳养生之理，神仙黄白之事，非有方术可传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163548_comment'></div>假令白日冲天，亦何益于世？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163548_comment'></div>圣上博达古今，深究治乱，真有道仁明之主，正是君臣同德，致理之秋，勤行修鍊，无出于此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163548_comment'></div>琪等皆称善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163548_comment'></div>以其语白上，上益重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163548_comment'></div>下诏曰：「华山隐士陈抟，晦迹丘樊，栖心岩穴，跌宕世表，涵味道腴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163548_comment'></div>往在周朝，物色幽遁，尝蒙鹄板之召，终遂鸿冥之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163548_comment'></div>自尔以来，多历年所，今复言迂高迹，来仪帝庭，不有嘉名，何彰清范？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163548_comment'></div>可赐号希夷先生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163548_comment'></div>上屡与之属和诗什。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163548_comment'></div>久之还山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163548_comment'></div>端拱初，忽谓弟子贾得升曰：「汝可于张超谷凿石为室，吾将憩焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163548_comment'></div>二年秋，石室成，手书数百言为表，其略曰：「臣抟大数有终，圣朝难恋，已于今月二十二日化形于莲华峰下张超谷中」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163548_comment'></div>如期而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163548_comment'></div>经七日支体犹温，有五色云蔽洞口，弥月不散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163548_comment'></div>抟好读《易》，手不释卷，自号扶摇子，著《指玄篇》八十一章，言导养及还丹之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163548_comment'></div>旧相王溥亦著八十一章，以笺其旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163548_comment'></div>又有《三峰寓言》及《高阳集》、《钓潭集》，诗六百馀首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163548_comment'></div>能逆知人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163548_comment'></div>斋中有大瓢挂壁上，道士贾休复心欲之而不言，抟谓休复曰：「子来非有他，盖欲吾瓢尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163548_comment'></div>呼侍者取而与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163548_comment'></div>有郭沆者，少居华阴，夜宿观下，抟中夜呼令趣归，沆未决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163548_comment'></div>复谓之曰：「可勿归矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163548_comment'></div>明日沆还家，果中夜母暴得心痛，几不济，食顷而愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163548_comment'></div>华阳隐士李琪，自言唐开元中郎官，人罕有见者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163548_comment'></div>关中逸人吕洞宾，有剑术，虽数百里顷刻辄至，以为神仙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163548_comment'></div>皆数至抟斋馆，与之酬唱如交友，时人异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163548_comment'></div>此皆旧史之文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163548_comment'></div>仁宗皇祐三年，云台观道士武元亨进《希夷先生传》，所载尤详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163548_comment'></div>云：初，先生居下方，茅茨不剪，蒿芜不除，有访先生者，窥其户，阒焉无人，但鸟声兽迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163548_comment'></div>或樵子山麓荐莽深处，有骸如腊，尘荄翳焉，迫而视之，乃先生也，扪其心独暖，良久，气还而兴曰：「睡适酣，奚为扰我」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163548_comment'></div>州将以闻周世宗，故召见，既不受官，赐号「白云先生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163548_comment'></div>故太皇御诗云：「曾向前朝出白云，后来消息杳无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163548_comment'></div>如今若肯随徵诏，总把三峰乞与君」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163548_comment'></div>既对于延英殿，华阳巾、垂绦、蹑屩，用宾礼见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163548_comment'></div>上欲征河东，先生请姑待，军已兴，不克下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163548_comment'></div>其再对也，言「天下一统矣」，果执刘继元，平并州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163548_comment'></div>密陈天命实在章圣，其所启沃，幽赞远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163548_comment'></div>太皇亦欲以为谏议大夫，先生恳辞，命遂不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163548_comment'></div>委化之年，盖百一十有八岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163548_comment'></div>自馀先几逆数，知来藏往，精微深妙，殆不可测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163548_comment'></div>至诸奇诡眩耀之事，则未尝为也，故先王之道浩然，莫得而揭厉之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163548_comment'></div>无贤愚贵贱，莫不闻其风而悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163548_comment'></div>大中祥符四年，真宗祀汾脽，驻跸华阴，再幸云台，阅先生遗像，伫立凝思久之，命除其观田租，召对道士武子华等，赐紫服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163548_comment'></div>舆驾还京，俾就御座所建本命元辰殿，内珰护作，绘睟容于北壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1163548_comment'></div>皇祐二年，构神御殿，严奉之礼始备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1163548_comment'></div>自先生去世，门人贾得升、武子华、元亨相承主持观事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1163548_comment'></div>至是殿成，元亨诣阙谢恩，仁宗令进歌诗，元亨应诏进三篇，帝属以御诗，又神笔飞白「清净」字赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1163548_comment'></div>元亨遂重修七殿，至于道院、斋堂，必葺一新，经营累年，为力勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1163548_comment'></div>某往来秦蜀，恭谒神御，既而瞻礼希夷堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1163548_comment'></div>惟神仙之云者，盖神本无方，道无不在，神也者，妙万物而为言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1163548_comment'></div>惟神也，故不疾而速，不行而至，漠然与合，兹谓至人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1163548_comment'></div>由是而后，可以出死生而通变化，虽非积学而至，非学则未知或至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1163548_comment'></div>夫九室、下方，岂徒与麋鹿为群，木石为伍而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1163548_comment'></div>治平四年九月一日记<span class='inlineComment2'>（《乐全集》卷三三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1163548_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_1163548'>先王：疑当作「先生」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1163548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年9月26日</a>　九月二十六日，与赵抃并除参知政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年9月</a>　九月，在京任参知政事，反对曾公亮欲用王安石为御史中丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年10月5日</a>　十月五日，在京任参知政事，父张尧卿卒。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='de75b9d6b32442eabeaf94a7c9771389_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("de75b9d6b32442eabeaf94a7c9771389");'><span id='de75b9d6b32442eabeaf94a7c9771389_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>，64岁</div><div id='de75b9d6b32442eabeaf94a7c9771389' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年1月</a>　正月，服除，授观文殿学士、知河南府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年1月26日</a>　正月二十六日，在京，由知河南府改判尚书都省兼提举集禧观，因与王安石不合，力辞，遂知陈州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年1月</a>　正月，在京陛辞神宗，上疏论变法之害。作品：论变更旧制事奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1163209' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163209' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163209?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论变更旧制事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁三年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163209")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163209_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163209'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163209'>臣蒙恩朝对，今已奉辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163209_comment'></div>窃惟孤陋之质，尚偶圣神之会，上膺眷遇，有异等伦，今承特诏而来，安敢缄默而去？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163209_comment'></div>辄献愚忠，上裨天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163209_comment'></div>臣闻人心惟危，患生所忽，动危甚易，安之实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163209_comment'></div>禁卫六军，边防三路，抚御之法，善制具存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163209_comment'></div>民心戎事，国之大本，动静之机，安危所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163209_comment'></div>若民心危摇，戎事兴动，策虑一失，绥辑非易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163209_comment'></div>祖宗谟烈，国家大计，甚所慎重，惟此二者不同小事，随宜改易，纵有利害，容得更张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163209_comment'></div>民犹水也，可以载舟，亦可以覆舟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163209_comment'></div>兵犹火也，可以焚物，亦可以自焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163209_comment'></div>焚溺之害，当在几之先见，造形而悟，已是后时，害成乃悔，何嗟及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163209_comment'></div>夫人臣之分，出处是常，家国大业，天下重器，譬之辎重，岂可轻离？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163209_comment'></div>愿陛下思所以置器于安，审所以藏身之固，广聪听于符同之外，采公议于得失之前，深察军民之情，厚为社稷之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163209_comment'></div>使人安其业，上下无怨，溥天之下，欣戴盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163209_comment'></div>高拱岩廊之上，保此泰山之安，朝廷尊而国体平，顺气应而嘉生遂，不亦休哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163209_comment'></div>臣疏外狂瞽，不识忌讳，以此愚言上答恩眷，退就诛殛，实所甘心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163209_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年1月</a>　正月，在京除知陈州，辟苏辙为陈州教授。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b9e237491a09447c8ef3c5d993ff25e9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b9e237491a09447c8ef3c5d993ff25e9");'><span id='b9e237491a09447c8ef3c5d993ff25e9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1075')">1074-1075年</a>，68-69岁</div><div id='b9e237491a09447c8ef3c5d993ff25e9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年12月4日</a>　十二月四日，入觐神宗，除宣徽北院使、判应天府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年12月11日</a>　十二月十一日，在京，由判应天府改知青州，告免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年12月</a>　十二月，在京于延和殿与神宗论御敌之策。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年1月23日</a>　正月二十三日，归宣徽院供职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年1月</a>　正月，在京任宣徽北院使，上疏论手实法。作品：论手实状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1163243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论手实状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163243")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163243'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163243'>臣窃闻昨有新制，开列条目，自府畿至诸路郡县令人户各自供通财产手实状，有所隐漏者，许人陈告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163243_comment'></div>近已施行，公私劳敝，乡闾甚扰，但忧增益赋调，不复更事生业，必有奸猾渐相告讦，窥图赏利，狱讼繁兴，政令寖以滋章，民德何以归厚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163243_comment'></div>况中户以下，鲜有盖藏，田蚕所收，岁有厚薄，户等耗登，何常之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163243_comment'></div>不惟扇惑人情，更有纷乱新法，以建议者内为之主，故当职者人无敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163243_comment'></div>向者朝廷所立法制，盖以便民为本，因成富国之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163243_comment'></div>今兹一事，专用挠人，徒搔挐于天下，实无济于国家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163243_comment'></div>伏望圣明博行体问，忠于国者必言其无益，虑于民者当明其非便，忧深思远，早垂止罢，令亿兆欣戴天恩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年4月21日</a>　四月二十一日，在京任宣徽北院使，除中太一宫使，上劄子辞免。作品：辞免中太一宫使劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163321' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163321' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163321?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免中太一宫使劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年4月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163321")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163321_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163321'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163321'>臣承閤门告报，已降敕命，差充中太一宫使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163321_comment'></div>臣近以奉朝请备位，而无所事，故乞一郡，以安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163321_comment'></div>伏蒙圣慈更加重职，愧尸素而有请，被恩典而愈优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163321_comment'></div>虚冒宠光，无施报称，切自省循，岂遑宁处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163321_comment'></div>所降敕命，不敢祗受，伏望据前所陈，乞特赐施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1163321_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年4月</a>　四月，在京任宣徽北院使，上表谢除中太一宫使。作品：谢除中太一宫使表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163322' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163322' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163322?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除中太一宫使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163322")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163322_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163322'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163322'>伏奉敕命差充中太一宫使，已赴本宫管勾讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163322_comment'></div>十精天之贵神，肇开靖馆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163322_comment'></div>五镇国之命祀，旧启灵祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163322_comment'></div>崇奉式严，典司为重，谬充使职，上出宸恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163322_comment'></div>伏念臣仕适逢时，材非济务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163322_comment'></div>智用同乎绠短，不可以汲深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163322_comment'></div>切实譬之拔扬，无得而成大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163322_comment'></div>昨领别都之钥，许觐中天之廷，祗荷明恩，俾升近缀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163322_comment'></div>既久陪于朝著，辄干请于郡章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163322_comment'></div>复膺温检之荣，兼领殊庭之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163322_comment'></div>披诚封奏，申锡诏音，嘉命是承，危悰增惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163322_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下惠深涵养，仁浃施生，猥加体貌之隆，奚取典刑之旧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163322_comment'></div>衰癃之质，极蒲柳之望秋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163322_comment'></div>云补之心，犹萤烛之向日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163322_comment'></div>念言谢事，近在踰年，敢希止足之风，庶免婆娑之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163322_comment'></div>实惟素志，敢昧大明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163322_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年4月</a>　四月，在京任宣徽北院使，又上劄子辞免中太一宫使。作品：免中太一宫使乞外任劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163323' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163323' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163323?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免中太一宫使乞外任劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163323")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163323_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163323'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163323'>臣窃惟人臣立朝，出处固有常分，茍失其节，必贻悔咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163323_comment'></div>人君之所以厚遇其下，非但优之以禄位而已，亦在察其志之所存，使处得其所，斯可以为厚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163323_comment'></div>臣早际圣明，特蒙察举，采诸群议之外，擢于执政之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163323_comment'></div>罢而外补，优以閒曹，甫及二年，复除便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163323_comment'></div>每垂记录，皆出渊衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163323_comment'></div>昨自陈州就移应天府，自念衰晚，前迫引年，若便道以之官，望清光而无日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163323_comment'></div>故因过阙，请来朝见，止一谢以眷怀，敢切希于宠利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163323_comment'></div>本期旬浃，即望辞行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163323_comment'></div>陛下特轸慈衷，俯矜旧物，发于中旨，处之近司，曲示敦留，俾奉朝请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163323_comment'></div>日趋严陛，俄仅半年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163323_comment'></div>昨逢诞庆之辰，已毕奉觞之礼，故求一郡，冀安素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163323_comment'></div>今蒙圣恩，更加宫使，名秩增重，优幸尤多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163323_comment'></div>今陛下厉精庶政，自朝至于日中昃，不遑暇食，中外事无大小，靡不经于神虑，观游娱宴，未尝留情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163323_comment'></div>辅臣百司，莫不夙夜，岂容浮冗独无所事于其间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163323_comment'></div>以一介孤远之踪，席贵戚恩泽之地，取讥清议，上累公朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163323_comment'></div>是敢虔沥恳诚，仰尘聪听，欲祈近南京一郡，退养衰疲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163323_comment'></div>则是宸造曲成，慈眷尤厚，始终保全，实繄洪覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163323_comment'></div>冒渎天威，仰祈察允。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1163323_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年闰4月12日</a>　闰四月十二日，在京任宣徽北院使，除知永兴军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年闰4月</a>　闰四月，在京任宣徽北院使，上劄子辞免判永兴军，诏依旧供职。作品：辞免判永兴军劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免判永兴军劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年闰4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163324")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163324_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163324'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163324'>臣自忝近司，奉朝供职，日趋严陛，俄仅半年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163324_comment'></div>昨逢诞庆之辰，已毕奉觞之礼，故求补外，退安素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163324_comment'></div>数倾情恳，未奉俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163324_comment'></div>今承差知永兴军，须至复有干黩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163324_comment'></div>伏以永兴大藩，寄委为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163324_comment'></div>但臣行将七十，筋力殚疲，目昏耳鸣，精神内竭，比及谢事，才馀半年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163324_comment'></div>今去乡闾程途颇远，虚烦吏民迎新送故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163324_comment'></div>伏冀圣慈检会臣前奏，乞改京东一郡，顾兹衰暮，得近松楸，致仕之日，归田为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163324_comment'></div>敢冀慈衷垂悯，宸造曲成，保全之恩，终始大幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163324_comment'></div>上冒天威，仰祈察允。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1163324_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年闰4月</a>　闰四月，在京任宣徽北院使，因王安石、吕惠卿之阻，未能出任枢密使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　夏、秋间，在京任宣徽北院使，上劄子乞外任。作品：陈乞外任劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163325' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163325' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163325?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈乞外任劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163325")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163325'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163325'>臣早遇圣明，特承眷奖，昨因朝觐，处之近职，仰依洪覆，实为优幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163325_comment'></div>然臣年齿迟暮，志气衰索，资本疏拙，无所取材，处则莫施补报之勤，出则不堪烦重之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163325_comment'></div>而一介之守，粗安常分，上不敢为诡洁之操，下不敢为贪冒之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163325_comment'></div>故求徐、兖一郡，所冀渐就田庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163325_comment'></div>荐沥恳诚，未蒙察允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163325_comment'></div>伏望天慈俯矜愚朴，特推保息之仁，获遂首丘之愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163325_comment'></div>干黩聪听，臣无任哀祈激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163325_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　夏、秋间，在京任宣徽北院使，再上劄子乞外任。作品：再陈乞外任劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1163326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再陈乞外任劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163326")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163326'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163326'>臣陈乞外任，方在私第俟命，伏蒙圣恩宣召，令奉朝供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163326_comment'></div>臣不避严诛，须至再陈诚恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163326_comment'></div>念臣齿发迟暮，志气衰索，累求一郡，退安拙守，干黩天听，未蒙委照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163326_comment'></div>虽进退之礼，慈衷曲示于眷怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163326_comment'></div>而出处之方，愚臣宜有以自处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163326_comment'></div>伏望圣明俯加矜察，特允前乞，以毕私幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163326_comment'></div>臣无任祈天俟命战越激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1163326_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年10月4日</a>　十月四日，在京任宣徽北院使，除宣徽南院使、检校太傅，出判应天府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年10月</a>　十月，在京，将赴知应天府任，上疏论新法之害。作品：论新法奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1163250' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163250' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163250?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论新法奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163250")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163250_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163250'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163250'>臣蒙恩在朝备员，经岁无施补益，每为深愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163250_comment'></div>今被命守藩，旦夕出国门，适值陛下以垂象之变，降御札，发德音，敕宰司率在廷之臣直言过失，改修政事之未协于民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163250_comment'></div>当陛下忧劳之际，老臣不为陛下开一言，则忠义之语无复至于天听，上负知眷，殁有馀责，敢以闻见，少报重恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163250_comment'></div>臣闻天尊地卑，而君臣之分定；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163250_comment'></div>君君臣臣，而后国体正，天下安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163250_comment'></div>故惟辟作福，惟辟作威，臣无有作福作威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163250_comment'></div>臣而有作福作威，其害于而家，凶于而国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163250_comment'></div>盖为国之体犹权衡，势不可使有所偏重，偏重之势，必成倾覆，历代成败，何不由此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163250_comment'></div>伏自近岁以来，灾异之作，率由阴侵于阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163250_comment'></div>陛下天纵聪明，前言往事无不洞鉴，不待臣说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163250_comment'></div>今圣心所以答天戒，责躬变礼，可谓精诚之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163250_comment'></div>谓天盖高，其听孔卑，故不旋日而星变以隐，感通昭答，足以明皇天眷祐我有宋之意至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163250_comment'></div>陛下应之以实，固当践所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163250_comment'></div>今夫政事之未协于民者固有之矣，大抵新法行已六年，事之利害非一二可悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163250_comment'></div>就中役法一事，为天下害实深，累经更变，竟无长策可以定其法，议论日以纷扰，公私日以劳敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163250_comment'></div>夫人为天地之心，天地之变，人心实为之，故和气不应，灾害荐作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163250_comment'></div>盖下令如流水之原，取其顺流之易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163250_comment'></div>经六年而事功莫效，故其事必有未协于民者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163250_comment'></div>法既未协，事资必改，若犹惮改，人将不堪，忧患一成，噬脐安及？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163250_comment'></div>陛下承六世之业，上有二宫，国家大事，愿陛下忧深而思远，宁忍于人情，不可忍于社稷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163250_comment'></div>忧患既成，人臣各有去就之分，家国之忧独在，圣人所以终日不离其轻重，谓此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163250_comment'></div>此臣所以为陛下痛心疾首，一夕而九兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163250_comment'></div>况今习俗奔竞，偷敝成风，交党相倾，势利相轧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163250_comment'></div>攻讦起于庙堂，辩讼兴于台阁，非所以昭圣化也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163250_comment'></div>毁誉移于好恶，赏罪偏于爱憎，非所以正王度也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163250_comment'></div>士大夫习尚如此，有为国家死节仗义，临艰虞而不易其操者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163250_comment'></div>昔尧、舜之为君，选于众，举十六官，而与皋、夔、稷、契共治天下，犹且明四目，达四聪，而后能协和万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163250_comment'></div>虽大圣贤，未有一人之心力而可以成天下之务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163250_comment'></div>陛下临御九年，中外臣庶皆在照临之下，其间必有知忠义、不二心之臣简在圣衷者矣，愿陛下召之左右，从容访逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163250_comment'></div>譬之金石，叩之则鸣，人各有心，激之则发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163250_comment'></div>吉人之辞寡，吉人讷于言，外若不足，其中诚也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163250_comment'></div>利口捷给，外若有馀，其中伪也，惟圣鉴精察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163250_comment'></div>若夫导之以言而不能尽者，使陈之简牍，必有所效者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163250_comment'></div>前代明君莫不以是考于下，故能广视听于扶同之外，究得失于几微之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163250_comment'></div>揽其权纲，执其柄鐏，虑所以藏身之固，思所以置器于安，此惟独决于神断而后可，非所以谋于人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163250_comment'></div>夫事有失于前者，不可不悔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163250_comment'></div>患有在于后者，不可不惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163250_comment'></div>如救焚溺，势不可缓，缓则无及于救矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163250_comment'></div>鱼不可脱于渊，国之利器不可以假人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163250_comment'></div>涓涓可以溃堤，荧荧至于燎原，衅端厉阶，不可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163250_comment'></div>臣之心惟愿国家之善政美事，陛下之盛德鸿烈，高越百王之上，流光万世之下，天之福祥休嘉之象生，而咎證之象不生，民之愁叹怨嗟之声不作，而颂声作，使兆民乐事劝功，尊君亲上，欣戴安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163250_comment'></div>臣退就田里，以至瞑目泉下，犹知怀此幸愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163250_comment'></div>老臣无状，为陛下虑不敢不精，为陛下言不敢不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163250_comment'></div>亦惟陛下察此至诚，俯垂省纳，实天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163250_comment'></div>候进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1163250_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
淮阳（宛丘）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2e49ef6b21fe49e8b412c6a82de392cc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2e49ef6b21fe49e8b412c6a82de392cc");'><span id='2e49ef6b21fe49e8b412c6a82de392cc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>，23岁</div><div id='2e49ef6b21fe49e8b412c6a82de392cc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　本年，与赵参邂逅于陈州，作序送之。作品：送赵参序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三四。）</span><div id='poem_1163460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送赵参序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163460")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163460'>圣上始亲录乡老之书，仆与晋人赵生参俱见遗于春宗伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163460_comment'></div>别去二年，居无何，邂逅于太昊氏之墟，喜而饮诸市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163460_comment'></div>酒酣，赵子击觥叹曰：「嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163460_comment'></div>使我独不当从衡时，得凭轼结靷驰乎秦、晋之郊，取卿相犹拾地芥尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163460_comment'></div>如在孔门，吾庶几子贡言语之科」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163460_comment'></div>于是仆请赵子持觞，为酌满，以让之曰：「赵子且默无躁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163460_comment'></div>夫为国者，孰不幸安而昌？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163460_comment'></div>孰不不幸危且亡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163460_comment'></div>居是邦也，既不忍其人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163460_comment'></div>于他邦也，则使其人皆无罪而就死地，君子兼济之心何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163460_comment'></div>若赐也，为鲁一出，矛楯四国，助田常无君之心，不可谓之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163460_comment'></div>劝吴出兵，教越袭其不备，不可言乎信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163460_comment'></div>致齐之民为吴之鱼肉，不可称夫仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163460_comment'></div>欲善晋而使亲鲁，则又诱吴之疲兵以成其伪，不可语诸义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163460_comment'></div>是则子贡一出，而忠、信、仁、义索焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163460_comment'></div>顾独存一区区之鲁，虽曰坟墓之托，不可不救，于道不宏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163460_comment'></div>赵子，君子藏器于身，与时消息，子前言过矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163460_comment'></div>于是赵子喜其异闻也，捧觞毕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163460_comment'></div>翌日，仆遂征淮西，赵子西走辇下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163460_comment'></div>逆旅萧索，秋风向高，挥袂拂鞭，各随蓬转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163460_comment'></div>思永交好，褚无琼玖，故寻醉论，书以识行，且以规赵子，使重其言也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1163460_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9f8f2bf6e0a949a68baf236527899bfa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9f8f2bf6e0a949a68baf236527899bfa");'><span id='9f8f2bf6e0a949a68baf236527899bfa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1071')">1070-1071年</a>，64-65岁</div><div id='9f8f2bf6e0a949a68baf236527899bfa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年2月</a>　二月，赴知陈州任途中得疾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年6月</a>　六月，在知陈州任，荐举苏轼、李大临为谏官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年1月15日</a>　正月望日，在知陈州任，为释拱辰所作《禅源通录》作序。作品：禅源通录序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1163465' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163465' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163465?labeling=true' target='_blank'>禅源通录序<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163465")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163465_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163465'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163465'>《楞伽阿跋多罗宝经》乃先佛所说第一真实妙义，故谓之佛语心品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163465_comment'></div>祖师达磨以付二祖，曰：「吾观震旦所有经教，惟此《楞枷》四卷可以印心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163465_comment'></div>祖祖相付，传为心要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163465_comment'></div>后至东山，以为《楞伽》义理深微，非浅智粗心所能窥测，故每用《金刚般若经》开示众等，令其易解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163465_comment'></div>逮于曹溪，以大慈悲一音演说，对答偈句，揭如日月，其所开导，直指本心，未尝离《楞伽》自證智觉之大旨也，由是领悟者多，法周沙界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163465_comment'></div>初，二祖常言此经四世之后变成名相，深可悲哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163465_comment'></div>自衣止不传，诸方分化，地殊南北，名标顿渐，参学之流各相祖述，道场相望，源流寖广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163465_comment'></div>去圣逾远，时风益薄，堪任大事，根器诚难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163465_comment'></div>然轻重不可欺于权衡，方圆不能出于规矩，但兔角龟毛，泥牛木马，务为深隐，巧愈弥甚，名相之言，谅非虚示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163465_comment'></div>初，六祖教诸门人说法，必令先定宗旨，虽以三科起用，究竟二法尽除，故知一问一答，岂茍而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163465_comment'></div>若其具无碍辩才，入净圆三昧，随其语默，佛法现前，缘与信合，事实稀有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163465_comment'></div>故黄檗禅师每谓众曰：「江西会下唱道之师八十馀席，得大寂、正眼三两人尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163465_comment'></div>则知为世度门，传佛法印，大善知识，岂易偶哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163465_comment'></div>自宾钵罗窟诸圣贤众相结集《多罗》等藏，其纪述之来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163465_comment'></div>至于中华，则有萧梁《续法》、元魏《付法藏传》，以至于唐，《宝林》、《心要》、《祖堂》等集，国朝《传灯录》，时代师承，本末详备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163465_comment'></div>近吴兴有具寿僧拱辰，道意纯熟，禅寂为乐，再启法筵，寻复舍众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163465_comment'></div>虽不显谈说而示人闻修之法，虽无所作受而为众利益之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163465_comment'></div>故阅上以来诸传集录，正其差讹，揽其精要，推明统本，总括横枝，若网在纲，条目不紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163465_comment'></div>依于义，不依语，依于法，不依人，不离文字，示解脱相，彻照今古，乃无尽灯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163465_comment'></div>又续法眼之后至治平之末达磨法嗣通十有九世，凡二十四卷，题曰《禅源通录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163465_comment'></div>时熙宁四年正月望日，乐全居士安道序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1163465_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年5月</a>　五月，在知陈州任，上疏论监司官多起刑狱。作品：陈州奏监司官多起刑狱。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二五。《宋朝诸臣奏议》卷九九系此文于熙宁五年五月，此时张方平已判南京御史台，故改系于熙宁四年五月。）</span><div id='poem_1163231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163231?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈州奏监司官多起刑狱<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁五年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163231")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163231_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163231'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163231'>臣伏以国朝自祖宗以至陛下，积德累仁，慎用刑辟，急深故之罪，宽纵出之罚，爱育下民，若保赤子，致其忠爱，可谓至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163231_comment'></div>近年监司之官，在所多起刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163231_comment'></div>至于州郡常程公事方行推问，未见情实，或已经检断，事理明白，于法平允，偶其所见爱恶异同，即别差官置司推覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163231_comment'></div>事本微小，张皇为大，因缘骚扰，株连枝蔓，至有往还数千里勾追證佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163231_comment'></div>盛暑严冬，淹留牢禁，其中甚有罪犯绝轻，亦有无罪之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163231_comment'></div>一身久系，家为破散，瘐病饥寒，愁痛无告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163231_comment'></div>及其结正，亦有不移前案者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163231_comment'></div>推勘官承望其意，巧文锻鍊，虽是平人，亦须以虚妄为坐，以一州一路为率，至于天下，衔冤抱枉，感伤和气，灾害用生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163231_comment'></div>狱者，人命所系，王者所当深慎者也，岂容官吏依势作威！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163231_comment'></div>事既自外专行，朝廷亦无由知得，臣到陈州，方此亲见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163231_comment'></div>自二月末赴本任，至四月中，所司呈公事一件，称有兵士指论冒请粮米事，系是去年十二月状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163231_comment'></div>自后行遣会问，回报始足，遂于四月十二日送司理院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163231_comment'></div>方行取勘，文案未具，当月十九日有转运判官张次山到州检点，取索一宗状词，将带前去，寻别差官置院推勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163231_comment'></div>四月末所差官到院，至九月初方始结绝，历一百二十馀日，前后所经禁系近六十人，往还三千馀里勾追照證，炎暑之月系累道路，自夏涉秋，其间病患相继，亦有军员枉遭刑禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163231_comment'></div>及至断遣，并止杖罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163231_comment'></div>推院缴送到所取款状二千一百三十一纸，净案六百七十张，诸杂行遣照證文字三十五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163231_comment'></div>当时若自本州勘结，不过十馀日可了，其滋章为弊如此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163231_comment'></div>今又有百姓樊宗望公事，已经本州奏断，近转运副使李南公到州点检，取索上件公案将带前去，又已差官令置院推勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163231_comment'></div>臣窃详樊宗望公事，本州勘结颇已详允，具案闻奏，法寺定断，寻已准朝旨断放讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163231_comment'></div>窃虑差官前来置院，依前追扰淹延，贫细之民饥寒失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163231_comment'></div>欲乞特下法寺取索上件公案看详，委有情节不圆，刑名差误，即乞别差官依公取勘施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163231_comment'></div>缘此置狱之弊，事干天下，伏乞朝廷特降约束，诸路非奉朝旨所置推院，令推勘官候结案日，具录监司所送公事因由，据到院出院月日，但系勾追禁系人数于在禁日有无病患、死亡，所追干系人州县程途近远，及断放刑名，开坐申中书，送御史台或法寺看详事状，其有不当，置院推鞫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163231_comment'></div>或淹延枝蔓，枉系无罪之人，诸有非理，伏乞议立条制颁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163231_comment'></div>所冀上合圣朝慎用刑辟之意，感召和气，以正治体<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163231_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1163231'>年月原无，据《宋名臣奏议》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1163231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163231'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1163231_0'>⑴ 《乐全集》卷二五。又见《宋名臣奏议》卷九九，《历代名臣奏议》卷二一六。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163231_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年7月</a>　七月，在知陈州任，有《读杜工部诗》作品：读杜工部诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_495399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读杜工部诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495399")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495399'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495399'>文物皇唐盛，诗家老杜豪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495399'>雅音还正始，感兴出离骚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495399'>运海张鹏翅，追风骋骥髦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495399'>三春上休苑，八月浙江涛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495399'>璀璨开鲛室，幽深闭虎牢。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495399'>金晶神鼎重，玉气霁虹高。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495399'>甲马腾千队，戈船下万艘。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495399'>吴钩铦莫触，羿彀巧无逃。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495399'>远意随孤鸟，雄筋举六鳌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495399'>曲严周庙肃，颂美孔图褒。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495399'>世乱多群盗，天遥隔九皋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495399'>途穷伤白发，行在窘青袍。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495399'>忧国论时事，司功去谏曹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495399'>七哀同谷寓，一曲锦川遨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495399'>妻子饥寒累，朝廷战伐劳。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495399'>倦游徒右席，乐善伐干旄。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495399'>旧里归无路，危城至辄遭。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495399'>行吟非楚泽，达观念庄濠。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495399'>逸思乘秋水，愁肠困浊醪。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495399'>耒阳三尺土，谁为剪蓬蒿。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495399'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_495399_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年7月</a>　七月，在知陈州任，有诗送苏轼。作品：送苏学士钱唐监郡。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷一。王智勇系此诗于元祐四年五月，兹不从。）</span><div id='poem_495355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送苏学士钱塘监郡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495355")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495355'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495355'>趣时贵近君独远，此情于世何所希。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495355'>车马尘中久已倦，湖山胜处即为归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495355'>洞庭霜天柑橘熟，松江秋水鲈鱼肥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495355'>地邻沧海莫东望，且作阮公离是非。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495355'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495355_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年8月26日</a>　八月二十六日，由知陈州改判南京御史台。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='da6845568eae449f92cb0c7d548a4138_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("da6845568eae449f92cb0c7d548a4138");'><span id='da6845568eae449f92cb0c7d548a4138_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>，68岁</div><div id='da6845568eae449f92cb0c7d548a4138' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年9月13日</a>　九月十三日，在知陈州任，为陈州赵犨祠堂作记。作品：唐太尉赵公祠堂记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1163550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163550' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163550?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐太尉赵公祠堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年9月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163550")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163550_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163550'>唐有天下三百年，其间大盗三发，明皇天宝末，安禄山反范阳，长驱陷两都，河北、河南、关辅罹其祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163550_comment'></div>德宗建中末，朱泚乘泾师仓卒之变，以构凶逆，兵不出畿甸，寻败亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163550_comment'></div>僖宗乾符初，草寇王仙芝、黄巢、秦宗权相踵作乱，流毒乃遍天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163550_comment'></div>起曹濮，袭荆汉，破江淮，残闽岭，东极海岱，北越河，遂荡覆京邑，剽岐陇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163550_comment'></div>所至无噍类，城府为丘墟，榛莽千里，烟火断绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163550_comment'></div>粮食既尽，啖人以饱，列巨碓数百，纳人臼中，糜肉而食，名为舂磨砦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163550_comment'></div>军行则盐尸以从，指乡聚曰：「尚有人焉，吾众何患饥也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163550_comment'></div>惴惴遗黎，靡所寄命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163550_comment'></div>于时惟朱全忠据汴，赵犨兄弟保陈，门之外即为贼境，汴去贼差远，全忠兵力足以自固；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163550_comment'></div>陈被攻围，势孤众寡，为犨难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163550_comment'></div>初，巢入长安，朝廷除犨陈州刺史，始领事，策巢出关必犯陈，即缮完以待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163550_comment'></div>既而巢果东奔趣项，犨击擒其爱将孟楷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163550_comment'></div>贼盛怒，志必屠陈以逞，合兵数十万围其城，疏堑五周，五道攻迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163550_comment'></div>犨以饥疲之众，无日不战，历三百日，竟全危城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163550_comment'></div>巢以此师老不振，卒溃灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163550_comment'></div>论者纪忠烈之事，名多重于死执，功每减于生全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163550_comment'></div>夫忠烈士志义所存，岂有意于死生之际也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163550_comment'></div>幸不幸，存焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163550_comment'></div>肃宗乾元中，陈州刺史尚死于史思明之难，后蒙褒赠，至今庙食于陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163550_comment'></div>赵公全城保民，享受宠命，顾其功名反出于死事者下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163550_comment'></div>兄弟三节度，皆著勋于王室，并终于僖、昭之世，而唐史不书德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163550_comment'></div>朱全忠之救以解其围，故事之谨，然未尝北面于梁，而梁史书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163550_comment'></div>史官无法，笔削两失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163550_comment'></div>国朝重修《唐书》，方为立传，昶、珝附焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163550_comment'></div>《梁书》谓珝为弟，《新书》以珝为子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163550_comment'></div>犨自有二子：麓、岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163550_comment'></div>意者珝其弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163550_comment'></div>熙宁三年，余守淮阳，州学教授苏辙为余言，赵太尉有画像在开元寺东庑僧院，以闻之不早，寻被代，不及见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163550_comment'></div>七年，复被命领州，往瞻其像，在殿之隅闇壁阖下，昼日不以烛不见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163550_comment'></div>公殁于龙纪中，距今百九十年，陈人莫知遗像之存于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163550_comment'></div>适邻有空院，一堂岿然，向明高爽，因命工葺饰，表为祠堂，绘素鼎新，神气如在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163550_comment'></div>《礼·祭法》曰：「能捍大患则祀之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163550_comment'></div>若太尉者，可谓能捍大患，宜列于法祀者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163550_comment'></div>故封为上公，祀为大神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163550_comment'></div>圣人立教，著在礼典，祠堂既立，为率僚属陈馈奠，乃告所司，春秋荐时，事比群祀，以其二弟从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163550_comment'></div>又为镵《新书》本传于石，立于堂之东楹，使陈人知遗育之至于今，公之力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163550_comment'></div>时大宋熙宁七年岁在甲寅九月十三日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1163550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年9月28日</a>　九月二十八日，在知陈州任，作祭赵犨文。作品：陈州祭唐赠太尉赵公文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈州祭唐赠太尉赵公文<span class='inlineComment2'>（犨）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年9月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163649")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163649'>维熙宁七年九月丙申朔，二十八日癸亥，具官谨以清酌庶羞之奠，敢昭告于唐赠太尉赵公：有唐之季，大盗移国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163649_comment'></div>封豕长蛇，践食区夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163649_comment'></div>生民涂炭，城邑丘墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163649_comment'></div>公于尔时，独保孤垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163649_comment'></div>攻围几年，浴血百战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163649_comment'></div>陈之遗黎，竟脱贼口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163649_comment'></div>兄弟三人，继登将相，并有功德，著于此邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163649_comment'></div>而其像貌，晦于闇壁，邦人不知，久不克享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163649_comment'></div>某祗膺朝命，再来领藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163649_comment'></div>惟公忠烈，能捍大患，写之绘素，神气凛然，乃建祠堂，式荐时事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163649_comment'></div>夫封为上公，祀为贵神，《春秋》之义，礼典攸著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163649_comment'></div>奉之庙食，永世无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163649_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1163649_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年10月2日</a>　十月二日，在知陈州任，因夫人马氏卒，徙知应天府。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
丰县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ada22917d986493a9da4d9e15fb89a75_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ada22917d986493a9da4d9e15fb89a75");'><span id='ada22917d986493a9da4d9e15fb89a75_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>，27岁</div><div id='ada22917d986493a9da4d9e15fb89a75' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>三月，自睢阳往游山东，过丰县，有诗。作品：过丰。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_495403' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495403' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495403?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过丰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495403")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495403_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495403'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495403'>刘季当年在古丰，芒砀王气已连空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495403_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495403'>天机先露由啼妪，人意冥符自董公。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495403_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495403'>历数有归徒胜负，风云相会尽英雄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495403_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495403'>不然樊郦萧曹辈，尽老屠商掾吏中。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495403_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495403'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495403_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>三月，自睢阳往游山东，览丰县中阳里汉高祖庙，题诗。作品：题中阳里高祖庙。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_495405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题中阳里高祖庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495405")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495405'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495405'>纵酒疏狂不治生，中阳有土倚兄耕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495405_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495405'>晚遭乱世成功业，更向公前与仲争。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495405_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495405'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495405_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
沛县
