-----title
昆山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='10f4d215986e420fa3022b3f6516a7de_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("10f4d215986e420fa3022b3f6516a7de");'><span id='10f4d215986e420fa3022b3f6516a7de_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1037')">1034-1037年</a>，28-31岁</div><div id='10f4d215986e420fa3022b3f6516a7de' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　本年，在知昆山县任，平息田讼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　本年，在知昆山县任，有书上宋绶。作品：上宋参政启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三二。）</span><div id='poem_1163440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宋参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1034年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163440")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163440'>伏以推扬士类，采拔人材，乃贤公之美名，抑清朝之本务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163440_comment'></div>近世何者，兹道阙如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163440_comment'></div>岂意猥才，亲逢真赏，滥首布衣之举，得窥黼座之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163440_comment'></div>推行量能，固出诸生之下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163440_comment'></div>乘风托景，遂成竖子之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163440_comment'></div>伏念某立节无奇，少文近野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163440_comment'></div>为学荒略，曾弗究于一家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163440_comment'></div>赋性阔疏，复靡堪于诸用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163440_comment'></div>但弓裘不可以废业，而箪瓢非所以养亲，聊干禄以代耕，实亡心于过分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163440_comment'></div>无何天幸，孤奉恩知，遂沾一命之荣，遽叨百乘之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163440_comment'></div>回瞻屏树，宛在霄衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163440_comment'></div>几疏记而欲通，比内函而辄止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163440_comment'></div>盖腾口说者为感之末，中心藏者实义之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163440_comment'></div>故将略其外而笃诸诚，舍乎薄而居其厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163440_comment'></div>此其志之所在，非敢引而自疏，仰料汪汪之宽，垂谅区区之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163440_comment'></div>恭惟某官懿文通理，吉德蹈中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163440_comment'></div>明净无瑕，若青天白日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163440_comment'></div>精粹不耀，如璞玉浑金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163440_comment'></div>掌邦家之衡绳，固名教之律度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163440_comment'></div>磊落大节，著于危疑之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163440_comment'></div>几微远猷，施于醇静之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163440_comment'></div>今夫璇玑在政，金铉调元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163440_comment'></div>明堂布政之宫，方资坐论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163440_comment'></div>东閤翘材之馆，尚接末游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163440_comment'></div>素琯候深，黄扉地隔，方引领于海上，徒驰神于日边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163440_comment'></div>伏惟作德逸休，代天燮友，神明所祐，戬谷具宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163440_comment'></div>更冀上为庙朝，倍绥福履。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1163440_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年7月</a>　七月，在知昆山县任，观稼，有诗。作品：昆山初秋观稼回县署与同僚及示姑苏幕府。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_495621' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495621' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495621?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昆山初秋观稼回县署与同寮及示姑苏幕府</a><span class='authorDate'>（1035年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495621")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495621_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495621'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495621'>邑民三万家，四边湖海绕。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495621'>家家勤穑事，市井商游少。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495621'>荐岁逢水沴，饥劳何扰扰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495621'>我来忝抚字，见此心如捣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495621'>去秋仅有年，膏田尚停潦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495621'>今幸风雨调，皆话天时好。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495621'>春喜鹊巢低，夏更蝉声早<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：吴民以此候旱潦饥穰焉。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495621'>秧船拿参差，葑岸萦回缭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495621'>艺插暮更急，车响转清晓。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495621'>纺筥犹挂壁，何暇张鱼鸟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495621'>我时行近郊，小艇穿萍藻。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495621'>渚长葭薍深，野沃𥝧稏倒。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495621'>孺子远饷归，閒暇颜色饱。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495621'>预喜省敲笞，租赋可时了。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495621'>归来轩馆静，旷荡盈怀抱。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495621'>衙退人吏散，庭庑阒窈窈。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495621'>露筱映孤亭，风荷动幽沼。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495621'>置身木雁间，兹焉愿终老。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495621'>颠蹶走荣利，况余拙非巧。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495621'>鲈脍饭紫芒，鹅脂酒清醥<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：紫芒、鹅脂，稻名。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495621'>怅然怀友生，虚斋为谁扫。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495621_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495621'></div><div id='poem_sentence_21_495621_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　本年，在知昆山县任，有书寄苏州太守陆若冲。作品：与苏州太守陆学士书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三一。陆若冲名，据李之亮《宋两浙路郡守年表》补。）</span><div id='poem_1163450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与苏州太守陆学士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163450")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163450'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163450'>惟古今天下之政事所以乱，率由下情不上通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163450_comment'></div>下情所以不上通，由在上者务贵自贤，在下者谄偷求容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163450_comment'></div>故帝尧之为君，谋于众，舍己从人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163450_comment'></div>伊尹之为臣，匹夫罔不获自尽，惟虑下情之塞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163450_comment'></div>朝廷耳目在牧守，牧守耳目在县令，县令与民最亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163450_comment'></div>自汉以来，郡县虽相摄制，而各得为政，刺史比课督奸而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163450_comment'></div>故州虽无良贰千石，而不害县有善令，吏民以是亲信，风绩以此成立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163450_comment'></div>盖上下之政不相侵，故贤不肖较然，上之发谪赏擢亦得以无滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163450_comment'></div>近者唐室失保民之道，方镇分地，一道百城，惨舒恩威，尽出节度、连率之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163450_comment'></div>悍卒鸱张，黩夫狼贪，郡县长官役属如隶人，关柅动静，臂指伸缩，奔走号令，制不在己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163450_comment'></div>故唐仅三百年，纪于循吏者无几，且治迹功状去汉远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163450_comment'></div>岂无良士？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163450_comment'></div>岂无仁人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163450_comment'></div>原其由然，盖事有牵制，才不专用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163450_comment'></div>今朝廷分局布吏，提纲振目，等级如堂陛，轻重如权衡，都邑相维，动有绳准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163450_comment'></div>然典刑具在，亦系人弛张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163450_comment'></div>县非其人，州得以请黜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163450_comment'></div>州非其人，县受其弊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163450_comment'></div>故知与天子共理者，实牧守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163450_comment'></div>某权不足以合道，才无长于经术，射策王庭，解褐通邑，亦惟天幸，遭二名侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163450_comment'></div>自明公于藩，再获请见，接君子之几席，闻长者之馀论，至于诚淳优博，温厚敦易，亦少得明公之所志者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163450_comment'></div>如是而下情不达，一州之政不和，则无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163450_comment'></div>且夫子之道至大，而曾子称之曰「忠恕而已矣」，得非以忠恕之道，可以总百行之要者欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163450_comment'></div>忠以事上，恕以体下，虽在闾巷之内、蛮貊之邦，行矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163450_comment'></div>而况纡墨绶长，百乘之邑，有民人焉，有社稷焉，是亦当效忠之地，得用恕之位者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163450_comment'></div>矧郡县相附，义犹心体，休戚同处，得失概及，上可言而不言，下当从而不从，阻下情，塞上听，岂忠恕之谓耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163450_comment'></div>辄条近符教之不宜于县尤甚者五条，以闻于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163450_comment'></div>倘明公宽其干冒，不挥而退之也，则谨当时有闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163450_comment'></div>若其出位而谋，越职而议，某非矫激沽鬻者，固不是为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163450_comment'></div>窃景夫忠恕之义，不可徒默焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1163450_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　本年，在知昆山县任，有书寄蔡齐。作品：寄上蔡参政书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_1163448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄上蔡参政书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163448")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163448'>伏念去门庭，官于海上，倏二年于兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163448_comment'></div>每思盛德垂抚之厚，忽若侍座下，见颜色，不知精神之驰乎屏树也，公且信是夫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163448_comment'></div>乃者某困穷不能养，彷徉乎天下，而未始有遭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163448_comment'></div>公独恤然，悯而衣食之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163448_comment'></div>乃者某尝有志乎学古之道，斐然为辞章，亦既自达乎闻人作者，而莫之或信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163448_comment'></div>公独乐而教育之，至以闻天子，取科名禄仕内之怀中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163448_comment'></div>公之遇某也如此，某之有心于公也，非谄而信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163448_comment'></div>且今之公卿大夫，其在上位者几人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163448_comment'></div>材能隽雄者，声光章灼者，即曰有矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163448_comment'></div>若乃大方全德，体仁合义，精粹不耀，如璞玉浑金，明净无瑕，如青天白日，诚淳优大，万美完足，则惟公一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163448_comment'></div>是故一睹公之气韵者，鄙吝之心悉去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163448_comment'></div>一闻公之绪言者，忠信之志皆起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163448_comment'></div>此某所以窃窃焉托名投迹，如七十子之不可去仲尼，岂特顾望公之贵势而趋之者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163448_comment'></div>虽然，公于今者当造物之炉冶，执裁制之尺度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163448_comment'></div>绕朝之清流贵客，侍宴閒而陪议论于前；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163448_comment'></div>四方之英才俊人，效技能而赞功德于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163448_comment'></div>是安得念某之江湖之上，窃窃然哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163448_comment'></div>某所守邑，三面江海，西与州接，渺然大泽，不通骑步，路所穷绝，故无宾游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163448_comment'></div>俗不识书，无有士子，民无大猾，廷无滞讼，适复善岁，萧然省事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163448_comment'></div>令之赋禄，足以供甘脆，仁族属；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163448_comment'></div>令之事任，足以抚疲羸，为善事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163448_comment'></div>以此言之，则是邑也天下之美地，而令也者，仕宦而得民者也，若是又何求焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163448_comment'></div>盖某之志于学，其思进而未止者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163448_comment'></div>今幸公宰政居中，大钧播物，某诚愿以县大夫之禄执经乡校，与好学者游，切磋讲习，咏歌先王之道，聊以卒岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163448_comment'></div>至乃驰徇于烨爚之地，趑趄乎声利之途，一介之守，所不能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163448_comment'></div>因感公恩知之厚，又欲以一披雪乎鄙怀之久存者，故写诚于兹书，伏惟论道之馀，赐采览焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1163448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　秋，在知昆山县任，以苏州太守蒋堂建议，著《刍荛论》十卷。作品：刍荛论。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷六至卷一五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　秋，在知昆山县任，与蒋堂宴集，有诗。作品：姑苏蒋公北池诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_495634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>姑苏蒋公北池诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495634")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495634'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495634'>浙江汤汤，南国之纪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495634'>句章之乡，居巢之里。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495634'>天子命公，二邦更治。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495634'>越人之嗟，吴人之喜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495634'>公之为政，简而易从。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495634'>不严而威，敏以有功。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495634'>孽不及牙，奸折其绪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495634'>孰施斧斤，不见铓露。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495634'>老稚晏起，壮服于亩。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495634'>椸有浣衣，廥有多稌。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495634'>公之退公，乐是北池。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495634'>飞阁渠渠，虚廊迟迟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495634'>鱼跳于藻，渚有凫鹥。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495634'>钓亭桧岛，其水涟漪。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495634'>公之退公，以豫以游。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495634'>邦人喜公，尚无疾忧。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495634'>邦人祝公，百禄是遒。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495634'>匪公其私，王家之休。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495634'>我思建官，公理众政。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495634'>与民最亲，惟时守令。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495634'>其有不臧，根心之螟。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495634'>小犹虮虱，肤皮是营。<div id='poem_sentence_21_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_495634'>于铄有宋，一统万方。<div id='poem_sentence_22_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_495634'>千里所付，几人曰良。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495634'>凡领王民，守土之吏。<div id='poem_sentence_24_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_495634'>有理如吴，帝道则粹。<div id='poem_sentence_25_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_495634'>我歌北池，爰颂公德。<div id='poem_sentence_26_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_495634'>以告后人，勿污勿塞。<div id='poem_sentence_27_495634_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_495634'></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_495634_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年9月</a>　九月，在知昆山县任，有书寄蒋堂，并献所著《刍荛论》作品：与蒋吏部书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三一。）</span><div id='poem_1163449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与蒋吏部书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163449")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163449'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163449'>某野而讷于辞，是以再见而未能自达乎腹心也，执事亦且何以见处哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163449_comment'></div>遂无言而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163449_comment'></div>窃有所不足，敢少布诚乎执事者而行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163449_comment'></div>某志轩旷而难遂，性刚介而鲜合，器不适乎诸用，艺不精乎一家，至于有意乎古之道，有心乎天下之务，虽则鄙愚，窃自谓可从于能者之后焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163449_comment'></div>始在乡闾，不求名誉，有田一廛，有宫一亩，随赋干禄，繄我慈亲旨甘之故，非所以求显荣为进取者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163449_comment'></div>天圣五年春，不遇春官氏，归耕于濉上，值济阳蔡公、常山宋公继来保釐，采乡人善者之论，辄辱解榻以待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163449_comment'></div>已而天子下诏取方闻之士，二公唱于朝，与一二贤卿大夫猥以不肖称于帝前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163449_comment'></div>由是得涉赤墀，历文陛，仰户牖之法座，条三道之大对，一命而获长是邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163449_comment'></div>且尝更三太守矣，其治可言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163449_comment'></div>范之为政也敏，而其失也疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163449_comment'></div>陆之为政也宽，其弊也弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163449_comment'></div>执事之为政，期三月矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163449_comment'></div>一之日符令之下于县者，三减其二焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163449_comment'></div>二之日追胥悍吏不至于县令之庭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163449_comment'></div>三之日事有条而令有章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163449_comment'></div>不敏以是知执事之能有成也，其无弊也，不敏之所愿从之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163449_comment'></div>执事之始至也，某不能来贺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163449_comment'></div>今之来也，阁下如有望焉，再见而不及以政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163449_comment'></div>且鬷蔑不言，叔向不知其贤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163449_comment'></div>赵子不言，魏绛不知其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163449_comment'></div>某独得不言，而责执事之不知我乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163449_comment'></div>今以近所著《刍荛论》两编十卷，冀执事少知不敏之于古之道，天下之务，六经之奥，诸家之言，历代治乱之由，百王沿革之法，亦尝曾慷慨持论，究详用心也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163449_comment'></div>不敏之为是书，将以献于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163449_comment'></div>惟执事当世之名儒，识者且欲咨而考之，凡此书之有所不宜言，言而非者，有所发焉，某得以存其是而黜其非，是求益之举也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1163449_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
阜阳（汝阴）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='72915b9d7b094437b090ffc34a2ef697_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("72915b9d7b094437b090ffc34a2ef697");'><span id='72915b9d7b094437b090ffc34a2ef697_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>，31岁</div><div id='72915b9d7b094437b090ffc34a2ef697' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　冬，归朝，途经颍州，有书上知州蔡齐。作品：上蔡内阁书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三一。蔡齐知颍州事，参李之亮《北宋京师及东西路大郡守臣考》）</span><div id='poem_1163445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上蔡内阁书<span class='inlineComment2'>（文忠公）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163445")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163445'>窃以师道之废久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163445_comment'></div>昔在两汉，公卿大臣咸门有诸生横经受业，书名录牒至数千人，师儒教尊，人知重学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163445_comment'></div>故在两汉，其政事本于经术，其议论据于王制，朝有名节之劝，士笃去就之行，美化雅俗，比隆三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163445_comment'></div>魏晋而下，中区版荡，诸戎扰乱，隔为南北，小雅尽废，文献不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163445_comment'></div>近在唐氏，风流寖薄，取士之制，专用虚辞，虽开元、元和变而几道，名公宗匠磊落相望，然治学传家，本原已废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163445_comment'></div>诸生后进奔走末路，以文求售，势同市贾，然犹屈伸系乎托迹，进退谋于所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163445_comment'></div>名士口吻，片言可以取重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163445_comment'></div>清流门地，一见可以为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163445_comment'></div>士风绰兮，顾亦近古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163445_comment'></div>清朝一统，丕冒无外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163445_comment'></div>鸟言鴂舌，知诵乎简书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163445_comment'></div>髽首卉裳，咸袭乎端甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163445_comment'></div>然循唐取士，而考言弥华，驾说之学用微，师资之礼遂绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163445_comment'></div>非有志乎远者大者，莫不嗜甘而排苦，采芳而遗实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163445_comment'></div>天未丧道，必将有主，主吾道者，阁下安得而让诸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163445_comment'></div>伏惟阁下风采发乎冠岁，光华耀于区域，早结明主，奋扬亨衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163445_comment'></div>其发策决科也，则江都之研经理，家令之切世务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163445_comment'></div>其代言密侍也，则文园之视草，中垒之纳忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163445_comment'></div>其抚藩屏也，则颍州之教，河南之威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163445_comment'></div>其毗大政也，则高陵之儒雅，平陵之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163445_comment'></div>兹可谓周才而通智者矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163445_comment'></div>某不佞，窃伏东鄙，承望下风，盖有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163445_comment'></div>蓄为潢污，莫能自通乎江海；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163445_comment'></div>覆诸盎缶，无以上觇乎日星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163445_comment'></div>今罢官吴中，言归故里，乃值阁下实此尹正，既再获见矣，而莫能展叙乎腹心也，得不少因文墨以自荐其诚欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163445_comment'></div>某世有仕籍，堂有尊亲，惧先绪之坠地，且养羞之不给，爰谋干禄，盖为代耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163445_comment'></div>既随计而西，不得志于有司，退居于濉上，仕意益薄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163445_comment'></div>景祐改元，天子复下诏举方闻之士，朝廷二三贤公猥录名字，章闻于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163445_comment'></div>由是获对法扆，躬承大问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163445_comment'></div>三道之要，四政之阙，承学良浅，非识所迨，报罢为幸，惧及知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163445_comment'></div>育材道广，取人路宽，一命雠书，庇身美邑，饱食海上，坐逾三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163445_comment'></div>时哉归欤，乃遇盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163445_comment'></div>某闻之：声同相应，高下不必均；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163445_comment'></div>气类相从，体质不必齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163445_comment'></div>故蜉蝣候阴而出，柱础因云而润，况心志之灵，能无所感！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163445_comment'></div>自国家之开诏举，由是路而进者，盖有人数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163445_comment'></div>今日之事，又阁下之所发，此某之所以伏幽陋而望下风，引领庶几，岁月以冀，以未尝得见为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163445_comment'></div>亦惟阁下所以抚接之意，其必有以当之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163445_comment'></div>谨录近所著《刍荛论》十卷两编以献，冀阁下少知某之于古之道，天下之务，抑为有心者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163445_comment'></div>某前所以援汉唐之事，叹师道之废者，是区区鄙中窃望于阁下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163445_comment'></div>倘阁下有振复古道之意而获预焉，受赐之大，无尚此已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163445_comment'></div>不胜感激之怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1163445_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州（钱塘）
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　秋，赴任睦州通判途中，过钱塘江，有诗。作品：初赴新定过钱塘江。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_495597' class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495597'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495597'>飏帆上渔浦，随潮宿雁湾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495597'>烟火指富阳，云树连萧山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----end



-----title
桐庐
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='72127b924c3943bba1c103d9ba3b46cd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("72127b924c3943bba1c103d9ba3b46cd");'><span id='72127b924c3943bba1c103d9ba3b46cd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>，32岁</div><div id='72127b924c3943bba1c103d9ba3b46cd' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，赴任睦州通判途中，过七里濑，有诗。作品：赴新定过七里濑。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴新定过七里濑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495557")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495557'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495557'>舟过严陵濑，凉秋水木清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495557'>鼓旗知郭近，鱼鸟见人惊。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495557'>云乱迷山色，滩长杂雨声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495557'>一毫名利事，搔首愧平生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495557_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495557'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495557_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，赴任睦州通判途中，有诗寄桐庐关太守。作品：新定道中寄桐庐关太守三首。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷四。关太守名不详。）</span><div id='poem_495594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新定道中寄桐庐关太守三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495594")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495594'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495594'>辟书来北门，召命自宣室。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495594'>朝廷搜英材，溪山及野质。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495594'>当世良有心，一得思造膝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495594'>署霞隐扶桑，已是长安日。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495594_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495594'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495594_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495595?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495595'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495595'>旦下乌石滩，暮泊严陵濑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495595'>潺湲卧溪声，惨澹宿山霭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495595'>所历已陈迹，不忘惟嘉话。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495595'>泪湿青云篇，抚襟惭慷慨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495595'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495595_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495595'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_495595_0'>⑴ 自注：关有诗相送云《青云篇》，送行诗也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495595_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_495596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495596?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495596'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495596'>帆挂桐君山，橹入富春渚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495596'>寒风荡江波，烟雨迷汀树。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495596'>煮茶论药经，挑灯数棋路。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495596'>全胜谢惠连，独望新安去<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495596'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495596'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_495596_0'>⑴ 自注：同行者蜀僧吉善医，茂材龚君美好奕。谢守赴新安，过富春渚有诗。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495596_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
建德
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7764bb5678aa48fdb830087b9be98222_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7764bb5678aa48fdb830087b9be98222");'><span id='7764bb5678aa48fdb830087b9be98222_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1040')">1038-1040年</a>，32-34岁</div><div id='7764bb5678aa48fdb830087b9be98222' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　冬，到睦州通判任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年7月15日</a>　七月十五日，在睦州通判任，作文祭蔡齐。作品：祭蔡参政文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭蔡参政文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年7月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163637")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163637'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163637'>维宝元二年岁次己卯，七月庚寅朔，十五日甲辰，具官某谨遣右都押衙许思义，以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于故参政、侍郎、赠礼部尚书、济阳文忠公之灵：呜呼公乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163637_comment'></div>以公之德之仁，而中年以殁世乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163637_comment'></div>天之报施，略茫昧乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163637_comment'></div>太夫人齿发高矣，喜惧侍养，晚乃得子，未及抚而名之，而公舍以长逝乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163637_comment'></div>公既生而不以家事为意，捐馆之日，柩无所归，家无所寓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163637_comment'></div>不然，孰知公之清节素志乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163637_comment'></div>呜呼公乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163637_comment'></div>以公之德之仁，何负于天，而至是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163637_comment'></div>公之事亲如事天，以为尽天下之美，不足以报也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163637_comment'></div>公之事君如事亲，以为竭心力之勤，不足以奉也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163637_comment'></div>公之待故旧朋友如待兄弟，义之尽也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163637_comment'></div>公之视四海之人，至于一物之细，如视赤子，爱之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163637_comment'></div>公之心如青天白日，光明旷达，华夏蛮貊同仰之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163637_comment'></div>公之行如浑金璞玉，精华温润，无贤不肖同宝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163637_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163637_comment'></div>邦家之务，生民之故，兹念兹忧，爱莫公助，如何难谌，云亡之遽！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163637_comment'></div>某爰始羁微，公实赏知，已衣其寒，复饱其饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163637_comment'></div>延誉于朝，闻荐于帝，再滥诏选，皆公引提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163637_comment'></div>公亦类举，非茍以私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163637_comment'></div>前年暮冬，见公颍川，姿神意气，和悦温然，违别恋恋，孰期终天？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163637_comment'></div>单官江外，万山阻延，不见裧帷，归旐翩翩，涕泪流膺，下沾九泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163637_comment'></div>公有慈亲，公有弱子，于焉展报，其不有年？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163637_comment'></div>呜呼公乎，庶几鉴旃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163637_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1163637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　本年，在睦州通判任，就元昊称帝上疏言事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　春，在睦州通判任，以宋夏战起，上《平戎十策》作品：平戎十策。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷一九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年4月</a>　四月，在睦州通判任，撰《吴兴郡守题名记》作品：吴兴郡守题名记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1163546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴兴郡守题名记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163546")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163546_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163546'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163546'>唐氏自天宝失驭而忘其利器，诸侯专土，奸猾乘隙，窃国而侯，坏法放命，不贡不享，更相禽猎，或自篡逐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163546_comment'></div>五代草草，乱靡有定，天下为战国者且二百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163546_comment'></div>我太祖武皇帝既擒诸僭王，创艾未大之弊，思拯涂炭，讲建长策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163546_comment'></div>因四方渐定，诸帅王觐者辄留宿卫，畜其族；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163546_comment'></div>京师罢节廉诸府，裂方镇之地而置转运使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163546_comment'></div>罢刺史，而遣士大夫行郡事，置其贰，陈其旅，以分其权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163546_comment'></div>郡长吏不敏，听理不明，则转运使纠其谬，以直民之曲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163546_comment'></div>郡长吏而才，足以自为政，不复摄属于连帅之为患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163546_comment'></div>故距兹八十年，天下如一家，政事如一体，关柅动静，臂指伸缩，无有不如意者，斯可谓大圣创制，从权合义，藏身之固，置器于安，规摹之闳远者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163546_comment'></div>吴兴，二浙之佳郡，自江左以来，以处名流令望，为养才用之宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163546_comment'></div>宝元二年，南阳滕君宗谅子京以尚书郎来领符竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163546_comment'></div>子京文雅风采，上林推为卿材国器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163546_comment'></div>早历谏官，以论事谔谔无回避，不得久留中，换郎外补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163546_comment'></div>至郡，见吏民，问病苦，有隐咸照，无弊不革，因其俗以教，狱市帖然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163546_comment'></div>始大庠序，育人材，诸生负笈自远方至，霅水之上，既同洙泗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163546_comment'></div>凡若因循，举兴悉复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163546_comment'></div>尝坐厅事，问前为郡者之名，而不纪，曰：「是非阙者欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163546_comment'></div>命录自钱氏奉图，朝廷所除吏，逮今三十人，推次备详，见谒以序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163546_comment'></div>盖闻诸长者，粗习朝家之故，惟皇祖经法之善，躬揽鐏柄，以遏乱略，及生人之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163546_comment'></div>大郡长吏由是专于为政，贤不肖之迹以辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163546_comment'></div>今列其名，非徒载年月，记到罢，亦俾览之者得以善善恶恶，而惩劝存焉，实《春秋》之意已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163546_comment'></div>至于纪星土，本风俗，郡之废置，吏之沿革，产毛之物，山水之胜，则于图牒焉观之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163546_comment'></div>时康定元年夏四月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1163546_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年6月</a>　六月，在睦州通判任，撰《湖州新建州学记》作品：湖州新建州学记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1163545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州新建州学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163545")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163545'>宝元二年，上命尚书祠部员外郎滕君守吴兴郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163545_comment'></div>始至，见吏民，问疾苦，披图牒，考风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163545_comment'></div>顾谓僚属曰：「古书建国君民，教学为先，四代之道，起于党遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163545_comment'></div>汉氏继周而王，惩秦非圣人之法以败，稍复遵用儒术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163545_comment'></div>循吏文翁兴学蜀郡，变巴夷如邹鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163545_comment'></div>汉廷多武人，莫或赞上褒广其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163545_comment'></div>以孝文之盛德，具王道而微者，所不至于王，一息尔，犹能富庶而不能教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163545_comment'></div>东都中兴，儒雅寖隆，公卿大臣咸门有诸生横经受业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163545_comment'></div>三分多难，微言仅绝，小雅尽废，文献不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163545_comment'></div>唐虽礼典甚讲，盖文具而实丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163545_comment'></div>是以后王研究理要，终莫致于三代者，顾所以化民成俗之道，育才官人之法，隳其根本矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163545_comment'></div>惟我治朝，丕冒出日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163545_comment'></div>鸟言鴂舌，知诵简册之言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163545_comment'></div>髽首卉裳，竞袭端甫之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163545_comment'></div>而庠序俶落乎睢澳，嗣音乎郏鄏，规摹大于齐魏，弦诵闻乎荆吴，且遍诸郡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163545_comment'></div>矧是吴兴，南国之奥，有佳山水，发为秀人，自江左而清流美士、馀风遗韵相续也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163545_comment'></div>凡为郡者，用民之力于署、于观、于诸不急，而学校不建，岂守臣布宣王家风教之意欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163545_comment'></div>僚属曰：「唯」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163545_comment'></div>吏民闻君子弟畜其人，将驱而之善也，相与输金，愿遂建学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163545_comment'></div>乃十二月，考景营基，鸠材类工，且以命教请于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163545_comment'></div>越明年夏四月，敕书先至，锡名州学，仍赐田五夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163545_comment'></div>六月，新学成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163545_comment'></div>重门沈沈，广殿耽耽，论堂邃如也，书阁屹如也，皆相次东西序，分十八斋，治业者群居焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163545_comment'></div>入门而右，为学官之署；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163545_comment'></div>入门而左，有斋宿之馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163545_comment'></div>又为窣道，距闉挟阁，构二亭，凡溪山之胜，眺望悉会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163545_comment'></div>庖圃有次，廥藏备设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163545_comment'></div>复立小学于东南隅，童子离经肄简，谅者聚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163545_comment'></div>凡为屋百有二十楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163545_comment'></div>既衅器用币，释菜成礼，客有兴于座曰：美哉学也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163545_comment'></div>若稽田，既勤敷菑，在所播植；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163545_comment'></div>惟学，敏厥修，念终始，在其所志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163545_comment'></div>君子学以聚之，问以辨之，举而措诸，可以成天下之务，斯得谓之士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163545_comment'></div>若其拘文牵义，龊龊近思，诵焉不通其变，习焉不达于用，此辟儒之大患也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163545_comment'></div>师乎师乎，记问云乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163545_comment'></div>能开达学者之志虑，使广大深实，知道之所以为用，兹可以为师矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163545_comment'></div>学乎学乎，艺文云乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163545_comment'></div>彼先王之糟粕，后世且得其味而尝诸，茍知道之所用，何学而非道者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163545_comment'></div>兹可以为学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163545_comment'></div>士充其业，上使其器，则致理之本，不在学校乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163545_comment'></div>以是而观滕志，其已远哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163545_comment'></div>某不敏，岂足以语道之大？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163545_comment'></div>命纪经始，不获让云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163545_comment'></div>时康定元年六月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1163545_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年12月</a>　十二月，在睦州通判任，撰《淮南转运使奖谕敕书记》作品：淮南转运使奖谕敕书记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1163549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮南转运使奖谕敕书记</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163549")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163549'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163549'>何以保大，曰兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163549_comment'></div>何以聚兵，曰财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163549_comment'></div>故国之大政，无先征赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163549_comment'></div>汉氏三分天下之入，以其一供边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163549_comment'></div>孝武事四夷，调用不足，兴杂算，设诸筦，笼山泽之利，而民始病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163549_comment'></div>唐既兵兴，蕃戎乘弊陷河湟，凡诸侯之师防秋塞上，暨勤王讨伐出本道之境，则食于度支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163549_comment'></div>有司商利，分毫析铢，民之膏泽竭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163549_comment'></div>盖戎狄侵略，何代不有，非所以为中夏之安危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163549_comment'></div>然率于军旅期会，应声卒办，奸吏因缘邀功市宠，为上歛怨，生事召乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163549_comment'></div>故中夏之安危，不在边防，而在闾里也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163549_comment'></div>国家自北方通好，戎酋款服，偃革无事且三十年，而黠羌饱飞，逸于牢圈，驱劫种落，内惊边人，顾其意虑，股掌中尔，乌足以烦灵诛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163549_comment'></div>朝廷思为不可犯之势，守备甚设，内外当财柄者稍复目动矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163549_comment'></div>时刑部郎中陈君、工部郎中张君转输淮服，当东南之津要，以山海为府藏，而二君有才术方略，贸迁弛敛，资用充富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163549_comment'></div>属王师吊伐，边城委输，惟淮南供具尤赡，而吏民不知有贡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163549_comment'></div>上多其勤，下诏褒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163549_comment'></div>某将赴都，道由山阳，刑曹出诏相示，愿纪其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163549_comment'></div>某伏观诏旨，以其无敛于民，谓之嘉绩，是以知上心之仁远也，其爱民也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163549_comment'></div>二君之体国也，其不害民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163549_comment'></div>深惟朝廷宽大之意，二君功利之优，足以使贪夫廉，懦夫起，彼邀功市宠，敛怨生事者，宜知愧畏，义可以示天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163549_comment'></div>故及前世备边大略，著本末云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163549_comment'></div>时康定元年十二月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1163549_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　冬，上疏论募额外弓手事。作品：论天下州县新添置弓手事宜奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二一。）</span><div id='poem_1163163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163163?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论天下州县新添置弓手事宜奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163163")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163163'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163163'>今月某日，本路转运司牒录到敕黄，以近日诸处拣移兵士上京，虑恐州县别有盗贼，特添弓手准备防护者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163163_comment'></div>兹诚朝廷约用兵农之法，深戒本末之备者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163163_comment'></div>伏缘天下州县之长吏，通明之才甚鲜，每诏令颁下，虽画一丁宁，及其施行，犹不能详举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163163_comment'></div>傥又示之大体，约束不尽，则诸郡县承用者驳，人自为见，措置乖宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163163_comment'></div>况今所差弓手遍于天下，赋役大事，理宜均当，经始出乎多算，虑终冀乎少弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163163_comment'></div>臣诚浅识，早尘诏选，敢以千虑，上裨万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163163_comment'></div>其敕文有条制未尽事件，及臣外有所见八条，谨具列于左：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1163163'>一、敕文：逐县除旧管弓手外，据见管主户，每一千户差点弓手五十人，一万户五百人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163163_comment'></div>如不满千户，及万户已上，据今所定分数比量差点者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163163_comment'></div>伏以天下大县有及五六万户者，若县管主户五万，则所差二千五百人，非惟人数过多，民户烦弊，或地处远险，或岁逢荐饥，或守令非人，或奸猾乘隙聚兵资寇，亦不可以不过虞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163163_comment'></div>欲乞诸万户已下县，所差人数一如敕文处分，即万户已上，亦以五百人为止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163163_comment'></div>缘虽小县，不可以无备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163163_comment'></div>虽大县，而选兵五百，亦足以自卫矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163163_comment'></div>如此，则轻重之势平，臂指之力均矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1163163'>一、敕文：其弓手须于见管帐籍主户差点者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163163_comment'></div>只如臣州管内户籍有升降帐，有桑功帐，并岁上于户部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163163_comment'></div>升降帐所管主户二万二千三百有馀，此盖官吏受俸约此户口数也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163163_comment'></div>桑功帐所管主户三万七千六百有馀，此乃州县户口岁有增益之数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163163_comment'></div>而州县赋役各有五等户版簿，常所据用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163163_comment'></div>切虑逐处拘于帐籍二字，致有点差异同，欲乞明降处分，州县止以见用五等版簿见管主户数为准，则天下之役均焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1163163'>一、敕文：所差点弓手，其第四第五等户如委实贫阙，虽有丁数，即不得一例差点者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163163_comment'></div>乞令诸州县先从物力人丁最高户差点，第一等不足即差第二等，第二等不足即于第三等比并资产、丁行高强者点定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163163_comment'></div>所有合供州县色役，依旧轮流差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163163_comment'></div>见供州县色役者暂免弓手，已毕役者却充弓手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163163_comment'></div>非惟先富强而宽贫弱，夫高赀之人，各有护惜家乡亲爱之意，故必重于犯法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163163_comment'></div>至于合用器仗，亦有力置办，各得精好，自然天下差点事体均当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1163163'>一、敕文：令逐县创置教场，每岁起十月后至正月终，常分番勾集教阅，自教阅时，每人支日食米二升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163163_comment'></div>十月后虽是农隙，集教日长，民亦不易，又约计逐岁人且支米二石四斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163163_comment'></div>今诸州郡仓廪除上供外，留州支遣例少储蓄，即如臣州在两浙中户口不多，所差点弓手若据主户实数，犹仅二千人，若据人数例支给日食，岁支米四千八百石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163163_comment'></div>将多补少，计天下支费，其数不啻百万斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163163_comment'></div>若令逐县所点弓手便作三番教习，当教习时即支与口食，已教放归，便截日住支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163163_comment'></div>即如三千户县弓手一百五十人，每番五十人赴教，每人岁习四十日而已，人不失业，官不费储，是减天下粮给之费三分之二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1163163'>一、敕文：自教阅时量借甲弩器械，教习披带，教罢便仰管辖官员收纳入库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163163_comment'></div>其弓箭、刀𨧱及木枪、杆棒之类，即许自置，以备本乡村教习者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163163_comment'></div>夫奋梃揭竿，犹足以资啸聚之势，况人知斗战，家有利兵，不可启也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163163_comment'></div>请令逐人所置弓箭器械各自标认，悉纳州县，每当教阅，及遇有盗贼勾抽会合之时，据数给付，事毕随纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163163_comment'></div>常令官吏点检，其有损动，即番次给出，各令修换。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1163163'>一、敕文：所差弓手，每五十人内选差会武艺、有身手者一名充节级，每五百人更选有家活、好身手、能武艺者一名充指挥使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163163_comment'></div>伏以内地州县与河朔不同，河朔所置乡军本备战守之用，故依军法立为阶级，以相摄制，又逐州军各屯强兵，势足弹遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163163_comment'></div>今内地州县人不习兵，但材力相雄，富役贫，强暴寡，其兼并豪猾之民，居常犹吞噬贫弱，为乡邑害，况公使之相制乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163163_comment'></div>夫能为五百人长，是必乡里之大猾者，非惟为贫弱之暴，更且有患之大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163163_comment'></div>彼前世之大寇乘饥扰之衅，奋臂犹足以为天下患，况使之有素练之士、甲兵之利乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163163_comment'></div>兹事体大，有安危之势焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163163_comment'></div>请令所点弓手每十人团为一甲，置节级一人，使岁一替换，依次更番补充；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163163_comment'></div>其指挥使之名，伏乞省去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163163_comment'></div>逐甲人少，则节级易为拘管呼集，更番补充，则不相摄服，亦驭民之深策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1163163'>一、敕文：所点弓手，须是少壮者充，与免户下诸杂差配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163163_comment'></div>伏以天下州县人户，大抵贫多富少，逐县五等户版簿，中等已上户不及五分之一，第四第五等户常及十分之九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163163_comment'></div>故国家诸杂赋役，每于中等已上户差科，所以惠贫弱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163163_comment'></div>今富强之家尽占为弓手，即诸杂科配悉出于贫弱，倘又奸吏因缘骚扰，即县乡益困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163163_comment'></div>今若分番教习，每岁赴教止四十日，而官与之食，富强之家未为有损，而乃虚免差配，贻患下户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163163_comment'></div>欲乞令州县诸杂差配一切仍旧，但严行条约，所差弓手除教阅外，州县不得有勾抽差借诸般追役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163163_comment'></div>或有强恶贼徒结成群党，勾抽会合之时，亦只许随近勾点，令佐亲自部勒掩逐，不得令公人押领，淹延团聚，如长役弓级耆壮等一例监捕之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163163_comment'></div>若县乡小小盗贼，至于持杖窃盗，非群行攻劫者，亦不得擅行勾抽，免致官吏接便恣意聚散，即其受利，过于免差配之惠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1163163'>一、每岁教阅之时，乞令逐州知州、通判一次巡行诸县，以按阅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163163_comment'></div>或所点人非壮健，器械不完利，行列不整，训习不精，移易簿帐，减削粮食诸事，其逐县令佐各行勘罚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163163_comment'></div>其弛慢甚者，具事闻奏，乞朝廷严行黜责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1163163'>右具如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163163_comment'></div>臣以不材，猥蒙郡寄，区区之诚，勉思裨补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163163_comment'></div>茍有所见，辄奏朝廷，伏乞圣虑裁择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163163_comment'></div>傥有可行事件，伏乞画一，列为条目，颁下州县，使榜揭之，戒勒官吏，务在举行<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1163163'>奏：宋刻本、清抄本作「闻」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1163163_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163163'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_59_1163163_0'>⑴ 《乐全集》卷二一。又见《续资治通鉴长编》卷一三一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163163_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
北京（南京）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e24238ee79ac494984e57980c9075c5f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e24238ee79ac494984e57980c9075c5f");'><span id='e24238ee79ac494984e57980c9075c5f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>，36岁</div><div id='e24238ee79ac494984e57980c9075c5f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　冬，假起居舍人、知制诰身份出使契丹。<br /></div>
