-----title
滁州（清流）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='264bad1c0cba499fb5cca1f94a1d8bad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("264bad1c0cba499fb5cca1f94a1d8bad");'><span id='264bad1c0cba499fb5cca1f94a1d8bad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1049')">1048-1049年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='264bad1c0cba499fb5cca1f94a1d8bad' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年10月</a>　十月，到知滁州任，有谢表。作品：滁州谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>滁州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163286")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163286'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163286'>昨蒙圣恩授臣依前右谏议大夫、知滁州军州事，已于十月初五日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163286_comment'></div>近班就列，早玷于清途；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163286_comment'></div>便郡庇身，复蒙于善地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163286_comment'></div>荷天之宠，循分知优<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163286_comment'></div>臣绪阀单平，材用疏短，谬登诏选，叨处仕途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163286_comment'></div>通籍朝闺，滥巾儒馆，擢升两禁，用践群司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163286_comment'></div>粗逃官尤，曾微风迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163286_comment'></div>比因病目，不堪簿领之烦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163286_comment'></div>遂剖丹诚，求还文翰之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163286_comment'></div>清衷加恤，慈旨垂矜，得就閒曹，少安散质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163286_comment'></div>事介有无之迹，议生疑似之间，睿鉴孔昭，朝论惟允，领麾殊幸，省己载兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163286_comment'></div>久依日月之光，荣陪法从；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163286_comment'></div>忽到淮山之上，恍复尘寰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163286_comment'></div>值岁大穰，与民同泰，俯仰优足，出处便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163286_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下一气均和，大圆广覆，动植之物并被生成之仁，小大之臣咸荷保全之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163286_comment'></div>矧在孤微之迹，尝叨任遇之恩，拙守有常，厚诬已辨，敢不勤恤民瘼，恪谨官箴，冀勉树于教条，期少资于化育。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163286_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年10月</a>　十月，到知滁州任，有谢启。作品：滁州谢上与两地启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三二。此启所上对象不详。）</span><div id='poem_1163438' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163438' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163438?labeling=true' target='_blank'>滁州谢上与两地启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163438")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163438_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163438'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163438'>昨奉敕差知滁州军州事，已于十月初五日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163438_comment'></div>两禁近班，历要途而知忝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163438_comment'></div>一麾支郡，蒙便地以为优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163438_comment'></div>早依坏冶之仁，适遂榆枋之分，俯仰知幸，成亏盖常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163438_comment'></div>伏念某与世阔疏，持身简易，上加怜于拙守，俯垂祐于孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163438_comment'></div>耻于諔诡之为，庶乎忠恕之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163438_comment'></div>萧然远籁，岂谐钟吕之音；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163438_comment'></div>泛若虚舟，不较波澜之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163438_comment'></div>践历清华之列，逡巡宠利之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163438_comment'></div>控地卑飞，谓见宽于雨弹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163438_comment'></div>曲辕蟠荫，竟不舍于风斤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163438_comment'></div>有恻仁心，免销毁骨，濒淮近甸，依山僻城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163438_comment'></div>值岁大穰，与民同泰，事务殊简，旨甘粗充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163438_comment'></div>悄悄危衷，虽未宁于臲卼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163438_comment'></div>𥉂𥉂病眼，得少啬于精明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163438_comment'></div>此盖某官衡度尽公，陛廉存体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163438_comment'></div>骇机初发，诚激矢以难留；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163438_comment'></div>和律徐吹，顾枯荄而必及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163438_comment'></div>敢不静循士检，动谨官箴，助德泽之微分，答陶埏之大造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1163438_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年10月</a>　十月，在知滁州任，为马诰作墓志铭。作品：朝请大夫行侍御史知桂州军州事上柱国赠礼部尚书扶风马公墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷四〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163622' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163622' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163622?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝请大夫行侍御史知桂州军州事上柱国赠礼部尚书扶风马公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　庆历八年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163622")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163622_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163622'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163622'>公讳诰，字仲谋，魏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163622_comment'></div>其先赵奢为赵将，破秦兵阏与下有功，号马服君，后因为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163622_comment'></div>汉武帝时，以吏二千石自邯郸徙茂陵，故中兴伏波将军援为扶风人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163622_comment'></div>魏建安中，有汉杰者从袁氏河朔，占籍清河，故唐中书令周为茬平人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163622_comment'></div>开成中，有继勋者事魏博节度使何进滔，徙家魏，故公为大名人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163622_comment'></div>曾祖崇义，善骑射，以材略闻，历魏军右职，奉罗洪信为帅，累战多，授怀州团练使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163622_comment'></div>绍威承袭，患牙兵横强，阴结汴人以除其逼，怀州亦遇害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163622_comment'></div>子士安，幼有气节，感家祸，晦居里墅，乃治产，居积逐时，以致厚赀，立信义，尝曰：「吾权敛财，散赈不赡，是亦为政矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163622_comment'></div>生昭美，明经笃行，以父晦居，亦不肯仕，即公之考也，公之登朝，赠殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163622_comment'></div>公弱不好弄，资性沉毅，及冠，奇表，长七尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163622_comment'></div>行纯孝谨，读书通大义，不为章句，与寇莱公准、张仆射咏友善，意气相得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163622_comment'></div>太平兴国五年，偕行就举，同登进士第，释褐授大理评事、知邵州邵阳县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163622_comment'></div>政多惠利，上官以课最闻，就迁将作监丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163622_comment'></div>代还，授著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163622_comment'></div>丁外艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163622_comment'></div>时朝廷急于用材，诏起公倚庐，除殿省丞、充御史台推直官，毁不堪命，辞弗能已，就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163622_comment'></div>俄迁太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163622_comment'></div>公外疏达，议论辩以裁，举中机节而合大体，太皇数称奖，因对，面赐五品服，遂改殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163622_comment'></div>属三司判官缺员，势政以公名上，上曰：「马某材器朕自知，朕行自用之，中书无议为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163622_comment'></div>后数日，命公使江淮，采访州县治状、民俗事宜，引入受旨，赐之装金袭衣、束带、鞯勒、马彯缨，宠章殊渥，搢绅耸观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163622_comment'></div>既到部，考群吏之课，慰荐廉善三十馀员，上辄次第甄擢，后亦多至达官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163622_comment'></div>其不修者，稍平镌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163622_comment'></div>因民便利，去其苦，彻伪朝弊事细大数十条，即拜侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163622_comment'></div>还属太宗晏驾，真皇纂服，公孤直少与，左右莫为之地，故先朝所以待公之意，上未及知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163622_comment'></div>属诏百寮言事，公奏疏复忤执权者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163622_comment'></div>真皇初临御，间问大臣所以抚绥远方之意，执权因白公才可用，即出知桂州兼总广南西路兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163622_comment'></div>岭外常燠，石药发疡而终于郡，享年五十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163622_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163622_comment'></div>士之幸而得展者宜希矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163622_comment'></div>功业视其材，用舍系诸时，穷亨属乎命，是三者契而后为全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163622_comment'></div>若公者遭时盛隆，见知英主，抟扶摇而直上，追逸景以遐骋，将相必至之地也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163622_comment'></div>而鼎湖不待，明离改照，机言旁发，南服于行，终身不还，赍志长谢，岂非命耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163622_comment'></div>夫人严氏，宽明有德，年七十二，后公二十五年以殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163622_comment'></div>三男：曰绛，理识清通，风节高劲，有公望于时，历御史三院，是以似之，今为太常少卿，故公累赠至礼部尚书，夫人东海县太君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163622_comment'></div>曰绎、曰绍，无禄早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163622_comment'></div>一女，归符氏鉴，终县大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163622_comment'></div>庆历七年，始命北都置留司御史台，而奉常请行，以便襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163622_comment'></div>八年戊子十月某日，葬我公、夫人于大名县某乡某里先茔之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163622_comment'></div>某托于姻媾，平日熟闻奉常语公之故矣，及是以志文见命，谨序所闻，属以铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1163622'>堂堂公之材兮，邈邃深而崔嵬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163622_comment'></div>既逢时而利见，谓功名之余谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163622_comment'></div>帝初命公，式是南方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163622_comment'></div>鞗革玱玱，为龙为光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163622_comment'></div>按节还朝，大明继照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163622_comment'></div>孰为巧言，于藩岭表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163622_comment'></div>公在桂林，慆慆不还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163622_comment'></div>士友无戚，公髦未斑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163622_comment'></div>番山绵延，越江浩渺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163622_comment'></div>吁嗟归途，翩翩素旐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163622_comment'></div>卜新宅兮并先茔，草树接兮水泉平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163622_comment'></div>尚宜子孙多才英，永春秋兮陈芬馨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1163622_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163622'><span class='label'>按：</span>《乐全集》卷四〇。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1163622_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年10月</a>　十月，在知滁州任，有诗酬琅琊山僧智先。作品：酬琅琊山僧智先相示禅册。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷四。王智勇系此诗于皇祐元年春，据诗中“昨夜秋风扫黄叶”句改。）</span><div id='poem_495637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酬琅邪山僧智先相示禅册</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495637")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495637'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495637'>种种诸法皆心生，心自无生岂有法。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495637'>祖师来意我不知，昨夜秋风扫黄叶。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495637_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495637'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495637_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　本年，在知滁州任，游琅琊山寺，有诗。作品：游琅琊山寺。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游琅邪山寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495492")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495492'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495492'>一径过萧森，幽提此独寻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495492'>俗游殊不意，僧话粗宽心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495492'>役役真何了，空空究竟深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495492'>尘劳何日脱，来伴远公吟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495492_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495492'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495492_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　本年，在知滁州任，游琅琊山寺，得《楞伽经》，有诗。作品：读楞伽经。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_495409' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495409' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495409?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读楞伽经</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495409")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_495409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495409'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495409'>楞伽三万六千偈，百八句中成自性。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495409'>法法非法离法尘，心心无心入心病。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495409'>渐熟当似庵罗果，顿照犹如大圆镜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495409'>龟毛兔角妄有无，海浪空华不清净。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495409'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495409_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年3月</a>　三月，在知滁州任，除端明殿学士、知江宁府。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京（上元）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4d4d72dd103d4f2e9cfcaeb4c7b7bb21_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4d4d72dd103d4f2e9cfcaeb4c7b7bb21");'><span id='4d4d72dd103d4f2e9cfcaeb4c7b7bb21_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1050')">1049-1050年</a>，43-44岁</div><div id='4d4d72dd103d4f2e9cfcaeb4c7b7bb21' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年4月</a>　四月，到知江宁府任，有谢表。作品：江宁府谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江宁府谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163287")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163287'>三月二十三日，进奏院递到官告、敕牒各一道，伏蒙圣恩授臣依前官充端明殿学士，移就知江宁府，仍放朝谢者，已于四月十七日到任讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163287_comment'></div>参华秘殿，被寄名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163287_comment'></div>从便道以治行，奉宽条而署事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163287_comment'></div>宠荣蕃集，愧汗交流<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163287_comment'></div>窃念臣世系单微，天资蒙浅，褫巾未久，通籍为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163287_comment'></div>乘善养于群材，遂叨尘于显列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163287_comment'></div>沾河汉之滋泽，依日月之光华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163287_comment'></div>寖亲户牖之严，备更台阁之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163287_comment'></div>物胜权而衡殆，形过鉴以照穷，久冒龙光，倏罹箕舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163287_comment'></div>仰繄能哲，俯察所存，寘两省之近班，假一麾于便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163287_comment'></div>危心未定，渥命亟颁，蔀屋照通，陈根脉起，垢疵悉荡，坯陶更新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163287_comment'></div>此盖皇帝陛下大度开容，至仁涵育，鉴丹诚之不昧，知拙守之有常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163287_comment'></div>申穆朝猷，曲回天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163287_comment'></div>禁帷密职，复近穆清之涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163287_comment'></div>方面通都，俾当雄重之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163287_comment'></div>敢不精心以虑，来效是图，庶有获于涓埃，用酬恩于天地。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年4月</a>　四月，到知江宁府任，有谢启。作品：江宁府谢上与两地启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三四。此启所上对象不详。）</span><div id='poem_1163435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江宁府谢上与两地启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163435")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163435'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163435'>伏蒙圣恩授前件职，就移知江宁府者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163435_comment'></div>参华秘殿，易守名藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163435_comment'></div>复亲帷幄之严，仍当方面之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163435_comment'></div>宠灵蕃集，优幸殊多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163435_comment'></div>伏念某阀绪单平，性资蒙固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163435_comment'></div>早遘嘉亨之运，荐更清要之涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163435_comment'></div>内省短材，实安拙分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163435_comment'></div>区区一介之守，义不自欺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163435_comment'></div>碌碌群居之间，心无与校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163435_comment'></div>知公朝之为恃，忽险俗而弗虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163435_comment'></div>姑勉宽身之仁，竟集图全之毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163435_comment'></div>骇机激矢，奔车共尘，鲁酒致邯郸之围，枸酱开昆崙之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163435_comment'></div>国章有体，庙论无私，解籍禁扃，假麾便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163435_comment'></div>方思补过，内惕于危衷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163435_comment'></div>岂意疏恩，遽还于荣路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163435_comment'></div>垢疵一荡，坏陶再新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163435_comment'></div>此盖某官道赞穆清，诚通化育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163435_comment'></div>折金投冶，钟鼎陈于大廷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163435_comment'></div>断木就工，牺象荐于清庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163435_comment'></div>故兹甄录，远逮空疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163435_comment'></div>敢不恪守官箴，期终素履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163435_comment'></div>风雨如晦，信晨警之匪渝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163435_comment'></div>雪霜既零，保后凋之靡变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163435_comment'></div>冀酬洪覆，用报大钧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1163435_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年4月</a>　四月，在知江宁府任，有谢范仲淹启。作品：谢杭州范资政启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三二。）</span><div id='poem_1163437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢杭州范资政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163437")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163437'>兹者承恩中检，还著内朝，复亲帷幄之华，仍忝藩垣之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163437_comment'></div>光灵下逮，优幸殊多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163437_comment'></div>伏念某治世为修，散才乏用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163437_comment'></div>荐更台阁之要，久依户牖之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163437_comment'></div>窃戒惧于奔沈，每逡巡于宠利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163437_comment'></div>知公朝之为恃，忽险俗而弗虞，解籍禁扃，假麾便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163437_comment'></div>方释骈枝之累，自容蓬艾之阴，反视听于希夷，收精神于蹇浅，安诸拙分，聊以穷年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163437_comment'></div>岂意中途，遽还近缀，炎凉未易，渥泽惟新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163437_comment'></div>此盖某官时取典刑，道恢忠恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163437_comment'></div>言发乎迩，世皆信其大公；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163437_comment'></div>己则为仁，物咸蒙于平施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163437_comment'></div>致兹甄录，爰暨空疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163437_comment'></div>自省蒙姿，粗存素守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163437_comment'></div>若钧与引，宁违权度之平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163437_comment'></div>终白且坚，岂受磷缁之变？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163437_comment'></div>庶几远节，用答厚知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年6月</a>　六月，在知江宁府任，作《江宁府祭蒋山庄武帝神文》作品：江宁府祭蒋山庄武帝神文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江宁府祭蒋山庄武帝神文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163650")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163650'>维皇祐元年六月一日，端明殿学士、朝散大夫、右谏议大夫、知江宁军府兼管内劝农使、提举宣歙等州军兵甲公事、轻车都尉、赐紫金鱼袋张某，谨以清酌时果之奠，敢告于蒋山庄武帝之神：霪雨作沴，浃旬未止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163650_comment'></div>民弗宁于厥居，惧无以输上经赋，供神常事，以至于饥且穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163650_comment'></div>某非才，为之长吏，虑政不敏，以致咎罚，谋于僚佐，所以徼福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163650_comment'></div>皆曰祈雨而雨，祷霁而霁，庇祐兹土，惟帝聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163650_comment'></div>属限诏条，不得躬谒以请也，谨差将仕郎、试秘书省校书郎、行上元县张康侯以告，帝尚降鉴，矜此下民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163650_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年6月</a>　六月，在知江宁府任，作《祭真武灵应真君文》作品：祭真武灵应真君文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭真武灵应真君文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163651")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163651'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163651'>维皇祐元年六月一日，具官某谨上启真武灵应真君：某典守兹土，既无惠政，何以徼天之福，下庇吏民？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163651_comment'></div>粤惟仲夏，嘉谷既殖，霪雨不止，惧成灾沴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163651_comment'></div>瞻言灵宇，肇自前朝，区区一方，久知依奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163651_comment'></div>敢稽旧礼，仰黩威神，尚俾山川，无作霖潦，垂祐黎庶，岁以顺成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163651_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1163651_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年6月</a>　六月，在知江宁府任，作《祭谢蒋山庄武帝神文》作品：祭谢蒋山庄武帝神文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭谢蒋山庄武帝神文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163652")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163652'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163652'>维皇祐元年六月七日，具官某谨遣上元县尉张康侯以清酌庶羞之奠，敢告于蒋山庄武帝之神：昔有吴氏之开国于江左也，封内之望，实维此山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163652_comment'></div>兹土兹民，获免于灾沴札瘥之患，惟帝之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163652_comment'></div>近苦霪雨，将害田稼，故致区区，以伸虔祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163652_comment'></div>伏蒙昭答，云收氛散，庶几农穑，遂以顺成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163652_comment'></div>敢荐熟腥，往谢灵贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163652_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年6月</a>　六月，在知江宁府任，有诗。作品：金陵府署池上草堂。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金陵府署池上草堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495485")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495485'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495485'>东方千骑忝藩侯，情味都如寓一丘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495485'>客气尽将还野马，机心聊自试沙鸥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495485'>时凭静几随飞蝶，强拂危冠笑沐猴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495485'>只向公斋得嘉遁，何须远逐赤松游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495485'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年11月7日</a>　十一月七日，在知江宁府任，作《祭杨侍郎文》作品：祭杨侍郎文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。杨侍郎名不详。）</span><div id='poem_1163640' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163640' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163640?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭杨侍郎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年11月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163640")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163640_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163640'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163640'>维皇祐元年岁次己丑，十一月庚寅朔，七日丙申，端明殿学士、右谏议大夫、知江宁军府事某，谨遣府吏奉清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于工部侍郎杨公之灵：惟公道德醇厚，山高渊默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163640_comment'></div>才允文武，好是正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163640_comment'></div>振迹朝绥，飞声霜策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163640_comment'></div>遂简帝心，外为内翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163640_comment'></div>殿抚方面，景从宸极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163640_comment'></div>训辑戎策，藻绘衮职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163640_comment'></div>敷经迩英，稽古之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163640_comment'></div>戊子暮春，公致为臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163640_comment'></div>年犹未也，萧然幅巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163640_comment'></div>老成去朝，我心惨辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163640_comment'></div>爰合常僚，闺台嘉宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163640_comment'></div>供帐净卢，以祖清尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163640_comment'></div>接膝晤言，街鼓振振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163640_comment'></div>权利见规，实书诸绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163640_comment'></div>阳羡钓舟，期从公游<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163640_comment'></div>沦胥出守，愿言不酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163640_comment'></div>徙麾建康，蠡渎比疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163640_comment'></div>区区未通，俄顷炎凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163640_comment'></div>视公吉履，谓斯齯齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163640_comment'></div>天奚难谌，遽遗杖几！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163640_comment'></div>有子而才，构业必伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163640_comment'></div>嵩高维岳，土厚如削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163640_comment'></div>远即幽宅，素旌绰绰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163640_comment'></div>复命曰常，收神冲漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163640_comment'></div>属叨藩寄，阻从吊位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163640_comment'></div>念言契阔，濡膺陨涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163640_comment'></div>吁嗟乎公，歆兹一酹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163640_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1163640_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163640'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_1163640_0'>⑴ 公即席赋诗留别饯客，断章云「阳羡溪中有钓舟」。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163640_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年11月19日</a>　十一月十九日，在知江宁府任，奉敕撰《江宁府重修府署记》作品：江宁府重修府署记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1163544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江宁府重修府署记<span class='inlineComment2'>（奉敕撰　皇祐元年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年11月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163544")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163544'>庆历八年正月癸巳，江宁府署火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163544_comment'></div>自唐失政，奸豪专土，更相禽猎，或自篡袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163544_comment'></div>紫色淫声，馀分闰位，李昪冒扬徐之业，开国江左，大筑城府，僭用王制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163544_comment'></div>圣朝治定，混一区略，戈船南渡，煜归京师，彻其伪庭，度留表署，然规模壮丽，犹雄诸藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163544_comment'></div>至是火焮徼人之庐，炀谯门，延东西序、公私寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163544_comment'></div>既焉府书焚室以闻，诏遣内侍韩从礼问故，且有后命，俾营如旧度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163544_comment'></div>除龙图阁直学士、知扬州张奎右谏议大夫，领军府事，属之经治，才选也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163544_comment'></div>命发运副使许元、转运使孙甫鸠材庀工，遂以从礼护作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163544_comment'></div>奎初下车，莽然垝垣，拨煨烬，略区址，计徒庸，程事期，以赋功于群吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163544_comment'></div>元调所部方湖汇泽，章荡桴集；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163544_comment'></div>甫效七州二军之卒，以待役费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163544_comment'></div>稽以尺籍，令以鼛鼓，斲者如风，筑者如雨，茨者云舒，墁者波卷，饩廪称事，忘劳竞劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163544_comment'></div>自闰正月至于八月，合役二十二万有奇，合材用无虑二百二十万，考室七百楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163544_comment'></div>台门崔嵬，前达通逵，以表命令，彰仪范；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163544_comment'></div>公堂隆深，中敞广庭，以颁诏条，听民成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163544_comment'></div>崇榭壮雄，东辟坦场，以训军乘，严戎备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163544_comment'></div>分曹布局，旧邦鼎新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163544_comment'></div>从礼抨图复命，上嘉奎之敏于事而器干足任，被之玺书，称饰其勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163544_comment'></div>将佐吏卒率有加赐，凡民工弛其户租之半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163544_comment'></div>盖《春秋》之义，新作必书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163544_comment'></div>有诏守臣，俾著经始。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1163544_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年6月28日</a>　六月二十八日，在知江宁府任，撰《蜀州修建天目寺记》作品：蜀州修建天目寺记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1163547' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163547' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蜀州修建天目寺记</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163547")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163547'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163547'>浮屠氏之教流而至诸华也，迨晋之东，其法益炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163547_comment'></div>以大设权，实示方便，指因报，明利益，故自世主至于士民，莫不甘心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163547_comment'></div>五方异禀，四夷殊类，气俗之别，欲恶不同，法制所弗齐，礼义所弗加，甚者至有不识父，而大率辄知奉佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163547_comment'></div>百家之聚，必有一窣堵焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163547_comment'></div>两楹之室，必有一龛像焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163547_comment'></div>矧名都通邑，塔庙固错落相望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163547_comment'></div>晋原在井络之维，处陆海之沃，玉垒、铜梁之阻，金沙、银砾之骁，控犍、牂，通滇、僰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163547_comment'></div>即山而鼓，民拥素封之资；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163547_comment'></div>厥篚之华，户赢玩巧之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163547_comment'></div>即安乐土，知植福田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163547_comment'></div>郡有天目寺，城郭之最形胜，缁素之所萃聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163547_comment'></div>殿焚寇火，区址莽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163547_comment'></div>先是，郡之善男女合施鸠材，僝工构缔，既已历载，功绪弗就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163547_comment'></div>至是尚书郎王君略领州，曲台杨君玙为之倅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163547_comment'></div>二君敏材，利用周行之彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163547_comment'></div>狱市平简，吏民便安，修弊起废，出于馀力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163547_comment'></div>越皇祐初年季春哉生朏，二君相造而诹曰：「按令式，前诞节韨精庐、启梵会以祝延，而栋宇未完，像设莫备，执事者为不虔矣，顾何以示远方」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163547_comment'></div>乃移县大夫杜君济勾考财簿，部护役事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163547_comment'></div>于是境内四邑之耆老更相勉曰：「府君之志，上以恭邦典，下以为吾属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163547_comment'></div>且吾属废居射利，墆不知发，譬虫食蓼而忘其苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163547_comment'></div>佛言人命在呼吸间，一息不属，虽至亲爱，莫相为救，何嗟及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163547_comment'></div>今此道场，近在闾闬，动步而至净土，举首而见化城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163547_comment'></div>壮者游焉，有以生善念；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163547_comment'></div>老者依焉，有以发后心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163547_comment'></div>是府君为之舟航，拯吾属于溺也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163547_comment'></div>于是乐输善舍，如趋期令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163547_comment'></div>既群朴斲，且涂塈茨，役效其勤，匠究其巧，岁未云半，仁祠鼎新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163547_comment'></div>为大殿八楹，环属四阿，廊庑回合，屹若山，灿如霞，桷雕栾文，㮰花鬘藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163547_comment'></div>盖中为大毗庐遮那像，文殊、普贤二大士左右之，相好殊胜，彩饰妙丽，紫金光聚，极于壮严，兜罗绵网，依然开合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163547_comment'></div>殿之四周，图华严九会，显佛国之神化，增法门之壮观也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163547_comment'></div>寺有阿育王塔，尝见光相，亶有灵迹，凌空危耸，与殿对峙，自兹宝地，方为具足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163547_comment'></div>既庆成，邑人大和会，踊跃赞叹，欷歔瞻礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163547_comment'></div>以为须弥灯座，宝华严饰，庵罗树园，金色明净，昔未尝有，乃今复现，信一方之功德海，四众之甘露门也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163547_comment'></div>二君皆余旧，置邮以布其事，请有以示之后者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163547_comment'></div>余详二君之为，抑可谓仁术也欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163547_comment'></div>君子之教民，驱而纳诸善而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163547_comment'></div>二君之为也，本于严朝章，因以导民善，是亦仁术也矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163547_comment'></div>异夫举土木之役，而事观游亭榭之娱者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163547_comment'></div>斯可以记矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163547_comment'></div>会中檀越、比丘众等，盖著之石阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163547_comment'></div>皇祐二年六月二十八日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1163547_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　夏，在知江宁府任，有诗呈韩综、令狐挺。作品：金陵久旱喜雨呈运使韩综学士提刑令狐挺祠部及示诸府僚。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_495434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495434' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金陵久旱喜雨呈运使韩综学士提刑令狐挺祠部及示诸府僚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495434")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495434_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495434'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495434'>江城风日燥将燃，喜此滂沱仅有年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495434_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495434'>诸泽气交阴压地，四溟水立阔围天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495434_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495434'>廓开紫宙清凉界，顿去骄阳跋扈权。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495434_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495434'>须信化工人可代，傅岩才业在三篇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495434_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495434'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495434_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　夏，在知江宁府任，有诗和令狐挺。作品：提刑祠部和前篇猥为祷祈之应辄复次韵且以见志。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_495435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>提刑祠部再和前篇猥为祷祈之应辄复次韵且以见志</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495435")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495435'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495435'>长吏忧民深望岁，诸侯闵雨著编年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495435'>鹅鲜聊用遵明诏，尪鼻何能感上天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495435'>五事肃时敛在宥，九功美利属持权。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495435'>守藩无状惟推分，必在蒙庄内外篇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495435_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495435'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495435_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　夏，在知江宁府任，送屐与韩综，有诗。作品：送屐韩仲文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送屐韩仲文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495486")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495486'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495486'>江南到梅暑，蒸湿鲜晴明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495486'>聊仿登山样，无妨涉水行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495486'>齿牢防易折，蜡滑亦加轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495486'>早幸还吾土，閒将挂后楹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495486_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495486'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495486_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年11月8日</a>　十一月八日，在知江宁府任，作文祭嵇颖。作品：祭舅氏翰林学士嵇公文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。）</span><div id='poem_1163638' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163638' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163638?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭舅氏翰林学士嵇公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1050年11月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163638")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163638_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163638'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163638'>维皇祐二年岁次庚寅，十一月甲申朔，八日辛卯，谨遣家仆，以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于故舅氏翰林学士、谯国公之灵：某粤在童年，早依外氏，惟舅文行，是亲是师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163638_comment'></div>广平君之严明<span class='inlineComment2'>（外王母宋氏。）</span>，南阳君之慈懿<span class='inlineComment2'>（舅前夫人滕氏。）</span>，训诲鞠育，遂偕宾兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163638_comment'></div>策名六科，入游两禁，历践台省，周旋显要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163638_comment'></div>舅繇文馆，乃登掖垣，十年京华，联步朝闼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163638_comment'></div>瞻言母党之重，实兼僚友之欢，休浣更过，笑言莫逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163638_comment'></div>漆园、柱下，《楞伽》、《净名》，相期逍遥之游，两忘契会之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163638_comment'></div>委势利于尘滓，遗生死于幻泡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163638_comment'></div>夫物芒芒，不屑顾已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163638_comment'></div>前年小子，遘闵南徂，仓卒去国，舅又卧疾，不及执手，折简叙违，永阳、秣陵，再周岁籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163638_comment'></div>岂谓此别，遂成永诀！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163638_comment'></div>前者七月，犹得手书，草札数行，盖已扶病，辞意悽怆，异于常时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163638_comment'></div>老母阅之，即为大戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163638_comment'></div>小子犹谓：兹无忧者，乃舅宿疾，间年辄发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163638_comment'></div>叔平讣至，竟如母言，承问骇怛，殒心摧臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163638_comment'></div>老母号绝，痛不忍闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163638_comment'></div>嗟嗟苍天，孰主张是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163638_comment'></div>吉人君子，胡不寿考？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163638_comment'></div>长子先逝，遗稚藐然，孤榇东归，匍匐莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163638_comment'></div>念言思此，悲来填膺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163638_comment'></div>戚丈信来，云有理命，百日之内，即安旧茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163638_comment'></div>先公夫人，南阳贤淑，复与爱子，共此泉壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163638_comment'></div>九原可作，神所慰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163638_comment'></div>戚信仍说，舅自卧疾，迨于顺化，晏然沉寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163638_comment'></div>一念不动，得《首楞严》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163638_comment'></div>本无去来，亦何所住？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163638_comment'></div>幻身虽灭，我又何悲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163638_comment'></div>寄怀此辞，示同世谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163638_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1163638_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年闰11月8日</a>　闰十一月八日，在知江宁府任，加龙图阁学士，迁给事中，移知杭州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
滑县（白马）
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　夏，在知滑州任，有谢赐新历日表。作品：滑州谢赐新历日表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163279?labeling=true' target='_blank'>滑州谢赐新历日表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163279")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163279_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163279'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163279'>王官底日，考历以正天端；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163279_comment'></div>侯御奉时，告朔而赋民政<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163279_comment'></div>伏以尊号皇帝陛下乾图绍统，宝数在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163279_comment'></div>推轩策于明堂，五气以治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163279_comment'></div>合舜时于方岳，七政以齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163279_comment'></div>臣罢职禁林，分符畿服，捧新书于芝检，增旧恋于蓂阶。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1163279_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年7月</a>　七月，在知滑州任，迁户部侍郎，徙知益州，以父老子幼，上表乞免知益州。作品：免知益州表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免知益州表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163292")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163292'>今月十五日递到告、敕各一道，伏蒙圣恩授臣端明殿学士兼翰林侍读学士、尚书户部侍郎、知益州军州事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163292_comment'></div>左户美官，西区重寄，敢期推择，俯及庸虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163292_comment'></div>惊惶失图，进退无措<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163292_comment'></div>臣涉猎经术，遭逢圣明，越分踰能，连阶累仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163292_comment'></div>周旋侍从之职，践更清要之途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163292_comment'></div>风议无长，猷为弗建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163292_comment'></div>向终苴制，择守辅藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163292_comment'></div>报政靡闻，方积简书之畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163292_comment'></div>陟恩逮下，遽当方面之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163292_comment'></div>地官亚卿，坤维巨屏，宠灵殊渥，跼蹐为增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163292_comment'></div>念臣父当传老之年，而臣抱终鲜之戚，有息皆幼，于宗弗蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163292_comment'></div>顾温甘之所须，岂晨昏之可舍？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163292_comment'></div>惟拜嘉之诚厚，敢有腼以自居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163292_comment'></div>情所不安，义亦何处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163292_comment'></div>伏惟尊号皇帝陛下宇宙同广，曜魄并明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163292_comment'></div>测远方之民，深期于镇辑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163292_comment'></div>访大廷之议，误致于简抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163292_comment'></div>圣治难逢，私怀为迫，敢期远照，俯及丹衷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163292_comment'></div>布朝家天地之仁，徇臣子庭闱之志，追寝成命，选除通材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163292_comment'></div>他日捐生，敢惜螳螂之臂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163292_comment'></div>此时反哺，幸伸乌鸟之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163292_comment'></div>辄竭寸诚，仰祈洪造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1163292_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年7月</a>　七月，在知滑州任，迁户部侍郎，徙知益州，以父老子幼，上劄子乞免知益州。作品：免知益州劄子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>免知益州劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163293")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163293'>臣伏蒙圣恩，除臣端明殿学士兼翰林侍读学士、尚书户部侍郎、知益州，已具表辞让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163293_comment'></div>章奏之文，不尽诚悃，敢披愚恳，再黩天聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163293_comment'></div>伏以益州方面至重，朝廷委任推择至精，臣以庸虚，猥当简寄，滥加崇秩，荣兼近职，揆才揣分，忝冒逾涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163293_comment'></div>但臣父年高，旁无兼侍，昨受秦州之命，亦尝缘此自陈，事播朝班，言存圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163293_comment'></div>况今益州除授，宠利两优，虽国家任人自有大体，而缙绅所指实贻清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163293_comment'></div>敢望大明委照，洪慈亭育，垂怜拙守，加悯孤踪，许臣以见官留满今任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163293_comment'></div>犬马之力，期后效于驱驰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163293_comment'></div>乌鸟微情，庶获伸于哺养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163293_comment'></div>望阙待命，不任陨越。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1163293_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
华阴
-----detail

-----end



-----title
华县（郑县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c8521271fa5f4cb7a8c67c8c2836c2e9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c8521271fa5f4cb7a8c67c8c2836c2e9");'><span id='c8521271fa5f4cb7a8c67c8c2836c2e9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>，48岁</div><div id='c8521271fa5f4cb7a8c67c8c2836c2e9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>十月，赴益州任，途经华州西溪，有诗。作品：华州西溪。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span><div id='poem_495521' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495521' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495521?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华州西溪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495521")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495521_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495521'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495521'>西溪殊近郭，少华更当轩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495521'>竹径通华表，松庭接绀园。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495521_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495521'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495521_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>十月，赴益州任，途经华州，有诗寄杜衍。作品：相国杜公旧里钱唐，有别墅在华下，公既得谢，留寓睢阳，因家焉。某近赴益部，过三峰，闻华人之望公舍而不还，又顾吾乡之独幸，国老处焉。因道西人之意，成长句四韵，奉寄杜公。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span><div id='poem_495529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>相国杜公旧里钱唐有别野在华下既得谢留寓睢阳因家焉某近赴益部过三峰闻华人之望公舍而不还又顾吾乡之独幸国老处焉因道西人之意成长句四韵奉寄杜公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495529")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495529_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495529'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495529'>谋国有劳新史在，挂车无第旧乡遥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495529'>睢阳图记光耆彦<span class='inlineComment2'>（季本、陶本、清抄本作旧）</span>，华下风烟遂寂寥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495529'>紫气尚劳关吏思，甘棠犹播陜民谣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495529'>莲花峰下仙人掌，高出云端若奉招。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495529_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495529'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495529_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

岐山

-----title

-----detail

-----title
略阳（长举）

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>，48岁</div><div id='0cb11ed8c26f46fc8c8d4583744a0035' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年10月</a>　十月，赴益州任，途经青泥岭，有诗。作品：青泥岭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span><div id='poem_495520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>青泥岭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495520")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495520'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495520'>斗峻凌霄出混茫，东西秦蜀此分疆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495520'>萦纡断涧千寻曲，回合危峦万叠苍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495520'>烟外孤村通鸟径，云间盘道绕羊肠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495520'>朝家方面非轻寄，何事徘徊望故乡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495520'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年10月</a>　十月，赴益州任，途经长举飞石阁，有诗。作品：兴州长举县西二十里阁道，立表曰飞石阁，告往来者急度勿停。予赴益部，兴州将吏来迎，皆至长举，因访老吏飞石之状，云昔尝有之，亦飘风暴雨之时也。予望山顶皆已垦耕，而行人熟虚名，至是皆驰过，因成一绝。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span><div id='poem_495526' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495526' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495526?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴州长举县西二十里阁道立表曰飞石阁告往来者急度勿停予赴益部兴州将吏来迎皆至长举因访老吏飞石之状云昔尝有之亦飘风暴雨之时也予望山顶皆已垦耕而行人熟虚名至是皆驰过因成一绝</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495526")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495526_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495526'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495526'>蜀道循山多险巇，行人独此策征羁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495526_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495526'>人情多为虚名怯，鹤唳风声走老氐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495526_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495526'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495526_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年10月23日</a>　十月二十三日，赴益州任，途经长举县东药水岩，有诗。作品：药水岩诗。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span><div id='poem_495539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>药水岩诗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495539")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495539_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_495539_0'>① 武兴长举县东十里药水亭下，官道三四里，乱石峥嵘，流泉迸激，峻岭十四盘而至石洞，悬乳三，皆径围二三尺。下有石臼，容可四五斗。石泉寻乳下滴臼中，溢而流入嘉陵江。洞外有大石砥平，云仙人鍊药台也。俗传此泉饮者愈宿痾。予过而步游焉。冰雪千岩，松风万壑，崎岖仅能至，不通骑也，因留长句。时甲午十月二十三日。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495539'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495539'>灵泉一派蜀江通，源出苍崖古洞中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495539'>乳滴云根苔臼满，药成仙灶石台空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495539'>琼缨珠络千岩霤，瑶瑟琅箫万壑风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495539'>杯勺已忻清病骨，刀圭敢望变衰容。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495539'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495539_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年10月</a>　十月，赴益州任，途经兴州飞仙岭，有诗。作品：飞仙岭阁。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span>乱石溪。<span <div class='label1' id='6bbf4f028a384852b0e11805de8dc8e3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6bbf4f028a384852b0e11805de8dc8e3");'><span id='6bbf4f028a384852b0e11805de8dc8e3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>，48岁</div><div id='6bbf4f028a384852b0e11805de8dc8e3' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em;
