color: gray;'>▪</span>十月，赴益州任，途经嘉川驿西散水岩，有诗。作品：散水岩漱玉亭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span><div id='poem_495531' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495531' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495531?labeling=true' target='_blank'>散水岩漱玉亭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495531")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495531_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_495531_0'>① 在嘉川驿西，水从峰顶迸落三节，而缘崖为瀑布，入涧合于江</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495531'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495531'>高从云际落崔嵬，疑决银潢一派来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495531'>散漫难收珠网绽，琤瑽不断玉山摧。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495531'>寻源谁到烟霞路，税驾聊倾沆瀣杯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495531'>向暮危亭上灯火，水精帘下烛房开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495531_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495531'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495531_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
剑阁（剑门）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='380e66b657bb46c4a6733c880ab68cfb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("380e66b657bb46c4a6733c880ab68cfb");'><span id='380e66b657bb46c4a6733c880ab68cfb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>，48岁</div><div id='380e66b657bb46c4a6733c880ab68cfb' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>十月，赴益州任，途经剑门关，有诗。作品：剑门关。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span><div id='poem_495527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>剑门关</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495527")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495527_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495527'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495527'>地维绝脉摧鳌足，天垒横霄壮井舆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495527'>谁轧祸萌通鸟道，古为风土感鱼凫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495527'>壶中日月邻方外，海内山河入帝图。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495527'>过此益知方面重，万兵开府一寒儒。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495527_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495527'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495527_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>十月，赴益州任，途经上亭驿，有诗。作品：上亭驿。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。系年据《乐全集》卷三《药水岩诗》序。）</span><div id='poem_495530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上亭驿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495530")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495530_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_495530_0'>① 在剑州武连县西四十里。传云唐明皇西幸到此，雨中闻铃声感怀，命伶人写之乐府，名《雨淋铃》</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495530'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495530'>雨中驻跸此闻铃，当日梨园写此声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495530'>忽忽悲心自多感，铃声何事怆人情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495530_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495530'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495530_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
成都（成都府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0f6f8dd9e5bc42eabbfbc0264cd56769_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0f6f8dd9e5bc42eabbfbc0264cd56769");'><span id='0f6f8dd9e5bc42eabbfbc0264cd56769_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1056')">1054-1056年</a>，48-50岁</div><div id='0f6f8dd9e5bc42eabbfbc0264cd56769' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年11月</a>　十一月，到益州任，有谢表。作品：益州谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163295' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163295' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163295?labeling=true' target='_blank'>益州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163295")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163295'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163295'>蜀控西面，益为大藩，临守之难，畀付为重，兹既署事，实深惴怀<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163295_comment'></div>伏念臣资地本寒，机悟殊浅，偶缘朴学，进会休辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163295_comment'></div>久尘侍从之涂，荐更华要之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163295_comment'></div>曾微云补之效，第忘内疚之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163295_comment'></div>一昨起奉慈宸，出分寰服，乌鸟之情甚乐，犬羊之鞟自宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163295_comment'></div>适偶清衷，深图远御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163295_comment'></div>庸殿一都之会，专钤两道之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163295_comment'></div>枯朽见雕，款段仍驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163295_comment'></div>复冒宠升之命，无容固让之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163295_comment'></div>锦里旧城，陆海千里，军屯整睦，民俗阜康，讼事不烦，邀嬉多暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163295_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下内全哲惠，旁达聪明，谓常预于枢机，知颇存于谨厚，可行宽诏，以抚遐方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163295_comment'></div>谨当精究事为，修明纪律，冀成安辑之效，持答圣神之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163295_comment'></div>愧腼瞻天，跼蹐无地。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1163295_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年11月</a>　十一月，在知益州任，遣散因妄言侬智高寇蜀所增弓手，罢筑城之役。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　冬，在知益州任，荐雷简夫知雅州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　冬，在知益州任，访蜀中异士，始知苏洵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年1月</a>　正月，在知益州任，值上元观灯，令三夜不闭城门以安蜀民。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年2月</a>　二月，在知益州任，因天旱，作祈雨词。作品：祈雨醮坛词。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三五。系年据文中“迄此仲春”一语。）</span><div id='poem_1163653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祈雨醮坛词<span class='inlineComment2'>（成都府）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163653")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163653'>臣闻惟天洪覆，斡万化之生成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163653_comment'></div>惟人至诚，通上灵之鉴格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163653_comment'></div>敢申悃愊，仰黩高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163653_comment'></div>粤兹井络之疆，遐处一都之会，田穰有限，生齿寖繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163653_comment'></div>民勤稼绩之功，岁无水旱之沴，顾赋租之仅给，犹衣食以不充，矧非顺成，即致荒散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163653_comment'></div>比从改岁，迄此仲春，三农作务之时，九种播殖之候，时晹过度，雨泽愆期，精祷未孚，众情同恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163653_comment'></div>臣忝膺朝寄，长此吏民，内愧匪才，不能称职，且惧政刑之谬，上累阴阳之和，宜以微躯，独当阴谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163653_comment'></div>所祈甘澍，早及大田，庶济黔黎，免罹灾害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163653_comment'></div>臣无任恳祷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163653_comment'></div>谨词。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1163653_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年3月</a>　三月，在知益州任，就益、梓、利、夔四路卖户绝庄田事上疏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　本年，在知益州任，与苏洵论古今治乱，并荐其为成都学官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　本年，在知益州任，奏闻毛安舆守孝事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年3月</a>　三月，在知益州任，撰书荐苏洵于欧阳修，以六科勉励苏轼、苏辙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　夏秋间，在知益州任，因蜀人乞求留任，朝廷赐诏奖谕，有谢表。作品：益州谢诏书奖谕表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>益州谢诏书奖谕表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163296")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163296'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163296'>进奏院递到敕书一道，以益州路转运使奏，据本州吏民乞留臣满三年，伏蒙圣恩特降奖谕者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163296_comment'></div>锡命自天，恍日星之下烛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163296_comment'></div>跼身无地，懔渊谷以内惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163296_comment'></div>惟功善之不闻，冒宠灵之误及，省循无状，愧懔兼怀<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163296_comment'></div>臣闻汉宣帝之励精，留思良吏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163296_comment'></div>唐明皇之求治，注意外官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163296_comment'></div>然如胶东、颍川，治有异等之效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163296_comment'></div>济阳、河内，事昭将顺之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163296_comment'></div>方被玺书之褒，而蒙丝言之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163296_comment'></div>前朝盛事，旧史美谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163296_comment'></div>如臣者所蕴虚疏，见拔孤远，早玷清华之选，久陪英俊之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163296_comment'></div>顷自禁严，外分藩翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163296_comment'></div>维益部一都之会，据坤隅千里之疆，气俗剽轻，货利繁错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163296_comment'></div>比守臣之弹治，习旧事之便宜，居然方面之雄，称为权寄之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163296_comment'></div>独顾行能之下，亦叨推择之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163296_comment'></div>然颇知狱市者为政所先，赋役者治人之本，戒诸苛扰，务在平均，良用拙勤，粗免隳斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163296_comment'></div>不意吏民举浮浅之迹，朝廷敦奖劝之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163296_comment'></div>细札十行，置邮百舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163296_comment'></div>善声不著，方虞责问之来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163296_comment'></div>荣号所加，适取虚名之诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163296_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下凝神象表，垂统化元，盛节隆乎中和，美利充乎高厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163296_comment'></div>君视臣如心膂，允谓至仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163296_comment'></div>天自民之聪明，故无遗听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163296_comment'></div>百城耸观，遐俗知荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163296_comment'></div>臣敢不上体宸慈，下修官业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163296_comment'></div>率励愚柔之性，无怠百千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163296_comment'></div>答扬覆照之恩，少裨万一。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1163296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年8月</a>　八月，在知益州任，迁三司使，有谢表。作品：谢除三司使表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除三司使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163297")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163297_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163297'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163297'>伏蒙圣恩授臣依前尚书户部侍郎充三司使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163297_comment'></div>驿遽奔涂，虔趋于严召；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163297_comment'></div>芝函锡命，进冒于宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163297_comment'></div>俾专筦计之烦，实玷难才之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163297_comment'></div>势名参重，腼汗交盈<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163297_comment'></div>伏念臣朴鄙孤生，孱疏近器，夙遌尧文之郁，荐膺汉诏之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163297_comment'></div>緤组朝闱，滥巾儒馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163297_comment'></div>职箴规于兽省，记言动于螭涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163297_comment'></div>蒙擢掖垣，遂登禁署，中司执宪，会府理财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163297_comment'></div>蹉跌外除，因循十稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163297_comment'></div>比自日畿之近，徙临蜀表之遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163297_comment'></div>勉布宽条，汔宁远俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163297_comment'></div>绩幽宜绌，覆广惟私，亟蒙瑞节之华，归奉燕朝之觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163297_comment'></div>不谓尚存睿眷，前出制音，繇左户之班联，商大农之功利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163297_comment'></div>夫以会计之重，赋入有经，惟货盈虚，系时休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163297_comment'></div>方今边警虽彻，而列屯犹厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163297_comment'></div>年谷鲜登，而沈冗为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163297_comment'></div>调度既繁，储用几蹶，岂宜懦品，窃假要权？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163297_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下乾健垂明，宸慈广爱，误以愚朴，目为干臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163297_comment'></div>谓岁代之最深，久更已试；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163297_comment'></div>察羁踪之自立，素不因人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163297_comment'></div>优以职仪，俾之器使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163297_comment'></div>敢不力求奸弊，颛讲富彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163297_comment'></div>事有可为，固自宜于竭尽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163297_comment'></div>众之所避，亦无惮于设施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163297_comment'></div>誓坚忠荩之忱，上答简求之造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1163297_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年8月</a>　八月，在知益州任，迁三司使，有除三司使笏记。作品：除三司使笏记。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三〇。）</span><div id='poem_1163399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除三司使笏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163399")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163399'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163399'>伏蒙圣恩赐臣官告、敕牒各一道，除臣前件职任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163399_comment'></div>聚人曰财，为国重务，非材冒据，危悃奚安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163399_comment'></div>伏念臣亲逢盛期，早登近缀，曩繇风宪，擢领利权，契阔十年，屯夷一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163399_comment'></div>召从僰道，还复计廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163399_comment'></div>精力耗于流年，忧责深于畴日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163399_comment'></div>宠灵踰分，熏厉交怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163399_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下天意念劳，慈衷轸旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163399_comment'></div>察官成之已试，谓岁伐之最深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163399_comment'></div>属兹筦计之烦，爰奉时才之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163399_comment'></div>敢不力图利弊，精讲盈虚，知无不为，思所未至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163399_comment'></div>庶积涓尘之效，少酬盖载之私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1163399_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
天水（成纪）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='03e76105156a41e39e2042a1ebb26b5e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("03e76105156a41e39e2042a1ebb26b5e");'><span id='03e76105156a41e39e2042a1ebb26b5e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1062')">1060-1062年</a>，54-56岁</div><div id='03e76105156a41e39e2042a1ebb26b5e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　夏，到知秦州任，有谢表。作品：秦州谢上表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二八。）</span><div id='poem_1163308' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163308' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163308?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163308")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163308_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163308'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163308'>昨奉敕命，差充秦凤路马步军都部署、经略安抚使、兼知秦州军州，已于今月二十七日到任署上讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163308_comment'></div>一都之会，控制西陲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163308_comment'></div>两使之符，谬膺中选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163308_comment'></div>爰此布条之始，实深思职之忧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163308_comment'></div>伏念臣起自孤平，表惟疏拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163308_comment'></div>入朝荷橐，蚤次于禁涂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163308_comment'></div>出守腰章，屡当于方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163308_comment'></div>任隆有责，效薄未酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163308_comment'></div>曩辞邦计之烦，获假留都之近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163308_comment'></div>迹依乡国，情展亲闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163308_comment'></div>方幸便安，俄叨简擢，进除省座，往殿冀门，护岐陇之师屯，抚洮河之种落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163308_comment'></div>虽连牧之寄尤重，顾晨昏之养难违，因上达于恳诚，屡烦纡于诏督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163308_comment'></div>曲形公议，莫徇私怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163308_comment'></div>驱畅毂以戒涂，敢稽严旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163308_comment'></div>奉安舆而至部，幸慰慈颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163308_comment'></div>此盖尊号皇帝陛下爱物无私，使人以旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163308_comment'></div>恢天下之度，何远而不柔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163308_comment'></div>付阃外之权，惟才而是用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163308_comment'></div>良惭菲陋，曷称旁求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163308_comment'></div>幸今边警之晏然，上体圣谟之共此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163308_comment'></div>敢不殚竭精虑，详求远图，期刑政之得中，副乾坤之平施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163308_comment'></div>内面丹阙，乃心一诚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1163308_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年9月</a>　九月，在知秦州任，上疏奏西夏事宜。作品：奏夏州事宜。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二二。系年据《乐全集》卷二二《秦州奏唂斯啰事第二状》）</span><div id='poem_1163180' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163180' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163180?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏夏州事宜</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163180")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163180_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163180'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163180'>近者夏戎寖骄慢，所遣贡贺首领辄假窃官号，凌僭之状暴著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163180_comment'></div>臣在秦州，虽去谅祚住坐处远，然边事相关，颇知其动静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163180_comment'></div>夏人数易西蕃，前年交兵，数为董毡摧败，忙宗、车明等族因此搆衅被诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163180_comment'></div>谅祚既除权迫，遂怀侈汰，观其妄作，盖是狂童野心，非同元昊之权谲变诈、豪勇神断者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163180_comment'></div>初，元昊欲阻命，先威服诸戎，潜通契丹，结辅车之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163180_comment'></div>法令明审，能用其众，战胜而无轻狃之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163180_comment'></div>虽覆军杀将，然不过邀卤获之利，所破城堡亦不能有也，不五七年，其力已自困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163180_comment'></div>况使一举而有所不利，其势固无以复振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163180_comment'></div>幸朝廷抚徕，遂至纳款，犹终不敢极上僭之恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163180_comment'></div>今此狂童，只缘诛三强族，自谓人莫我敢忤，辄尔骄盈，北连兵于契丹，南结仇于邈川，睥睨中国，欲负恩信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163180_comment'></div>其经事旧人盖惧其敢行诛戮，虽有忠谋善意，莫为之尽其实，上下离贰，其部族苦于苛敛，若其妄动，恐或是其自取亡散之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163180_comment'></div>以臣愚见，惟望朝廷严戒边吏，但远斥候，缮堡壁，除戎器，虏寇或至，谨据要害，以守境保民，勿与争锋逐利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163180_comment'></div>精遣间谍，重开赏募，以招纳其亡叛，而溃其心腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163180_comment'></div>此今日御戎之上策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163180_comment'></div>且戎寇屯集，不能旷月日相持，恃持重可以敝之，但使集而无大利，自难再举矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163180_comment'></div>傥忿不思难，虐用其众，契丹窥其衅，邈川乘其敝，至于帐下之变，势且有之，天其或者昊贼之馀殃，其将降罚此虏也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1163180_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年5月</a>　五月，在知秦州任，闻宋祁卒，作诗悼之。作品：闻翰林承旨宋子京尚书捐馆。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。据《续资治通鉴长编》卷一九三，宋祁卒于嘉祐六年五月丁酉（十五日））</span><div id='poem_495451' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495451' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495451?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻翰林承旨宋子京尚书捐馆</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495451")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495451_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495451'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495451'>平昔雍容两禁游，共陪帷幄奉咨谋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495451'>功名不到麒麟阁，词赋空传鹦鹉洲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495451'>事业三朝虚物望，声华一代擅风流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495451'>清时只作文章老，谁识深怀蕴九畴。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495451_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495451'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495451_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年8月</a>　八月，在知秦州任，上疏奏唂斯啰事。作品：秦州奏唂斯啰事第一状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二二。系年据《乐全集》卷二二《秦州奏唂斯啰事第二状》）</span><div id='poem_1163178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦州奏唂厮啰事第一状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163178")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163178'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163178'>唂厮啰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，本名欺南陵温篯逋，西域武三咩人，盖唐吐蕃之裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163178_comment'></div>吐蕃在唐为大国，威长夷狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163178_comment'></div>大中以后，部族衰散，然其种贵，羌戎至今尊服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163178_comment'></div>武三咩去今唂厮啰所居青唐城，经隔诸番极远，其祖父名字未详，但传自唐已来世袭为结逋<span class='inlineComment2'>（据译：结逋，天子之号，乃僭也。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163178_comment'></div>太宗朝，李继迁大为边患，西鄙不堪其扰，设重购以募诸戎讨贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163178_comment'></div>既而西凉府首领潘罗支应募杀继迁，赏典未行而德明纳款，朝廷受之，潘罗支竟为德明所破，盖无遗类，以故西蕃无主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163178_comment'></div>蕃部耸昌厮均等远赴三咩，迎温篯逋以保其地，时年十二岁，欲就河州起立文法<span class='inlineComment2'>（起立文法，盖施设号令统众之意。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163178_comment'></div>有宗哥城蕃僧李遵与邈川首领温逋奇诱略温篯逋入国州城<span class='inlineComment2'>（即唐廓州。）</span>，遂成立文法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163178_comment'></div>渐次蕃部归顺，赴宗哥城住坐，娶李遵女，以遵为论逋<span class='inlineComment2'>（论逋，汉语宰相也。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163178_comment'></div>祥符八年秋，唂厮啰遣蕃部杜作往秦州东北断头山扇动蕃部，欲别立文法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163178_comment'></div>至九年春，南市蕃部郭厮敦引唂厮啰，复遣李遵、鱼角蝉等领众寇边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163178_comment'></div>曹玮令蕃官李厮那金伺知情实，领兵邀战，于三都谷口大败贼众，遁归本道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163178_comment'></div>明年，又遣免药耳丁等诸羌兵马入寇三都谷度龙口，曹玮复破之，蕃众退由野吴谷，截山过永宁等寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163178_comment'></div>玮又遣兵追至哑儿硖西再战，汉兵不利而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163178_comment'></div>鱼角蝉遂留古渭，欲招集番部，玮令首领张小哥<span class='inlineComment2'>（今讷支蔺毡祖。）</span>挠散之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163178_comment'></div>李遵又使唂厮啰领兵往西凉府，有所讨伐，而以败归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163178_comment'></div>唂厮啰怨为李遵所使，因而搆憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163178_comment'></div>李遵侄讷厮结等窃诱唂厮啰往邈川城，就温逋奇住坐，以温逋奇为论逋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163178_comment'></div>至天圣九年十二月，温逋奇遣𡖦𡖦赍番字鞍马、乳香入汉，告称唂厮啰乞通和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163178_comment'></div>秦州以闻，蒙朝廷宣赐唂厮啰、温逋奇对衣、金束带、银器、衣著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163178_comment'></div>后又差人入汉进谢恩马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163178_comment'></div>准天圣十年九月六日宣，唂厮啰除宁远大将军、爱州团练使，每月支大䌽一十五疋，角茶一十五觔，散茶五十觔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163178_comment'></div>温逋奇除归德将军，月支大䌽十疋，角茶五觔，散茶五十觔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163178_comment'></div>因赐物有差，温逋奇复叛，幽唂厮啰，置阱中防守，而身领兵他出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163178_comment'></div>防守人同谋出唂厮啰，收集人马，以拒温逋奇，闭城相持，温逋奇败死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163178_comment'></div>因此，遂于青唐城住坐至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163178_comment'></div>景祐二年十二月，除授保顺军节察留后，月支大䌽三十疋，角茶三十觔，散茶一百觔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163178_comment'></div>宝元元年十二月，除保顺军节度使，每年支大䌽一千疋，角茶一千觔，散茶一千五百觔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163178_comment'></div>至康定二年正月，除保顺、河西等军节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163178_comment'></div>自后郊禋并蒙加恩，至祫享恩命，即今系推诚顺化忠亮翊戴功臣、西番邈川大首领、保顺河西等军节度使、洮州凉州管内观察处置押番落等使、特进、检校太尉、使持节洮州凉州诸军事、洮州凉州刺史、兼御史大夫、上柱国、武威郡开国公、食邑九千户、食实封二千四百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163178_comment'></div>见住青唐历精耶卑城，唐廓州也，去汉约一千二百馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163178_comment'></div>盖番俗以其慈厚，故呼为唂厮啰，年约六十五六岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163178_comment'></div>即不知所管部族兵马的确，谨具本末奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1163178_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163178'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_1163178_0'>⑴ 据译：佛谓唂，儿为厮啰，汉语佛儿也。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163178_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年2月</a>　二月，在知秦州任，于秦州后园春宴，有诗赠刘几。作品：秦州后园春宴赠部署刘几阁使。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦州后园春宴赠部署刘几阁使<span class='inlineComment2'>（几深晓音律）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495481")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495481'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495481'>柳暗三眠困，花繁二月香<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495481'>情怀当酒尽，兴味为春长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495481'>叠鼓渔阳节，清讴北里妆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495481'>阶前乐无误，席上有周郎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495481'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495481_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495481'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_495481_0'>⑴ 自注：秦州后园有二月花，开最早，每艳甚盛，绝有清香。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495481_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年2月</a>　二月，在知秦州任，晚宴即席赋诗。作品：秦州晚宴即席示诸宾僚。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦州晚宴即席示诸宾僚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495482")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495482'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495482'>秦川节物似西川，二月风光已不寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495482'>犹去清明三候远，忽惊烂漫一春残。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495482'>香随芳树频移席，晴爱遥山久凭栏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495482'>却忆京华胜游处，常为暮景促归鞍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495482_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495482'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495482_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　春，在知秦州任，有诗。作品：秦州即事。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。王智勇系此诗于嘉祐五年，此诗写春景，又据诗末“戍满归心动，先随渭水东”句，当作于嘉祐七年春。）</span><div id='poem_495480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦州即事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495480")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495480'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495480'>边清羽书息，事简使君慵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495480'>地僻俗客少，日长春睡浓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495480'>平安三路火<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，昏晓两山钟<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：南山、北山皆有钟。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495480'>戍满归心动，先随渭水东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495480'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495480'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_495480_0'>⑴ 自注：秦州烽火候，自沿边三路而来。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495480_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年8月10日</a>　八月十日，在知秦州任，因司马光劾奏其怯懦轻举，徙知应天府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　本年，在知秦州任，有诗。作品：陇西郡麦积山有献白鹿者洁如霜雪驯养逾年放归旧山十二韵。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_495483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陇西郡麦积山有献白鹿者洁如霜雪驯养逾年放归旧山十二韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495483")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495483'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495483'>地得金方正，山藏灵物珍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495483'>月宫遗玉兔，仙仗失霜麟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495483'>乳窦冰泉冷，晴原露草春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495483'>清风生涧壑，高格对松筠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495483'>久卧常存息，凝思若养神。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495483'>烟崖一蹭蹬，华馆久埃尘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495483'>我意本云水，无心爱佩绅。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495483'>平生厌俗客，待尔当嘉宾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495483'>萧洒襟情远，虚恬气韵真。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495483'>桧轩同鹤静，竹渚伴鸥驯。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495483'>龟智沾骊血，牺纯被绣巾。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495483'>放归旧林麓，好去避虞人。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495483_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495483'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_495483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　本年，在知秦州任，再上疏奏唂斯啰事。作品：秦州奏唂斯啰事第二状。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷二二。系年据《乐全集》卷二二《秦州奏唂斯啰事第二状》）</span><div id='poem_1163179' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163179' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163179?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦州奏唂厮啰事第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163179")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163179_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163179'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163179'>臣自受命知秦州，到任体问边事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163179_comment'></div>本州西路堡寨熟户蕃部之外，即与西蕃唂厮啰地界相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163179_comment'></div>顷年唂厮啰有长男瞎毡，第二男磨毡角，皆叛其父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163179_comment'></div>瞎毡在河州，磨毡角与母安康郡君李氏在宗哥耶卑城住坐，分据土地部族，各立文法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163179_comment'></div>其磨毡角与夏国及邈川首领温郢成俞龙通和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163179_comment'></div>温郢成俞龙父温逋奇早年为唂厮啰所杀，结为世雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163179_comment'></div>有此三部分牵制，事力不得齐一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163179_comment'></div>嘉祐三年二月中，瞎毡、磨毡角并因患亡殁，各有子蒙朝廷补署承袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163179_comment'></div>又缘瞎毡长男木征，自父在日，即被青唐族蕃官瞎厮铎心并男瞎药勾扇，出离河州，见在近汉地名搮纳城居止，即未能统服蕃部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163179_comment'></div>其河州侧近虽有木征弟瞎吴叱等，系军主名目，亦无力量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163179_comment'></div>所有磨毡角男瞎只欺丁及祖母李氏，已与诸酋领归顺唂厮啰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163179_comment'></div>当年十二月，唂厮啰遂离本住青唐，即日见在宗哥耶卑城与李氏并瞎只欺丁同居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163179_comment'></div>其温郢成俞龙亦已于嘉祐四年四月因患亡殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163179_comment'></div>后来唂厮啰第三男董毡不住领人马攻劫郢成俞龙男温塌波讷令支地分，收降通斫令等城并人口孳畜不少，见更侵迫邈川城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163179_comment'></div>又自嘉祐五年秋冬至今年春以来，与夏戎连兵相持，多是董毡总率兵马斗战，屡次摧破，夏人枝梧不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163179_comment'></div>自去年夏秋，不住据沿边探报称，有西界首领忙迷等赍送金器、锦帛并骆驼般驮信物，赴唂厮啰投下，商量和断结婚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163179_comment'></div>夏戎屡遣使人，唂厮啰久未听许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163179_comment'></div>已上事节，臣已于嘉祐五年九月及嘉祐六年八月两次具状奏闻讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163179_comment'></div>缘秦州寨外熟户有顺汉者，有顺夏州者，有顺西蕃者，有并不顺属名生户者，参杂住坐，以此道路不通，商贾不行，自来只凭边寨蕃官体探事宜，所以难尽情实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163179_comment'></div>去秋窃闻夏戎遣首领诣阙，已是妄有邀求，大作点集，兵压秦境，其置寨处去边界止七八十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163179_comment'></div>威远、古渭熟户蕃部逃入山林，依险自固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163179_comment'></div>谓必乘势侵轶，不意渐却抽还，料是与唂厮啰和断未成，惧董毡乘虚袭其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163179_comment'></div>自后经冬以至今春，缘边探报二虏绝不复交兵，窃虑已是通和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163179_comment'></div>近复闻夏戎所遣使辄僭称官号，不循常礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163179_comment'></div>若二虏果通，恐遂搆边患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163179_comment'></div>又董毡娶契丹女为妻，契丹与西蕃本自异类，风马牛不相及，而忽万里通婚，情实不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163179_comment'></div>唐时吐蕃规图川蜀，以维州岩险，控其要害，遂潜将妇人嫁与此州阍者，而生二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163179_comment'></div>二十年后，蕃妇所生子为内应，开门以纳蕃兵，维州遂陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163179_comment'></div>臣详观西蕃，向时唂厮啰、瞎毡、磨毡角分据地界，各统部族，今既并合为一，力量足见强盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163179_comment'></div>又唂厮啰已是年老，一旦殂殁，董毡承袭，其人骁悍善斗战，已为众所服，而又连婚契丹，合从夏戎，臣恐边陲之忧，其所结连深固，阴谋交通，不可不过虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163179_comment'></div>前西事之时，寇兵虽不曾深入秦州境内，然昊贼犹尝略地至古渭，以唂厮啰不与之通，故不能定而还<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163179_comment'></div>迨兹事势，颇异当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163179_comment'></div>今勘会秦州管下所统蕃部蕃官一千五百馀人，诸族帐共一十九万八千有馀人骑，平时羁縻，外为屏蔽，若缓急欲纠合，不可恃以为用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163179_comment'></div>而西路诸部族率多富实，盖秦州南通巴蜀，控引诸蕃，自关中诸路商旅之所萃止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163179_comment'></div>又自展置古渭一带堡寨深在蕃界，蕃部交易为便，故货利凑集近里诸寨，城市为之寥索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163179_comment'></div>凡此皆所以召戎者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163179_comment'></div>但以向时未尝被寇，故守备诸事尤为因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163179_comment'></div>朝廷所遣偏裨将佐，颇比内地不出精选，驻泊禁军多见抽减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163179_comment'></div>即今见戍数虽不少，然秦州堡寨四十馀所，其系要害屯守处多，又本州寨户例皆单弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163179_comment'></div>臣自到任，常切招补，安存训练，然非泾原、环庆之比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163179_comment'></div>今戎狄之情衅已萌，是边镇预备之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163179_comment'></div>若夫抚和戎落，蒐补卒乘，缮完堡壁，除治器械，此边臣职分，敢不励力！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163179_comment'></div>至于绥怀戎狄，选练将帅，长策远御，事在岩庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163179_comment'></div>臣忝当方面，职思其忧，臆度事几，愧于愚短，谨具状奏闻，冀加图议。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1163179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1163179'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_30_1163179_0'>⑴ 昨修筑城寨时，古渭之人犹以为辞。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1163179_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　本年，在知秦州任，诱董毡入贡，为吴中复劾奏以擅以官爵许戎狄。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
东平（须城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='717135b7400d47869f4e0a21594d7e31_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("717135b7400d47869f4e0a21594d7e31");'><span id='717135b7400d47869f4e0a21594d7e31_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1065')">1064-1065年</a>，58-59岁</div><div id='717135b7400d47869f4e0a21594d7e31' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　本年，在知郓州任，识拔马默。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　本年，在知郓州任，为友人韩综作墓志铭。作品：朝奉郎尚书刑部员外郎知制诰同知审官院上骑都尉赐紫金鱼袋昌黎韩君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1163609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝奉郎尚书刑部员外郎知制诰同知审官院上骑都尉赐紫金鱼袋昌黎韩君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　治平二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163609")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163609'>仁宗朝国老韩忠宪公清德流光，实多才子，其第二子曰综，以文雅政事著名于时，而世家益显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163609_comment'></div>君字仲文，幼以父任将作监主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163609_comment'></div>忠宪领益州，奏授签书凤翔府判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163609_comment'></div>陇蜀间一都会，号烦剧，君试从事，吏文精敏，上官更荐其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163609_comment'></div>郡缺倅，君摄职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163609_comment'></div>时禁省灾，大兴缮修，仰材关右，赋诸州县，君督采伐丁夫冒寒山谷，时食而均其力，役不告劳，先期输送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163609_comment'></div>朝廷录其勤，将加恩，君推而不处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163609_comment'></div>新宫成，覃恩改太常寺太祝，寻迁大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163609_comment'></div>天圣八年，举进士擢第，除通判邓州，不行，领马步军专勾理、大理寺丞、充群牧判官，更通判天雄军，改殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163609_comment'></div>丞相吕许公镇魏，府事多以属君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163609_comment'></div>河水泛溢金堤，府县危迫，惧冲决为害，君请行营护之，濒河民徙就高丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163609_comment'></div>水大至，老弱号呼，君出令：能致一人予千钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163609_comment'></div>民操桴筏往救，悉得全济，水已冒丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163609_comment'></div>是日活数百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163609_comment'></div>许公复相，荐君文行宜在台阁，擢集贤校理、知太常礼院、开封府推官，赐五品服，太常博士、三司户部判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163609_comment'></div>忠宪公薨，去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163609_comment'></div>免丧还朝，同修起居注，判三司度支勾院，迁尚书祠部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163609_comment'></div>庆历六年，使契丹，容止酝藉，善占对，北主属目，使问系阀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163609_comment'></div>初，忠宪公在先北主世，亦尝奉使，君对及之，北主喜谓君：「二国通好，至于行人仍世将命，盍酌酒劝我」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163609_comment'></div>君请与同使者五人偕进，北主益喜，举觞爵，自离席就饮君及同使者各一卮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163609_comment'></div>君还奏事，执政非君不当辞，除知滑州，众论以为问及而言，无所辱命，将何谴！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163609_comment'></div>得徙知许州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163609_comment'></div>卫帅许怀德有田在属邑，讼久不决，因三司判官杨仪书嘱君，君不答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163609_comment'></div>仪别坐请求事，被诏推，辞上，当君不闻仪书，夺校理，徙知袁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163609_comment'></div>君无故再黜，士大夫为君不平，故君至袁州之月，复校理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163609_comment'></div>未几，就除江东转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163609_comment'></div>寻召还，复修起居注、判三司都磨勘司，改刑部员外郎，换度支勾院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163609_comment'></div>顷之，召试知制诰，赐服三品，知审官院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163609_comment'></div>审官自尚书省五品以下按籍除补中外员，而官簿无伦，吏缘为奸，君大为簿书，条次有序，至今用焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163609_comment'></div>契丹使来，君受命馆伴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163609_comment'></div>时北主通书，称北朝而去契丹号，意以自尊大，君诘之，谓曰：「自古未有建国而无号者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163609_comment'></div>北使愧屈，后遂复旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163609_comment'></div>皇祐四年五月暴疾不起，年四十五，时皆叹惜其才之未及用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163609_comment'></div>君既殁，契丹使来，有请于朝，择可遣报者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163609_comment'></div>仁宗识君前馆伴时语，谓左右曰：「若韩某在，足为朕办此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163609_comment'></div>追悼久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163609_comment'></div>君资孝悌，事忠宪公承颜无违，尽其诚志，怡怡其和也，懔懔其肃也，仕而在远，其心若未尝离膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163609_comment'></div>友于兄弟，爱顺无间，协睦内外姻族，莫不备尽情理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163609_comment'></div>善与人交，主忠信，致力其急难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163609_comment'></div>其行己立志，博而有守，约而有容，介不诡时，随不违正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163609_comment'></div>其莅官临事，推之己而不愿，不以施诸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163609_comment'></div>果于去弊，不以得情为明，亦可谓通人周材矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163609_comment'></div>忠宪公之配：安定太夫人蒲氏，遂宁郡太夫人王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163609_comment'></div>君，王氏出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163609_comment'></div>真皇庙宰相太尉文正公，外王父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163609_comment'></div>君娶刘氏，封寿安县君，先卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163609_comment'></div>三子：宗道，进士及第，今任太常博士，有行谊器识，克家者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163609_comment'></div>宗良、宗直，太常寺太祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163609_comment'></div>七女：适秘书丞刘攽，都官员外郎胥元衡，常州司理参军苏注，比部员外郎王景华，太常寺奉礼郎钱长卿，所从皆名族佳士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163609_comment'></div>二人幼，未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163609_comment'></div>治平二年乙巳某月某日，葬许州长社之嘉禾乡，从先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163609_comment'></div>宗道来请曰：「先人之交公最深，盍书铭」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163609_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1163609'>君孝于亲，友于兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163609_comment'></div>资以事君，忠诚自至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163609_comment'></div>与朋友交，实笃信义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163609_comment'></div>施之及民，政以慈惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163609_comment'></div>行成于身，既有本根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163609_comment'></div>发于事业，举逢其原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163609_comment'></div>措诸廊庙，王体以尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163609_comment'></div>率是承流，风俗乃敦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163609_comment'></div>吁嗟仲文，维本之得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163609_comment'></div>英华粹纯，用罔不适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163609_comment'></div>亦既遭时，已服近职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163609_comment'></div>足以有为，奚年之啬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163609_comment'></div>长社之原，嘉禾之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163609_comment'></div>先公亲卜，以启幽堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163609_comment'></div>君归可作，尚奉萧芗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163609_comment'></div>后人令人，君兮不忘。</div><div id='poem_sentence_67_1163609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　本年，在知郓州任，加翰林侍读学士，徙知定州，以亲老乞归养，改知徐州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　本年，在知郓州任，有诗寄曾公亮、赵概。作品：被命中山以亲老不赴书怀寄集贤曾公参政赵公。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《乐全集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_495421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>被命中山以亲老不赴书怀寄集贤曾公参政赵公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_495421")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495421'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495421'>野怀常逐白云飞，疏拙那能合世机。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495421'>偶似曹溪一宿觉，已多蘧瑗九年非。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495421'>略呈幻事何须了，惟愿朝恩早放归。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495421'>它日莲华峰下去，犹期话道过黄扉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495421'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495421_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　本年，在知郓州任，为友人时舜举作墓志铭。作品：将仕郎扬州司法参军时府君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《乐全集》卷三九。王智勇系此文于治平四年，据文中“今适守东平”云云，改系于治平二年。）</span><div id='poem_1163616' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1163616' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1163616?labeling=true' target='_blank'>将仕郎扬州司法参军时府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　治平四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25657, "北宋", "张方平", "poem_title_1163616")'>张方平</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1163616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1163616'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1163616'>府君讳□，字舜举，世著籍彭城之滕县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1163616_comment'></div>考旦，累典藩郡，以政事知名，终于尚书屯田郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1163616_comment'></div>君少举进士，以父任太庙斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1163616_comment'></div>不乐仕宦，学通古今，重意气然诺，四方之英才名士，多从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1163616_comment'></div>君虽隐居，常慨然而有忧世之志，见时事有未便者，辄以效于朝廷，不敢为私议，士大夫尤以此多之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1163616_comment'></div>仁宗始封升王，君至京师，上书请问言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1163616_comment'></div>章圣召对于便殿，进曰：「升王宜日侍御所，预闻政事，以资其聪明，且使天下早熟其睿闻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1163616_comment'></div>帝心喜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1163616_comment'></div>执政者曰：「位卑而言高，僭也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1163616_comment'></div>罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1163616_comment'></div>君曰：「致吾心而已矣，吾何求哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1163616_comment'></div>李文定与君雅厚，尝从容语，叹时人事，怨德已甚，且言「丁谓寘余于死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1163616_comment'></div>向余守洛，厚恤其家，谀我者构其子孙之罪，余反坐之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1163616_comment'></div>先是，刘随为谏官，以刚直忤时，摈于外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1163616_comment'></div>文定时作相，有不足于随者，不与之进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1163616_comment'></div>君因曰：「公之为德也，奚于正则否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1163616_comment'></div>文定曰：「正人为谁」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1163616_comment'></div>君曰：「刘随也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1163616_comment'></div>文定嘉纳其言，即迁随于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1163616_comment'></div>夏戎叛命，君复诣阙，上攻守之策十有二，谓所亲曰：「国家有事于边鄙，师久无功，天下共其劳，智者宜效其谋，勇者当致其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1163616_comment'></div>吾虽一命微且远，思虑所及，不可不自尽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1163616_comment'></div>故自官制、法令、国家货利、军储、马牧之事，有便于时，有救于敝者，罔不为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1163616_comment'></div>既以闻，而遂行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1163616_comment'></div>是时公卿重人如蔡文忠、范补之流辈十数公，皆与君交厚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1163616_comment'></div>富丞相在东平，欲辟君参佐，君曰：「吾老矣，不能事人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1163616_comment'></div>并帅孙元规复致意，亦以是辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1163616_comment'></div>嘉祐四年五月三日卒，年七十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1163616_comment'></div>君为人仁而尤孝，先君卒于京师，徒跣扶柩以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1163616_comment'></div>居乡里，恂恂如也，唯谨尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1163616_comment'></div>赀素赡而好施，羁旅之士造者如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1163616_comment'></div>人一见之，必曰长者也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1163616_comment'></div>而弥知其所存，必曰君子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1163616_comment'></div>矜寡废疾，日月给薪饩，冬予苧絮，岁饥，出粟赈乏绝，有遗稚乳于路，收而字之，多所济活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1163616_comment'></div>死不能举，为之衣榇，凡掩藏暴胔且数千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1163616_comment'></div>平生未尝断杀生物之命，昆虫草芥之细，莫之伤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1163616_comment'></div>将启手足，顾诸子训以孝悌忠恕，一不及于家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1163616_comment'></div>祖延岳，仕至国子博士，赠尚书都官员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1163616_comment'></div>母蒋氏，封晋陵县君，三娶阎氏、王氏、宋氏，皆先府君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1163616_comment'></div>子男五人：材，乡贡进士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1163616_comment'></div>尧，楚州司法参军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1163616_comment'></div>孝基，河南府渑池主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1163616_comment'></div>并亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1163616_comment'></div>德基，兴化军录事参军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1163616_comment'></div>世基，郊社斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1163616_comment'></div>八女：适尚书职方员外郎申屠正，光禄卿、直秘阁李及之，尚书都官郎中晁仲绰，兖州莱芜主簿苗总，尚书兵部员外郎兼起居舍人吕晦，国子博士孔承休，尚书职方员外郎何世昌，太常博士闾丘孝直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1163616_comment'></div>孙、曾孙十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1163616_comment'></div>在《易》，《乾》之四德，《文言》曰「贞者事之干」，「贞固足以干事」，君实有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1163616_comment'></div>故以此修身而修，治家而治，诚推而广之，是谓通才远业，足以经国阜民，独卷而怀之，足乎己而已尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1163616_comment'></div>仆昔游丰沛、山东，始见君于汶上，三纪于兹，熟君之风义久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1163616_comment'></div>今适守东平，而其子来请，欲以丁未某月某日葬君于县北之某乡，丐有以传后者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1163616_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1163616'>邹鲁之乡，士多儒服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1163616_comment'></div>洙泗之滨，已为楚俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1163616_comment'></div>滕介其间，实同风土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1163616_comment'></div>故君之材，质有文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1163616_comment'></div>学其远者，资亦逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1163616_comment'></div>一命家居，蕴不以施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1163616_comment'></div>秉义忼慨，数言世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1163616_comment'></div>与民同忧，匪躬之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1163616_comment'></div>以此为政，何用不臧？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1163616_comment'></div>岂夫不遭，我实未遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1163616_comment'></div>有孚惠心，愿无伐善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1163616_comment'></div>人斯忱斯，其微自显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1163616_comment'></div>我邦我里，幼无所养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1163616_comment'></div>至为鞠育，死归之壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1163616_comment'></div>谓天盖高，鉴于克仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1163616_comment'></div>君之受祉，非止其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1163616_comment'></div>子孙众多，必有兴者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1163616_comment'></div>遗德在人，盍配于社？</div><div id='poem_sentence_67_1163616_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

徐州（彭城）
